
-----title
桂林 (出生地)
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='4ca72923b8644f09b35bf8d0a40cdc0c_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("4ca72923b8644f09b35bf8d0a40cdc0c");'><span id='4ca72923b8644f09b35bf8d0a40cdc0c_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1137&endYear=1138')">1137-1138年</a>，1-2岁</div><div id='4ca72923b8644f09b35bf8d0a40cdc0c' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1137&endYear=1137')">1137年2月17日</a>　吕祖谦生。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1138&endYear=1138')">1138年</a>　曾几被罢，旋除广西转运副使，吕祖谦随外祖父离开桂林，徙荆南路。<br /></div>
-----end

id='poem_sentence_2_94055'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_94055_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: /></div><div class='label1' id='f76789d2a50f452a866e21bc3eccd863_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("f76789d2a50f452a866e21bc3eccd863");'><span id='f76789d2a50f452a866e21bc3eccd863_link' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年1月13日</a>　授严州桐庐县尉。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年1月23日</a>　长子岳孙出生，旋即夭折。<br ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年12月</a>　林之奇来访。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='133c9d97e0d84a5d8c9bd35c634c9f80_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("133c9d97e0d84a5d8c9bd35c634c9f80");'><span id='133c9d97e0d84a5d8c9bd35c634c9f80_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年3月28日</a>　归自临安。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年4月</a>　吕大器除知黄州，代父作谢表。作品：《代仓部知黄州谢表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷二。）</span>《代仓部知黄州谢宰执启》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷四。）</span>《代仓部知黄州通张魏公启》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷四。）</span>《代仓部知黄州谢从官启》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷四。）</span><div id='poem_1275119' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275119' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275119?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代仓部知黄州谢表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1162年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275119")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275119_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275119'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275119'>提边符而乘障，愧非御侮之材；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275119_comment'></div>佩郡绂以长民，莫称承流之寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275119_comment'></div>抚躬跼蹐，涖事凌兢<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275119_comment'></div>窃以群万国之舆图，大一王之统御。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275119_comment'></div>地分远迩之别，政有先后之差。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275119_comment'></div>繄牧守必得夫循良，则黔黎庶底乎康乂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275119_comment'></div>眷惟小垒，介于长淮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275119_comment'></div>虽事简而俗醇，实望轻而责重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275119_comment'></div>登览故迹，多名胜啸咏之馀；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275119_comment'></div>参考前闻，亦豪杰驰驱之旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275119_comment'></div>肆求其理，必柬异能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275119_comment'></div>如臣者朴拙孤踪，凋残遗族。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275119_comment'></div>冥心造化，已绝意于紫青；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275119_comment'></div>屈首簿书，第研精于朱墨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275119_comment'></div>偶滥尘于论荐，遂误畀于蕃宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275119_comment'></div>自揣庸虚，若为称塞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275119_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下锡天勇智，受命溥将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1275119_comment'></div>日月光华，悉在照临之下；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1275119_comment'></div>乾坤高厚，咸归覆焘之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1275119_comment'></div>凡兹铜虎之颁，尤谨玉关之戍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1275119_comment'></div>曾何疏贱，亦预选抡！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1275119_comment'></div>臣敢不宣布诏条，辑宁闾里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1275119_comment'></div>挈瓶守器，誓力保于封陲；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1275119_comment'></div>毁瓦画墁，敢坐縻于廪禄！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1275119_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1275119_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1275470' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275470' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275470?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代仓部知黄州谢宰执启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1162年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275470")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275470_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275470'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275470'>点近臣之荐牍，内愧疏庸；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275470_comment'></div>佩边垒之守符，外分忧顾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275470_comment'></div>俯微躬而怵惕，仰洪造以归依。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275470_comment'></div>窃观云梦之南州，素号江淮之要地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275470_comment'></div>黄堂胜概，传王、杜之风流；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275470_comment'></div>赤壁威声，想曹、刘之雄烈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275470_comment'></div>会启恢图之运，实当控扼之冲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275470_comment'></div>疏亭障以制襟喉，远烽燧以明耳目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275470_comment'></div>辑宁封部，储峙刍粮，拊凋瘵而民气苏，严赏罚而士心奋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275470_comment'></div>有此数者，当求通济之才；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275470_comment'></div>岂无他人，独预蕃宣之寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275470_comment'></div>如某者禀资甚薄，涉世多奇，费日月于簿书，窘风霜于邮传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275470_comment'></div>锥处囊而立见，自愧无闻；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275470_comment'></div>金跃冶而不祥，益思难进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275470_comment'></div>崎岖末路，踸踔穷途。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275470_comment'></div>肆法宫轸共理之良，而从橐受举贤之诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275470_comment'></div>遽尘论奏，偶成误墨之蝇；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1275470_comment'></div>滥被选抡，岂称乘轓之鹿！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1275470_comment'></div>叨逾若此，报效阙然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1275470_comment'></div>此盖伏遇某官名世真儒，际天奥学，冠压群公之表，典司大政之元。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1275470_comment'></div>远至迩安，罔间重轻之势；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1275470_comment'></div>出长入治，兼收钜细之能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1275470_comment'></div>凡畀付于郡条，必参稽于舆诵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1275470_comment'></div>于何椎钝，亦费陶镕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1275470_comment'></div>某敢不力务中行，勉求实效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1275470_comment'></div>措诸事业，愿师三折肱之医；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1275470_comment'></div>畏此简书，莫伸九顿首之礼。</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1275470_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1275472' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275472' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275472?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代仓部知黄州通张魏公启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1162年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275472")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275472_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275472'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275472'>仰夫子之门墙，夙有依归之愿；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275472_comment'></div>瞻元戎之旌纛，获承节制之尊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275472_comment'></div>敢以丹诚，寓之缃简。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275472_comment'></div>恭惟某官佐王硕辅，命世真儒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275472_comment'></div>先知觉后知，传斯文之正统；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275472_comment'></div>小德役大德，为善类之宗盟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275472_comment'></div>扶日毂于庆霄，握斗枢于宥府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275472_comment'></div>入则赞一日万几之务，出则专五侯九伯之征。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275472_comment'></div>震叠龙荒，焜煌麟阁，处消息盈虚之变，适行藏进退之宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275472_comment'></div>肆琴瑟之更张，首弓车之聘召。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275472_comment'></div>献言申戒，避宠就闲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275472_comment'></div>羽檄交驰，旧疏果符于龟策；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275472_comment'></div>玺书狎至，陪都载绾于麟符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275472_comment'></div>当虞舜之四巡，延晋文之三觐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275472_comment'></div>运筹坐胜，聚精会神，锡鈇钺以抚师，总江淮而分陕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275472_comment'></div>落毡裘之危胆，沸鹖弁之欢谣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275472_comment'></div>旗帜精明，鼓角欢亮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1275472_comment'></div>国家再造，高鸿烈于汾阳；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1275472_comment'></div>天地重开，翊丕图于建武。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1275472_comment'></div>冠钧衡于廊庙，下膏泽于幅员。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1275472_comment'></div>若智若愚，以祷以颂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1275472_comment'></div>某荒芜晚学，蹭蹬孤踪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1275472_comment'></div>每原念于衰宗，常屡投于化冶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1275472_comment'></div>志勤事左，心亲地疏，误分边垒之忧，幸效辕门之役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1275472_comment'></div>虽迹遥履舄，莫伸罄折之恭；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1275472_comment'></div>然气激肺肝，窃效钟鸣之应。</div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1275472_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1275471' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275471' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275471?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代仓部知黄州谢从官启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1162年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275471")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275471_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275471'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275471'>岸江之壤，条教用希；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275471_comment'></div>被边之州，忧虞实重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275471_comment'></div>曾是迂疏之质，膺兹推择之馀，庀事有初，抚躬无所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275471_comment'></div>窃以填拊凋残之俗，辑宁荒远之区，参稽前闻，具载成绩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275471_comment'></div>卫文大布，马遂至于三千；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275471_comment'></div>羊祜轻裘，田爰开于八百。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275471_comment'></div>克绥疲瘵，于变富强。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275471_comment'></div>阙然近世之亡称，邈矣风流之将绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275471_comment'></div>怯者拘小文而牵制，诞者张空簿以浮夸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275471_comment'></div>井邑萧条，版图湮坠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275471_comment'></div>岂特威权之素夺，正唯劳来之不先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275471_comment'></div>匪求循吏之能，孰还平世之旧？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275471_comment'></div>如某者秉心椎鲁，降命奇穷，才能不及于中庸，名实未加于上下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275471_comment'></div>问羊问马，既乏于政声；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275471_comment'></div>学箕学裘，又颓于世业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275471_comment'></div>敢居迩列，误玷荐书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275471_comment'></div>严虎落以捍城，任当御侮；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1275471_comment'></div>佩鱼符而临众，责在长民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1275471_comment'></div>合是两端，萃于一己，凌兢拜命，黾勉效官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1275471_comment'></div>靖言忝冒之由，实出帡幪之庇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1275471_comment'></div>恭惟某官留意人物，尽忠国家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1275471_comment'></div>乐拔茅连茹之多，举无遗善；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1275471_comment'></div>思采葑下体之略，恕不求全。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1275471_comment'></div>凡宣化以承流，必集长而去短。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1275471_comment'></div>故斯孱陋，亦玷使令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1275471_comment'></div>某敢不外饬营屯，内齐封部。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1275471_comment'></div>形格势禁，庶成襟带之勋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1275471_comment'></div>仁渐义摩，敢望裤襦之咏！</div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1275471_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年6月7日</a>　次子齐孙出生。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='cb328292c6324e7a9784d89e54ee83ed_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("cb328292c6324e7a9784d89e54ee83ed");'><span id='cb328292c6324e7a9784d89e54ee83ed_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年</a>，26岁</div><div id='cb328292c6324e7a9784d89e54ee83ed' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年8月</a>　以韩氏丧归婺州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年9月26日</a>　归葬韩氏于武义县明招山。韩元吉有墓志。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年9月</a>　次子齐孙夭折。<br /></div>
-----end

-----title
绍兴

-----title
福州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='6a4550daa4ea4fd8acdeb0aacc1ef263_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("6a4550daa4ea4fd8acdeb0aacc1ef263");'><span id='6a4550daa4ea4fd8acdeb0aacc1ef263_link' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1155&endYear=1155')">1155年</a>　吕大器为福建提刑司干官，吕祖谦待次汀州长汀尉，随父在福唐。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1155&endYear=1155')">1155年3月</a>　从林之奇学《论语》、《孟子》及古文，林之奇许以“远且大”<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1155&endYear=1155')">1155年</a>　结识李樗。为林之奇《观澜文集》作集注类编、为李樗、黄櫄《毛诗集解》作音义。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1155&endYear=1155')">1155年</a>　已有声名，与朱熹相识。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1156&endYear=1156')">1156年</a>　应福建转运司进士举，为首选。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='62ff62b4c913453cb426562088c2a5cc_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("62ff62b4c913453cb426562088c2a5cc");'><span id='62ff62b4c913453cb426562088c2a5cc_link' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1157&endYear=1157')">1157年夏</a>　有诗。作品：《夏日》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷一。）</span><div id='poem_94061' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_94061' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/94061?labeling=true' target='_blank'>夏日<span class='inlineComment2'>（婺绍兴二十七年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1157年夏）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_94061")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_94061_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_94061'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_94061'>阶前水乐元无谱，檐外风琴不用弦。<div id='poem_sentence_0_94061_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_94061'>待唤青奴与黄奶，为君极意作今年。<div id='poem_sentence_1_94061_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_94061'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_94061_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
杭州

class='poemContent' id='poem_content_94140'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_94140'>许由不耐事，逃尧独参寥。<div id='poem_sentence_0_94140_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_94140'>行至箕山下，盈耳康衢谣。<div id='poem_sentence_1_94140_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_94140'>谓此污我耳，临流洗尘嚣。<div id='poem_sentence_2_94140_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_94140'>水中见日驭，劳苦如尧朝。<div id='poem_sentence_3_94140_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_94140'>尧天接山际，尧云抹山椒。<div id='poem_sentence_4_94140_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_94140'>谁云能避世，处处悉逢尧。<div id='poem_sentence_1_94157_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_94157'>林端横宿霭，未放群山青。<div id='poem_sentence_2_94157_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_94157'>藕花断复续，莫辨浦与汀。<div id='poem_sentence_3_94157_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_94157'>初闻露花香，一洗廛市腥。<div id='poem_sentence_4_94157_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_94157'>清景竟难挽，晨光著邮亭。<div id='poem_sentence_5_94157_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_94157_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_94157'>凉燠一机耳，愠喜谁使令。<div id='poem_sentence_8_94157_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_94157_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_94112' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_94112' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/94112?labeling=true' id='poem_content_94112'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_94112'>城峻先迎月，帘疏不隔风。<div id='poem_sentence_0_94112_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_94112'>棋声传下界，雁影没长空。<div id='poem_sentence_1_94112_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_94112'>岛屿秋光里，楼台海气中。<div id='poem_sentence_2_94112_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_94112'>登临故待晚，雨外夕阳红。<div id='poem_sentence_3_94112_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_94112'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_94112_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1157&endYear=1157')">1157年春</a>　试礼部，不中。赴铨试，得下等第三人。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='1f46917f262542689c47cca24fc939b0_label'><a href='javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1160&endYear=1160')">1160年6月</a>　赴临安铨试，上等第二人。馆于伯舅粮料院曾逢寓舍。始师事汪应辰、胡宪。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='51ddeb0307f54934b5b84678844e453d_label'><a href='javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年3月</a>　在临安。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='8ac83f62fc594097beb6a98ed799663d_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("8ac83f62fc594097beb6a98ed799663d");'><span id='8ac83f62fc594097beb6a98ed799663d_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年</a>，26岁</div><div id='8ac83f62fc594097beb6a98ed799663d' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年6月23日</a>　韩氏妻卒于临安，吕祖谦自绍兴赴临安。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='bb0a6e935b664696b09c2d74184136f4_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("bb0a6e935b664696b09c2d74184136f4");'><span id='bb0a6e935b664696b09c2d74184136f4_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1163')">1162-1163年</a>，26-27岁</div><div id='bb0a6e935b664696b09c2d74184136f4' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年</a>　与陈亮同试漕台，结下友谊。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1163&endYear=1163')">1163年春</a>　试礼部，奏名第六人。与潘景宪、丘崇、楼钥、袁枢、詹仪之、赵雄、黄度等为同年。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1163&endYear=1163')">1163年4月12日</a>　赐进士及第，改左迪功郎。又中博学宏词科。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1163&endYear=1163')">1163年春</a>　有《策问》两卷，《宏词进卷》两卷。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1163&endYear=1163')">1163年春</a>　作谢启谢两科主司。作品：《中两科谢主司启》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷四。）</span><div id='poem_1275481' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275481' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275481?labeling=true' target='_blank'>中两科谢主司启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1163年春）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275481")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275481_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275481'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275481'>问津邹、鲁，未知经术之渊源；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275481_comment'></div>学步班、扬，讵识词章之统纪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275481_comment'></div>揣己初无于一可，逢辰乃幸于兼收，得之若惊，荣不盖愧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275481_comment'></div>窃以自昔广招贤之路，若时开入仕之门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275481_comment'></div>众俊朋来，烝髦辐集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275481_comment'></div>略于始进，罔拘流品之浊清；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275481_comment'></div>考以终身，徐待是非之坚定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275481_comment'></div>故上无甚重甚轻之弊，而下无必贵必贱之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275481_comment'></div>气俗敦庬，风声醇厚，高弗以此自满，卑弗以此自惭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275481_comment'></div>道丧质衰，辞繁用寡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275481_comment'></div>执笔操牍，阔视承明之庐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275481_comment'></div>蹑蹻担簦，平步高门之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275481_comment'></div>一升俊造之列，即为腾耀之阶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275481_comment'></div>指日而须，若偿所负。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275481_comment'></div>虽怀经济之蕴，堕在冗散之流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275481_comment'></div>抗颜议事为病狂，刺口论文为犯分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275481_comment'></div>仰望云汉，邈无津涯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1275481_comment'></div>异意者方痛诋而力排，知己者特熟视而窃叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1275481_comment'></div>彼此之势既激，怨隙之萌遂形。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1275481_comment'></div>间生英豪，大振颓靡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1275481_comment'></div>邓攸在晋，不去王官而举孝廉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1275481_comment'></div>德裕仕唐，耻与诸生而从乡试。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1275481_comment'></div>夫岂厌清华之选，又非避博雅之名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1275481_comment'></div>察其所存，则亦有说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1275481_comment'></div>盖欲安常业于夸诩之际，抑浇风于奔竞之馀，示以不争，固将自反。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1275481_comment'></div>惟国朝发进士之举，肆绍圣立宏词之科。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1275481_comment'></div>屈、宋比肩，渊、骞接袂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1275481_comment'></div>然观抑扬之深意，少知阖辟之微权。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1275481_comment'></div>柳崇仪素号儒宗，晚纾武弁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1275481_comment'></div>韩黄门奋由世禄，尝主文闱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1275481_comment'></div>俾于陟降之间，莫见厚薄之迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1275481_comment'></div>凡名为士，当识此心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1275481_comment'></div>如某者章句谀闻，箕裘衰绪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1275481_comment'></div>信书滞固，几类鲁人之皋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1275481_comment'></div>涉世舒迟，殆同齐俗之缓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1275481_comment'></div>妄睎畯轨，辄簉词场。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1275481_comment'></div>千里驱驰，变星霜于邮传；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1275481_comment'></div>连年胶扰，付编简于尘埃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1275481_comment'></div>以椎鲁僻陋之资，加废忘捍格之久，应敌类夏侯之疏略，序事多马迁之繁芜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1275481_comment'></div>敢梦寐于末行，矧觊觎于叠中？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1275481_comment'></div>顾浅缪如此其极，犹且得之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1275481_comment'></div>谓奇杰必出于斯，亦以疏矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1275481_comment'></div>论科目之难尚，至鄙贱而益明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1275481_comment'></div>独惭驽蹇之踪，上致权衡之误。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1275481_comment'></div>此盖伏遇某官典司文柄，培养化源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1275481_comment'></div>为桷为杗，坐致群材之用；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1275481_comment'></div>采葑采菲，每思下体之遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1275481_comment'></div>旁及孱愚，亦容忝冒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1275481_comment'></div>某谨当服膺古训，尚志前修。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1275481_comment'></div>书子张之绅，力行笃敬；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1275481_comment'></div>锄不疑之色，深戒骄矜。</div><div id='poem_sentence_50_1275481_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1163&endYear=1163')">1163年6月7日</a>　以连中两科特授左从政郎，改差南外敦宗院宗学教授。未赴任。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='18efe53c749d4645b1d27ce3fc1e44e8_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("18efe53c749d4645b1d27ce3fc1e44e8");'><span id='18efe53c749d4645b1d27ce3fc1e44e8_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1164&endYear=1164')">1164年</a>，28岁</div><div id='18efe53c749d4645b1d27ce3fc1e44e8' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>侍父自黄州赴临安奏事。<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>张浚卒，代父作祭文。作品：《代仓部祭张魏公文》<div id='poem_1275688' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275688' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275688?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代仓部祭张魏公文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1164年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275688")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275688_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275688'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275688'>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275688_comment'></div>鼎分三极，中贯至诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275688_comment'></div>扶世建俗，经幽纬明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275688_comment'></div>明此北面，庞臣鸿弼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275688_comment'></div>侯皋侯夔，侯旦侯奭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275688_comment'></div>前援后承，皆原于一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275688_comment'></div>降秦迄唐，中间几息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275688_comment'></div>既极乃通，是开魏公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275688_comment'></div>有远其传，有统其宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275688_comment'></div>匪符匪节，匪券而同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275688_comment'></div>厥初事亲，自诚而孝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275688_comment'></div>基德寝门，参骞是蹈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275688_comment'></div>肆其事君，自诚而忠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275688_comment'></div>四朝一心，本始末终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275688_comment'></div>昔在建炎，为国驰骛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275688_comment'></div>蟊贼内讧，将祲天路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275688_comment'></div>乃义其旗，驰囊走羽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1275688_comment'></div>爝彼妖焰，万河并注。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1275688_comment'></div>扫除黄道，手扶日驭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1275688_comment'></div>勾陈太微，莫不顺序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1275688_comment'></div>始命枢极，再命台衡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1275688_comment'></div>柄是文武，内拊外征。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1275688_comment'></div>我雨我露，我雷我霆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1275688_comment'></div>熛起蜂屯，随指而平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1275688_comment'></div>区脱之酋，毡毳之渠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1275688_comment'></div>威名所加，失戈堕车。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1275688_comment'></div>既其无为，里忻户愉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1275688_comment'></div>群献具来，翼帝之图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1275688_comment'></div>熟柅其成，放迹江湖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1275688_comment'></div>已贵不贱，已丰不约。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1275688_comment'></div>零陵之居，韦布所愕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1275688_comment'></div>披剥万象，独全至乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1275688_comment'></div>身外鸾台，梦中麟阁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1275688_comment'></div>戎马饮江，夺公閒燕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1275688_comment'></div>臣毂高幢，陪都是殿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1275688_comment'></div>大人继明，登我元臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1275688_comment'></div>尔衮尔钺，坯冶载新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1275688_comment'></div>瞋目语难，熊罴貔虎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1275688_comment'></div>闻公之升，屯歌垒舞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1275688_comment'></div>野耕肆商，秀眉垂髫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1275688_comment'></div>闻公之升，连手嬉遨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1275688_comment'></div>北边有兴，祃牙祭纛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1275688_comment'></div>志之所期，欲无遐徼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1275688_comment'></div>挈舆地图，还之清庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1275688_comment'></div>炯炯丹衷，日月所照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1275688_comment'></div>帝闵公劳，佚以殊廷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1275688_comment'></div>歘骑箕尾，上比列星。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1275688_comment'></div>殄瘁之悲，五方同声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1275688_comment'></div>某顷以孱陋，远戍边城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1275688_comment'></div>敌情叵测，民力弗胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1275688_comment'></div>条利画病，狂言屡兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1275688_comment'></div>朝扣暮应，是奖是称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1275688_comment'></div>筹恩权惠，丘山犹轻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1275688_comment'></div>几几赤舄，庶几快睹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1275688_comment'></div>未目德辉，已耳凶讣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1275688_comment'></div>扁舟西还，飞旐南去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1275688_comment'></div>只鸡斗酒，莫展情素。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1275688_comment'></div>公视死生，犹旦与暮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1275688_comment'></div>一气阖辟，新新故故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1275688_comment'></div>默友造物，冒此下土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1275688_comment'></div>我独何为，泪落彫俎。</div><div id='poem_sentence_60_1275688_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1275688'><span class='label'>按：</span>《东莱吕太史文集》卷八。又见清抄一百五十卷本《圣宋名贤五百家播芳大全文粹》卷一三四，《金华文徵》卷一八。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1275688_comment'></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1'
