href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年</a>，31岁</div><div id='c0fc5d8909cb42bf80a29fd1f38e800c' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年4月</a>　如临安省父。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='cd92abcc89c345cd93df35f94ecffb1f_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("cd92abcc89c345cd93df35f94ecffb1f");'><span id='cd92abcc89c345cd93df35f94ecffb1f_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1170')">1169-1170年</a>，33-34岁</div><div id='cd92abcc89c345cd93df35f94ecffb1f' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年10月18日</a>　之官严州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年10月21日</a>　到官交接事务，有《通柳严州启》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷四。）</span><div id='poem_1275483' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275483' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275483?labeling=true' target='_blank'>通柳严州启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1169年10月21日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275483")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275483_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275483'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275483'>奉几杖于双清，久托通家之旧；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275483_comment'></div>职简编于半水，幸陪属吏之馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275483_comment'></div>揆日俶装，指期敛板。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275483_comment'></div>窃以内外学官之设，举选昔均；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275483_comment'></div>远近阙次之差，流冗今极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275483_comment'></div>弊云甚矣，议者厌之，乃思改命之图，乃下增员之令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275483_comment'></div>参其资格，既无退绌之嫌；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275483_comment'></div>赋以饩牵，复免滞淹之叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275483_comment'></div>矧席帡幪之庇，曲容铅椠之寒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275483_comment'></div>如某者受性颛愚，降材椎钝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275483_comment'></div>晚菘早韭，夙屏迹于丘樊；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275483_comment'></div>朝齑暮盐，偶得官于庠序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275483_comment'></div>前顾瓜期之邈，方私家食之安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275483_comment'></div>清庶寀于中都，占閒曹于近甸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275483_comment'></div>魏舒襆被，固窃自量；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275483_comment'></div>孙宝请邻，夫何不满！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275483_comment'></div>重恃眷怜之素，预宽旷败之忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1275483_comment'></div>恭惟某官德峻儒宗，望隆民表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1275483_comment'></div>温恭有恪，历夷险以不渝；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1275483_comment'></div>悃愊无华，冠蕃宣而独最。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1275483_comment'></div>每奖成于后辈，荷长育之深诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1275483_comment'></div>敢意孱庸，亦供指顾！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1275483_comment'></div>某趋承惟迩，闿怿倍增。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1275483_comment'></div>贡彝礼于缄縢，顾惭拙讷；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1275483_comment'></div>溯馀光于棨戟，罙切战兢。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1275483_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年10月</a>　到官交接事务，有《通严州郑教授启》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷四。）</span><div id='poem_1275484' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275484' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275484?labeling=true' target='_blank'>通严州郑教授启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1169年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275484")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275484_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275484'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275484'>宦牒推移，阙然觌德；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275484_comment'></div>郡庠诵说，幸矣亲仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275484_comment'></div>敢凭竿牍之传，先效门阑之敬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275484_comment'></div>窃以营道同术之谓友，联事合治之谓僚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275484_comment'></div>惟此两端，难乎共贯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275484_comment'></div>尊罍啸咏，每多离合之嗟；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275484_comment'></div>几案鞭笞，岂复渐摩之暇！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275484_comment'></div>至若有编简讨论之益，无簿书期会之烦，允谓难并，厥惟至愿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275484_comment'></div>恭惟某官闳材英发，奥学精微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275484_comment'></div>心追游、夏之渊源，笔掞卿、云之黼黻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275484_comment'></div>词林艺圃，撷百氏之菁华；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275484_comment'></div>隽轨英躔，冠诸儒之领袖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275484_comment'></div>小淹泮水，行践石渠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275484_comment'></div>及召驷之未驱，尚均茵之少遂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275484_comment'></div>某甫兹捧檄，行即升阶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275484_comment'></div>渴闻教载之馀，涤去颛蒙之蔽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275484_comment'></div>坐縻廪稍，预怀骈拇枝指之惭；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1275484_comment'></div>日接官曹，将丐补劓息黥之赐。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1275484_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年10月</a>　赴严州州学教授任，整顿学舍。远近士人多来从学。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年10月</a>　书约潘景宪来严州。作品：《答潘叔度》二十七。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷十。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年10月</a>　始取经史诸书其事可为法者编《阃范》以教导生徒。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年10月</a>　闻张栻将除严州，有书两通，冀早日成行。作品：《与张荆州》一。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷七。）</span>《答张荆州》二。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷七。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年10月</a>　合朱熹校订《伊川易传》与家中旧藏尹焞标注《易传》而校，交周汝能、楼锷等在东阳刊出。作《书校本伊川先生易传后》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷七。）</span><div id='poem_1275511' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275511' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275511?labeling=true' target='_blank'>书校本伊川先生易传后</a><span class='authorDate'>（1169年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275511")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275511_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275511'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275511'>伊川先生遗言见于世者，独《易传》为成书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275511_comment'></div>传摹浸舛，失其本真，学者病之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275511_comment'></div>某旧所藏本，出尹和靖先生家，标注皆和靖亲笔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275511_comment'></div>近复得新安朱熹元晦所订，雠校精甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275511_comment'></div>遂合尹氏、朱氏书，与一二同志手自参定，其同异两存之，以待知者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275511_comment'></div>既又从小学家是正其文字。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275511_comment'></div>虽未敢谓无遗恨，视诸本亦或庶几焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275511_comment'></div>会稽周汝能尧夫、鄮山楼锷景山，方职教东阳，乃取刊诸学官。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1275511_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年10月</a>　作学规《乾道五年十月关诸州在籍人》七条。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷五《家范五·学规》）</span><div id='poem_1275622' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275622' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275622?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乾道五年十月关诸州在籍人</a><span class='authorDate'>（1169年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275622")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275622_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275622'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275622'>一、在籍人将来通书止用一幅，不许用虚礼<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275622_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1275622'>一、通书不许用劄目，不许改名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275622_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1275622'>一、通书止许商搉所疑，自叙实事<span class='inlineComment2'>（谓自叙出入行止之类。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275622_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1275622'>一、通书不许以币帛玩物为信<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275622_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1275622'>一、在籍人将来相见，不用名纸门状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275622_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1275622'>一、在籍人不幸有丧，仰同州同县在籍人依规矩吊慰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275622_comment'></div>仍具书寻便报知堂上，道路虽远，无过半年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275622_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_1275622'>一、在籍人如有不遵士检，玷辱斋舍，同籍人规责不悛者，仰连名具书报知堂上，当行除籍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275622_comment'></div>如共为隐蔽，异时恶声彰闻，或冒犯刑法，同州同县人并受隐蔽之罚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275622_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1275622'>右关诸州在籍人，各仰递相传报遵守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275622_comment'></div>年月日，掌仪位关。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1275622_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1275622'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_0_1275622_0'>⑴ 谓如「学际天人」及「即膺召用」、「台候神相」、「百拜」、过呼官职之类。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_1275622_1'>⑵ 玩谓图画及几案玩具，物谓研扇凡什物之类。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1275622_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年10月</a>　代刘夙作《祭忠简赵公文》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《五百家播芳大全文粹》卷九十四。）</span><div id='poem_1275690' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275690' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275690?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代刘衢州祭赵忠简公文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1168年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275690")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275690_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275690'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275690'>惟公高风懿躅，照映今昔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275690_comment'></div>下自管葛，所在不数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275690_comment'></div>中遭谗逐，以卒于死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275690_comment'></div>下至行路，为公出涕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275690_comment'></div>不三十年，是非一定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275690_comment'></div>中兴名相，一夔而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275690_comment'></div>有来假守，敢言尚德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275690_comment'></div>南望楸梧，去我百里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275690_comment'></div>官箴有常，莫克敬告。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275690_comment'></div>归心典刑，有如卮酒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275690_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1275690_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年10月</a>　应门人毛大年请，为其父作墓志铭。作品：《金华毛君将仕墓志铭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷十。）</span><div id='poem_1275645' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275645' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275645?labeling=true' target='_blank'>金华毛君将仕墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（乾道五年十月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275645")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275645_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275645'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275645'>毛在衢以姓著，君故衢徙也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275645_comment'></div>始君曾大父广，名数籍衢之江山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275645_comment'></div>大父达，游金华，乐土风迁焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275645_comment'></div>父扆，宣和间材进士，娄上礼部，留落无所遇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275645_comment'></div>君甫学而孤，不忍以门内细故忧母夫人，置其业，躬井臼劳事，纲理勤甚，细大咸有节法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275645_comment'></div>资简朴，与人语，倾尽无留藏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275645_comment'></div>女弟以嫠归君，终君之世，字其孤不怠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275645_comment'></div>兄之子大方，稚失父，君使偕其子学，程督提掖，姻族莫能名厚薄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275645_comment'></div>其将殁也，诸子前受所欲言，独饬以学，不它属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275645_comment'></div>君讳公亮，字明叔，卒年四十有六，乾道三年十一月十有二日也，娶陈氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275645_comment'></div>子四，良能、大年、大节、大任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275645_comment'></div>女五，长适进士邢文昌，馀未行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275645_comment'></div>乾道五年十月二十有四日，葬于智者山之右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275645_comment'></div>先葬，大年迹君之实来谒铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275645_comment'></div>予虽未尝与君际，然大方、大年俱从予讲画，且联里闬，是宜铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275645_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_1275645'>阳宇阴竁，诞惟民彝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275645_comment'></div>遹严厥终，铭以昭之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1275645_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年</a>　整顿学政，革除旧弊。与潘景宪等书信，督其缮写《程氏易传》作品：《答潘叔度》一。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史外集》卷五。）</span>《与学者及诸弟》二。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷十。）</span><div id='poem_1275412' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275412' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275412?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与学者及诸弟书<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1169年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275412")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275412_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275412'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275412'>诸友来，收书，知比来为况安适。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275412_comment'></div>某官次粗遣，他无足言者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275412_comment'></div>仲益送到《同窗录》，已收。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275412_comment'></div>课程只须如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275412_comment'></div>《中庸》且专看龟山解为佳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275412_comment'></div>纯夫只就侍旁开会，甚得策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275412_comment'></div>欲求繁冗中不妨课程之术，古人每言「整暇」二字，盖整则暇矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275412_comment'></div>颖叔在下塘，良便近，日玩绎何书？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275412_comment'></div>学问以致知为本，知不至则行必不力也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275412_comment'></div>叔度兄弟，丧礼更与讲论，有疑即报来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275412_comment'></div>元晦所干若毕，早趣装为善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275412_comment'></div>少望临安之行在何时？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275412_comment'></div>经由毋惜为数日留。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275412_comment'></div>张守引进士子，孳孳不倦，又此间诸公问学者亦多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275412_comment'></div>张守馆客吴翌晦叔，向与张守同师胡先生，不从事科举已二十年，议论操履甚平正，相处亦有益也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275412_comment'></div>子先所问，已见叔度书中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275412_comment'></div>来严陵受《葬仪》，本无嫌疑，盖叔度兄弟岂世俗富家比！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1275412_comment'></div>况来此间又非往它处也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1275412_comment'></div>要先须遣人往张伯安处，取向日《葬仪》，携来参酌为善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1275412_comment'></div>《仪礼疏》旬日间有便先寄来，此间无借处也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1275412_comment'></div>天锡辞朱氏馆，量而后入，政当如此，今莫已有定所否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1275412_comment'></div>今岁曾作文字，因便寄一二篇，然为学要须日用间实下工夫乃得力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1275412_comment'></div>城中如叔度、叔昌兄弟，及颖叔、德奉、子先、仲益、季益诸人，皆可往还也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1275412_comment'></div>天锡如见叶秀实，为致意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1275412_comment'></div>近日读书不辍否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1275412_comment'></div>有近作亦可寄数篇来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1275412_comment'></div>今因人回，略此为问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1275412_comment'></div>它惟力学自爱。</div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1275412_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年11月</a>　作与诸弟书，强调提倡实学，移俗美政。作品：《与学者及诸弟》三。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷十。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年11月</a>　郡庠渐得整顿。蒋从道卒，致书慰问并作祭文。作品：《答潘叔度》二十八。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷十。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年11月</a>　蒋从道卒，为作祭文。作品：《祭蒋从道文》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷八。）</span><div id='poem_1275692' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275692' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275692?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭蒋从道文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1169年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275692")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275692_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275692'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275692'>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275692_comment'></div>弁服之襜然，弦歌之锵然，子游其间兮，呻吟挟策而累然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275692_comment'></div>贾区之嚣然，怪珍之错然，子庐其间兮，讲诵下帷而嗒然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275692_comment'></div>貌甚癯兮志则坚，力既惫兮道方邅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275692_comment'></div>出门轴折兮，沦昼景于虞渊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275692_comment'></div>大块噫兮化机旋，森回薄兮纷纠缠，夭寿不贰兮又奚怨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275692_comment'></div>猗朋游兮昔蝉联，交一臂兮失九泉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275692_comment'></div>跽传觞兮江之壖，暮山合兮横苍烟。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1275692_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年11月</a>　程《易》在婺州付梓。有《答潘叔度》书，邀潘景宪、潘景愈兄弟来严州。三。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史外集》卷五。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年11月</a>　有《通张严州启》，陈乡风之情。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷四。）</span><div id='poem_1275485' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275485' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275485?labeling=true' target='_blank'>通张严州启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1169年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275485")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275485_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275485'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275485'>伏审温诏起家，仁声先路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275485_comment'></div>四封欢动，不胜朝夕之思；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275485_comment'></div>一世瞻观，独任春秋之责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275485_comment'></div>敬陈悃愊，上彻崇严。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275485_comment'></div>恭惟某官传世精忠，潜心正学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275485_comment'></div>弥纶开济，尚期素定于胸中；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275485_comment'></div>牧养拊摩，夫亦何劳于掌上！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275485_comment'></div>然君子之诚本无息，而儒者之效久不明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275485_comment'></div>在昔诸贤，固尝有志，或远近未孚而夺于时命，或内外未合而窒于物情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275485_comment'></div>讥评交兴，疑信相半，思少伸于此恨，顾将付于何人？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275485_comment'></div>历访缙绅，咸推墙仞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275485_comment'></div>惟魏国既行而复尼，惟衡山有韫而莫施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275485_comment'></div>今兹一来，任是二责，实系斯文之兴废，岂徒阖境之戚休？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275485_comment'></div>必将尊其所闻，奠而后发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275485_comment'></div>临事而惧，佩洙泗之格言；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275485_comment'></div>视民如伤，奉涧瀍之遗训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275485_comment'></div>使群议蔑毫发之隙，则吾道增丘山之崇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1275485_comment'></div>某久矣乡风，于焉效役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1275485_comment'></div>写拙诚于简牍，敢为骈俪之虚辞；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1275485_comment'></div>委陋质于斧斤，尚赖琢磨之厚赐。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1275485_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年12月</a>　张栻除严州，与张栻首次会面。将废尼寺改为学宫。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年12月</a>　作书与潘景宪，称许张栻。嘱留意刊刻《易传》事。作品：《答潘叔度》二。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史外集》卷五。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年12月</a>　与张栻论胡宏《知言》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年</a>　本年为门生讲授《易》、《诗》、《春秋》等，编撰教材《己丑课程》、《己丑所编》、《春秋讲义》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷十二。）</span>《春秋讲义》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷十三。）</span><div id='poem_1275505' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275505' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275505?labeling=true' target='_blank'>春秋讲义序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1169年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275505")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275505_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275505'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275505'>学欲切而思欲近，吾夫子作《春秋》，盖以深切自命，而传经者亦谓拨乱世反之正莫近《春秋》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275505_comment'></div>君子将用力于切近之地，置是经其何从？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275505_comment'></div>昔者某尝读是经矣，降隐讫哀，阅君十二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275505_comment'></div>其褒者既往之功也，其贬者既往之罪也，其国其爵，其氏其名，皆既往之陈迹也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275505_comment'></div>终日历数古人之臧否而我无与焉，不识所谓切近者果何等语。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275505_comment'></div>意者夫子之褒贬，借古而警今邪！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275505_comment'></div>生同世，居同里，荣悴戚休，尚有旁观平睨茫然如不见考，况用尝罚于冢中枯骨若今人何，圣人作经殆不如是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275505_comment'></div>然则《春秋》所谓切近者，岂无所在邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275505_comment'></div>通古今为一时，合彼己为一体，前和后应，彼动此随，然后知吾夫子之笔削本非为他人设。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275505_comment'></div>苟尚有丝发之蔽，判然已为二物矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275505_comment'></div>经非疏我而我则疏经，盍内讼我之未近，不当妄疑经之远也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275505_comment'></div>某始学者也，切近用力之地何足以知之，敬因诸君问津焉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1275505_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年</a>　作学规《乾道五年规约》五条。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷五《家范五·学规》）</span><div id='poem_1275621' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275621' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275621?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乾道五年规约</a><span class='authorDate'>（1169年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275621")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275621_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275621'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275621'>凡与此学者，以讲求经旨、明理躬行为本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275621_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1275621'>肄业当有常，日纪所习于簿，多寡随意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275621_comment'></div>如遇有干辍业，亦书于簿，一岁无过百日，过百日者同志共摈之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275621_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1275621'>凡有所疑，专置册记录，同志异时相会，各出所习及所疑，互相商榷，仍手书名于册后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275621_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1275621'>怠惰苟且，虽漫应课程而全疏略无叙者，同志共摈之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275621_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1275621'>不修士检，乡论不齿者，同志共摈之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275621_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1275621'>同志迁居，移书相报。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1275621_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年</a>　门人巩丰、詹仪之、卢汝雱等从游。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1170')">1170年1月</a>　潘景宪父卒，为作祭文。作品：《祭潘朝散文》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷八。）</span><div id='poem_1275694' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275694' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275694?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭潘朝散文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1170年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275694")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275694_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275694'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275694'>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275694_comment'></div>昔我见公，子舍是阶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275694_comment'></div>入拜于堂，笑言欢咍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275694_comment'></div>时公谢客，毡寒榻埃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275694_comment'></div>一见倾倒，童仆惊猜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275694_comment'></div>亟问亟劳，厚礼莫偕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275694_comment'></div>我官旁郡，音问踵来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275694_comment'></div>尺牍未报，赴车告哀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275694_comment'></div>承问潸然，亟走舆台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275694_comment'></div>潜德幽光，孰发氛霾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275694_comment'></div>日薄事丛，莫知所裁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275694_comment'></div>矧公视世，澹兮寒灰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275694_comment'></div>万镒千箱，振穷恤灾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275694_comment'></div>弃而如遗，况此也哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275694_comment'></div>诸子之孝，希参并柴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275694_comment'></div>必诚必信，典训罔乖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275694_comment'></div>礼门久阖，自今其开。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1275694_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1275694'><span class='label'>按：</span>《东莱吕太史文集》卷八。又见清抄一百五十卷本《圣宋名贤五百家播芳大全文粹》卷一三七，《永乐大典》卷一四○四九。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1275694_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1170')">1170年1月</a>　将《奠礼》寄潘景宪，冀其以古礼革陋俗。作品：《与潘侍郎》二。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷九。）</span><div id='poem_1275246' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275246' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275246?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与朱侍讲元晦书<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其四十六 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1170年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275246")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275246_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275246'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275246'>某伏蒙垂喻，固深悉雅意，即一一达之当路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275246_comment'></div>而其意确然不移，又以已有不许辞免旨挥，不敢再将上，遂复有趣行堂帖，谨以拜纳，恐须免强一至治所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275246_comment'></div>若相事势果不可为，则引疾丐祠，却是常程事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275246_comment'></div>辞免则碍旨挥，到任丐祠则非辞免也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275246_comment'></div>又载疾之官，亦见奉命之共，才文字到便可得，却无今日许多牢攘也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275246_comment'></div>况江东帅、漕、宪、监，皆旧相知，或素慕用，上下相应，当无龃龉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275246_comment'></div>或粗可施展，使一方之民息肩，亦岂小补哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275246_comment'></div>钦夫得书，亦以为须一出为善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275246_comment'></div>虽去就出处，素有定论，然更须斟酌消息，勿至已甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275246_comment'></div>苟一向固拒，则上之人谓贤者不肯为用，于大体却有害也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275246_comment'></div>程侍郎《禹贡图》，潘叔昌曾录得，可径问渠取，不然稍暇亦可录去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275246_comment'></div>黄叔张陛辞，甚见领略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275246_comment'></div>一二年来，小小灌溉，岂无萌蘖之生，但寒者众耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275246_comment'></div>专介回，谨此拜禀，它乞为斯文护重。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1275246_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1170')">1170年1月</a>　有书与潘景宪，与门人讨论丧礼。作品：《答潘叔度》二。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷十。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1170')">1170年1月</a>　作书与潘景宪，议卜宅兆事当准伊川“五说”、司马光“书仪”，不可从阴阳家说。作品：《答潘叔度》三。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷十。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1170')">1170年1月</a>　专人致书潘景宪，勉其行古礼革陋俗。作品：《与潘侍郎》三。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷九。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1170')">1170年1月</a>　与门人书信，嘱看杨时《中庸解》，与潘景宪讲究丧礼。作品：《与学者及诸弟》一。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷十。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1170')">1170年1月</a>　为张栻作《乞免丁钱奏状》，痛揭朝政弊端，主张减免百姓赋税。作品：《为张严州作乞免丁钱奏状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷三。）</span><div id='poem_1275155' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275155' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275155?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为张严州作乞免丁钱奏状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1170年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275155")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275155_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275155'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275155'>右，臣昨者恭奉圣旨差权发遣严州军州事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275155_comment'></div>内窃省循，以未信之学，遽当民社，深惧识眊力浅，疏阔舛缪，仰负皇帝陛下责成共理之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275155_comment'></div>敬陈悃愊，恳辞弗俞，黾勉遵承，皇灼无地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275155_comment'></div>爰自就道，遍访本州利病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275155_comment'></div>往来者皆言，严之为郡，地瘠人贫，丁盐钱绢额数繁重，民不聊生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275155_comment'></div>此赋不除，永无息肩之日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275155_comment'></div>臣瞻望威颜之始，冒昧控诉，天慈悯恻，许令到任条具以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275155_comment'></div>仰见陛下至仁博临，勤恤民隐，虽古先圣王之用心，不是过也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275155_comment'></div>臣自到任，延问耆老，咨诹僚吏，参稽案籍，始知本州丁盐钱绢为民大害，向来所闻，百不一二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275155_comment'></div>谨条具本末，上干天听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275155_comment'></div>臣照对本州丁盐钱绢之起，据父老称，自承平时每一丁官支给盐一㪷，计五斤，每一斤计钱三十一文二分省，共计钱一百五十六文省，却纳绢一丈二尺八寸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275155_comment'></div>数内一半系本色绢，一半系折纳见钱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275155_comment'></div>是时绢每一匹直钱一贯文省，每丁计纳绢六尺四寸，计价钱一百六十文省，又折帛见钱一百六十文省，两项通计三百二十文省。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275155_comment'></div>将官中所给盐斤价钱百五十六文省比折外，每丁实陪贴纳钱百六十四文省，所纳不多，公私两便，未见其害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275155_comment'></div>后来蔡京改变盐法，令大商入纳买钞，支给袋盐货卖，从此官司更不支给丁盐，徒令纳绢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275155_comment'></div>盐给既停，绢价复长，浸久浸增。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275155_comment'></div>目今绢一匹估计折纳七贯文省，民力殚竭，职此之由。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1275155_comment'></div>臣请为陛下详言之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1275155_comment'></div>两浙东、西路共管十五州军，户口物力无若本州之贫，丁盐钱税亦无若本州之重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1275155_comment'></div>本州地形阻隘，绝少旷土，山居其八，田居其二，涧曲岭隈，浅畦狭陇，苗稼疏薄，殆如牛毛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1275155_comment'></div>细民崎岖，力耕劳瘁，虽遇丰稔，犹不足食，惟恃商旅般贩斗斛为命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1275155_comment'></div>旬日不雨，溪流已涸，客船断绝，米价腾踊，大小嗷嗷，便同凶年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1275155_comment'></div>每岁合六县所纳苗米，除折纳糯米外，粳米止管八千七百五十一硕，犹不及湖、秀富民一户所收之数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1275155_comment'></div>所有官兵米粮，逐年婺州应副一万五千硕补助支遣，尚阙一万三千一十硕，其为困乏，不言可见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1275155_comment'></div>重以坊郭乡村边溪去处，每经巨浸，垣墙颓仆，庐舍倾摧，资用散失，生计萧然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1275155_comment'></div>若遇寇盗，整葺未全，复遭漂荡，民素穷乏，又加此厄，虽使止存两税，犹惧输纳不前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1275155_comment'></div>今乃经赋之外，每丁使之重纳丁钱盐绢一丈二尺八寸，其双丁以上折科每疋计钱七贯文省，凋瘵之民，其何以堪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1275155_comment'></div>且以两浙诸郡论之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1275155_comment'></div>平江府、秀、婺、衢等四州，自蠲免丁钱，明州每丁止纳钱六十文足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1275155_comment'></div>惟湖州丁盐钱绢在两浙最号为重，其乌程、归安、长兴、安吉、德清五县，三丁共纳绢一匹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1275155_comment'></div>本州三丁共纳绢三丈八尺四寸，比乌程等五县每三丁共少一尺六寸，一丁止少五寸三分三釐，相去不远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1275155_comment'></div>其武康一县，每四丁共纳绢一匹，则反轻于本州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1275155_comment'></div>截长补短，本州丁盐钱绢较之湖州犹自颇重，至于他郡，重轻相绝，可以类推。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1275155_comment'></div>本州民力在两浙十五军州之下，而赋歛反在十五军州之上，以至贫之民纳至重之赋，人情物理，恐不应尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1275155_comment'></div>臣谨按本州丁籍：建德县第一等至第四等户计一千八百四十九丁，第五等有产税户计一万七千八百九十八丁，无产税户计三千八百二十二丁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1275155_comment'></div>遂安县第一等至第四等户计二千三百三十七丁，第五等有产税户计八千九百六十四丁，无产税户计一万八百八十六丁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1275155_comment'></div>寿昌县第一等至第四等户计九百七十七丁，第五等有产税户计七千六百二十九丁，无产税户计四千二百一十八丁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1275155_comment'></div>分水县第一等至第四等户计五百六丁，第五等有产税户计一万三千七百五丁，无产税户计九百七十八丁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1275155_comment'></div>淳安县第一等至第四等户计三千六百五十丁，第五等有产税户计八千三百三丁，无产税户计一万八千二百七十四丁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1275155_comment'></div>桐庐县第一等至第四等户计一千三百九十九丁，第五等有产税户计一万五千四百八十丁，无产税户计二千一十八丁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1275155_comment'></div>通计六县第一等至第四等户止有一万七百一十八丁，其第五等有产税户共管七万一千四百七十九丁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1275155_comment'></div>虽名为有产，大率所纳不过尺寸分釐升合秒勺，虽有若无，不能自给。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1275155_comment'></div>其无产税户共管四万一百九十丁，并无寸土尺椽，饥寒转徙，朝不谋夕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1275155_comment'></div>本州统管一十二万二千三百九十三丁，而第五等有产税户、无产税户共管一十一万一千六百七十五丁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1275155_comment'></div>是十分之中，九分以上尪瘠困迫，无所从出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1275155_comment'></div>从前官吏明知其害，迫于上司督责之严，汗颜落笔，蹙頞用刑，笞箠缧系，殆无虚日，愁叹之声，闾里相接。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1275155_comment'></div>彊悍者穷塞无聊，散为攘窃，四方遂指严州为多盗之区。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1275155_comment'></div>非犷俗独钟于此土，盖丁钱偏重于它邦，原其情状，实可怜悯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1275155_comment'></div>臣体访得深山穷谷至有年三十馀颜状老苍，不敢裹头，县吏恐丁数亏折，时复搜括相验，纠令输纳，谓之「貌丁」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1275155_comment'></div>民间既无避免之路，生子往往不举，规脱丁口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1275155_comment'></div>一岁之间，婴孺夭阏，不知其几。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1275155_comment'></div>小民虽愚，岂无父子之爱？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1275155_comment'></div>徒以阨于重赋，忍灭天性，亲相贼杀，伤动和气，悖逆人理，莫斯为甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1275155_comment'></div>臣闻之不觉涕下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1275155_comment'></div>窃自惟念本州实光尧寿圣太上皇帝基命之地，陪辅行都，最为密迩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1275155_comment'></div>皇帝陛下方以不忍人之心行不忍人之政，岂容辇毂百里之间，斯民颠顿愁悴，父子不能相保。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1275155_comment'></div>意者未有以实上闻者，臣职在拊摩，尚复便文自营不言，死有馀罪，用敢竭诚悉意，上彻旒扆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1275155_comment'></div>臣恭睹绍兴十四年十月二十二日敕：「三省同奉圣旨：永、道、郴州、桂阳监及衡州茶陵县民户于二税之外，尚循马氏旧法，添纳丁身钱绢米麦，流弊未除，朕甚悯之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1275155_comment'></div>可将逐州县丁身钱绢米麦并与除放」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1275155_comment'></div>臣窃惟永、道、郴、桂阳监、茶陵四郡一县，邈在湖广，太上皇帝明见万里之外，不遗远方，捐赋子民；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1275155_comment'></div>本州幸在阙门之侧，反不得如遐方荒裔，沾濡德泽，臣窃痛之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1275155_comment'></div>欲望圣慈特降睿旨，将严州丁盐钱绢，依永、道、郴州、桂阳监、衡州茶陵县及衢、婺、秀州、平江府例，尽行蠲除，使一方仰父俯子，吏不至门，复有生民之乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1275155_comment'></div>不然，乞如明州例，每丁纳钱六十文足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1275155_comment'></div>又若以国用未裕，则乞蠲免一半，粗宽民力，亦为厚幸，然终不若沛然尽蠲为渗漉无穷之泽也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1275155_comment'></div>臣诚过虑，恐议者或谓蠲免严州，恐诸郡援例申请，必致有亏经费。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1275155_comment'></div>臣窃谓圣人之治，俾万邦惟正之供，丁盐钱绢出于一切，本非常赋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1275155_comment'></div>陛下约己节用，凡以为民，异时帑藏充溢，蠲免之令，固将次第而举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1275155_comment'></div>今虽调度尚虚，犹当先其尤急者，用示省赋之渐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1275155_comment'></div>以地则莫如本州之近，以民则莫如本州之困，以害则莫如本州之重，先后之序，宜自本州始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1275155_comment'></div>况太上皇帝潜龙旧镇，亦非诸州遽敢援例。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1275155_comment'></div>惟愿睿断不疑，俯赐开允，俾一邦亟解倒垂之急。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1275155_comment'></div>臣言语短拙，不能尽写困迫之状，惟与合郡吏民澡心涤虑，延颈跂足，以俟鸿厖之施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1275155_comment'></div>冒犯天威，臣无任战慄悚惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1275155_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1275155_comment'></div>谨奏。</div><div id='poem_sentence_74_1275155_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1170')">1170年1月</a>　奏状上，下诏捐严州赋税半额，为张栻作《谢免丁钱表》作品：《为张严州作谢免丁钱表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷二。）</span><div id='poem_1275126' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275126' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275126?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为张严州作谢免丁钱表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1170年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275126")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275126_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275126'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275126'>奏牍既升，方虞闻罢，免符亟下，稍示复除。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275126_comment'></div>曷贱悃之遽伸，本至仁之易感<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275126_comment'></div>惟严为郡，介国之隅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275126_comment'></div>呻叹讴吟，宜朝传而暮达；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275126_comment'></div>抚摩涵养，当月裕而岁丰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275126_comment'></div>孰知凋瘵之馀，尚困赋租之重！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275126_comment'></div>畴先民瘼，最甚丁徭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275126_comment'></div>自古邦家，惟欲编氓之繁阜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275126_comment'></div>于今闾里，反忧孙子之众多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275126_comment'></div>皇明岂忍于遐遗，下吏未闻于控告。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275126_comment'></div>而臣过以谫薄，□□顾忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275126_comment'></div>鸿雁于飞，亲见嗷嗷之□；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275126_comment'></div>□□□□，□□恳恳之诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275126_comment'></div>曾谓琐微，骤蒙开可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275126_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下监观邦本，恢养治原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275126_comment'></div>制赋欲均，期复大禹九州之正；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275126_comment'></div>施仁有渐，姑从文王四者之先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1275126_comment'></div>雨露旁流，槁乾胥浃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1275126_comment'></div>臣敬掸厚泽，下逮穷民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1275126_comment'></div>观其拜赐之时，犹有乞怜之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1275126_comment'></div>既勤深恤，得少愒于今年；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1275126_comment'></div>终觊大恩，俾尽夷于旁郡。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1275126_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1170')">1170年1月</a>　为前任严州太守柳楹离任送行。作品：《送柳严州解官趋朝》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷一。）</span><div id='poem_94119' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_94119' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/94119?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送柳严州解官趋朝<span class='inlineComment2'>（楹）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1170年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_94119")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_94119_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_94119'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_94119'>一叶初秋已趣装，玺书屡下驻归艎。<div id='poem_sentence_0_94119_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_94119'>少留北阙三年最，多借西州半岁强。<div id='poem_sentence_1_94119_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_94119'>身外宠荣元自薄，眼前凋瘵故难忘。<div id='poem_sentence_2_94119_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_94119'>书囊知有朝天草，不是中和乐职章。<div id='poem_sentence_3_94119_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_94119'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_94119_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1170')">1170年4月</a>　汪应辰出知平江府，为代作谢表谢启。作品：《为汪尚书作知平江府谢表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷二。）</span>《为汪尚书作知平江府谢宰执启》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷四。）</span><div id='poem_1275138' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275138' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275138?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为汪尚书作知平江府谢表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1170年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275138")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275138_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275138'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275138'>隆委难胜，期于颠踣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275138_comment'></div>鸿私曲被，遗以便安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275138_comment'></div>分书殿之荣光，借侯藩之壮调，度越常典，昭明异恩<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275138_comment'></div>伏念臣际会两朝，推移三纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275138_comment'></div>爵久踰于始愿，学浸失于暮年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275138_comment'></div>越从蜀道之归，亟冠禁涂之邃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275138_comment'></div>经帷词禁，史观铨衡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275138_comment'></div>持凌瘁之孤身，萃高华之极选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275138_comment'></div>志凋气馁，日惭职守之隳；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275138_comment'></div>责厚忧深，居有简书之畏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275138_comment'></div>眚灾狎至，疾疹相乘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275138_comment'></div>蕲外假于郡章，觊远收于朝迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275138_comment'></div>眷兹茂苑，近在修门，置身未外于函关，顾影忍违于文陛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275138_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下圣神立极，中正体乾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275138_comment'></div>宇万物以兼容，陶成罔间；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275138_comment'></div>品群材而并用，陟降无私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275138_comment'></div>眇然簪履之微，假以盖帷之施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1275138_comment'></div>臣敢不播敷诏令，怀辑里闾？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1275138_comment'></div>增主之明，废任莫追于前悔；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1275138_comment'></div>务民之义，疚心尚补于夙愆。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1275138_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1275488' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275488' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275488?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为汪尚书作知平江谢宰执启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1170年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275488")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275488_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275488'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275488'>献讷论思，每窃忧于累国；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275488_comment'></div>蕃宣屏翰，辄自诡于临民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275488_comment'></div>贲然书殿之华，增此辕门之重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275488_comment'></div>载惟光宠，实匪故常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275488_comment'></div>伏念某学朴材疏，齿衰志落。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275488_comment'></div>曩召从于蜀道，亟冠冒于禁途。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275488_comment'></div>显秩华资，兼诸儒之盛选；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275488_comment'></div>师言公议，负众正之深期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275488_comment'></div>名实未孚，形神交病，思均劳于外服，庶逃责于馀年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275488_comment'></div>曾谓曲成，竟从私愿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275488_comment'></div>恭惟某官懋隆民极，协建邦经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275488_comment'></div>爱惜人材，伤恐加于毫发；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275488_comment'></div>扶持善类，恩不啻于丘山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275488_comment'></div>有如衰谢之踪，犹在保全之数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275488_comment'></div>凡所见州闾之纤悉，当尽控闻；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275488_comment'></div>及未归田里之须臾，用为报塞。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1275488_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1170')">1170年4月</a>　在严州改革学制。有书与朱熹论学。《易传》初刊毕，印送朱熹就正。作品：《与朱侍讲》二。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷七。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1170')">1170年4月</a>　应潘景宪之请，为其父作墓志铭。作品：《朝散潘公墓志铭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷十。）</span>《答潘叔度》四。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷十。）</span><div id='poem_1275647' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275647' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275647?labeling=true' target='_blank'>朝散潘公墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（乾道六年九月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275647")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275647_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275647'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275647'>乾道六年春正月庚午，右朝散郎、赐绯鱼袋致仕潘公卒于婺之里第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275647_comment'></div>越三月，诸孤状公之寿年、里系、履迹，属某铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275647_comment'></div>某虽侍公晚，一见意浃，屈年辈，尽悃款，异乎世俗，所以相期者，此意其可负？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275647_comment'></div>矧公子景宪，在岁癸未，实偕以进士拜敕于庭，视公盖丈人行也，敢他诿？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275647_comment'></div>遂次其语曰：公讳好古，字敏修，一字伯御，处之松阳人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275647_comment'></div>曾祖干，以耋老望其里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275647_comment'></div>祖珂，以谨力厚其家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275647_comment'></div>考宗回，以文艺官其族。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275647_comment'></div>传三世而门益大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275647_comment'></div>始公之考开迹农亩，拔科级，校中秘书，浸光显矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275647_comment'></div>中更忧患，无复当世意，专林丘之乐者数十年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275647_comment'></div>晚得复州，非其雅志，将辞行，章未上而卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275647_comment'></div>公乐易安恬，甚似其先人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275647_comment'></div>自为童子时，祓除遨嬉，委己于学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275647_comment'></div>母叶夫人爱之尤，每抑止之，公愈自力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275647_comment'></div>少长，入成均，从四方士游，闻见日博。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275647_comment'></div>京都失守，有谍虏剽诸生者，公方与同舍郎环坐，虏且至，众骇詟，或劝趣自裁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1275647_comment'></div>公徐晓坐人曰：「死当择所，未见虏逆自毙，与自经沟渎伍耳」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1275647_comment'></div>既虏入两斋，亡所得，舍去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1275647_comment'></div>事定，众皆以识度归公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1275647_comment'></div>公事复州孝，昼夜淬厉，蕲世科以慰满其意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1275647_comment'></div>再试礼部，辄不偶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1275647_comment'></div>郊祀任子，复州娄欲上公名，公固辞，复州亦不能彊也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1275647_comment'></div>后子景圭秩，得封其亲，命书数下，公以前尝止复州之奏，慨然曰：「辞父泽而安子荣，宁吾志耶」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1275647_comment'></div>平居不御簪裳，不书爵品，终其身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1275647_comment'></div>其没也，诸子始敢以朝服敛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1275647_comment'></div>公始自松阳改筑临江。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1275647_comment'></div>临江，婺之郊也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1275647_comment'></div>晚岁徙郊而城其居，盖三徙焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1275647_comment'></div>绍兴丙辰，岁大侵，婺米斗千钱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1275647_comment'></div>公既发廪不足，则橐厚赀致他郡粟，下其直十之三以贷之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1275647_comment'></div>秋稔，民劝趣偿惟恐后，公闵民偿之不易也，视初贷复绌其一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1275647_comment'></div>甲子岁水，并舍有僧庐，公挈孥栖其危。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1275647_comment'></div>水怒张，屋廪廪欲仆，众方左右视，迫怵亡计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1275647_comment'></div>隃望波涛间，有棹舟至者，呼公亟济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1275647_comment'></div>僮仆相贺更生，前扶公即舟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1275647_comment'></div>公顾同避者尚数十人，叹曰：「吾去，是曹其鱼矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1275647_comment'></div>乃谕舟人，姑寘己，先载馀人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1275647_comment'></div>舟人曰：「吾德公长者，故犯险脱公耳，馀子何为者」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1275647_comment'></div>公曰：「此距平陆不十里，汝不惮一往反之劳，厄此者皆汝生之也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1275647_comment'></div>舟人义而从之，众毕济，公乃济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1275647_comment'></div>其于死生缓急之际，先人后己如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1275647_comment'></div>甲戌盗发旁郡，流殍交道，里民穷空，竞持破硙败絮来质。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1275647_comment'></div>主帑者以白公，公曰：「第与之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1275647_comment'></div>居数日，填溢栋宇，公有喜色，益市官粟，舟相衔下，以平贵籴，比闾不复知有艰岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1275647_comment'></div>后民稍稍入金请所质，亡绐者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1275647_comment'></div>婺田恃陂塘为命，天不雨，尺竞寸攘，斗阋毙踣者相望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1275647_comment'></div>公有塘曰叶亚，溉数百顷，独听民取之，不为禁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1275647_comment'></div>斥塘下田以广潴蓄，或献疑以膏腴可惜者，公曰：「乡邻安则吾安矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1275647_comment'></div>别墅占婺之西湖旁，两塘废不治，公发钱数十万新之，人赖其利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1275647_comment'></div>时公未尝有寸田居其间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1275647_comment'></div>其他如代官逋、弛私责、恩鳏寡、逮困疾，旁及棺槥、飧药、桥梁、井泉之属，给予除治亡所靳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1275647_comment'></div>松阳学故有田，军兴调度急，吏质其田而学废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1275647_comment'></div>公以钱百二十万赎归之，学以复兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1275647_comment'></div>其后为吏者不复顾省，学又废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1275647_comment'></div>公不得已，归诸郡庠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1275647_comment'></div>处之学所以裕于养士者，繇公之助也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1275647_comment'></div>顾尝耆浮屠、老子说，颇留意塔庙土木事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1275647_comment'></div>浙河以东为二氏徒者，多借其声以行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1275647_comment'></div>暮年觉其尤谬妄者，稍谢绝之，而乡儒者浸笃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1275647_comment'></div>游士亡资者月馈之，使就业焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1275647_comment'></div>公隆于教子，训导严饬，宾礼善士，相与浸灌砻磨，故多乡方者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1275647_comment'></div>季弟好仁卒，未几又丧其壮子，公收其遗孤教养之，甚有恩意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1275647_comment'></div>家政俭而肃，有妾治衣栉垂三十年，挟宠微骄媢，公一旦资遣之，人咨其断。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1275647_comment'></div>岁时赋租，必差择精好者先众输之官，惟敬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1275647_comment'></div>尤乐佐公上之急，虏亮瞰江，公以钱千万奉军费，诏增秩，加赐五品服，而公意初不在赏也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1275647_comment'></div>独喜著书，有《诗》、《春秋》、《语》、《孟》、《中庸说》合五十一卷，他书亦数百卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1275647_comment'></div>其九月丁酉，葬于婺之金华县庆云乡东弥塘，享年七十。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1275647_comment'></div>公先娶孙氏，赠安人，左朝奉大夫夙之女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1275647_comment'></div>再娶陈氏，封宜人，左奉议郎枢之女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1275647_comment'></div>子男六人：景圭，右朝散郎、大理正、重修敕令所删修官，兼权尚书刑部郎官；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1275647_comment'></div>次景参；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1275647_comment'></div>次景宪，左迪功郎、新太平州州学教授；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1275647_comment'></div>次景愈；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1275647_comment'></div>次景泌；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1275647_comment'></div>次景良。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1275647_comment'></div>女四：长适右承奉郎、两浙东路安抚司主管机宜文字汤矼，再适右通直郎、新知太平州芜湖县苏诵；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1275647_comment'></div>次适将仕郎赵善蔚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1275647_comment'></div>次适右迪功郎、新监行在太平惠民局王注；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1275647_comment'></div>次尚幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1275647_comment'></div>孙男五人，自厚、自得，馀未名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1275647_comment'></div>女七人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1275647_comment'></div>自公之殁逮其葬，稚耄矜寡尝受公施者，拜走号哭于堂、于门、于途，其声相及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1275647_comment'></div>乡之人虽涧隈山曲，承公讣，皆倚耒投耜，戚戚有惋怛色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1275647_comment'></div>呜呼，是岂茍然者哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1275647_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_85_1275647'>丰昃盈变，惟理之常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1275647_comment'></div>积而能散，我施用光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1275647_comment'></div>万木造天，郁其高冈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1275647_comment'></div>是曰善富，潘公之藏。</div><div id='poem_sentence_88_1275647_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1170')">1170年5月</a>　致书潘景宪，讲究丧礼.言及刘清之荐刘德循来学。作品：《答潘叔度》五。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷十。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1170')">1170年5月7日</a>　除太学博士命下。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1170')">1170年5月9日</a>　朱熹以所撰《太极图解》、《中庸》首章之旨来讨论。吕祖谦作书与朱熹讲论劝诫。作品：《与朱侍讲》三。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷七。）</span><br /></div><div class='label1' id='dc57b97d87234478bc59e44c29101c3f_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("dc57b97d87234478bc59e44c29101c3f");'><span id='dc57b97d87234478bc59e44c29101c3f_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1171')">1170-1171年</a>，34-35岁</div><div id='dc57b97d87234478bc59e44c29101c3f' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1170')">1170年闰5月9日</a>　还严州。始刊《阃范》，张栻为作序。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1170')">1170年闰5月</a>　以太学博士入对，对孝宗痛陈治国方略，有对札。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1170')">1170年6月</a>　潘景宪有书问及礼物，回书，并将五月对札录与潘景宪。作品：《答潘叔度》十三。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷十。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1170')">1170年6月</a>　作书与潘景宪，忧虑国事。作品：《答潘叔度》九。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷十。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1170')">1170年6月</a>　刘朔卒于福建，与芮烨、林谦之等遣人往祭。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1170')">1170年7月6日</a>　访周必大。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1170')">1170年7月</a>　有《乾道六年轮对札子》二首。其一言恢复之事当求真儒，求实学，兴圣学。其一。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷三。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1170')">1170年7月</a>　有《乾道六年轮对札子》二首。其二言恢复要规模当定，方略当审。其二。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷三。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1170')">1170年7月</a>　复朱熹来书。并托吴翌口信与朱熹商榷讲论。作品：《与朱侍讲》四。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷七。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1170')">1170年7月</a>　婺州所刊《易传》已毕。有书信与朱熹并寄本月《轮对札子》作品：《与朱侍讲》五。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷七。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1170')">1170年7月</a>　戴衍初仕，书写部分《官箴》相勉励。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1170')">1170年7月</a>　致书戴衍相勉励劝诫。作品：《与戴在伯》一。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷十。）</span><div id='poem_1275411' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275411' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275411?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与戴在伯书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1170年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275411")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275411_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275411'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275411'>某到官垂两月矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275411_comment'></div>其初殊有龃龉处，近日稍稍按堵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275411_comment'></div>大抵坐谈常觉从容，临事常觉迫切，乃知学问工夫无穷，当益思所未至也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275411_comment'></div>吾友初官，又非此比，切须柔巽和裕而不失正乃善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275411_comment'></div>尊长所命非甚害义，皆当曲从，然先须委曲几谏，必不得已然后斟酌曲从也<span class='inlineComment2'>（通家之类是也。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275411_comment'></div>上官招饭，则不可拘旬假，要之但守非旬假不作会，则与世俗稍通也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275411_comment'></div>某所居乃在旧王承宣园<span class='inlineComment2'>（今号东百官宅。）</span>，政与张丈寓舍相望，于讲论甚便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275411_comment'></div>行期果已定日否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275411_comment'></div>它惟力学自爱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275411_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1275411'>居官临事，外有龃龉，必内有窒碍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275411_comment'></div>盖内外相应，毫发不差，只有「反己」两字，更无别法也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1275411_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1170')">1170年8月</a>　在都改革学政。致书潘叔度。与张栻同巷居住讲论学问。作品：《答潘叔度》十一。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷十。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1170')">1170年8月</a>　致书刘子澄论修身。作品：《与刘衡州》三。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷九。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1170')">1170年8月</a>　陈傅良入太学，为言本朝文献相承条序。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1170')">1170年8月</a>　致书邢世材，论学。作品：《与邢邦用》二。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷十。）</span><div id='poem_1275404' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275404' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275404?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与邢邦用书<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1170年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275404")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275404_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275404'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275404'>某自春来为建宁之行，与朱元晦相聚四十馀日，复同出至鹅湖，二陆及子澄诸兄皆集，甚有讲论之益。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275404_comment'></div>自此却无出入，可闭户读书也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275404_comment'></div>前书所论甚当，近已尝为子静详言之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275404_comment'></div>讲贯诵绎，乃百代为学通法，学者缘此支离泛滥，自是人病，非是法病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275404_comment'></div>见此而欲尽废之，正是因噎废食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275404_comment'></div>然学者苟徒能言其非，而未能反己就实，悠悠汩汩，无所底止，是又适所以坚彼之自信也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275404_comment'></div>尊兄试深思之，以为如何？</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1275404_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1170')">1170年12月</a>　以太博召试为国史院编修官，实录院检讨官。有《馆职策》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷五《策·馆职策》）</span><div id='poem_1275558' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275558' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275558?labeling=true' target='_blank'>馆职策</a><span class='authorDate'>（1170年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275558")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275558_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275558'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275558'>治道有大原，不本其原，徒欲以力救斯世，君子许其志不许其学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275558_comment'></div>天下之事，要不可以力为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275558_comment'></div>忧世之士、喜功名之人，慷慨摩厉，将欲挽一世而回之，其意气岂不甚壮矣哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275558_comment'></div>激之欲其急而听者愈缓；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275558_comment'></div>邀之欲其坚，而守者终渝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275558_comment'></div>未逢其原而倚办于区区之力，固不可耶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275558_comment'></div>汉至文帝，县内昌阜，烟火万里，仰视成、康虽小歉，俯视春秋、战国以降，则既有馀矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275558_comment'></div>痛哭者一，流涕者二，长叹息者六，贾谊之论，何其不与事俪也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275558_comment'></div>意者危言骇世，姑一快胸中之愤耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275558_comment'></div>长沙之归，历变履险，动心忍性，少年之气，剥落向尽，固未易以故意待谊，是殆必有所以，而论者或未之竟也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275558_comment'></div>谊诚见文帝，以如此之质，得如此之时，顾乃湛于庳陋，安于小成，爱之深，望之切，大声疾呼，几其一悟耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275558_comment'></div>虽然，谊诚爱君也，诚望治也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275558_comment'></div>开道扶掖，岂其无术，何至遂攘臂以仍之耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275558_comment'></div>文帝之齿长矣，阅天下之事众矣，四体伸缩，宁不自谙？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275558_comment'></div>谊乃激其言，张旦夕之忧以迫之，宜其付之嘻笑，待以书生之论也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275558_comment'></div>若昔圣贤急天下之病，岂后于谊，稽其猷告，自源徂流，具有条理，未尝置本而言末也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275558_comment'></div>伯益论来四夷，儆以怠荒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1275558_comment'></div>召公论格远人，首以谨德；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1275558_comment'></div>而仲尼为鲁虑，亦缓颛臾而急萧墙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1275558_comment'></div>圣贤之言，自有次第如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1275558_comment'></div>谊序天下之事，所先者外忧，所后者内治，于为治之大原似未深讲也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1275558_comment'></div>当是时，近有专土桀骜之诸侯，远有乘边侵侮之匈奴，汉庭公卿玩细娱而忘远虑，谊之忧亦岂可厚非哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1275558_comment'></div>至于不寻其原，遽欲斧其髀而系其颈，则疏矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1275558_comment'></div>天下之患，懦者常欲一切不为，锐者常欲一切亟为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1275558_comment'></div>甲兵朽，鈇钺钝，养痈护疽，媮取爵秩，各饱其欲，而日朘月削之患，独归国家，是滔滔者既不可胜诛，号为有意斯世者，又复不审前后，不量彼己而轻发之，终无于是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1275558_comment'></div>两者之间，参订审裁，立其本，循其序，摹之于前而收之于后者，此谊与汉庭公卿俱堕一偏，文帝卒罔知所倚，虽略行其策，迄不能并三五之隆也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1275558_comment'></div>谊而概尝有闻，肯堕其说于一偏，而挈诸侯、匈奴为发语之端哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1275558_comment'></div>必将首明帝学，大定其本，而嗜卑惮高，令今可行之言不肯出也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1275558_comment'></div>必将继论储贰，趣择师傅，而刑名惨刻、术数临制之习不能入也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1275558_comment'></div>必将深绝私昵，防微杜渐，而近戚幸臣、干法嫚朝之恶不敢肆也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1275558_comment'></div>今揽其疏，或汎数而置四五之间，或遗落而无一言之及，谊尚得为知大原乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1275558_comment'></div>大原既失，无惑乎用力虽劳，言者急而听者缓也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1275558_comment'></div>若夫姚崇在唐，埒之于谊，则非匹矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1275558_comment'></div>自下求上，贾谊之于文帝也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1275558_comment'></div>自上求下，玄宗之于姚崇也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1275558_comment'></div>一则蹻足而觊其听，一则虚心而俟其言，孰可同日而道哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1275558_comment'></div>玄宗始初，清明求治之意如川之方至，钦迟崇之旧德夙望，起于藩维而相之，徯于崇者何如也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1275558_comment'></div>崇苟学知大原，则一举其纲而天下定矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1275558_comment'></div>方且逡巡不拜，历述十事，邀其诺而后就位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1275558_comment'></div>仇敌相交则有盟，市道相质则有券，君相聚精会神之际，而用要约焉，吁，何薄也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1275558_comment'></div>将闿端垂统，基一代之治，而君相畀付之初，已恃要约以为固，则为治之大原已隳矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1275558_comment'></div>虽力邀强制，仅致小康，时改意衰，必溃决而不可遏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1275558_comment'></div>纽解丝棼，不待观天宝之季，固已兆于开元之元也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1275558_comment'></div>傅说旦胥靡而暮辅相，以匹夫而躐处父兄百官之上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1275558_comment'></div>《说命》三篇，其对扬何其甚暇而有馀耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1275558_comment'></div>始之曰「后从谏则圣」，盖溯大原之舟楫也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1275558_comment'></div>申之曰「惟厥攸居，政事惟醇」，盖指大原而示之也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1275558_comment'></div>终之曰「念终始，典于学」，盖造大原而使勿失之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1275558_comment'></div>合堂同席而议，如甲胄，如衣裳，如官爵，如祭祀，棋布绳联，源流会通，亦非缕数条陈而力邀之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1275558_comment'></div>然则相天下之道可知已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1275558_comment'></div>崇肩随管、晏，固不敢以傅说自命，然资权谲，亦足以逆料其君之锐始怠终也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1275558_comment'></div>故及其眷之方新，画是十条，以坚其君之心虑，以终吾世而已，何暇恤其后哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1275558_comment'></div>考之于史，玄宗渝其约，不待他日，方崇持国秉之时，既班班见矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1275558_comment'></div>问以峻法绳下之约，曷为而按钟绍京之狱，犹有待于崇之救也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1275558_comment'></div>问以法行自近之约，曷为而疑王仙童之劾，犹有待于崇之奏也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1275558_comment'></div>问以班序荒杂之约，曷为而许阎楚圭之官，犹有待于崇之却也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1275558_comment'></div>此犹力争而幸胜者耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1275558_comment'></div>高力士、杨思勖名出宫壸，骎骎乎宦者预政之渐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1275558_comment'></div>薛讷、契丹之师，不惟骤弃崇谏，又增重其事权而遣之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1275558_comment'></div>至郭虔瓘募兵击安西，崇虽以为不然，已喑默而不敢争矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1275558_comment'></div>是不倖边功之约，玄宗视之亡如也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1275558_comment'></div>身未去位而约已寒，况上印绶之后乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1275558_comment'></div>不务格其君之心而以力邀之，此已事之明效大验也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1275558_comment'></div>盖尝读贾谊之书，而得文帝之所以克终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1275558_comment'></div>次姚崇之本末，然后知蛊玄宗之心者，有自来矣，岂独一李林甫之罪哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1275558_comment'></div>谊之一书，肆言不忌，前此数十年，必抵诽谤之辟，后此数十年，亦伏非所宜言、大不敬之诛矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1275558_comment'></div>文帝虽未尽用，不斥不愠，待之有加。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1275558_comment'></div>帝非徒谓容纳为帝王之盛德，实以言路通塞，乃人主切身之利害也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1275558_comment'></div>侈心邪念，阙政舛令，出于我而恬不自觉者，夫岂一端？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1275558_comment'></div>而乱萌祸机，群情众论，隐匿壅阏而不得上闻者，亦何可胜数哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1275558_comment'></div>待言者之饬正宣达，不啻疹之待砭、躄之待杖也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1275558_comment'></div>容养奖纳，此自吾切身利害，其逊其悖，彼盖言者事，吾何为预之哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1275558_comment'></div>谊虽气激辞愤，阔于事情，姑善之以劝来者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1275558_comment'></div>自时厥后，冯唐、申屠嘉之属，规儆辅拂，不绝于朝，终置文帝于寡过之地，是固有以召之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1275558_comment'></div>人主进德之验，他未即见，惟于谏者之言先见之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1275558_comment'></div>言之委曲迁就，是君德未信于人，而犹有所畏也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1275558_comment'></div>言之剀切侵讦，是君德已信于人，而既无所畏也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1275558_comment'></div>委曲迁就，剀切侵讦，在言者之得失则二，在人主为进德之验则一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1275558_comment'></div>谊之论虽未协于中，文帝独不可自贺而为进德之验乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1275558_comment'></div>一时风俗，犹皆醇厚，虽前日害谊之宠者，不过尤其纷乱诸事，所谓求名归过之论，当时之人盖未解作此等语也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1275558_comment'></div>至隋炀帝而始有谏以求名之忿，至唐德宗而始有矜衒归过之疑，其所见亦既狭矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1275558_comment'></div>风雨霜露，无一气而非天；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1275558_comment'></div>芽甲根荄，无一物而非地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1275558_comment'></div>天下之善，谁非人主之善乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1275558_comment'></div>小夫窭人，借隙光以自饰，窃勺水以自多，要不出范围之内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1275558_comment'></div>天覆地载，岂与是琐琐者争衡哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1275558_comment'></div>炀帝、德宗，忘其君道之大，下与一士较短论长，若闾巷侪辈互相夺攘者，何其小也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1275558_comment'></div>茍文帝之世此论已立，谊之所遭，岂直吊湘赋鵩而已哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1275558_comment'></div>史称姚崇善应变，以成天下之务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1275558_comment'></div>然变或非正，失亦随之，其尤大章明者两端焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1275558_comment'></div>玄宗在藩，侠气已盖诸王，手锄逆韦太平之难，肇履大位，隽逸英毅，若太阿出柙，莫之敢干，所虑者轻视天下而不自抑畏也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1275558_comment'></div>厖臣硕辅，政当厉之以畏天之诚，启之以尊儒重道之实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1275558_comment'></div>左右规矩，犹惧或肆，崇复以水济水，投弃准绳，略无龃龉于其间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1275558_comment'></div>日食历差，而以不亏班贺；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1275558_comment'></div>太室自坏，而以材朽献谀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1275558_comment'></div>畏天之说，典谟训诰，誓命之书，异篇而同指者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1275558_comment'></div>崇矫诬上天，一旦破其扃鐍而芟夷之，使其君荡然无所顾忌，驯致渔阳之变，撤其防而导其侈者，实崇也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1275558_comment'></div>度崇始意不过容悦迎逢耳，亦不自知其祸之至此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1275558_comment'></div>末流氾滥，虽崇尚存，亦非捧土所能塞矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1275558_comment'></div>莫大于天而犹不畏焉，于一崇乎何有？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1275558_comment'></div>自有书契，严畏天之说以相付者，岂以人君尊无与敌，复借天以压之哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1275558_comment'></div>兢业祗惧，是乃天心之所存，而尧、舜、禹、汤、文、武所传之大原也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1275558_comment'></div>上帝临汝，无贰尔心，贰之以适莫偏诐之私，则作于心、害于事，凶于而家而国矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1275558_comment'></div>崇学不足此而遽敢慢之，此崇之大失一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1275558_comment'></div>崇之捕蝗也，议者方哗，玄宗问焉，崇以庸儒泥文而不知变对。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1275558_comment'></div>除蝗之法，列于古训，杂然而议者，信庸儒也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1275558_comment'></div>然玄宗尊儒重道之意，本不自笃，崇又以泥文不知变之语入其心，使益加姗侮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1275558_comment'></div>继自今以往，虽先王之典训不便于己者，亦可以是语断之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1275558_comment'></div>自张九龄、韩休之去，儒者尽绌，坐于朝、议于堂、捍于边，皆便捷轻锐、知变而不泥文者也，其效今可睹矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1275558_comment'></div>崇徒见所谓庸儒者拘挛固滞，遂概厌薄之，亦尝循其本而思之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1275558_comment'></div>以一人而制六合，下至众而上至寡也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1275558_comment'></div>群天下之所乐、萃天下之所贵而集有之，虽悍彊很暴，屈首尊戴，无敢不驯者，以君臣之典叙于天，而儒者实品节扶持之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1275558_comment'></div>今恶庸儒而并废其品节扶持者，是理既泯，万目睽睽，见利则逝，见便则夺，上之人其危哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1275558_comment'></div>儒者舌敝唇腐，本为谁计，而轻欲销废之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1275558_comment'></div>此崇之大失二也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1275558_comment'></div>并置十事二失而委之天下，夫人而能平其功罪之轻重矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1275558_comment'></div>参谊、崇而论之，所到固有浅深，其未知大原之所在则一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1275558_comment'></div>明天子方屈群策以图大业，尚论前世，谊与崇之所条，固已久经乙夜之览，亦既采取而时措之事业矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1275558_comment'></div>愚不敢复踵其论，顾私窃有所疑焉，幸因奏篇之上而附见其说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1275558_comment'></div>古之兴王，所以震服天下者，不过一二大政，而薄物细故，则初未尝躬其劳也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1275558_comment'></div>汉高帝之约法三章，齐威王之诛赏阿、即墨大夫，终身尤可称者财此事，皆足以随世而就功名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1275558_comment'></div>明天子嗣服以来，天造神断，自古庸主依违牵制数十年而不能改者，决之于一日；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1275558_comment'></div>自古谏臣恳切覼缕千百疏而不能回者，从之于一言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1275558_comment'></div>大经画、大黜陟、大因革，历数其目，既已兼前代之长，徐计其成，尚未能半。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1275558_comment'></div>前代之效，雠耻未复，版图未归，风俗未正，国用未充，民力未厚，军政未核，覆按谊、崇为汉、唐忧者，亦十居其五六焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1275558_comment'></div>是独何说也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1275558_comment'></div>意者统宗会元，尚有可思者耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1275558_comment'></div>汉高、齐威之事浅矣，然就其规摹论之，亦粗能持其初说者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1275558_comment'></div>如使约三章之明岁，而苛法复生，诛赏阿、即墨之后日，而嬖倖复听，则首尾衡决，人谁信之哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1275558_comment'></div>今日大政数十，皆绝出汉、唐之表，惟其统宗会元者，尚有可思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1275558_comment'></div>故除一弊事，是一事而已也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1275558_comment'></div>去一小人，是一人而已也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1275558_comment'></div>四海九州之广，万官亿丑之众，博揽远驭，焉能无毫发之遗哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1275558_comment'></div>德意志虑，所示者未及遍孚，所遗者已或先见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1275558_comment'></div>命令之布，黎献稚耋，䜣怿未已而惶惑继之，激昂未已而解弛继之，惕息未已而侥觊继之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1275558_comment'></div>向若淳固专壹，无间杂之病，则所谓大政数十者，出其一二已足以鼓舞群动而立丕丕之基，宁至宵旰十年，尚勤愿治之叹乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1275558_comment'></div>此愚所以冒昧而献统宗会元之说也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1275558_comment'></div>诚储神为治之大原，提其统，据其会，则出治者无一出一入之累，而观治者亦无一喜一惧之移矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1275558_comment'></div>讲大原之所在，閒燕咨访，将有人焉，愚不敢躐等而议。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_138_1275558'></div><div id='poem_sentence_138_1275558_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1170')">1170年12月</a>　芮烨时为国子司业，与共修学政，有《答学者所问》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷十六。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1170')">1170年12月</a>　致书朱熹论学，言及《易传》、《二程遗书》等的刊刻事宜。讨论胡宏《知言》作品：《与朱侍讲》六。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷七。）</span><br /><a href="javascript:
