ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1171&endYear=1171')">1171年</a>　为人代作谢表谢启。作品：《为虞丞相作辞册宝进封增邑表》《为梁参政作辞册宝转官表》一。《为梁参政作辞册宝转官表》二。《为虞丞相作辞郊恩表》《为梁参政作辞郊恩表》《为宰臣作端诚殿贺南郊礼成笏记》《为芮直讲作庆王辞增邑表》《为芮直讲作庆王生皇孙锡名谢太上皇帝表》《为芮直讲作庆王生皇孙锡名谢太上皇后笺》《为梁参政作乞解罢政事表》一。《为梁参政作乞解罢政事表》二。<div id='poem_1275127' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275127' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275127?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为虞丞相作辞册宝进封增邑表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1171年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275127")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275127_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275127'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275127'>至德要道，焕丕册于贲文；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275127_comment'></div>厚赏薄功，下昕廷之涣汗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275127_comment'></div>忱辞既贡，渊听尚高<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275127_comment'></div>窃以尊亲者礼之隆，养志者孝之实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275127_comment'></div>虽百王之未举，用以扬名；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275127_comment'></div>必万物之咸和，始为锡类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275127_comment'></div>将增光于鸿业，当诿属于近司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275127_comment'></div>如臣之愚，受责宜最。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275127_comment'></div>所忧吁咈，督熙载之庶尤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275127_comment'></div>敢意宠嘉，录相仪之微效！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275127_comment'></div>矧命秩建邦之异数，非畴劳懋赏之常科。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275127_comment'></div>伏望皇帝陛下稽用邦彝，惠绥人欲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275127_comment'></div>谓奉承慈极，不专典章容物之间；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275127_comment'></div>则期望弼臣，岂止宾赞摈承之末。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275127_comment'></div>亟收还于前诏，以饬厉于后勋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275127_comment'></div>再用控诚，迄期得请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275127_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1275127_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1275128' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275128' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275128?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为梁参政作辞册宝转官表<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1171年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275128")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275128_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275128'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275128'>奏牍升闻，娄干聪听；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275128_comment'></div>诏函宠答，尚閟俞音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275128_comment'></div>辄忘难犯之威，敢述终辞之义<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275128_comment'></div>伏念臣志虽许国，材不逮人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275128_comment'></div>高位难居，久弗胜于指顾；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275128_comment'></div>厚恩未报，姑少缓于乞身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275128_comment'></div>若繇庆典之成，重拜明纶之渥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275128_comment'></div>既躐崇秩，复荒大邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275128_comment'></div>则异时避宠之言，皆为虚语；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275128_comment'></div>平日恶盈之戒，自负初心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275128_comment'></div>苟必强之受而纳之贪，孰若听其辞而全其守？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275128_comment'></div>伏望皇帝陛下俯矜恳款，深体精诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275128_comment'></div>察其累疏之陈，非敢片辞之饰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275128_comment'></div>九关霄汉，倘吁告之莫通；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275128_comment'></div>一舸江湖，将归休之继请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275128_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1275128_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1275129' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275129' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275129?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1171年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275129_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275129'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275129'>显册昭融，光于二典；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275129_comment'></div>需章恳款，閟以九关。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275129_comment'></div>不胜坠谷之忧，嗣上循墙之请<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275129_comment'></div>伏念臣起繇疏贱，滥与几微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275129_comment'></div>肆惟竣事于明禋，并奏鸿名于慈极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275129_comment'></div>职是讨论之重，独出鼎司；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275129_comment'></div>凛然绘画之难，莫穷坤载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275129_comment'></div>敢图诏綍，概陟官联。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275129_comment'></div>历考前闻，邈无近比。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275129_comment'></div>欲展终辞之微志，敢循再渎之常科。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275129_comment'></div>崇听益高，奏封复却。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275129_comment'></div>虽隆威之难犯，觊拙守之获伸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275129_comment'></div>伏望皇帝陛下鉴厥忱诚，体其控诉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275129_comment'></div>厉弼谐之廉耻，用振四维；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275129_comment'></div>改庆赐于英材，以全三乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275129_comment'></div>曲收成命，少穆师言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275129_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1275129_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1275130' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275130' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275130?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为虞丞相作辞郊恩表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1171年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275130")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275130_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275130'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275130'>泰畤均釐，泽覃无外；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275130_comment'></div>路朝敷命，宠及罔功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275130_comment'></div>不胜坠谷之忧，敬致循墙之请<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275130_comment'></div>窃以大臣之义，固非饰小节以为廉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275130_comment'></div>国典之常，亦难徇一夫而违众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275130_comment'></div>既郊而赉，于古有稽，敢为喋喋之忱辞，将贡惓惓之愚虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275130_comment'></div>为臣不易，当翼厥后以思艰；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275130_comment'></div>惟天无亲，实监有邦之敬德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275130_comment'></div>傥自安于居宠，斯大戾于协恭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275130_comment'></div>伏望皇帝陛下寅畏以答天休，隆宽以从人欲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275130_comment'></div>与其尽循故事，为邦家焜耀之光；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275130_comment'></div>孰若少抑近司，示君臣兢惧之实？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275130_comment'></div>庶或上助持盈之治，岂徒私逃招损之危！</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1275130_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1275131' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275131' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275131?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为梁参政作辞郊恩表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1171年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275131")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275131_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275131'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275131'>天命匪懈，载储滋至之休；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275131_comment'></div>地道无成，弥惧大来之福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275131_comment'></div>敢辞娄渎，尚冀终从<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275131_comment'></div>伏念臣久以琐材，辱于宰枋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275131_comment'></div>内积食浮之愧，岂独危身；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275131_comment'></div>仰思覆餗之忧，将难报国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275131_comment'></div>于昭明祀，克相盛时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275131_comment'></div>颙若显承，皆群工之祗肃；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275131_comment'></div>穆然昭假，本上圣之寅恭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275131_comment'></div>顾惭老臣，曾何报效，乃飏涣汗之号，乃增汤沐之封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275131_comment'></div>诚悃虽殚，俞音尚閟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275131_comment'></div>伏望皇帝陛下俯矜拙守，博采师言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275131_comment'></div>纾其负乘之惭，裁此告廷之渥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275131_comment'></div>虽多邑不惜，固仲尼爱繁缨之心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275131_comment'></div>然足欲故亡，亦晏婴辞邶殿之义。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1275131_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1275132' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275132' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275132?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为宰臣作端诚殿贺南郊礼成笏记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1171年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275132")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275132_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275132'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275132'>竣事泰坛，扬八銮而返轸；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275132_comment'></div>受釐皇邸，旅万玉以充庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275132_comment'></div>伏惟皇帝陛下对越穆清，肃将纯嘏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275132_comment'></div>本以宸心之恪，登兹熙事之成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275132_comment'></div>陈安止谟，念几康而昭受；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275132_comment'></div>进敬之戒，监陟降于显思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275132_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1275132_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1275133' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275133' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275133?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为芮直讲作庆王辞增邑表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1171年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275133")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275133_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275133'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275133'>有命自天，被宠灵之祥异；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275133_comment'></div>无功报国，□□□以滋多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275133_comment'></div>义所当辞，言非敢饰<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275133_comment'></div>伏念臣□□□□，□□自量。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275133_comment'></div>进依日月之光，但私临照；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275133_comment'></div>幸服诗书之泽，聊助见闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275133_comment'></div>常忧居养之移，易忽骄盈之戒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275133_comment'></div>陛下慈恩益厚，宠数弥加。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275133_comment'></div>微横草之效，而增邑赋、进国封；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275133_comment'></div>蔑维城之称，而兼节镇、备藩翰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275133_comment'></div>是皆厉世摩钝之具，以待功能；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275133_comment'></div>顾于扬庭孚号之时，猥及微陋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275133_comment'></div>思圣世岂无失职之寒士，而边外必有服劳于下僚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275133_comment'></div>与其专于戚亲，孰若均之臣庶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275133_comment'></div>筹量至熟，恳请实宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275133_comment'></div>伏望皇帝陛下推从欲之仁，俾安愚分；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275133_comment'></div>察由衷之义，姑寝误恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1275133_comment'></div>苟私惠之不行，则众心之自服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1275133_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1275133_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1275134' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275134' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275134?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为芮直讲作庆王生皇孙锡名谢太上皇帝表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1171年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275134'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275134'>列第环宫，方极奉承之乐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275134_comment'></div>周庐设卫，载延似续之荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275134_comment'></div>舄奕观瞻，凌兢佩戴<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275134_comment'></div>窃以东平诸子，印犹限于能趋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275134_comment'></div>鲁国五名，类仅称于同物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275134_comment'></div>畴若覃庞恩于襁褓，矧惟锡美称于冕旒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275134_comment'></div>继继承承，爰笃曾孙之庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275134_comment'></div>愿弼成于幼学，用克对于鸿私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275134_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1275134_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1275135' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275135' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275135?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为芮直讲作庆王生皇孙锡名谢太上皇后笺</a><span class='authorDate'>（1171年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275135")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275135_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275135'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275135'>温凊承颜，慈极夙承于椒屋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275135_comment'></div>焜煌发命，光风初转于兰芽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275135_comment'></div>吉语甫传，微躬载惕<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275135_comment'></div>窃以元气两仪之运，资始资生；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275135_comment'></div>天枝四叶之祥，以嗣以续。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275135_comment'></div>庆流繁衍，爵及携持。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275135_comment'></div>此盖伏遇太上皇后殿下德冠河洲，化孚宫阃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275135_comment'></div>周邦胥喜，惠既笃于曾孙；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275135_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1275135_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1275137' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275137' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275137?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为梁参政作乞解罢政事表<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1171年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275137")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275137_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275137'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275137'>诚悃升闻，所期得请；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275137_comment'></div>温言赐却，未即报俞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275137_comment'></div>进忘难犯之威，仰吁盖高之听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275137_comment'></div>伏念臣气昏质弱，材薄虑疏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275137_comment'></div>闻国论之几微，坐弥三载；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275137_comment'></div>问政途之诿寄，何补一毫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275137_comment'></div>惭愧相乘，疾疹交作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275137_comment'></div>眊然瞻视，于文牍而已艰；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275137_comment'></div>惫矣步趋，虽会朝而犹惮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275137_comment'></div>涉冬浸剧，与日俱增。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275137_comment'></div>引大体而□远猷，素非所及；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275137_comment'></div>效小勤而躬细务，今又不能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275137_comment'></div>若复自安，可谓无耻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275137_comment'></div>荐归诚而控愬，觊从欲以悯怜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275137_comment'></div>公其尸旷之诛，岂容善罢；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275137_comment'></div>私以奉承之旧，尚许免归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275137_comment'></div>怵迫之诚，殚竭于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1275137_comment'></div>伏望皇帝陛下至明烛隐，大度包荒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1275137_comment'></div>若爱其去而积其愆，必难覆护；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1275137_comment'></div>惟遂其诚而解其责，乃尽始终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1275137_comment'></div>赋以真祠，还之故里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1275137_comment'></div>则臣忧危既释，卫养可专。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1275137_comment'></div>假其休愒之期，少加砭剂；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1275137_comment'></div>付以烦劳之事，敢惮驱驰？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1275137_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1275137_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1171&endYear=1171')">1171年2月</a>　应门人徐人杰之请，为其父作墓志铭。作品：《义乌徐君墓志铭》<div id='poem_1275648' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275648' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275648?labeling=true' target='_blank'>义乌徐君墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（乾道七年二月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275648")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275648_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275648'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275648'>同义之徐，在乌伤为右族。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275648_comment'></div>先老所传，版籍故隶诸暨，尝有官吴越为常侍者，游乌伤之同义，乐其土俗，迁焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275648_comment'></div>其谱牒可见者，腊生舜臣，舜臣生世都，世都实生君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275648_comment'></div>君讳文献，字德之，质厚惇饬，以严见惮于里中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275648_comment'></div>治家训子，咸有节法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275648_comment'></div>母朱夫人弃世，君方稚，已能自持。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275648_comment'></div>及父没，传家政，奉后母余夫人尤笃，虽乡人之习于徐氏者莫知其异出也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275648_comment'></div>比邻竞者平之，病者药之，负责不能偿者已之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275648_comment'></div>天大寒，视并舍茕独困殍，日赋之食，至于春乃罢，帅以为常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275648_comment'></div>乾道四年六月十八日，终于家，享年六十有六。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275648_comment'></div>七年二月四日己酉，葬于白马之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275648_comment'></div>娶刘氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275648_comment'></div>三子，长人杰；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275648_comment'></div>次人鉴，将仕郎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275648_comment'></div>次人瑞，蚤亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275648_comment'></div>孙男八人，侃、俨、倬，馀未名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275648_comment'></div>孙女三，长适进士余棣，馀在室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1275648_comment'></div>曾孙男四，女二，尚幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1275648_comment'></div>自禨祥禁忌之说兴，士始死其亲而徼利，巫争觋讼，客其柩宇下，远者或数十载，盖有骴腐骨销而终不掩者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1275648_comment'></div>予窃骇其然，力薄不能起俗，独私与从游者道之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1275648_comment'></div>人杰以书来曰：「先君之丧再期矣，宅兆未卜，侃、倬幸从诸生后，与闻绪论，敢不敬戒以终大事？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1275648_comment'></div>吾子其赐之铭，以卒相人杰也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1275648_comment'></div>乃铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_1275648'>厥终惟考，厥封惟时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1275648_comment'></div>有嘉徙义，瑑此铭诗。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1275648_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1171&endYear=1171')">1171年春</a>　与内兄曾集通信。作品：《与内兄曾提刑（致虚）》二。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷九。）</span><div id='poem_1275306' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275306' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275306?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与内兄曾提刑致虚书<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其四 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1171年春）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275306")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275306_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275306'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275306'>某官次粗遣，但俯仰碌碌，无所裨补。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275306_comment'></div>又史课趣迫，终日翻阅，殊少暇也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275306_comment'></div>深居里闬，优游涵养，想有馀味。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275306_comment'></div>交游亦不乏人否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275306_comment'></div>朱丈再辞，诸公不为将上，又南康签判以迟发迓吏罢黜，其势不得不黾勉一出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275306_comment'></div>若到郡数月丐祠，却自稳惬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275306_comment'></div>已作书再三勉之，不知肯起否。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275306_comment'></div>丘宗卿以接伴例外问北使一二事，遂得外祠，今已到江阴矣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1275306_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1171&endYear=1171')">1171年4月22日</a>　继室韩螺生女。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1171&endYear=1171')">1171年9月</a>　如临安条对。有书与朱熹言条对事。作品：《与朱侍讲》九。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷七。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1171&endYear=1171')">1171年秋</a>　有《与某少卿帖》，其人不详。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷七。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1171&endYear=1171')">1171年10月</a>　复朱熹来书，相与讲论，并将朝对之策寄与朱熹讨论。作品：《与朱侍讲》十一。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷七。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1171&endYear=1171')">1171年11月</a>　作书与朱熹，并寄与所订《知言疑义》，详论各章。作品：《与朱侍讲》十二。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷七。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1171&endYear=1171')">1171年12月</a>　以门人叶诞请，为其父叶臻作墓志铭。作品：《兰溪叶君墓志铭》<div id='poem_1275650' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275650' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275650?labeling=true' target='_blank'>兰溪叶君墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（乾道七年十二月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275650")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275650_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275650'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275650'>始予道兰溪，叶君介其子来见，视其貌，恢然长者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275650_comment'></div>进之，语朴质，少雕琢，意䜣然喜之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275650_comment'></div>是后岁一再舣舟溪浒，君宾送下上亡怠容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275650_comment'></div>今年秋复过焉，事薄不暇接君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275650_comment'></div>居亡何，里生周祥以书至，曰：「噫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275650_comment'></div>君死矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275650_comment'></div>其孤诞累然衰绖，不敢释丧次躬请铭于门下，使祥以告」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275650_comment'></div>予既数面君，而诞实从予游，乃序而铭之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275650_comment'></div>君讳臻，字子益。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275650_comment'></div>上世寿昌人，移其版于婺之兰溪者四传矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275650_comment'></div>曾祖昌世，祖逢，考固。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275650_comment'></div>君虽浮湛里闾，而协族辑邻，若尝知书者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275650_comment'></div>家故窭，缩衣啬食，资其子学，甫收一科以养，而君不能待也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275650_comment'></div>卒以乾道七年十月二十九日，寿五十有七。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275650_comment'></div>娶胡氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275650_comment'></div>男一，诞也，今为左迪功郎、新临江军清江县主簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275650_comment'></div>女三，长适蒋黼，次适陈良士，次在室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1275650_comment'></div>其年十二月二十日，葬于县之清江里应氏坞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1275650_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_1275650'>置也馌之，簋也夺之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1275650_comment'></div>罔极之酬，匪爵是縻。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1275650_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1171&endYear=1171')">1171年冬</a>　陆九渊至临安考试，二人初会。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1171&endYear=1171')">1171年冬</a>　以巩丰秋试失利，以书信勉以实学。作品：《与巩仲至》一。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史外集》卷五。）</span><div id='poem_1275459' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275459' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275459?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与巩仲至书</a><span class='authorDate'>（乾道七年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275459")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275459_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275459'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275459'>秋闱垂翅，乃所以进德修业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275459_comment'></div>如吾友之文，用于课试，盖无馀憾矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275459_comment'></div>不必更费心神，惟留意实学，持之以厚而守之以默，则所愿望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275459_comment'></div>令伯有还辕之问否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275459_comment'></div>他惟以时自爱。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1275459_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1171&endYear=1171')">1171年</a>　芮烨卒，作祭文。作品：《祭芮祭酒文》<div id='poem_1275695' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275695' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275695?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭芮祭酒文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1171年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275695")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275695_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275695'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275695'>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275695_comment'></div>耒耜挂壁，未试菑畬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275695_comment'></div>饥者见之，喜动眉须。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275695_comment'></div>实之感人，如鼓应桴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275695_comment'></div>见诸功用，则皆其馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275695_comment'></div>通都大逵，赴车相及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275695_comment'></div>匪戚匪姻，越肥秦瘠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275695_comment'></div>独公之丧，交吊聚泣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275695_comment'></div>公微权势，人栽户培。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275695_comment'></div>彼拳拳者，果何为哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275695_comment'></div>升屋三号，万事冰泮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275695_comment'></div>谁絷维之，至此不畔！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275695_comment'></div>矧维某等，事公泽宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275695_comment'></div>临风一恸，吾道其穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275695_comment'></div>前日之祖，今日之酹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275695_comment'></div>觞酒未酸，俛仰千载。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1275695_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1171&endYear=1171')">1171年</a>　王十朋卒，作挽章。作品：《王詹事挽章》二首之一。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷一。）</span>《王詹事挽章》二首之二。<span id='poem_title_94081_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_94081'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_94081'>大使交旃日，元戎解甲秋。<div id='poem_sentence_0_94081_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_94081'>先鸣惊众寐，孤愤压<span class='inlineComment2'>（原校：一作厌）</span>群咻。<div id='poem_sentence_1_94081_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_94081'>羽翼新鸿鹄，声华旧斗牛。<div id='poem_sentence_2_94081_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_94081'>断桥亡恙否，落月照寒流。<div id='poem_sentence_3_94081_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_94081'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_94081_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1171&endYear=1171')">1171年</a>　有《李粹伯侍御母挽章》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷一。）</span><div id='poem_94098' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_94098' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/94098?labeling=true' target='_blank'>李粹伯侍御母夫人挽章</a><span class='authorDate'>（1171年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_94098")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_94098_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_94098'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_94098'>对仗峨冠日，鲸牙汹九渊。<div id='poem_sentence_0_94098_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_94098'>堂萱不改色，台柏故参天。<div id='poem_sentence_1_94098_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_94098'>共识吾君圣，今知此母贤。<div id='poem_sentence_2_94098_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_94098'>丁宁刘子□，□事一时编。<div id='poem_sentence_3_94098_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_94098'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_94098_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1171&endYear=1171')">1171年</a>　有《代宰臣虞允文恭书皇帝御书崔实证论下方》<div id='poem_1275514' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275514' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275514?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代宰臣虞允文恭书皇帝御书崔寔政论下方</a><span class='authorDate'>（乾道六年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275514")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275514_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275514'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275514'>皇帝临御之九年，恩浃教孚，方内顺适。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275514_comment'></div>小大之臣，既材诸位，欢曰：「天下事今治，宜勿复有为」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275514_comment'></div>皇帝曰：「嘻，是乌足究其极！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275514_comment'></div>维予九年于兹，夙寝晨兴，将笃我祖宗成烈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275514_comment'></div>凡奔走先后，以就予事，惟时公卿大夫，而安习所见，谓足以止，其何以底于大宁」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275514_comment'></div>于是数用「治道不进」谯谕一二大臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275514_comment'></div>已乃亲御宸翰于汉议郎崔寔《政论》，幸赐臣允文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275514_comment'></div>若曰：士俗流失，使天下事格而不得为，如崔寔所指，臣允文当任其责云耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275514_comment'></div>臣允文承受震悸，自惟驽散，幸以际遇待罪宰相，日闻德音，弗克以时风晓在庭，俾谕上旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275514_comment'></div>而恬于积习，节趋不立，以仰烦云章奎画，明示大训，使知今日急政所在，其何以为报？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275514_comment'></div>用三复寔言，冀万一服行少分，以称隆旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275514_comment'></div>窃尝究观汉自安、顺以降，天下荡然，无复典法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275514_comment'></div>一世贤者，如杨震、杜乔、李固、陈蕃诸人，继起为辅，莫不欲整天纲、正官邪，以清四海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275514_comment'></div>然志卒不遂而祸辱随之者，寔惟悠悠之谈，乐宽弛而羞法制，使当时国论靡有所定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275514_comment'></div>此则寔之论所由兴也，而其大率不过以达权救弊，与俗士相上下，若切切于数君子之见掎夺者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275514_comment'></div>故司马光论之曰：「汉法严矣，而崔寔犹病其宽，何哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275514_comment'></div>衰世之君，率常庸凡，愚庸之俗，惟知姑息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1275514_comment'></div>是以权倖之臣，有罪不坐，豪猾之民，犯法不诛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1275514_comment'></div>仁恩所施，止于目前，奸宄得志，纲纪不立」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1275514_comment'></div>谓寔之论以矫一时之枉也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1275514_comment'></div>光之言可谓尽寔之心矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1275514_comment'></div>以陛下天德地业，皇帝王之事惟所欲用，顾于寔眷焉独有所求，遂使匹夫之遗言，一旦炜然震发于昭回之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1275514_comment'></div>非圣哲独观，有以见天下之动，孰知夫寔之有味其言哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1275514_comment'></div>然遭汉季，无复一君足望救时之敝，亦安能使之纯法八世致理于时？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1275514_comment'></div>其曰参以霸政，其心盖有抑郁而未之尽者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1275514_comment'></div>至所谓大定其本，师五帝而式三王，弃苟全之政，蹈稽古之踪，此陛下圣学之缉熙，在今日所当讲明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1275514_comment'></div>特稷、契之佐，伊、吕之辅，曾未如卒章所云，此则臣之所甚惧也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1275514_comment'></div>惟陛下选建其人，必极于三五之隆，而后税驾，诚不胜老臣惓惓之义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1275514_comment'></div>敢以宸翰镂之乐石，昭垂训戒，于万斯年，为乡方砥节之劝，并昧死附见下方云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1275514_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1171&endYear=1171')">1171年</a>　为方季肃作祭文。作品：《祭方季肃文》<div id='poem_1275696' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275696' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275696?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭方季肃文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1171年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275696")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275696_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275696'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275696'>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275696_comment'></div>我来自西，访旧闾里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275696_comment'></div>巾褐蔼然，朋簪胥会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275696_comment'></div>历数坐间，独子不至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275696_comment'></div>问所以然，曰既长逝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275696_comment'></div>土方即学，如鼓作气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275696_comment'></div>时不待人，将驾已税。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275696_comment'></div>烹鸡炊黍，寓哀一酹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275696_comment'></div>匪惟子哀，尚儆同志。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1275696_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1171&endYear=1171')">1171年</a>　作书与朱熹，感慨前辈多逝。劝朱熹严择弟子。作品：《与朱侍讲》十。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷七。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1172&endYear=1172')">1172年2月</a>　在试院，为省试考官。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1172&endYear=1172')">1172年2月4日</a>　获悉父病，请假离临安归婺。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='be9bdfa392ef41d5b571ab8c8bc53757_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("be9bdfa392ef41d5b571ab8c8bc53757");'><span id='be9bdfa392ef41d5b571ab8c8bc53757_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1172&endYear=1172')">1172年</a>，36岁</div><div id='be9bdfa392ef41d5b571ab8c8bc53757' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1172&endYear=1172')">1172年春</a>　在临安为省试考官，识拔陆九渊、舒璘等进士及第。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='b2a2abd238644e4aafe1fdcc2b15d266_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("b2a2abd238644e4aafe1fdcc2b15d266");'><span id='b2a2abd238644e4aafe1fdcc2b15d266_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1176&endYear=1179')">1176-1179年</a>，40-43岁</div><div id='b2a2abd238644e4aafe1fdcc2b15d266' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1176&endYear=1176')">1176年10月29日</a>　赴临安任职。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1176&endYear=1176')">1176年10月</a>　应张杰请作《张监镇墓志铭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷十三。）</span><div id='poem_1275674' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275674' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275674?labeling=true' target='_blank'>张监镇墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（淳熙三年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275674")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275674_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275674'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275674'>乾道五年，信安张杰赴于其友吕某曰：「先君以七月二十五日弃诸孤，敢告于执事」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275674_comment'></div>某既与使者为礼，即办装，粤十月二日会其葬于衢之西安县靖安乡九龙山已下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275674_comment'></div>杰拜且哭曰：「先君之葬也，遽未有辞以识诸幽，将惟子是属」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275674_comment'></div>授以汴人赵焯行状一通，某再拜兴受，退而于役于仕，于丧于疾，栖置笔研，未克具藁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275674_comment'></div>杰以书趣曰：「己丑之会，吾子尝坠言焉，今墓木之叶七易矣，吾子独无意乎」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275674_comment'></div>某矍然惊谢，乃序而铭之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275674_comment'></div>君讳淑坚，字正卿，其先自开封迁于衢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275674_comment'></div>曾祖智全，尚书都官郎中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275674_comment'></div>祖咏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275674_comment'></div>考彦琦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275674_comment'></div>君蚤向意文学，虽以季父任为承信郎，年馀四十，足未尝至吏部门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275674_comment'></div>研索典籍，矻矻如诸生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275674_comment'></div>周览旁浃，星历、方剂、篆籀之属，无所不窥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275674_comment'></div>浮湛里闾，遇疾痛呻吟者，或和药饮之，随失其疾，世医莫能识其节度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275674_comment'></div>谒者浸众，君悠然应之，不为彼此薄厚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275674_comment'></div>晚岁始出，监信州汭口镇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275674_comment'></div>镇居往来之冲，课额夥甚，前政数负殿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1275674_comment'></div>君通商平酤，经入用登。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1275674_comment'></div>铜官铁官漕卒，将输如织，颉颃侵暴，镇官素不能令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1275674_comment'></div>自君之至，道镇境者皆抑首屏气，无敢哗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1275674_comment'></div>庀局甫四月，卒官下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1275674_comment'></div>镇民相与负其柩还衢，其孤强之僦直，委去不顾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1275674_comment'></div>盖君于是年四十有八，官止承节郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1275674_comment'></div>有《诗》、《书》解合三十卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1275674_comment'></div>始君程督诸子，诵肄蚤夜不置。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1275674_comment'></div>已而长子策名，人意其绳约当少宽，君所以训厉之者益峻，甚于他子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1275674_comment'></div>然则君之期其子，其诸异乎人之期者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1275674_comment'></div>娶叶氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1275674_comment'></div>三子：杰，迪功郎、宁国府府学教授；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1275674_comment'></div>次皋、次舆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1275674_comment'></div>一女，适袁焕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1275674_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_31_1275674'>缓己之进，匪辰之竞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1275674_comment'></div>急人之忧，匪艺之羞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1275674_comment'></div>期子之大，匪胜之怠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1275674_comment'></div>不怠其昌，视此石章。</div><div id='poem_sentence_34_1275674_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1176&endYear=1176')">1176年11月5日</a>　以秘书郎兼实录院检讨官与修《徽宗实录》，以清原正本为己任。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1176&endYear=1176')">1176年12月</a>　修《徽宗实录》。有书与朱熹，探问朱熹妻子刘氏病况。作品：《与朱侍讲》十一。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷八。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1176&endYear=1176')">1176年12月</a>　同馆杨恂卒，有挽章。作品：《杨信伯郎中挽章二首》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷一。）</span><div id='poem_94100' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_94100' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/94100?labeling=true' target='_blank'>杨信伯郎中挽章二首<span class='inlineComment2'>（洵）</span><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1176年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_94100")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_94100_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_94100'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_94100'>象魏三千法，瀛洲十八人。<div id='poem_sentence_0_94100_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_94100'>南宫占列宿，少海近重轮。<div id='poem_sentence_1_94100_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_94100'>闻道清羸极，犹有职业亲。<div id='poem_sentence_2_94100_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_94100'>榴皮馀屋壁，零落独无神<span class='inlineComment2'>（续金华本作痕）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_94100_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_94100'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_94100_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_94099' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_94099' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/94099?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1176年12月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_94099_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_94099'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_94099'>并舍游从旧，同朝分义深。<div id='poem_sentence_0_94099_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_94099'>时时坠书札，得得到山林。<div id='poem_sentence_1_94099_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_94099'>北去先移棹，南来后盍簪。<div id='poem_sentence_2_94099_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_94099'>死生离合地，搔首一悲吟<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：前岁某还朝，公方去国。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_94099_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_94099'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_94099_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1176&endYear=1176')">1176年12月</a>　应门人时铸请，为其父作墓铭。作品：《金华时君德懋墓志铭》<div id='poem_1275675' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275675' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275675?labeling=true' target='_blank'>金华时君德懋墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（淳熙三年十二月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275675")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275675_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275675'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275675'>隆兴改元，天子赐进士第于廷，东阳郡登名者十有八人，时铸、吕某皆在选中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275675_comment'></div>淳熙二年四月丙辰，铸执父丧，某往吊焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275675_comment'></div>铸拜稽颡，哭且请曰：「吾父劬躬教子，里人莫不闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275675_comment'></div>铸也甫得一官以养，阅日未久，吾父遽大弃之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275675_comment'></div>所以忍死须臾者，惟楄柎窀穸之事不克终是惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275675_comment'></div>子幸哀而赐之铭，以卒相铸也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275675_comment'></div>某辞不获命，退考其谱牒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275675_comment'></div>其先盖开封人，五季之乱，始自占于金华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275675_comment'></div>君讳汝功，字德懋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275675_comment'></div>曾祖则，祖理，考焕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275675_comment'></div>君生而惇质，亡遨逸浮靡之习。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275675_comment'></div>宣和中，盗发青溪，兵锋所及，人自求生，至亲或不相保。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275675_comment'></div>君财十馀岁，已能从其父母，崎岖兵间，扶携负挈，跬步不失，左右见者异焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275675_comment'></div>稍长，夺于家事，不得日对编简，慊然常若不满。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275675_comment'></div>中年，乃筑室买书，饬厉其子不少置。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275675_comment'></div>已而铸以命服拜堂下，贺者塞门，咸曰此善人之报也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275675_comment'></div>久之，铸尉鄂之嘉鱼，戒板舆请君俱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1275675_comment'></div>君曰：「吾幸有先人故田庐，朝姻暮戚，足以自娱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1275675_comment'></div>行矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1275675_comment'></div>守汝身，庀汝职，无干官常，以为吾忧」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1275675_comment'></div>复曰：「湖外俸入薄，吾且损伏腊调度，以佐汝费，其勿以衣食自累」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1275675_comment'></div>君之遇其子，它皆类此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1275675_comment'></div>于兄弟尤笃，晚岁哭其仲弟，过时而哀不衰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1275675_comment'></div>以至辑柔宗姓，承宁乡邻，逢迎旧故，率用和厚，内外无违言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1275675_comment'></div>其终也，享年六十有八。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1275675_comment'></div>娶邵氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1275675_comment'></div>三子：长曰鉴；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1275675_comment'></div>次则铸，今为从政郎、新隆兴府南昌县丞；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1275675_comment'></div>季曰镇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1275675_comment'></div>三女，长适邵澄，次适汪旦，季适邵庚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1275675_comment'></div>孙男曰澜、道、济、梁、潜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1275675_comment'></div>君没之明年十二月甲申，葬于县之惠日乡九里原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1275675_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_32_1275675'>十年之计，侯杞侯梓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1275675_comment'></div>百年之计，则惟孙子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1275675_comment'></div>庙鼎之陈，有禄自天，嗣德不怠，尚封其阡。</div><div id='poem_sentence_34_1275675_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1177&endYear=1177')">1177年1月</a>　修《徽宗实录》。有书与朱熹吊问朱熹妻子刘氏去世。作品：《与朱侍讲》十一。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷十一。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1177&endYear=1177')">1177年1月</a>　闻潘景宪病，致书劝其宽心自养。作品：《答潘叔度》二十五。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷十。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1177&endYear=1177')">1177年3月9日</a>　实录院进《徽宗皇帝实录》二百卷，吕祖谦为审订，删削数百条。作程颢、程颐传。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1177&endYear=1177')">1177年春</a>　李椿守婺，有《答潘叔度书》为婺州贺。作品：《答潘叔度》二十三。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷十。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1177&endYear=1177')">1177年春</a>　致书内兄曾集，叹三馆无奈。作品：《与内兄曾提刑》三。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷十九。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1177&endYear=1177')">1177年春</a>　为鲁某作挽章。作品：《鲁少卿挽章》<div id='poem_94127' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_94127' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/94127?labeling=true' target='_blank'>鲁少卿挽章<span class='inlineComment2'>（淳熙四年春）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1177年春）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_94127")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_94127_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_94127'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_94127'>庆源衮衮接天流，老桂传香次第秋。<div id='poem_sentence_0_94127_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_94127'>人物西都九卿选，光华南国十州游。<div id='poem_sentence_1_94127_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_94127'>翛然径下滕王阁，已矣长怀范蠡舟。<div id='poem_sentence_2_94127_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_94127'>身后楚骚谁著录，灵光旧草合兼收<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_94127_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_94127'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_94127_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_94127'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_94127_0'>⑴ 自注：王文考逸之子作《灵光赋》而夭，宗教君实似之。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_94127_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1177&endYear=1177')">1177年春</a>　与韩元吉雨中游西湖。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1177&endYear=1177')">1177年4月29日</a>　以与修《实录》有劳，减一年磨勘，转承议郎，罢检讨，仍兼史职。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1177&endYear=1177')">1177年4月</a>　致书朱熹为刘氏择墓地勿信阴阳家说，并勉其丧后切须保重身体。作品：《与朱侍讲》十三。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷八。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1177&endYear=1177')">1177年4月</a>　以秀州守吕正己约请，作《秀州陆宣公祠堂记》<div id='poem_1275598' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275598' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275598?labeling=true' target='_blank'>秀州陆宣公祠堂记<span class='inlineComment2'>（淳熙间）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1177年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275598")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275598_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275598'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275598'>古者建学，先圣先师，各因其国之故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275598_comment'></div>国无其人，然后合他国而释奠焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275598_comment'></div>由汉以来，先圣先师之位虽定于一，然郡邑先贤，亦往往祠于学宫，犹古意也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275598_comment'></div>《唐史》载陆宣公贽，苏州嘉兴人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275598_comment'></div>石晋时，吴越王元瓘奏以嘉兴置秀州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275598_comment'></div>城东桥以宣公名者，先老相传公所生之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275598_comment'></div>郡学故有公祠，今郡守直显谟阁吕侯正己复缉而新之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275598_comment'></div>维秀陪翼行都，典治为天下剧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275598_comment'></div>侯独置将迎期会之烦，表公以风厉多士，其亦知本务矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275598_comment'></div>初，公事德宗，入翰林为学士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275598_comment'></div>方禁旅四出伐叛，公深以根本为虑，论居重驭轻之势至熟悉也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275598_comment'></div>未几，泾卒内讧，迄如公忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275598_comment'></div>奉天艰难之际，虽号亲近而志实不大纾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275598_comment'></div>职在书诏，因得具著天子悔过罪己之意，闻者流涕，人心已离而复合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275598_comment'></div>以使事抵李怀光，于立谈顷拔李晟之军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275598_comment'></div>已而平贼泚，收长安，独晟军是赖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275598_comment'></div>官守所及，觕见一二，已足以再造唐室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1275598_comment'></div>茍帝以国听焉，其所成就何如哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1275598_comment'></div>起建中、历贞元，垂二十年，离合从违之变繁矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1275598_comment'></div>确乎其不移，温乎其不怼，亹亹乎其不厌，所积之厚，岂世所易窥耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1275598_comment'></div>晚节为相，经世之业，出之固有次第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1275598_comment'></div>始建白台省长官各举其属，议辄见格，然纲条本末，具载于章奏者，尚可覆也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1275598_comment'></div>既贬忠州，阖户人不识其面，专以方药自娱，盖畏天命、畏大人，负罪引慝于幽閒隐约之中，其志念深矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1275598_comment'></div>虽德宗雄猜忌克，犹劳问有加，非公之忠敬有以发之耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1275598_comment'></div>彼谓避谤不著书，殆知公之细者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1275598_comment'></div>秀维公里，隽彦林立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1275598_comment'></div>公之精缊，列于乡论者旧矣，故于祠宇之成，诵所闻以质其中否焉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1275598_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1177&endYear=1177')">1177年4月</a>　作《祭邢邦用》文。<div id='poem_1275707' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275707' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275707?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭邢邦用文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1177年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275707")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275707_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275707'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275707'>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275707_comment'></div>子之于学笃矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275707_comment'></div>质性淳固，可谓有学之资；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275707_comment'></div>兄弟雍和，可谓有学之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275707_comment'></div>婿于德门，左右观法，则既知学之实；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275707_comment'></div>游于四方，师友讲论，则益知学之方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275707_comment'></div>小试曹掾，素怀得伸，若使其信学之坚，还归乡闾，儒风方起，若多其共学之助，天之相子者何其多耶！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275707_comment'></div>眚灾狎至，哭其二季未已，而身从之，夺之者又何其骤也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275707_comment'></div>大时不齐，消息盈虚之理，子其闻之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275707_comment'></div>全而归之，于子何憾？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275707_comment'></div>一觞之恸，盖故旧之义，姻戚之情，所不能已也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275707_comment'></div>日者邦杰之丧，其奠辞盖曰将见仲氏而致此哀焉，庸讵知未及见子而复哀子耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275707_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉！</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1275707_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1177&endYear=1177')">1177年5月</a>　作书与曾季狸，道向往之情并言及赵景明、赵景昭兄弟来访。作品：《与艇斋曾先生》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷七。）</span><div id='poem_1275188' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275188' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275188?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与艇斋曾先生裘父书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1177年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275188")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275188_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275188'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275188'>某区区之迹，自罹忧患，屏居五年，阖户温习故书，粗似安适。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275188_comment'></div>去秋偶复有册府之命，黾勉此来，供职亦踰半载，湛浮窃食，殊愧初心，诲警箴规，惟门下是望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275188_comment'></div>先人交游，凋落向尽，海内父执如契丈不过一二人而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275188_comment'></div>所以惓惓归诚，非若简牍之虚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275188_comment'></div>赵景明兄弟来，能具道比来启处之详，虽未获侍坐，亦足少慰间阔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275188_comment'></div>偶因景明遣人还，辄此附拜起居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275188_comment'></div>向暑，敢祈厚为道义护重。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1275188_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1177&endYear=1177')">1177年5月</a>　应门人宋甡之请，为其父作墓铭。作品：《宋郴州墓志铭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷十三。）</span><div id='poem_1275676' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275676' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275676?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宋郴州墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（淳熙四年五月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275676")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275676_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275676'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275676'>朝奉郎、主管台州崇道观宋公讳有，字子华，以淳熙四年正月丁卯卒于婺之里第，五月壬寅，葬于赤松乡糁岭原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275676_comment'></div>其孤以迪功郎、监潭州南岳庙刘峤状来谒铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275676_comment'></div>去年秋，某与公别，愀然忽以死事见付，时公寝食固自如也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275676_comment'></div>呜呼，孰知未半岁而竟铭公乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275676_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1275676'>睦来之宋，版于金华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275676_comment'></div>以农相传，黄壁之窊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275676_comment'></div>八世曰正，始厌耒耞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275676_comment'></div>相攸近郊，城西是家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275676_comment'></div>九世曰裕，繄公祢庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275676_comment'></div>逮公之幼，载教载诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275676_comment'></div>养虽弗洎，光远有辉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275676_comment'></div>以朝大夫，即第而告。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275676_comment'></div>公初筮学，帮寇叛天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275676_comment'></div>号擗兵间，家祸之延。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275676_comment'></div>靖康建炎，烽燧属连。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275676_comment'></div>策士如林，公往参焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275676_comment'></div>有离有合，有逢有牾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1275676_comment'></div>晚名一官，主善化簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1275676_comment'></div>潭大都会，运艘所聚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1275676_comment'></div>阨于侵牟，或系其孥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1275676_comment'></div>慨然建白，弊剔患祛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1275676_comment'></div>贼荼黄七，横行里闾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1275676_comment'></div>乘吏惰媮，培痈护疽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1275676_comment'></div>亟填牢户，良民用苏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1275676_comment'></div>盐官在温，司仓是徙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1275676_comment'></div>劬躬勤事，陵储阜偫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1275676_comment'></div>江夏龙泉，閒剧异施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1275676_comment'></div>公宰两邦，左右具宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1275676_comment'></div>陪贰于潭，旧所习知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1275676_comment'></div>阖府诵叹，不见瑕疵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1275676_comment'></div>千里上游，郴古分郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1275676_comment'></div>帝心远民，俾公往镇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1275676_comment'></div>闭閤无为，临以清静。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1275676_comment'></div>年至而归，上还符印。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1275676_comment'></div>乃脂我车，我车我徒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1275676_comment'></div>乃行我田，我田我庐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1275676_comment'></div>社腊逢迎，共相嬉娱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1275676_comment'></div>齿八十一，寿则有馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1275676_comment'></div>厥配杜嫔，前归其墟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1275676_comment'></div>长子维佖，实嗣宗职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1275676_comment'></div>沆也蚤亡，孙数则七。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1275676_comment'></div>九龄既夭，甡林角立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1275676_comment'></div>朋行弜珏，长幼秩秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1275676_comment'></div>女孙之伯，婿蒋端益。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1275676_comment'></div>仲季叔倪，其二在室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1275676_comment'></div>施于曾孙，男一女一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1275676_comment'></div>维松有乡，维糁有宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1275676_comment'></div>维窆有石，系载初终。</div><div id='poem_sentence_47_1275676_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1177&endYear=1177')">1177年夏</a>　与李焘论文，深悔永嘉文体之病，将以平正朴实为先。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1177&endYear=1177')">1177年7月</a>　致书潘景宪劝其常养胸次。作品：《答潘叔度》十九。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷十七。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1177&endYear=1177')">1177年8月</a>　有书与朱熹说对札的准备情况，表示将尽平生所学。作品：《与朱侍讲》十八。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷八。）</span><div id='poem_1275206' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275206' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275206?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与朱侍讲元晦书<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其六 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1174年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275206")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275206_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275206'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275206'>某官下粗遣，学浅力薄，视职业日增愧负。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275206_comment'></div>虽不敢苟简自恕，然殊未能大有所釐正耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275206_comment'></div>至于区区课试之末，则固未尝深较也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275206_comment'></div>张丈邻墙，日夕相过讲论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275206_comment'></div>士子有志于此者，亦有一二辈，切摩工夫，粗不歇灭断续。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275206_comment'></div>又时阅来诲，策厉警省者殊多，但书不尽意，终不若侍坐隅、难疑答问为亲切耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275206_comment'></div>邪说诐行，辞而辟之，诚今日任此道者之责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275206_comment'></div>窃尝谓异端之不息，由正学之不明，此盛彼衰，互相消长，莫若尽力于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275206_comment'></div>此道光明盛大，则彼之消铄无日矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275206_comment'></div>孟子所谓「吾为此惧，闲先圣之道」，旧说以闲为闲习，意味甚长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275206_comment'></div>杨、墨肆行，政以吾道之衰耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275206_comment'></div>孟子所以不求之它，而以闲习吾先圣之道为急先务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275206_comment'></div>而淫辞诐行之放，则固自有次第也，不知吾丈以为如何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275206_comment'></div>所以为此说者，非欲含糊纵释，黑白不辨，但恐专意外攘，而内修处工夫或少耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275206_comment'></div>向来所论智仁勇，终恐难分轻重，盖三者天下之达德，通圣、贤、常人而言之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275206_comment'></div>在圣人则智也仁也勇也，皆生知安行也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275206_comment'></div>在贤人则智也仁也勇也，皆学知利行也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1275206_comment'></div>在常人则智也仁也勇也，皆困知勉行也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1275206_comment'></div>恐难指定智为学知利行，勇为困知勉行，龟山之说，终不免有疑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1275206_comment'></div>周子「仁义中正主静」之说，前书所言「仁义中正」皆主乎此，非谓中正仁义皆静之用而别有块然之静也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1275206_comment'></div>人生而静，天之性也，乃中正仁义之体，而万物之一源也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1275206_comment'></div>中则无不正矣，必并言之曰中、正、仁，则无不义矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1275206_comment'></div>必并言之曰仁、义，亦犹元可以包四德，而与亨、利、贞俱列；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1275206_comment'></div>仁可以包四端，而与义、礼、智同称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1275206_comment'></div>此所谓合之不浑，离之不散者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1275206_comment'></div>昨所云文理密察，盖亦如来谕，初非以为秘密之密，观察之察也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1275206_comment'></div>谓如《易传》中以形体谓之天，以主宰谓之帝，以功用谓之鬼神，以妙用谓之神，以性情谓之乾等语，铢分粒剖，各有攸当而未尝有割裂杌󷽥之病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1275206_comment'></div>析理精微如此，乃可谓之文理密察耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1275206_comment'></div>阴阳仁义之说，鄙意未达，终觉未安，当更潜思玩味，续得求教也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1275206_comment'></div>《中庸》「不可能」、「道不远人」两章，反覆思之，龟山之说诚为奇险，非子思本指。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1275206_comment'></div>向日不觉其非者，政缘为程文时，考观新说，馀习时有在者故耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1275206_comment'></div>所与诸生讲说《左氏》，语意伤巧，病源亦在是，自此当力扫除也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1275206_comment'></div>婺本《易传》，纳三本去，不敢加装治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1275206_comment'></div>误字皆已改，但卦画粗细、行数疏密之类，不能如人意悉釐正耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1275206_comment'></div>《遗书》建本未到，已用去冬所寄本刊板，故其间一两段更易次序处，姑仍其旧，馀皆以建本为正，闻旦夕亦毕工矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1275206_comment'></div>《二程先生集》，款曲亦当令婺人刊之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1275206_comment'></div>然新添伊川二子所为序引，殊无家风，恐适足为先生之累，欲削去之，更望一报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1275206_comment'></div>见所寄张丈所论时事，一一精当，不胜叹服，此间所共讲者亦十八九同也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1275206_comment'></div>知言往在严陵时，与张丈讲论亦尝疏出可疑者数十条，今观来示，其半亦相类，见与张丈参阅，续当咨请也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1275206_comment'></div>其馀已见于张丈书者，更不重出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1275206_comment'></div>相去之远，惟祈因便时赐教督，不惜语言，痛加砭治，乃所愿望。</div><div id='poem_sentence_40_1275206_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1177&endYear=1177')">1177年8月</a>　有书与潘叔度说对札的准备情况，表示将尽平生所学。作品：《答潘叔度》三十一。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷十。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1177&endYear=1177')">1177年8月</a>　对策，有《轮对札子》，批评朝政，极言直谏。作品：《淳熙四年轮对札子二首》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷三。）</span><div id='poem_1275158' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275158' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275158?labeling=true' target='_blank'>淳熙四年轮对劄子<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1177年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275158")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275158_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275158'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275158'>臣窃惟皇帝陛下临御以来，惟绍复大业是志，惟计安县内是图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275158_comment'></div>前代帝王聪明勤俭仅得陛下万分之一者，莫不随世而就功业，未有如陛下汲汲望治十有六年而焦劳未解者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275158_comment'></div>意者殆群臣不足以佐下风欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275158_comment'></div>陛下自履尊极，政令屡有所更革，人材屡有所易置矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275158_comment'></div>方其未更也，方其未易也，群臣有能先事建白以起发圣意者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275158_comment'></div>其所以敝未极而变患未甚而消者，独赖陛下生知天纵，随即觉悟而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275158_comment'></div>故举偏救弊，维持至于今日者，实由陛下圣明独运，而非群臣之助也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275158_comment'></div>然志勤道远，迁延至于今日者，亦由陛下圣躬独劳，而无群臣之助也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275158_comment'></div>陛下初岂乐于独劳哉，良以群臣不能仰助如前所陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275158_comment'></div>加之总揽既久，图事揆策者多不如陛下之精审，议法定令者多不如陛下之明习。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275158_comment'></div>甚则私意小智，又多不逃陛下之识察，陛下遂谓天下之事既知之矣，天下之人既见之矣，所以慨然益坚独运万机之意也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275158_comment'></div>夫独运万机之说，其名甚美，其实则不可不察焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275158_comment'></div>臣请序而言之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275158_comment'></div>人主一心，实治乱安危之所从出，所患者夺于多欲则其心昏蔽而不能宰制万事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275158_comment'></div>今陛下于声色、于游畋，澹然无一毫之欲，惟其有意于独运万机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275158_comment'></div>故琐微繁细，悉经省览，酬酢区画，日不暇给，而天下大计，或有所遗，治效不进，反与多欲者同，岂不甚可惜乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275158_comment'></div>此独运万机之说不可不察也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1275158_comment'></div>厥今虏势陆梁而国雠未雪，民力殚尽而邦本未宁，法度具存而穿穴蠹蚀，实百弊俱极之时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1275158_comment'></div>官寺充满而媮惰苟且，无庶绩咸熙之效；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1275158_comment'></div>降附布于郡县，而未免于疑沮；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1275158_comment'></div>帑藏耗于军屯，而未免于怨嗟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1275158_comment'></div>陛下欲宽宵旰之忧，要必得非常之材委属之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1275158_comment'></div>然非常之材类皆不肯舍规矩准绳而徇人，惟忘势尽礼有宾友之义，推诚笃信有父子之亲，而后可致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1275158_comment'></div>苟独运万机则非能受控御者鲜或在列，上益务损其权，下益得逃其责，阴拱熟视，沈浮取容，陛下宵旰之忧，谁与图之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1275158_comment'></div>此独运万机之说不可不察也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1275158_comment'></div>治道体统，上下内外不相陵夺而后安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1275158_comment'></div>乡者大臣往往不称倚任，陛下不得已而兼行其事，大臣亦皆亲细务而行有司之事，外至监司、守令，职任率为其上所侵而不能令其下，故豪猾玩官府，郡县忽省部，掾属陵长吏，贱人轻柄臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1275158_comment'></div>平居患犹未尽见也，一旦有事，谁与招麾而伸缩之耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1275158_comment'></div>由一命而上，大小相承，积而至于人主，然后尊重无以复加。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1275158_comment'></div>苟万机独运，大臣而下皆为人所易，则人主岂能独尊重哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1275158_comment'></div>如曰臣下权任太隆，惧其不能无私，则有给舍以出纳焉，有台谏以纠正焉，有侍从以询访焉，诚得端方不倚之人分处之，自无专恣之虑，何必屈至尊以代其劳哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1275158_comment'></div>此独运万机之说不可不察也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1275158_comment'></div>陛下至公无我，左右之臣虽素号亲密，至其有过，威断力行，何尝有所牵制？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1275158_comment'></div>可否黜陟，裁自圣心，所谓左右之臣，不过供指顾、传命令，何尝假以事权？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1275158_comment'></div>天下徒闻陛下独运万机，事由中出，听其声不察其实，妄意在旁者或微有所预也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1275158_comment'></div>而其陪侍习熟，工于揣摩，亦能时以一二事取验于外，故人稍稍乡之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1275158_comment'></div>此在英主之世，本非大患，惟明扬贤隽，各还其职，公议而公行之，则人自无所疑，而为左右者亦得全其恩意，保其宠禄矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1275158_comment'></div>狷介之士忿激过当，至以汉、唐权倖为比，诚非所拟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1275158_comment'></div>然人之关鬲经络，少有壅滞，久则生疾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1275158_comment'></div>陛下之于左右，虽不劳操制，苟玩而弗虑，则声势浸长，趋附浸多，过咎浸积，内则惧为陛下所谴而益思壅蔽，外则惧为公议所疾而益思诋排。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1275158_comment'></div>及是时，忿激者之所忧将见之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1275158_comment'></div>此独运万机之说不可不察也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1275158_comment'></div>臣愿陛下虚心屈己，以来天下之善，居尊执要，以总万事之成，勿以图任或误而谓人多可疑，勿以聪明独高而谓智足遍察，勿详于小而遗远大之计，勿忽于近而忘壅蔽之萌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1275158_comment'></div>诚意笃而远迩各竭其忠，体统正而内外各得其职，则二帝三王之治，不能加毫末于此矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1275158_comment'></div>臣愚戆不识大体，惟陛下裁赦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1275158_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_45_1275158_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1275159' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275159' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275159?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1177年8月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275159_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275159'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275159'>臣窃惟国朝治体，有远过前代者，有视前代犹未备者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275159_comment'></div>以宽大忠厚建立规摹，以礼逊节义成就风俗，当俶扰艰虞之后，其效方见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275159_comment'></div>如东晋之在江左，内难相寻，曾无宁岁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275159_comment'></div>自驻跸东南以来，踰五十年无纤毫之虞，则根本至深可知矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275159_comment'></div>此所谓远过前代者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275159_comment'></div>文治可观而武绩未振，名胜相望而干略未优，虽昌炽盛大之时，此病已见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275159_comment'></div>如西夏元昊之难，汉、唐谋臣从容可办，以范仲淹、韩琦之贤，皆一时选，曾莫能平殄，则事功不竞可知矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275159_comment'></div>此所谓视前代犹未备者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275159_comment'></div>陛下慨然念雠耻之未复，版图之未归，故留意功实，将以增益治体之所未备，至于本朝立国之根本，盖未尝忘也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275159_comment'></div>而臣下不足以测知宸指，献言者多以小辩破大体，治民者多以苛政立威名，逼蹙拘制而士气不舒，争夺驰骛而仕路益隘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275159_comment'></div>凡所谓宽大忠厚、礼逊节义之属，皆诋以为陈腐、为迂阔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275159_comment'></div>范防既彻，无复畏葸，何所不为？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275159_comment'></div>圣虑将益焦劳矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275159_comment'></div>夫浮华可抑也，繁文可减也，清谈高论、不切事情者可黜也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275159_comment'></div>至于祖宗化成风俗，所以维持天下者，其可朘削之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275159_comment'></div>臣窃谓今日治体其视前代未备者，固当激厉而振起，其远过前代者，尤当爱护而扶持。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275159_comment'></div>议者乃徒欲事功之增而忘根本之损，陛下清閒之时，岂可不永念其故哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1275159_comment'></div>又况宽大则豪杰得以展尽，忠厚则群众不忍欺诬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1275159_comment'></div>礼逊兴则潜消跋扈飞扬之心，节义明则坐长捐躯殉国之气，然则图维事功，亦未有舍根本而能立者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1275159_comment'></div>惟陛下加圣心焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1275159_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1275159_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1177&endYear=1177')">1177年8月</a>　秘阁修撰萧之敏卒，有挽章。作品：《萧果卿祭酒挽章》其一。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷一。）</span><div id='poem_94124' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_94124' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/94124?labeling=true' target='_blank'>萧果卿祭酒挽章二首<span class='inlineComment2'>（之敏）</span><span style='margin: 0 "poem_title_94124")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_94124_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_94124'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_94124_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1177&endYear=1177')">1177年8月</a>　托叶适带书、茶与陈亮，且以荀子语录勉陈亮当抑怒涛为伏槽循岸。作品：《与陈同甫》三。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史外集》卷五。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1177&endYear=1177')">1177年10月</a>　在三馆，李焘为子李垕所累，赴常德任，吕祖谦致书安慰。作品：《与李侍郎》一。<span
