ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1177&endYear=1177')">1177年11月2日</a>　娶芮烨季女为继室，甚觉勉强。作品：《通芮氏订婚启》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷四。）</span><div id='poem_1275494' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275494' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275494?labeling=true' target='_blank'>通芮氏定婚启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1177年11月2日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275494")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275494_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275494'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275494'>合父兄师友之契，畴若高门；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275494_comment'></div>联婚姻甥舅之亲，敢于他族？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275494_comment'></div>问名之始，在礼有初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275494_comment'></div>某人绪论与闻，曾是渐摩之旧；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275494_comment'></div>伏承令侄女素风不改，谅惟淡泊之安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275494_comment'></div>永愧诸生，自老西河之上；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275494_comment'></div>尚蕲季女，肯来南涧之滨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275494_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1275494_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1177&endYear=1177')">1177年11月</a>　作书慰陈亮勿以试闱得失为念。作品：《与陈同甫》五。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史外集》卷五。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1177&endYear=1177')">1177年11月9日</a>　以秘书郎入对，得丞相赵汝愚、礼部尚书周必大荐，被旨校正《圣宋文海》始尽取秘府藏书，旁求士大夫所藏，悉行编类。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1177&endYear=1177')">1177年11月</a>　陈傅良、郑景望在太学，常与相聚。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1178&endYear=1178')">1178年1月</a>　怀念汪应辰有挽诗二首。作品：《端明汪公挽章》二首之一。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷一。）</span><div id='poem_94130' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_94130' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/94130?labeling=true' target='_blank'>端明汪公挽章二首<span class='inlineComment2'>（淳熙五年正月）</span><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1178年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_94130")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_94130_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_94130'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_94130'>异时忧世士，太息恨才难。<div id='poem_sentence_0_94130_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_94130'>每见公身健，犹令我意宽。<div id='poem_sentence_1_94130_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_94130'>彫零竟何极，回复岂无端。<div id='poem_sentence_2_94130_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_94130'>此理终难解，天风大隧寒。<div id='poem_sentence_3_94130_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_94130'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_94130_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_94129' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_94129' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/94129?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1178年1月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_94129_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_94129'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_94129'>四海膺门峻，亲承二纪中。<div id='poem_sentence_0_94129_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_94129'>论交从父祖，受教自儿童。<div id='poem_sentence_1_94129_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_94129'>山岳千寻上，江河万折东。<div id='poem_sentence_2_94129_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_94129'>微言藏肺腑，欲吐与谁同。<div id='poem_sentence_3_94129_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_94129'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_94129_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1178&endYear=1178')">1178年2月</a>　应泰州守魏钦绪请，作《泰州修桑子河堰记》成。<div id='poem_1275599' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275599' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275599?labeling=true' target='_blank'>泰州修桑子河堰记</a><span class='authorDate'>（淳熙四年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275599")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275599_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275599'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275599'>淳熙元年夏六月，泰州东部潮大上，败捍海堰，诏州与两使者参治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275599_comment'></div>维堰初作于文正范公，首起海陵，尾属盐城，衡两县间百馀里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275599_comment'></div>及是，半圮于水，有司缮筑，未几以讫工闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275599_comment'></div>独桑子河以南径如皋境，缭许氏庄后，皆文正规略所未及，春夏霖雨，海汐暴兴，田庐冒没，版籍日耗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275599_comment'></div>诏以诿今魏侯，侯不以造端立始、无前模可袭为惮，慨然闵民病之不可宿，凡土功之政令，与其具脩，悉蒐悉讲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275599_comment'></div>发命以四年十月乙酉，甫半月堰成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275599_comment'></div>其袤三十有五里，其崇寻有三尺，趾广二丈四尺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275599_comment'></div>积工一十有七万。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275599_comment'></div>郡人拥府门欢贺，又走书蕲记，侯弗能御。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275599_comment'></div>昔史起引漳水以溉邺，追咎西门豹之遗利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275599_comment'></div>杜预将桥大河，或者以商周所都，历圣贤而不作，殆必难立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275599_comment'></div>二者之论胥失也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275599_comment'></div>斯民之生理无极，而陵陆川浸之势屡迁，颛守陈迹者，既不足与合变，至于因时建置，虽由己出，然前人仁心仁闻经启区画之馀业，盖有以起之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275599_comment'></div>侯名父子，逮见前辈，习于群公先正之源委，一旦身履其迹而手赋其功，宜所乐为者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275599_comment'></div>用能先事不惑，已事不矜，以兴泰人之长利，以终文正公之遗绪，以助成明天子实边之大计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275599_comment'></div>后之为政者，将于此乎考。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275599_comment'></div>侯名钦绪，历阳人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1275599_comment'></div>涖役者，海陵尉朱棣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1275599_comment'></div>督护者，知如皋县耿汉、知海陵县穆沂。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1275599_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1178&endYear=1178')">1178年2月</a>　作《书伯祖紫微翁赠青溪先生子诗后》<div id='poem_1275518' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275518' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275518?labeling=true' target='_blank'>书伯祖紫微翁赠青溪先生子诗后</a><span class='authorDate'>（1178年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275518")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275518_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275518'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275518'>临川耆旧汪、谢、饶，皆出荥阳公之门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275518_comment'></div>德操既遁世不耀，无逸亦以布衣死，志节稍见于世者，独青溪先生而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275518_comment'></div>紫微伯祖与青溪忘年交，序引所述备矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275518_comment'></div>后一诗，勉戒其子，笃至严正，真前辈丈人行语也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1275518_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1178&endYear=1178')">1178年2月</a>　作《书伯祖紫微翁、外祖曾文清公所寄许子礼吏部诗后》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1178&endYear=1178')">1178年3月7日</a>　作《书焦伯强殿丞帖后》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1178&endYear=1178')">1178年3月13日</a>　磨勘，转朝奉郎。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1178&endYear=1178')">1178年3月</a>　史浩拜相，荐吕祖谦等。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1178&endYear=1178')">1178年春</a>　为殿试考官。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1178&endYear=1178')">1178年春</a>　陈亮来访，旋别去。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1178&endYear=1178')">1178年春</a>　福清人邓林来访。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1178&endYear=1178')">1178年4月</a>　书慰陈亮科举不利，代德远、少望廷试漏落抱憾。作品：《与陈同甫》二十。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史外集》卷十。）</span><div id='poem_1275332' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275332' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275332?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与陈同甫书<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其十一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1174年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275332")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275332_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275332'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275332'>近悤悤奉答，未究所欲言者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275332_comment'></div>人至，荐拜手字，欣审秋暑犹剧，孝履宁谧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275332_comment'></div>某还舍近半月，适此酷暑，疲损犹未甚苏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275332_comment'></div>此月二十五日，刘国华葬，须往泉溪会之，因留明招数日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275332_comment'></div>闻月交为入城之行，若路过内白，幸遣一介至明招问某所止，庶不参差也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275332_comment'></div>《三国纪年》序引及诸赞，累日已详看，用意高深处，亦或得其一二，但大纲体制犹有未晓处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275332_comment'></div>《序》云：「魏于是乎有书，吴、蜀合而附之《魏书」》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275332_comment'></div>又云：「魏终不足以正天下，于是为《三国纪年」》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275332_comment'></div>终焉不知《魏书》与《纪年》是一书，为复两书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275332_comment'></div>观三国诸君赞，却似迁、固史法，每君为纪而参赞于后者，而《三国纪年》冠以甲子，而并列魏、蜀、吴，则又似合三国为一者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275332_comment'></div>所谓魏武以下诸赞，必不可参于此<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>，不知系于何处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275332_comment'></div>岂《三国纪年》之外，复叙每君之本末而系以赞耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275332_comment'></div>此皆未晓之大者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275332_comment'></div>《魏武赞》述来历甚当<span class='inlineComment2'>（但其末「舜、禹之事」两语未晓。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275332_comment'></div>魏文帝两赞深味词意，予夺甚有味<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275332_comment'></div>《昭烈赞》论其君臣反复于天意人事之际，所谓妙体本心，但费诗之议，却似不达时变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275332_comment'></div>汉统既绝，昭烈安得不承之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1275332_comment'></div>非高祖时比也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1275332_comment'></div>后主盖亦甚庸，所以安之不疑者，乃诸葛公工夫耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1275332_comment'></div>《武侯赞》论「以国政归丞相」，甚善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1275332_comment'></div>但谓汉侍中、中书令、尚书令皆宦者为之者，考之《汉书》，亦不皆如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1275332_comment'></div>篇末「王者之作，天犹以为未疏哉」，感慨之意甚长，但不若《后主赞》所谓「天命果可畏」辞严而义正也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1275332_comment'></div>《武烈赞》论汉末守文之弊，及启桓、王之翱翔，甚妙甚妙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1275332_comment'></div>下三赞亦然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1275332_comment'></div>鄙意窃谓吴四赞尤能尽其规摹之所止，殆无遗憾也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1275332_comment'></div>《庞统赞》论兼弱之义，甚正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1275332_comment'></div>《关羽赞》亦稳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1275332_comment'></div>但来教谓「司马子长虽高，不欲学」，而诸赞命意及笔势往往似之，何耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1275332_comment'></div>因便并望见教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1275332_comment'></div>朱元晦工夫，亦谓大概如此耳。</div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1275332_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1275332'><span class='label'>按：</span>《东莱吕太史别集》卷一○。又见邓广铭点校《陈亮集》增订本卷一六。<br /><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_10_1275332_0'>⑴ 既并列三国之年，必是通书三国事，今每君为赞，必知不系于此后。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_14_1275332_0'>⑵ 但《文帝赞》意颇晦，又文帝三驾伐吴，谓「中国庶几息肩」，亦未协。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1275332_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1178&endYear=1178')">1178年4月23日</a>　以有志于世，持论不阿，除著作佐郎兼史职。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1178&endYear=1178')">1178年4月</a>　致书朱熹荐刘尧夫。作品：《与朱侍讲》十五。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷八。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1178&endYear=1178')">1178年5月</a>　以能文学、知典故、有学问，得周必大荐于孝宗。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1178&endYear=1178')">1178年5月</a>　致书潘景宪，称许林谦之缴谢廓然除命之举，以为过江后未有。作品：《答潘叔度》四。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史外集》卷五。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1178&endYear=1178')">1178年6月13日</a>　兼权礼部郎官。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1178&endYear=1178')">1178年6月</a>　《中兴馆阁书目》七十卷、《序例》一卷撰成，著录图书44486卷，秘书省进御。以与修故减二年磨勘。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1178&endYear=1178')">1178年6月</a>　书慰陈亮，冀其宽裕从容。作品：《与陈同甫》二。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史外集》卷五。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1178&endYear=1178')">1178年闰6月</a>　在馆中与袁枢、石子重多相见。复书朱熹，阐述为文必以平正朴实为先。作品：《与朱侍讲》十六。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷八。）</span><div id='poem_1275214' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275214' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275214?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与朱侍讲元晦书<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其十四 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1178年闰6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275214")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275214_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275214'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275214'>某二月四日试院中，奉先人感疾之问，仓皇奔归，七日未后至家，先人既以巳午间易箦，酷痛冤毒，贯彻肺腑，求死无所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275214_comment'></div>去秋庐陵之归，自处极安裕，齿发饮食，皆胜往时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275214_comment'></div>违侍旁未半年，遽至大故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275214_comment'></div>一官拘縻，疾不奉药饵，没不闻理命，不孝之罪，上通于天矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275214_comment'></div>忍死营办，以五月十六日敬终襄事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275214_comment'></div>音容永隔，攀号摧裂，哀慕无穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275214_comment'></div>扶力布禀执笔，气塞不能多述。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275214_comment'></div>丧礼，乡无恙时娄戒饬令一遵典制，毋参以慝礼，今不敢有违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275214_comment'></div>祭礼数年来尤勤催督，竟不及裁定，俟暑退亦欲稍稍讲订。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275214_comment'></div>往时吾丈所定条目，便望早付下，或有暇更为参酌，令使可遵行，尤幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275214_comment'></div>某自遭变故，穷苦危迫，粗有困而反则意思，颇知前此汗漫之非，但意绪荒塞，未能详求诲益耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275214_comment'></div>忧居罕遇，便今复属韩丈附达，迟速未可料。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275214_comment'></div>瞻望函丈，第深惨怆。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1275214_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1178&endYear=1178')">1178年闰6月</a>　李焘在常德任上，致书李焘言及朝政，抄《说文系传》寄李焘并赠建茶。作品：《与李侍郎》二。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史外集》卷五。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1178&endYear=1178')">1178年闰6月</a>　与修《四朝正史志》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1178&endYear=1178')">1178年夏</a>　作《祭林宗丞文》，阐述中原文献之传的基本特征。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷八。）</span><div id='poem_1275708' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275708' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275708?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭林宗丞文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1178年夏）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275708")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275708_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275708'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275708'>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275708_comment'></div>昔我伯祖西垣公躬受中原文献之传，载而之南，裴回顾瞻，未得所付。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275708_comment'></div>踰岭入闽，而先生与二李伯仲实来，一见意合，遂定师生之分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275708_comment'></div>于是嵩洛关辅诸儒之源流靡不讲，庆历、元祐群叟之本末靡不咨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275708_comment'></div>以广大为心，而陋专门之暖姝，以践履为实，而刊繁文之枝叶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275708_comment'></div>致严乎辞受出处而欲其明白无玷，致察乎邪正是非而欲其毫发不差。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275708_comment'></div>昕夕函丈，闻无不信，信无不行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275708_comment'></div>前望圣贤，大路九轨，自诡以必可至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275708_comment'></div>三岁一诏，士子莫重焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275708_comment'></div>先生方上名于春官，慨然惜会合之难而绪业之未竟也，亟改辕解鞅而辍行，其视内外轻重之分可谓审矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275708_comment'></div>里居之良，若方、若陆，旁郡之士，若胡、若刘，更唱迭和于寂寞之滨，韬积渟蓄，固未有舍所为为人意也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275708_comment'></div>未几声光四出而不可遏，州党推择居东面之席，踵门请起，至再至三，不得已而临之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275708_comment'></div>长乐之士，知乡大学，知尊前辈，知宗正论，则皆先生与二李公之力焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275708_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275708_comment'></div>西垣公既不及公道之伸，而二李亦皆以布衣死，独先生甫入东观，若将有为而病辄随之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275708_comment'></div>中原诸老之规模，迄不得再白于世，其用舍必有所系矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275708_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1275708_comment'></div>心迹之判，固非达者之论，区区专信耳目，而量君子之用心，则亦有大谬不然者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1275708_comment'></div>先生所遇，多迕少合，意虽可寻，而事不大见，中虽无愧而外不及知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1275708_comment'></div>悠悠斯世，识此心者几何人哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1275708_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1275708_comment'></div>先生之卧家，左支废，右支缓，手不能指授，口不能剧谈，若无与乎世道之升降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1275708_comment'></div>抑不知百围之木，颠童立枯，犹足为丘樊之镇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1275708_comment'></div>一旦仆地，则意象衰落，无复故国之遗矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1275708_comment'></div>呜呼痛哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1275708_comment'></div>某未冠，缀弟子之末行，期待之厚，独出于千百人之右，顾谫薄安所取此！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1275708_comment'></div>实惟我西垣公之故，施及其后人，培植湔祓，闵闵焉如农夫之望岁也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1275708_comment'></div>齿发日衰，业弗加修，愚不自惜，大惧先生之功力为虚施，每腼然惭、惕然恐也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1275708_comment'></div>闻先生之丧，念以辞侑奠，而思虑不专，条贯靡究，笔屡下而复柅也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1275708_comment'></div>既半岁矣，而所言者乃止于是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1275708_comment'></div>盖至善难名，至痛无文，而迄不能成章也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1275708_comment'></div>先生之存，音问虽阔疏，举首南望，犹有虞焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1275708_comment'></div>今遽撤其所畏，几何而不为小人之归也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1275708_comment'></div>惟当与二三子尊所闻，行所知，使先生未伸之志犹有考也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1275708_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉！</div><div id='poem_sentence_34_1275708_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1178&endYear=1178')">1178年8月</a>　致书朱熹，劝其合乎圣贤出处之道，奉旨知南康军。作品：《与朱侍讲》二十。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷八。）</span><div id='poem_1275255' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275255' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275255?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与朱侍讲元晦书<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其五十五 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1173年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275255")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275255_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275255'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275255'>丐祠虽未惬雅志，然诸公不欲贤者家食，虽未必由衷，然亦善意也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275255_comment'></div>但有畏不能容贤者之谤，比之全不分皂白者亦有间矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275255_comment'></div>张荆州病中请祠，亦有苦劝当途令从其请者，亦以向来之嫌，畏人议论不能容之，遂坚不肯从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275255_comment'></div>但作帅与小军垒不同，但须内外至诚相与，首尾相应，乃不误事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275255_comment'></div>既非心相与，则自有首尾衡决处，如来教数条皆是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275255_comment'></div>符节在身，不得擅去，此所以忧而至于病，病而至于死，每诵量而后入，不入而后量之语，为之泫然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275255_comment'></div>至于南康地既非要害，民又非浩穰，虽事之不如人意处固多，然无旦夕立至之忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275255_comment'></div>若且耐烦忍垢，拊摩疲民，苟稍成头绪，子重继之，必能遵守，使一方之民小小休息，亦不为无补也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275255_comment'></div>今去终更才半年馀耳，交印后身便自由，惟吾志所欲，无不可者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275255_comment'></div>或未终更，别有除改，半道引疾而归，亦甚省力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275255_comment'></div>陆子寿前日经过，留此二十馀日，幡然以鹅湖所见为非，甚欲著实看书讲论，心平气下，相识中甚难得也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275255_comment'></div>近因荆州之赴，深思渠学识分晓周正如此，而从游之士，往往不得力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275255_comment'></div>记得往年相聚时，虽未能尽领解渠说话，然觉得大段有益，不知其它从游者何故乃如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275255_comment'></div>盖五十丈不能察人情虚实，必如某之专愚毋它，其教诲乃有所施耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275255_comment'></div>若胸中多端者，虽朝夕相处，未必能有益也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275255_comment'></div>《中庸》论尽己之性，又继之以尽人之性，尽物之性，工夫无穷如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275255_comment'></div>此岂追往事，亦要高明深勉之耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1275255_comment'></div>五十丈所作《濂溪祠堂记》，告妆褫一本送示，欲挂壁间观省耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1275255_comment'></div>亲旧间多相勉撤去书册，固知此理，但旧所偏嗜，未能顿去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1275255_comment'></div>近亦十减五六矣，如时文却不曾与人看。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1275255_comment'></div>受之在此作课，亦只是舍弟辈为之点检也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1275255_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1178&endYear=1178')">1178年8月</a>　史浩请吕祖谦劝朱熹出仕，再致书朱熹勉其早出，以见儒者之效。作品：《与朱侍讲》二十一。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷八。）</span><div id='poem_1275255' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1178&endYear=1178')">1178年9月</a>　九月十二日，车驾幸秘书省观书、赐宴，作诗赐群臣。有《代宰臣史浩等恭书御制<秋日幸秘书省近体诗>下方》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷七。）</span><div id='poem_1275520' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275520' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275520?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代宰臣史浩等恭书御制秋日幸秘书省近体诗下方</a><span class='authorDate'>（淳熙五年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275520")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275520_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275520'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275520'>臣等仰惟皇帝陛下宵旰万几，身济大业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275520_comment'></div>雕琢夸诩浮靡虚桥之习，是抑是黜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275520_comment'></div>囿游池籞宴豫虞乐之奉，是损是蠲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275520_comment'></div>居焉非本实不亲，动焉非法义不举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275520_comment'></div>眷兹三馆，乃储藏典训、长育英畯之地，自绍兴清跸下临，迄今三十有四年，思欲仪刑丕彝，以增光圣绪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275520_comment'></div>粤九月辛酉朔，诏有司戒期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275520_comment'></div>十有二日壬申，幸秘书省，受朝右文殿，移御秘阁，䌷光尧太上皇帝宝章以视群臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275520_comment'></div>既又修太平兴国故事，张宴右文，酒五行罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275520_comment'></div>越翼日癸酉，内出御制诗赐臣浩以下，昭回渊曜，参贲图书，鸿大闳深，匹休《雅》、《颂》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275520_comment'></div>臣等下拜登受，相与斋祓，敷绎宸指。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275520_comment'></div>盖在昔圣人以开物之智，立经陈纪，通于万世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275520_comment'></div>惟有道之主，为能监世盈虚，则象成宪，立一王法，是之谓稽古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275520_comment'></div>文武并用，久长之术，惟崇起经艺，褒表儒学，用能章明大谊，驯服雄暴，俾咸知尊君亲上，茂集骏功，是之谓右文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275520_comment'></div>国以人为轻重，士气之肆拘信屈，论世者必观焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275520_comment'></div>惟虚己忘势，然后群献辐凑，展布四体，乐尽其心，是之谓礼贤下士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275520_comment'></div>大哉王言！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275520_comment'></div>尧、舜、禹、汤、文、武之隆，由此其选，固非墨客椠人所得私以为荣观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1275520_comment'></div>臣等昧死，请勒诸琬琰，贻诸亿载，与日月云汉同垂无极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1275520_comment'></div>制曰可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1275520_comment'></div>谨具著其语下方，以风示县内德意志虑之所乡云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1275520_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1178&endYear=1178')">1178年9月</a>　九月十二日，车驾幸秘书省观书、赐宴，作诗赐群臣，有和诗。作品：《恭和御制秋日幸秘书省近体诗》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷一。）</span>《贺车驾幸秘书省二首》之一。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷一。）</span><div id='poem_94121' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_94121' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/94121?labeling=true' target='_blank'>恭和御制秋日幸秘书省近体诗<span class='inlineComment2'>（淳熙五年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1178年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_94121")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_94121_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_94121'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_94121'>麟阁龙旂日月章，中兴再见赭袍光。<div id='poem_sentence_0_94121_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_94121'>仰观焜耀人文盛，始识扶持德意长。<div id='poem_sentence_1_94121_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_94121'>功利从今卑管晏，浮华自昔陋卢王。<div id='poem_sentence_2_94121_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_94121'>愿将实学酬天造，敢效明河织女襄。<div id='poem_sentence_3_94121_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_94121'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_94121_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_94116' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_94116' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/94116?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺车驾幸秘书省二首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1178年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_94116")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_94116_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_94116'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_94116'>麟台高柳识雕舆，共记中兴幸省初。<div id='poem_sentence_0_94116_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_94116'>黄道再传天子跸，青编重入史臣书。<div id='poem_sentence_1_94116_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_94116'>需云下际君恩盛，晨露高张乐节舒。<div id='poem_sentence_2_94116_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_94116'>若写鸿猷参大雅，定非<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_94116", 94116, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>周鼓</span>颂田渔。<div id='poem_sentence_3_94116_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_94116'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_94116_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_94115' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_94115' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/94115?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1178年9月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_94115_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_94115'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_94115'>紫清丹极与天邻，阖辟乾坤系笑嚬。<div id='poem_sentence_0_94115_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_94115'>独为斯文回一顾，坐令吾道重千钧。<div id='poem_sentence_1_94115_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_94115'>先王旧物参差见，列圣明谟次第陈。<div id='poem_sentence_2_94115_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_94115'>墨客区区感荣遇，岂知深意在彝伦<span class='inlineComment2'>（以上《东莱吕太史文集》卷一）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_94115_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_94115'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_94115_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1178&endYear=1178')">1178年9月14日</a>　获赐《中兴馆阁书目》一部。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1178&endYear=1178')">1178年9月27日</a>　以幸省恩转朝散郎。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1178&endYear=1178')">1178年9月</a>　诏吕祖谦主持测验淳熙历法。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1178&endYear=1178')">1178年秋</a>　为陈亮上书事，劝其自我反观。作品：《与陈同甫》二十一。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷十。）</span><div id='poem_1275332' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275332' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275332?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与陈同甫书<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其十一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1174年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275332")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275332_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275332'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275332'>近悤悤奉答，未究所欲言者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275332_comment'></div>人至，荐拜手字，欣审秋暑犹剧，孝履宁谧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275332_comment'></div>某还舍近半月，适此酷暑，疲损犹未甚苏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275332_comment'></div>此月二十五日，刘国华葬，须往泉溪会之，因留明招数日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275332_comment'></div>闻月交为入城之行，若路过内白，幸遣一介至明招问某所止，庶不参差也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275332_comment'></div>《三国纪年》序引及诸赞，累日已详看，用意高深处，亦或得其一二，但大纲体制犹有未晓处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275332_comment'></div>《序》云：「魏于是乎有书，吴、蜀合而附之《魏书」》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275332_comment'></div>又云：「魏终不足以正天下，于是为《三国纪年」》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275332_comment'></div>终焉不知《魏书》与《纪年》是一书，为复两书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275332_comment'></div>观三国诸君赞，却似迁、固史法，每君为纪而参赞于后者，而《三国纪年》冠以甲子，而并列魏、蜀、吴，则又似合三国为一者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275332_comment'></div>所谓魏武以下诸赞，必不可参于此<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>，不知系于何处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275332_comment'></div>岂《三国纪年》之外，复叙每君之本末而系以赞耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275332_comment'></div>此皆未晓之大者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275332_comment'></div>《魏武赞》述来历甚当<span class='inlineComment2'>（但其末「舜、禹之事」两语未晓。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275332_comment'></div>魏文帝两赞深味词意，予夺甚有味<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275332_comment'></div>《昭烈赞》论其君臣反复于天意人事之际，所谓妙体本心，但费诗之议，却似不达时变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275332_comment'></div>汉统既绝，昭烈安得不承之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1275332_comment'></div>非高祖时比也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1275332_comment'></div>后主盖亦甚庸，所以安之不疑者，乃诸葛公工夫耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1275332_comment'></div>《武侯赞》论「以国政归丞相」，甚善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1275332_comment'></div>但谓汉侍中、中书令、尚书令皆宦者为之者，考之《汉书》，亦不皆如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1275332_comment'></div>篇末「王者之作，天犹以为未疏哉」，感慨之意甚长，但不若《后主赞》所谓「天命果可畏」辞严而义正也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1275332_comment'></div>《武烈赞》论汉末守文之弊，及启桓、王之翱翔，甚妙甚妙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1275332_comment'></div>下三赞亦然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1275332_comment'></div>鄙意窃谓吴四赞尤能尽其规摹之所止，殆无遗憾也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1275332_comment'></div>《庞统赞》论兼弱之义，甚正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1275332_comment'></div>《关羽赞》亦稳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1275332_comment'></div>但来教谓「司马子长虽高，不欲学」，而诸赞命意及笔势往往似之，何耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1275332_comment'></div>因便并望见教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1275332_comment'></div>朱元晦工夫，亦谓大概如此耳。</div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1275332_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1275332'><span class='label'>按：</span>《东莱吕太史别集》卷一○。又见邓广铭点校《陈亮集》增订本卷一六。<br /><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_10_1275332_0'>⑴ 既并列三国之年，必是通书三国事，今每君为赞，必知不系于此后。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_14_1275332_0'>⑵ 但《文帝赞》意颇晦，又文帝三驾伐吴，谓「中国庶几息肩」，亦未协。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1275332_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1178&endYear=1178')">1178年秋</a>　陈亮函候，复书陈亮赞其“真有力者”<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1178&endYear=1178')">1178年10月17日</a>　除著作郎，兼权礼部郎官如故。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1178&endYear=1178')">1178年10月</a>　有《礼部代宰臣以下进三祖下第六世仙源类谱仁宗皇帝玉牒毕贺表》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1178&endYear=1178')">1178年10月</a>　有《代宰臣以下进三祖下第六世仙源类谱毕贺太上皇帝表》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1178&endYear=1178')">1178年10月</a>　陈傅良求外补，吕祖谦欲留陈傅良为编修官不果。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1178&endYear=1178')">1178年10月</a>　致书朱熹，勉其出知南康军，以使世见儒者之效。《文海》初成。作品：《与朱侍讲》二十三。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷八。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1178&endYear=1178')">1178年10月</a>　陈亮书来，复书言朋友散落，胸中不快。作品：《与陈同甫》十五。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷十。）</span><div id='poem_1275332' class='_poem'><div id='poem_sentence_15_1275332_comment'></div>汉统既绝，昭烈安得不承之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1275332_comment'></div>非高祖时比也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1275332_comment'></div>后主盖亦甚庸，所以安之不疑者，乃诸葛公工夫耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1275332_comment'></div>《武侯赞》论「以国政归丞相」，甚善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1275332_comment'></div>但谓汉侍中、中书令、尚书令皆宦者为之者，考之《汉书》，亦不皆如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1275332_comment'></div>篇末「王者之作，天犹以为未疏哉」，感慨之意甚长，但不若《后主赞》所谓「天命果可畏」辞严而义正也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1275332_comment'></div>《武烈赞》论汉末守文之弊，及启桓、王之翱翔，甚妙甚妙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1275332_comment'></div>下三赞亦然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1275332_comment'></div>鄙意窃谓吴四赞尤能尽其规摹之所止，殆无遗憾也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1275332_comment'></div>《庞统赞》论兼弱之义，甚正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1275332_comment'></div>《关羽赞》亦稳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1275332_comment'></div>但来教谓「司马子长虽高，不欲学」，而诸赞命意及笔势往往似之，何耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1275332_comment'></div>因便并望见教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1275332_comment'></div>朱元晦工夫，亦谓大概如此耳。</div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1275332_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1275332'><span class='label'>按：</span>《东莱吕太史别集》卷一○。又见邓广铭点校《陈亮集》增订本卷一六。<br /><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_10_1275332_0'>⑴ 既并列三国之年，必是通书三国事，今每君为赞，必知不系于此后。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_14_1275332_0'>⑵ 但《文帝赞》意颇晦，又文帝三驾伐吴，谓「中国庶几息肩」，亦未协。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1275332_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1178&endYear=1178')">1178年10月</a>　同馆胡晋臣知汉州，有送别诗。作品：《送胡子远著作出守汉州分韵得行字》<div id='poem_94153' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_94153' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/94153?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送胡子远著作知汉州分韵得行字<span class='inlineComment2'>（淳熙五年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1178年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_94153")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_94153_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_94153'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_94153'>定交不在蚤，意合盖已倾。<div id='poem_sentence_0_94153_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_94153'>胡侯西南来，两载同书檠。<div id='poem_sentence_1_94153_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_94153'>与人徐有味，于世初无营。<div id='poem_sentence_2_94153_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_94153'>虚舟澹容与，未易宠辱惊。<div id='poem_sentence_3_94153_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_94153'>鱼龙同一波，中有千丈清。<div id='poem_sentence_4_94153_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_94153'>道气自深稳，名言常简明。<div id='poem_sentence_5_94153_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_94153'>南宫接东观，天衢势方亨。<div id='poem_sentence_6_94153_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_94153'>梦回得远信，窥檐<span class='inlineComment2'>（金华本作园）</span>渚鸿鸣。<div id='poem_sentence_7_94153_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_94153'>开书见连环，归兴浩已盈。<div id='poem_sentence_8_94153_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_94153'>子政方校录，令伯俄陈情。<div id='poem_sentence_9_94153_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_94153'>都门日毂击，杂袭炎凉并。<div id='poem_sentence_10_94153_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_94153'>谁知此麾盖，独为思亲行。<div id='poem_sentence_11_94153_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_94153'>夹道皆叹息，始识真重轻。<div id='poem_sentence_12_94153_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_94153'>古来聚散地，雪野天峥嵘。<div id='poem_sentence_13_94153_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_94153'>别袖不可挽，宿昔洲渚生。<div id='poem_sentence_14_94153_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_94153'>君臣有大义，忠孝相持衡。<div id='poem_sentence_15_94153_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_94153'>勉哉楙明德，清庙须栋甍。<div id='poem_sentence_16_94153_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_94153'></div><div id='poem_sentence_17_94153_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1178&endYear=1178')">1178年10月</a>　有与内兄曾集书。作品：《与曾提刑》四。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷九。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1178&endYear=1178')">1178年12月14日</a>　中风，为庸医所误，给假半月将治。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1178&endYear=1178')">1178年12月</a>　复书李焘，论《说文解字》、修史刊书等事宜。作品：《与李侍郎》三。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史外集》卷五。）</span><div id='poem_1275445' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275445' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275445?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与李侍郎仁父书<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1178年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275445")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275445_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275445'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275445'>某官次觕遣，但块处索居，所怀偪塞，无与纾写，默默随群，寖就颓弛，日积愧腼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275445_comment'></div>比复同舍，例摄省户，偶占礼曹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275445_comment'></div>虽目前文牍极清简，然稍有讨论，便系典礼，责诿政自不轻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275445_comment'></div>开府之始，酬酢经理，想亦小劳区画。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275445_comment'></div>飘飖江渚之久，今行李既遂按堵，亦可少就休愒也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275445_comment'></div>远方人士，亦有可与语者否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275445_comment'></div>史事诸志，自冬春来虽各粗成编沓，然首尾不完，节目断绝，殊未有次序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275445_comment'></div>今期限在冬末，已是第三次展，不免趣办，第恐牴牾处多耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275445_comment'></div>徐锴《通释》绍兴本近方得之，比馆中本阙十卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275445_comment'></div>盖此书本名《说文系传》，各分子门，其前三十卷谓之《通释》，乃印本所有，后十卷各别有名，乃印本所无，今谨钞录送去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275445_comment'></div>但此本蠹蚀阙字极多，若得暇以《说文》参校，义理亦可推寻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275445_comment'></div>潘义荣《编年》谨纳上，唯伯祖履历及其他文字，累往家叔处取，犹未到，当更趣之，才得即寻便转致次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275445_comment'></div>仲信祠禄文字，前此与傅景仁同将上，独见却，势须更待少时耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275445_comment'></div>季修闻尚留蜀中，莫非久还侍旁否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275445_comment'></div>近事邸报中可得大略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275445_comment'></div>周文自春来请去之章已四上，李寿翁亦以病告经月，陈能之入史院一日即得眩瞀之疾，迨今未平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275445_comment'></div>大抵目前善类或去或病，悒悒殊鲜况也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1275445_comment'></div>武陵民淳事简，公退想多闲暇，《长编》莫曾下手再整顿否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1275445_comment'></div>远地士子固难得，亦有可与语者否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1275445_comment'></div>建茶三十口谩助午啜，敢幸笑留。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1275445_comment'></div>所论《长编》乍到，固知多事，今条教既定，莫渐可整顿否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1275445_comment'></div>虽远方难得人商榷，然暇日极难得，似不可放过也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1275445_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1178&endYear=1178')">1178年12月</a>　《祭仪》成。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1178&endYear=1178')">1178年12月</a>　以“害大体”为说，勉朱熹出知南康。作品：《与朱侍讲》二十四。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷八。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1179&endYear=1179')">1179年1月1日</a>　诏与州郡差遣。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1179&endYear=1179')">1179年1月16日</a>　又诏与添差参议官差遣，免谢辞。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1179&endYear=1179')">1179年1月24日</a>　枢密使王淮宣旨，问所编《文海》次第，遂将一百五十卷《文海》缴进。有《进编次<文海>札子》陈述编次意旨、方法。<div id='poem_1275160' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275160' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275160?labeling=true' target='_blank'>进编次文海劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1179年1月24日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275160")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275160_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275160'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275160'>右，某先于淳熙四年十一月内承尚书省劄子：「勘会已降指挥，令临安府校正开雕《圣宋文海》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275160_comment'></div>十一月九日，三省同奉圣旨：委吕某专一精加校正」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275160_comment'></div>某窃见《文海》元系书坊一时刊行，名贤高文大册尚多遗落，遂具劄子，乞一就增损，仍断自中兴以前铨次，庶几可以行远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275160_comment'></div>十一月十五日，三省同奉圣旨依。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275160_comment'></div>某寻将秘书省集库所藏本朝诸家文集，及于士大夫家宛转假借，旁采传记他书，虽不知名氏而其文可录者，用文选古诗十九首例，并行编类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275160_comment'></div>凡六十一门，为百五十卷，目录四卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275160_comment'></div>某窃伏自念本朝文字之盛，众作相望，诚宜采掇英华，仰副圣意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275160_comment'></div>而某学问荒浅，知识卑陋，不足以知前辈作述之指。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275160_comment'></div>黾勉承命，今已经年，简牍浩繁，纂辑缪戾，加以缮写才毕，偶婴末疾，尚恐疏略牴牾，未敢遽以投进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275160_comment'></div>今月二十四日，伏蒙辅臣具宣圣谕，缘某已除外任，俯询所编次第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275160_comment'></div>自惟稽缓，不胜震惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275160_comment'></div>所有编次到《圣宋文海》一部，共一百五十四册，并临安府元牒到御前降下《圣宋文海》旧本一部，计二十册，并用黄罗夹复，封作七复，欲望特与敷奏缴进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275160_comment'></div>某不胜惶惧俟罪之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1275160_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1179&endYear=1179')">1179年2月3日</a>　因编类《文海》，得旨除直秘阁。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1179&endYear=1179')">1179年</a>　中使李裕文奉旨宣赐银绢三百匹两。吕祖谦具表辞谢，并辞免除职。有辞免札子。作品：《进所编<文海>赐银绢谢表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷二。）</span>《除直秘阁辞免札子》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷三。）</span><div id='poem_1275149' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275149' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275149?labeling=true' target='_blank'>进所编文海赐银绢谢表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1179年2月4日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275149")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275149_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275149'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275149'>右臣今月四日承中使李裕文宣谕圣旨，以臣所编《文海》精当，赐银绢三百疋两者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275149_comment'></div>奏篇无取，锡命有加，既叨中秘清切之除，复拜内府便蕃之锡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275149_comment'></div>人微恩厚，感极涕零。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275149_comment'></div>兹盖伏遇皇帝陛下圣学高明，皇猷渊懿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275149_comment'></div>粲然众作，思采摭以无遗；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275149_comment'></div>蕞尔小臣，惧讨论之不称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275149_comment'></div>已逃罪戾，仍被眷私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275149_comment'></div>抱椠怀铅，曷副右文之意；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275149_comment'></div>赐金增秩，徒惭稽古之荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275149_comment'></div>臣无任。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1275149_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1275161' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275161' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275161?labeling=true' target='_blank'>除直秘阁辞免劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1179年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275161")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275161_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275161'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275161'>某先奉圣旨，编类《文海》，近因宣谕，缮写投进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275161_comment'></div>今月四日，承尚书省劄子：「三省同奉圣旨：吕某编类《文海》，采摭精详，可与除直秘阁」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275161_comment'></div>又蒙圣恩赐银绢三百疋两。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275161_comment'></div>某窃自揆度，问学浅陋，知识卑凡，实不足以称讨论之选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275161_comment'></div>黾勉承命，冒昧奏篇，疏略舛差，无所逃罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275161_comment'></div>敢谓上恩隆厚，宠数过宜！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275161_comment'></div>蚤夜以思，不遑宁处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275161_comment'></div>人心初不相远，窃闻果有驳章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275161_comment'></div>诚以编次此书，止是将前人文集略从其类，徒淹岁月，何有勤劳？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275161_comment'></div>又况去取之间，岂能允当？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275161_comment'></div>方圣上责实之日，尤重职名，非有显功，未尝除授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275161_comment'></div>兼某已拜金缯厚赐，至于寓直中秘，实为太优，岂宜贪冒宠私，重烦公论？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275161_comment'></div>欲望朝廷矜怜，特与敷奏，将所除直秘阁恩命速赐寝罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275161_comment'></div>干渎朝听，某下情无任悚慄之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1275161_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1179&endYear=1179')">1179年2月</a>　孝宗以为《文海》“有益治道”，遂拜命。《文海》赐名《皇朝文鉴》，后因遭诋毁不得刊印。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1179&endYear=1179')">1179年2月</a>　致书李焘，言染疾之由与奏《文海》始末。作品：《与李侍郎》七。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史外集》卷五。）</span><div id='poem_1275238' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275238' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275238?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与朱侍讲元晦书<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三十八 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1179年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275238")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275238_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275238'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275238'>某官次粗遣，迩来同舍例权郎，偶占礼曹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275238_comment'></div>虽目前文书极简省，然偶有讨论，便系礼典，责任实不轻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275238_comment'></div>长夏不知愒息何地，密庵去山大近，岚雾蒸薄，要非可久处之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275238_comment'></div>却是寒泉平旷，于度暑为宜耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275238_comment'></div>比得桂林书，犹未闻移漕之命，计今当出岭矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275238_comment'></div>书中具道所以箴戒儆厉之意，不胜感悚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275238_comment'></div>去冬舍弟转致教赐，一一深中膏肓之疾，朝夕玩省不敢忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275238_comment'></div>独所论永嘉文体一节，乃往年为学官时病痛，数年来深知其缴绕狭细，深害心术，故每与士子语，未尝不以平正朴实为先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275238_comment'></div>去夏与李仁甫议文体，政是要救此弊，恐传闻或不详耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275238_comment'></div>前此拜答时匆匆，偶不及之，非敢忽忘也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275238_comment'></div>人苦不自知，离群索居，尤易得颓弛，惟觊继此时赐砭治，不胜厚幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275238_comment'></div>石子重、袁机仲时相见，子重已请得般家假，七月初当可去此，机仲轮对亦即在数月间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275238_comment'></div>日来轮对者，亦间有正论，虽尘雾未必能裨益，要且得气脉不断耳。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1275238_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1179&endYear=1179')">1179年3月24日</a>　病稍愈，出修门散心。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1179&endYear=1179')">1179年4月7日</a>　租船离临安返婺州。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
醴陵
-----detail

-----title
天台

-----title
上饶
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='cc7844d1df924c508f0c72cd52b25de6_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("cc7844d1df924c508f0c72cd52b25de6");'><span id='cc7844d1df924c508f0c72cd52b25de6_link' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1157&endYear=1157')">1157年12月16日</a>　如信州完婚。有诗。作品：《晚望》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷一。）</span><div id='poem_94156' class='_poem'><div class='authorDate'>（1157年12月16日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", id='poem_sentence_0_94156'>独立荒亭数过帆，横林疏处见沧湾。<div id='poem_sentence_0_94156_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_94156'>故知不入豪华眼，送与凫鸥自在看。<div id='poem_sentence_1_94156_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_94156'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_94156_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1157&endYear=1157')">1157年12月29日</a>　亲迎韩元吉长女韩氏（复）。与韩元吉论学及生死大义。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='87ed2a3505ca48a583ee1fd4ff9e3b92_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("87ed2a3505ca48a583ee1fd4ff9e3b92");'><span id='87ed2a3505ca48a583ee1fd4ff9e3b92_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年</a>，26岁</div><div id='87ed2a3505ca48a583ee1fd4ff9e3b92' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年1月8日</a>　携韩氏夫人赴信州省视岳父韩元吉。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='d9626a8133004fdfa55b51ee2cff73c5_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("d9626a8133004fdfa55b51ee2cff73c5");'><span id='d9626a8133004fdfa55b51ee2cff73c5_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年</a>，39岁</div><div id='d9626a8133004fdfa55b51ee2cff73c5' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年3月27日</a>　宿柳树，见福州进士潘子嘉。过江下市，游祝氏园，见主人祝大举。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年3月28日</a>　宿沙溪，徐良肱来谒。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='2efd2ff3ba5c488d9e5c9771efbcb1dd_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("2efd2ff3ba5c488d9e5c9771efbcb1dd");'><span id='2efd2ff3ba5c488d9e5c9771efbcb1dd_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年</a>，39岁</div><div id='2efd2ff3ba5c488d9e5c9771efbcb1dd' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年6月</a>　过信州，访伯祖门人上饶学正徐季益，论诗。有作，强调吕本中重学甚于文学。作品：《酬上饶徐季益学正》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷一。）</span><div id='poem_94159' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_94159' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/94159?labeling=true' target='_blank'>酬上饶徐季益学正<span class='inlineComment2'>（淳熙二年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1175年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_94159")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_94159_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_94159'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_94159'>吾家紫微翁，独守固穷节。<div id='poem_sentence_0_94159_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_94159'>金銮罢直归，朝饭尚薇蕨。<div id='poem_sentence_1_94159_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_94159'>峨峨李杜坛，总角便高蹑。<div id='poem_sentence_2_94159_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_94159'>暮年自誓斋，铭几深刻责。<div id='poem_sentence_3_94159_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_94159'>名章与俊语，扫去秋一叶。<div id='poem_sentence_4_94159_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_94159'>冷淡静工夫，槁乾迂事业。<div id='poem_sentence_5_94159_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_94159'>有来媚学子，随叩无不竭。<div id='poem_sentence_6_94159_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_94159'>辞受去就间，告戒意尤切。<div id='poem_sentence_7_94159_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_94159'>典刑自耆老，护持何敢阙。<div id='poem_sentence_8_94159_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_94159'>嗟予生苦晚，名在诸孙<span class='inlineComment2'>（金华本作生）</span>列。<div id='poem_sentence_9_94159_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_94159'>拊头虽逮事，提耳未亲接。<div id='poem_sentence_10_94159_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_94159'>徐侯南州秀，少也尝鼓箧。<div id='poem_sentence_11_94159_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_94159'>示我百篇诗，照坐光玉雪。<div id='poem_sentence_12_94159_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_94159'>因之理前话，讲绎霏谈屑。<div id='poem_sentence_13_94159_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_94159'>两都弟子员，家法严城堞。<div id='poem_sentence_14_94159_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_94159'>取善则未周，守旧犹有说。<div id='poem_sentence_15_94159_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_94159'>同门风雨散，孤学丝桐绝。<div id='poem_sentence_16_94159_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_94159'>怀哉五马桥，寒径寻遗屧。<div id='poem_sentence_17_94159_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_94159'></div><div id='poem_sentence_18_94159_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

金华

ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1163&endYear=1163')">1163年12月</a>　朱熹到婺州与吕祖谦见面，同游诸山，访申大度、申太康墓，并论学。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='0784126e22ff4427a8063cee5fbf3311_label'><a href='javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1164&endYear=1164')">1164年闰11月</a>　归婺州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1165&endYear=1165')">1165年1月</a>　函候汪应辰，请其造福一方。作品：《与汪端明》二。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷七。）</span><div id='poem_1275186' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275186' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275186?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与汪端明圣锡书<span class='inlineComment2'>（一六　淳熙元年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1165年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275186")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275186_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275186'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275186'>上饶之居，有定议否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275186_comment'></div>朱元晦约来春至婺，因为天台、雁荡之游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275186_comment'></div>或谓渠久不出，今虽寻山，然适当一二公登用之时，自远而近，恐不察者或以为疑，此诚过虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275186_comment'></div>告试为斟酌，倘渠出果有嫌，则某却当入闽访之，往还必皆得款侍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275186_comment'></div>若元晦可出，亦须送之至衢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275186_comment'></div>度侍见之期，要不出三两月间，预以为慰。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1275186_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1165&endYear=1165')">1165年2月</a>　代父作《汤教授母潘夫人墓志铭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷十。）</span><div id='poem_1275644' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275644' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275644?labeling=true' target='_blank'>汤教授母潘夫人墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（代父仓部作　乾道元年二月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1165年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275644")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275644_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275644'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275644'>潘氏望荥阳，别居金华者为大族。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275644_comment'></div>孺人幼明悟，其在傅，织纴组紃，敏而艺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275644_comment'></div>父母爱之尤，环里中相厥对，惟汤君伟协，乃女焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275644_comment'></div>既嫔汤氏，釐身治家，皆应仪矩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275644_comment'></div>姑俞夫人晚丧明，孺人时寒燠、奏甘毳、躬饎爨，视药物之良者而敬进之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275644_comment'></div>朝夕虞侍，俞夫人至忘其疾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275644_comment'></div>于内外姻属，承趋宾接，无一间言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275644_comment'></div>恩妾媵童奴，皆得其欢心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275644_comment'></div>族党以病告者，脱珥弛服亡所爱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275644_comment'></div>汤氏先故无仕者，孺人开其夫以训子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275644_comment'></div>子烈，始士其服，委身于学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275644_comment'></div>客至，孺人立屏间耳其语，或肄经订史，欣然供具甚设，烈用是居隐约而多致诸公长者，卒就其业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275644_comment'></div>中绍兴二十一年进士第，主明州奉化县簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275644_comment'></div>联板舆之官，里人纪之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275644_comment'></div>二十九年正月朔旦，天子称觞慈宁宫，劳问高年，以差受宠，有秩者父若母庆赐有加。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275644_comment'></div>汤君以子故，即其家拜右承务郎致仕，孺人实偕被命书，集享成福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275644_comment'></div>乡先生之评贤母者，孺人必在其间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1275644_comment'></div>隆兴二年闰十一月十五日，以疾终于正寝，享年七十有三。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1275644_comment'></div>于是承务君没五年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1275644_comment'></div>考讳亮，妣胡氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1275644_comment'></div>男二人：长即烈，今为左从政郎、新差充建宁府府学教授；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1275644_comment'></div>次曰照，业儒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1275644_comment'></div>女四人，长适右迪功郎朱熙绩，馀未行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1275644_comment'></div>孙男一人，曰椿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1275644_comment'></div>子烈等将以乾道元年二月五日，祔于赤松东关原汤君之墓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1275644_comment'></div>前葬，状其行谒铭，予与其子游旧矣，其又何辞？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1275644_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_1275644'>汤世圹僚，委祉于后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1275644_comment'></div>徂相我初，内德之茂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1275644_comment'></div>厥承惟饬，发身以文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1275644_comment'></div>纳诗幽宫，尚远其闻。</div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1275644_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1165&endYear=1165')">1165年4月</a>　致书汪应辰两通，冀其奖掖人物，共扶儒道。作品：《与汪端明》三。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷七。）</span>《与汪端明》四。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷七。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1165&endYear=1165')">1165年6月</a>　代人作《戒谕两淮守令恤农诏》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史外集》卷三。）</span><div id='poem_1275116' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275116' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275116?labeling=true' target='_blank'>戒谕两淮守令恤农诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1165年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275116")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275116_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275116'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275116'>朕观周宣之治，还定安集而劬劳矜寡，离散之民，咸安其居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275116_comment'></div>中兴之业，人到于今称之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275116_comment'></div>朕初承基绪，兢兢业业，以计安天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275116_comment'></div>深惟两淮之间疮痍未平，民力大屈，流移交迹，转为悯隶，乃眷北顾，用震悼于厥心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275116_comment'></div>间者太上皇帝数申饬守令，怀辑疲瘵，督趣农桑，蠲赋省徭，以佐百姓之急。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275116_comment'></div>临遣左右侍从之臣，分行疆埸，复调旁近郡耕牛，振业新附，所以加惠元元者，视周宣有光焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275116_comment'></div>朕临政愿治，仰遵慈训，夙夜不敢忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275116_comment'></div>而边籴翔贵，生齿益落，自古版籍者裁什二三，侨居浮寄，无所系心，劝之勤而应之怠，其咎安在？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275116_comment'></div>岂下吏未能奉称，而尽地力之教不先欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275116_comment'></div>将豪夺暴役与东作争而害农者蕃欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275116_comment'></div>夫两淮吾所重也，异日沃𡐨上腴，为天下最，今乃侪于荒远彫敝之区，几不为郡，长民者独安取此！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275116_comment'></div>继自今其悉乃心，销沮游末，力穑惇本，以称朕安集之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275116_comment'></div>有能帅先垦辟为诸郡倡者，部使者上其名，以差受宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275116_comment'></div>若纵弛怠傲，不如吾诏者，亦纠劾以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275116_comment'></div>时则有显，罚不可逭，朕言维服，尚听毋忽。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1275116_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1165&endYear=1165')">1165年8月</a>　吕大器为池州守，代父作谢表、谢启。作品：《代仓部知池州谢表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷二。）</span>《代仓部知池州谢宰执启》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷四。）</span>《代仓部知池州答教官启》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷四。）</span><div id='poem_1275120' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275120' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275120?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代仓部知池州谢表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1165年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275120")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275120_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275120'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275120'>淮壖乘障，初无固圉之功；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275120_comment'></div>江表干城，复玷承流之寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275120_comment'></div>甫祗职业，参布诏条<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275120_comment'></div>伏念臣缪膺世赏之延，滥缀官联之末。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275120_comment'></div>投身冗散，降命奇穷，曩随牒以戍边，通传烽而儆备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275120_comment'></div>当戎马之侵轶，屡濒至危；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275120_comment'></div>赖王师之奋张，卒获自保。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275120_comment'></div>偶逃龟椟之毁，复玷鱼符之分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275120_comment'></div>矧池阳之奥区，乃江表之重地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275120_comment'></div>干戈载戢，则必佩服包桑之戒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275120_comment'></div>兵农杂居，则必洽比细柳之屯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275120_comment'></div>匪时闳材，畴荷隆委？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275120_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下刚健中正，齐圣广渊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275120_comment'></div>赐十行之书，留神万国；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275120_comment'></div>考三载之绩，久任官师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275120_comment'></div>自惊留落之踪，亦预使令之列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275120_comment'></div>臣敢不悉循侯度，祗若政经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1275120_comment'></div>辑宁凋瘵之馀，咨度弛张之要。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1275120_comment'></div>道上德意，如瞻咫尺之光；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1275120_comment'></div>同众戚休，敢顾斗升之禄！</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1275120_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1275473' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275473' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275473?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代仓部知池州谢宰执启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1165年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275473")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275473_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275473'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275473'>考课边城，讫无善状；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275473_comment'></div>承流泽国，复出洪钧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275473_comment'></div>既诹日以涖官，敢寓书而彻听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275473_comment'></div>窃以朝廷之上，每以休息生养为心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275473_comment'></div>郡邑之间，宜以还定安集为事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275473_comment'></div>矧池阳之都会，实江表之要冲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275473_comment'></div>如虎如貔，旁穆万屯之聚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275473_comment'></div>载芟载柞，俯绥千耦之耕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275473_comment'></div>承里闾艰食之馀，当师旅劳还之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275473_comment'></div>欲畀拊循之任，必求通达之材。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275473_comment'></div>如某者名迹湮微，性质固陋，偶袭箕裘之绪，久安州县之劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275473_comment'></div>顷佩左符，往守孤垒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275473_comment'></div>属遽书之驰骛，纷疆事之绎骚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275473_comment'></div>顾当地势之必争，适会敌锋之不至，幸终更而去彼，荷新渥以来斯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275473_comment'></div>爰考唐朝，有杜牧把麾之旧；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275473_comment'></div>其临秋浦，亦齐安解组之馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275473_comment'></div>虽后先迁徙之偶同，顾今昔风流之非匹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1275473_comment'></div>退思侥倖之极，尽出陶成之私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1275473_comment'></div>恭惟某官经纬皇猷，弥纶王度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1275473_comment'></div>权衡有信，揣轻重而得宜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1275473_comment'></div>坯冶无心，俾小大而为用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1275473_comment'></div>近柬周行之彦，远咨共理之良。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1275473_comment'></div>何此孱庸，亦容忝冒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1275473_comment'></div>某敢不蠲除民瘼，和辑师屯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1275473_comment'></div>歌《小雅》飞雁之诗，敢忘劳来；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1275473_comment'></div>读西京循吏之传，益务慰安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1275473_comment'></div>庶几一得之愚，或有万分之补。</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1275473_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1275474' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275474' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275474?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代仓部知池州答教官启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1165年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275474")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275474_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275474'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275474'>并玉关而出戍，已愧罔功；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275474_comment'></div>朌铜虎以分符，荐膺因任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275474_comment'></div>方愧驰书之缓，乃蒙坠翰之先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275474_comment'></div>伏惟某官心醉六经，学关百氏，赫奕词林之誉，从容泮水之游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275474_comment'></div>自幸衰踪，获联王事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275474_comment'></div>虽费日簿书之末，无预师儒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275474_comment'></div>然移风俎豆之间，冀资郡政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275474_comment'></div>风飙载厉，灯火可亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275474_comment'></div>愿益厚于节宣，庶导迎于休宠。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1275474_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='39f2bca2ccb34a3298c1b9166a06762a_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("39f2bca2ccb34a3298c1b9166a06762a");'><span id='39f2bca2ccb34a3298c1b9166a06762a_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1166&endYear=1166')">1166年</a>，30岁</div><div id='39f2bca2ccb34a3298c1b9166a06762a' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1166&endYear=1166')">1166年5月</a>　外祖曾几卒，代父作祭文。作品：《代仓部祭曾文清公文》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷八。）</span><div id='poem_1275689' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275689' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275689?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代仓部祭曾文清公文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1166年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275689")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275689_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275689'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275689'>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275689_comment'></div>邈丘壑之韵者，身清而命未必厚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275689_comment'></div>鸿彝鼎之勋者，命厚而身未必清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275689_comment'></div>判两涂而分骛，犹参商与渭泾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275689_comment'></div>昔香山之退傅，遗簪组而沈冥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275689_comment'></div>澹酬风而酢月，陶至乐于林坰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275689_comment'></div>蹇降命之多奇，屡哭殇于颓龄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275689_comment'></div>若汾阳之元老，庇九族以咸宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275689_comment'></div>驱缌繐而扫迹，纷角羁而忘名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275689_comment'></div>极二纪之豪华，醉世味而未醒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275689_comment'></div>盖挹其至清，则厚福不得而多取；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275689_comment'></div>居其至厚，则清趣不可以力争。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275689_comment'></div>惟丈人之所享，合内外而俱亨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275689_comment'></div>还紫橐而却蒲轮，颓然天放者既专物外之乐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275689_comment'></div>道板舆而奉鸠杖，驩然色养者又擅区中之荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275689_comment'></div>等之香山则无其惨戚，权之汾阳则未尝满盈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275689_comment'></div>全古人之未全，旷千载其难并。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1275689_comment'></div>乘至全而反真，夫何憾于泉扃！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1275689_comment'></div>然而坠一世之师表，夺四朝之典型。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1275689_comment'></div>涸洙泗之渊源，绝风骚之统盟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1275689_comment'></div>朋椠人与墨客，胥霣涕而失声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1275689_comment'></div>眇孤生之孱陋，夙受室于门庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1275689_comment'></div>辈子侄以拊育，迨衰发之星星。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1275689_comment'></div>归印绶以尽哀，迫科法之见绳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1275689_comment'></div>传壶觞而往酹，泪随河之东倾。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1275689_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='8f8d5d1a7fe5413e975c897b83fb96cc_label'><a href='javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1166&endYear=1166')">1166年11月1日</a>　母卒舟中，护丧归婺州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年1月22日</a>　葬母亲曾氏于明招山。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='57632c2ad37f4d46a958e0a19d180377_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("57632c2ad37f4d46a958e0a19d180377");'><span id='57632c2ad37f4d46a958e0a19d180377_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1168')">1167-1168年</a>，31-32岁</div><div id='57632c2ad37f4d46a958e0a19d180377' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年5月</a>　回明招山。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年夏</a>　应朱熹共同编史之约，作编史条例。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年夏</a>　潘景宪、彭仲刚等三百多人来学。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年9月</a>　函候汪应辰，劝谏当任天下之重有补吾道。作品：《与汪端明》五。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷七。）</span><br /><a href="javascript:
