href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年</a>　门人巩丰来学。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1168&endYear=1168')">1168年5月</a>　岳父韩元吉知建宁府，代作谢表。作品：《为韩尚书作知建宁府谢表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷二。）</span><div id='poem_1275139' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275139' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275139?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为韩尚书作知建宁府谢表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1168年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275139")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275139_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275139'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275139'>辅郡罔功，方吁天而沥恳；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275139_comment'></div>潜藩非据，乃易地以疏恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275139_comment'></div>优假至深，凌兢曷已<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275139_comment'></div>伏念臣奋繇平进，亲受异知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275139_comment'></div>参言语侍从之流，遭逢厚甚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275139_comment'></div>责献纳论思之效，称塞缺然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275139_comment'></div>假宠清厢，分忧近甸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275139_comment'></div>拊摩无术，幸及于食新；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275139_comment'></div>全度有加，讫蒙于念旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275139_comment'></div>惟建溪之作屏，实代邸之启封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275139_comment'></div>属此丐闲，眷焉改畀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275139_comment'></div>宦游未远，驱驰尚记于壮时；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275139_comment'></div>民力已殚，凋瘵顿殊于前日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275139_comment'></div>姑勉图于综理，恐终负于使令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275139_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下明烛万微，惠绥群献。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275139_comment'></div>本末轻重，咸归统御之中；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275139_comment'></div>小大短长，不出范围之外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1275139_comment'></div>顾如衰钝，亦获便安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1275139_comment'></div>臣敢不上体曲成，益思尽瘁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1275139_comment'></div>土风里俗，虽粗识其二三；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1275139_comment'></div>王泽国章，曷布宣于万一！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1275139_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1275139_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1168&endYear=1168')">1168年9月</a>　制定学规《乾道四年九月规约》十一条，强调孝弟忠信。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1168&endYear=1168')">1168年秋</a>　自明招山归城。吕大器出知吉州，代作谢表、谢启。作品：《代仓部知吉州谢表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷二。）</span>《代仓部通吉州交代钱吏部启》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷四。）</span>《代仓部通吉州胡邦衡侍郎启》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷四。）</span><div id='poem_1275125' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275125' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275125?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代仓部知吉州谢表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1168年秋）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275125")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275125_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275125'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275125'>俟罪仓曹，无裨邦计；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275125_comment'></div>分忧江国，尚玷藩条。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275125_comment'></div>丁宁临遣之荣，怵惕拊摩之责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275125_comment'></div>庀官甫始，拊己载兢<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275125_comment'></div>维是庐陵，介于楚甸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275125_comment'></div>土膏而人瘠，物夥而俗贫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275125_comment'></div>万室连甍，剽夺时鸣于桴鼓；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275125_comment'></div>千艘衔尾，转输日困于舳舻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275125_comment'></div>匪时通材，畴荷隆委？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275125_comment'></div>如臣者赋资谫薄，涉世阔疏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275125_comment'></div>两郡民编，蔑矣慰安之效；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275125_comment'></div>二年省掾，居然尸素之惭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275125_comment'></div>亟求襆被之行，复与剖符之寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275125_comment'></div>力绵识眊，责重事丛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275125_comment'></div>惟仰恃于乾坤，或俯资于尘露。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275125_comment'></div>兹盖伏遇皇帝陛下配天立极，继圣御图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275125_comment'></div>恢举闳模，网在纲而不紊；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1275125_comment'></div>操持大柄，臂使指而必从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1275125_comment'></div>虽远在于江湖，犹近临于轩陛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1275125_comment'></div>臣敢不布宣诏令，怀辑里闾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1275125_comment'></div>急效近功，忍自谋于宠利；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1275125_comment'></div>深根固本，誓勉尽于拙诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1275125_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1275125_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1275475' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275475' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275475?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代仓部通吉州交代钱吏部启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1168年秋）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275475")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275475_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275475'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275475'>列戟相望，夙托门阑之旧；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275475_comment'></div>拥麾归觐，复承矩矱之新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275475_comment'></div>接武有期，拊躬载抃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275475_comment'></div>恭惟某官德隆门表，识贯邦仪，赜阴阳消长之原，极文武弛张之用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275475_comment'></div>河山带砺，骍旄传百世之盟；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275475_comment'></div>彝鼎蒸尝，膰脤袭五王之庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275475_comment'></div>尚矣典刑之未替，蔚然文献之可观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275475_comment'></div>早涉要津，浸敷华问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275475_comment'></div>大邦维屏，泽久浃于侯藩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275475_comment'></div>太微积星，望夙高于郎位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275475_comment'></div>越从閒燕，申命拊循，衡经律以参稽，权恩威而并用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275475_comment'></div>鲁公报政，方当入辅之年；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275475_comment'></div>楚尹告新，其在合符之日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275475_comment'></div>某昔勤展对，今幸规随，瞻遐躅以益高，策羸躯而自愧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275475_comment'></div>受雄剧浩繁之责，窃有惧焉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275475_comment'></div>承渐摩绥辑之馀，则知免矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275475_comment'></div>气和青律，日靖黄堂，愿毖护于节宣，用宁承于眷倚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1275475_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1275476' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275476' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275476?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代仓部通吉州胡邦衡侍郎启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1168年秋）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275476")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275476_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275476'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275476'>避盖公之舍，夙愿趋承；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275476_comment'></div>倚韩子之门，尚虞麾斥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275476_comment'></div>敢陈尺牍，恪布寸诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275476_comment'></div>恭惟某官名冠伦魁，学穷根柢，贯大忠于日月，际浩气于堪舆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275476_comment'></div>早抗危言，力扶正论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275476_comment'></div>帝臣蹇蹇，岂容藜藿之干；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275476_comment'></div>王道平平，忍使荆榛之塞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275476_comment'></div>风波万里，金石一心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275476_comment'></div>逮鼎鬯之承尧，首弓旌而聘尹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275476_comment'></div>屹中流之砥柱，坐阅颓波；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275476_comment'></div>澹欲晓之长庚，独高众宿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275476_comment'></div>浸□□□，□□□□。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275476_comment'></div>□汲直于淮阳，□孚舆论；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275476_comment'></div>见贾□□□□，□柬宸衷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275476_comment'></div>共期三接之馀，亟奉四邻之拜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275476_comment'></div>某素思慕用，兹幸瞻依。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275476_comment'></div>秣马膏车，已溯风于墙屏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1275476_comment'></div>墨笔操牍，先展敬于缄縢。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1275476_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1168&endYear=1168')">1168年11月</a>　代刘夙作《祭忠简赵公文》作品：《代刘衢州祭赵忠简公文》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷八。）</span><div id='poem_1275690' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275690' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275690?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代刘衢州祭赵忠简公文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1168年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275690")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275690_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275690'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275690'>惟公高风懿躅，照映今昔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275690_comment'></div>下自管葛，所在不数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275690_comment'></div>中遭谗逐，以卒于死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275690_comment'></div>下至行路，为公出涕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275690_comment'></div>不三十年，是非一定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275690_comment'></div>中兴名相，一夔而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275690_comment'></div>有来假守，敢言尚德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275690_comment'></div>南望楸梧，去我百里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275690_comment'></div>官箴有常，莫克敬告。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275690_comment'></div>归心典刑，有如卮酒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275690_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1275690_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='42d052b2dff84f0b93dde97ab857c029_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("42d052b2dff84f0b93dde97ab857c029");'><span id='42d052b2dff84f0b93dde97ab857c029_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1168&endYear=1168')">1168年</a>，32岁</div><div id='42d052b2dff84f0b93dde97ab857c029' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1168&endYear=1168')">1168年</a>　本年修《东莱公家传》，盛赞吕好问。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='2c5a23300412454ea18d0205b67324cc_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("2c5a23300412454ea18d0205b67324cc");'><span id='2c5a23300412454ea18d0205b67324cc_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年</a>，33岁</div><div id='2c5a23300412454ea18d0205b67324cc' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年3月4日</a>　自宣城返回婺州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年4月</a>　作《书杨次渊之父所藏旧游诸公手简后》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》目录第七卷。）</span><div id='poem_1275510' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275510' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275510?labeling=true' target='_blank'>书杨次渊之父所藏旧游诸公手简后</a><span class='authorDate'>（1169年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275510")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275510_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275510'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275510'>盛山十二诗，前唱后和者，长庆间皆集阙下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275510_comment'></div>败楮瘴墨，奕奕顿有生气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275510_comment'></div>今杨侯自放林壑间，其视韦阆州老身廊庙，未知孰得孰失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275510_comment'></div>而同帖四君，皆发闻于时，嗣德有继。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275510_comment'></div>异时一笑相遇，细数盛山诗轴中人，必将曰：「尔何曾比予于是」？</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1275510_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年4月</a>　应门人叶重开之请，为其祖父叶洵仁作墓志铭。作品：《松阳叶君墓志铭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷十。）</span><div id='poem_1275646' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275646' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275646?labeling=true' target='_blank'>松阳叶君墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（乾道五年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275646")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275646_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275646'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275646'>宣和中，盗发帮源，旁郡奸侠，謼嘂趋和，贼势怒张。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275646_comment'></div>大吏或叛官守、亡城社、羞污印韨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275646_comment'></div>闾里以气自许者，望旗鼓迎，自屈陨名队节，项背相望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275646_comment'></div>当是时，松阳叶君独以孝著。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275646_comment'></div>君以眇然儒者，奉其父匿山中，猝与贼遇，奋前翼蔽其父，被三四创犹不少却。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275646_comment'></div>贼内刃相顾曰：「是乃以死代父，孝子也，杀之不祥」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275646_comment'></div>逡巡引去，父子迄皆全。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275646_comment'></div>乡老尝在兵间者，道叶君至今不去口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275646_comment'></div>呜呼，是可轶其传哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275646_comment'></div>君讳洵仁，字行中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275646_comment'></div>曾祖某，祖某，父某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275646_comment'></div>君少耆学，游场屋辄不耦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275646_comment'></div>既孤，家益落，太夫人忧劳甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275646_comment'></div>君不忍私其力于铅椠，乃罢举治耕稼，以宽亲意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275646_comment'></div>居亡何，资用饶衍，侪辈交劝君卒业，君固已倦游，不复言课试事矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275646_comment'></div>暇日亲程课子孙以学，复为儒家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275646_comment'></div>晚节传家政，觞咏自适，盖年八十有一而终，乾道四年四月十四日也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1275646_comment'></div>娶潘氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1275646_comment'></div>男四，长瑅，次楠，次󰥁，次瑴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1275646_comment'></div>󰥁先君卒，楠、瑴出继。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1275646_comment'></div>女二，长适秉义郎邵绩，次适进士周炤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1275646_comment'></div>孙男五，重开、重光、重熙、重规、重易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1275646_comment'></div>孙女五。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1275646_comment'></div>曾孙景先，尚幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1275646_comment'></div>后一岁某月某日，瑅奉公丧葬于某山某原，重开来谒铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1275646_comment'></div>重开尝从予游，道君之葬，稽参古制，凡慝礼夷教悉屏弃勿用，其不怵于俗如此，可谓难也已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1275646_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_1275646'>寇方兴，时大棘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1275646_comment'></div>孚虓嚚，祗子职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1275646_comment'></div>瑑之坚，竁之密。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1275646_comment'></div>维旌君，诏无极。</div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1275646_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年5月</a>　与李丙、戴衍等游灵洞。有《戴衍字序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷六。）</span><div id='poem_1275594' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275594' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275594?labeling=true' target='_blank'>戴衍字序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1169年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275594")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275594_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275594'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275594'>己丑之夏，予将有馀不之役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275594_comment'></div>舟既戒，谋休樯息缆之地，篙师举手东其指曰：「道双溪三十里，灵洞在焉，盍趣棹以逋午暑」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275594_comment'></div>予款其名久，适与心会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275594_comment'></div>戚友尊稚蕲共载者八九人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275594_comment'></div>舟尾炊未熟，已就岸，相与屐巇燧闇，目随步改，大巧巨丽，皆前人之所未品。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275594_comment'></div>竣事，念胜游之不可虚也，属昭武李仲南大疏偕来者里系次其齿识壁间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275594_comment'></div>吾友戴衍景杜，班在八，仲南倚笔请曰：晞古乡贤，著名字以示不忘，固多前比，然祁公言论风旨犹相接，若兼氏而书，东行西行者，或援避贤邮以病灵洞壁，则何如」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275594_comment'></div>戴子瞿然谒予更其字。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275594_comment'></div>予尝读《易》矣，《需》之既济曰：「需于沙」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275594_comment'></div>孔子象之，曰衍在中也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275594_comment'></div>天下之至险莫如水，水与泥际，而泥复与沙际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275594_comment'></div>繇沙望水，其险浸已远矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275594_comment'></div>履深淖而并惊澜，虽纵臾使疾驱且不敢，至于碛平如砥，万辔一驰，独能柅方奔之足于险未迫之时，夫岂徒哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275594_comment'></div>是中非躁迫者所能驻，舒徐容与，久在此而不前，殆必博大广衍、绰有馀地者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275594_comment'></div>《易》象既言衍而踵以在，意者将视所居以占所养欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275594_comment'></div>在南曰橘，在北曰枳，失其所在则名去之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275594_comment'></div>心不在广莫之乡而强以衍自许，畴诺之哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1275594_comment'></div>貌示閒暇，嗜利逞欲，以蹈大险，如晋之衍，盖辱其名矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1275594_comment'></div>洗此名之辱者，惟吾子是托，故以在伯侑子名，子其勉之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1275594_comment'></div>毋躁毋迫，毋厌淡泊，无失子之真在，则口是名于席，笔是名于牍，俯仰皆无愧也，子其勉之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1275594_comment'></div>在伯，志士也，所自期者远甚，故予不敢置孔子而言它。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1275594_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='9ff01f36f5f14be38700ca5214ea4e18_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("9ff01f36f5f14be38700ca5214ea4e18");'><span id='9ff01f36f5f14be38700ca5214ea4e18_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年</a>，33岁</div><div id='9ff01f36f5f14be38700ca5214ea4e18' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年8月11日</a>　自德清归婺州。以继室韩夫人庙见。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年8月25日</a>　以太学博士补外，添差严州学教授。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年</a>　以考满改秩，致书虞允文，示以要勉自讲习，求所未至。作品：《与虞丞相》一。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷十一。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年9月23日</a>　韩元吉等来婺州，与之同游兰溪灵洞。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='99187e0d586d455994388fdb7c436594_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("99187e0d586d455994388fdb7c436594");'><span id='99187e0d586d455994388fdb7c436594_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年</a>，33岁</div><div id='99187e0d586d455994388fdb7c436594' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: id='poem_1275605' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275605' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275605?labeling=true' target='_blank'>横山吴君佚老庵记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1169年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275605")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275605_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275605'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275605'>横山吴君珉治别室之西偏，榜以佚老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275605_comment'></div>休工归役，斤斧收声，辑杖立于前荣，闻窃语于阶者曰：「棋垄绳畦，坻粟京稼，筹算挂壁，万货四凑，此吾主人翁所以佚其老也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275605_comment'></div>少进至于门，闻行语于涂者曰：「丰林邃宇，尊俎静嘉，鸥鹭不惊，风月相答，此吾豪长者所以佚其老也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275605_comment'></div>又进至于郊，闻聚语于塾者曰：「培嗣以学，既楙既敷，秩壸以礼，既序既饬，此吾乡丈人所以佚其老也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275605_comment'></div>他日吴君为予道之，予曰：「夫三者之言何如」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275605_comment'></div>吴君曰：「阶得吾粕，涂得吾漓，塾得吾醇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275605_comment'></div>出浸远而说浸近，吾名吾室义，其究于此乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275605_comment'></div>予曰：「未既也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275605_comment'></div>畏峤登舆，身閒心慄；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275605_comment'></div>厌市筑墉，目静耳喧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275605_comment'></div>君虽善自佚，踰闑以往，肩赪腹枵者，踵相接，岁或不升，尪瘠困惫，呻吟交于大逵，专一室之佚，乐乎哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275605_comment'></div>君里中望也，盍劝相族党，愒劳赈乏，己责纾逋，同其佚于是乡，则尽横山表里，皆君佚老庵也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275605_comment'></div>其视尺椽半席，广狭何若」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275605_comment'></div>吴君谢曰：「厚矣，子之拓吾境也」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275605_comment'></div>顾童奴陷其说于壁间，以为券。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1275605_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='035bc82957ce4c62a7718b79602bb2e3_label'><a href='javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1170')">1170年闰5月4日</a>　吕大器自吉州还，吕祖谦自严州归婺侍父。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1170')">1170年闰5月8日</a>　会诸生于丽泽，有学规《规矩七事》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷六。）</span><br /></div><div class='label1' id='6b8d120a4798494b8ea9a7e0f2d839b8_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("6b8d120a4798494b8ea9a7e0f2d839b8");'><span id='6b8d120a4798494b8ea9a7e0f2d839b8_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1171&endYear=1171')">1171年6月8日</a>　归婺州治韩氏妻丧。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1171&endYear=1171')">1171年6月13日</a>　张栻以论张说事出知袁州。吕祖谦作书与朱熹论及朝政，并赠所刻《易传》三本。作品：《与朱侍讲》七。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷七。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1171&endYear=1171')">1171年6月17日</a>　葬妻子于明招山。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1171&endYear=1171')">1171年6月</a>　致书邢世材，述说丧事、国事，心绪不佳。作品：《与邢邦用》三。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷十。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1171&endYear=1171')">1171年</a>　作《祔韩氏志》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷十。）</span><div id='poem_1275649' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275649' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275649?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祔韩氏志</a><span class='authorDate'>（乾道七年六月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275649")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275649_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275649'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275649'>乾道七年夏六月庚申，左从政郎，太学博士、兼国史院编修官、兼实录院检讨官吕某，祔其继室于元配之兆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275649_comment'></div>始某踰冠授室，盖今尚书左司郎中韩元吉长女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275649_comment'></div>既五年而夭，左司公实识其葬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275649_comment'></div>后七年复女焉，越二年又夭，寿二十有七。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275649_comment'></div>改月而葬，与长姊同域异穴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275649_comment'></div>惟内外辨位而司家政者，名不出壸，虽敬戒以祗妇道，犹其常也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275649_comment'></div>兹用不书，以附《春秋》之义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275649_comment'></div>土姓氏系列于前志者，亦不再见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275649_comment'></div>二女，长曰复，幼曰螺。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1275649_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='bacb5dcf07df43a7b0a0071a99c9e05e_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("bacb5dcf07df43a7b0a0071a99c9e05e");'><span id='bacb5dcf07df43a7b0a0071a99c9e05e_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1171&endYear=1171')">1171年</a>，35岁</div><div id='bacb5dcf07df43a7b0a0071a99c9e05e' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1171&endYear=1171')">1171年</a>　侍父归婺州。作书与执政请祠侍亲，不许。作品：《与虞丞相》二。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷十一。）</span>《与梁参政》二。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷十一。）</span><div id='poem_1275436' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275436' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275436?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与虞丞相书<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1171年7月8日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275436")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275436_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275436'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275436'>某琐微之迹，自托炉锤，身非己有，去来出入，固当肃听造命，不当自必。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275436_comment'></div>然私义迫切，用敢犯渎尊之谴而终布之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275436_comment'></div>某亲年浸高，而诸弟皆未更事，左右就养，不可远违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275436_comment'></div>前此固尝控闻钧听，今兹冒暑远归，百绪皆未有条理，尤重轻去膝下而以其劳遗老者，恳恳之诚，在所悯察，傥蒙畀以祠禄，以为甘旨之奉，于其馀暇，温习旧学，二三年间，稍稍就绪，自当袖书光范，求备大厦一木之用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275436_comment'></div>悃愊披露，惟孚其实而怜其情，不胜幸愿。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1275436_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1275129' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275129' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275129?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为梁参政作辞册宝转官表<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1171年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275129")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275129_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275129'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275129'>显册昭融，光于二典；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275129_comment'></div>需章恳款，閟以九关。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275129_comment'></div>不胜坠谷之忧，嗣上循墙之请<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275129_comment'></div>伏念臣起繇疏贱，滥与几微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275129_comment'></div>肆惟竣事于明禋，并奏鸿名于慈极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275129_comment'></div>职是讨论之重，独出鼎司；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275129_comment'></div>凛然绘画之难，莫穷坤载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275129_comment'></div>敢图诏綍，概陟官联。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275129_comment'></div>历考前闻，邈无近比。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275129_comment'></div>欲展终辞之微志，敢循再渎之常科。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275129_comment'></div>崇听益高，奏封复却。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275129_comment'></div>虽隆威之难犯，觊拙守之获伸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275129_comment'></div>伏望皇帝陛下鉴厥忱诚，体其控诉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275129_comment'></div>厉弼谐之廉耻，用振四维；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275129_comment'></div>改庆赐于英材，以全三乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275129_comment'></div>曲收成命，少穆师言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275129_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1275129_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1171&endYear=1171')">1171年7月24日</a>　以通历任四考，改左宣教郎。召试馆职。以侍亲为由，再与虞丞相书请祠归乡。作品：《与虞丞相》三。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷十一。）</span><div id='poem_1275436' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275436' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275436?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与虞丞相书<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1171年7月8日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275436")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275436_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275436'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275436'>某琐微之迹，自托炉锤，身非己有，去来出入，固当肃听造命，不当自必。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275436_comment'></div>然私义迫切，用敢犯渎尊之谴而终布之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275436_comment'></div>某亲年浸高，而诸弟皆未更事，左右就养，不可远违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275436_comment'></div>前此固尝控闻钧听，今兹冒暑远归，百绪皆未有条理，尤重轻去膝下而以其劳遗老者，恳恳之诚，在所悯察，傥蒙畀以祠禄，以为甘旨之奉，于其馀暇，温习旧学，二三年间，稍稍就绪，自当袖书光范，求备大厦一木之用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275436_comment'></div>悃愊披露，惟孚其实而怜其情，不胜幸愿。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1275436_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1171&endYear=1171')">1171年</a>　写信与邢世材，言欲一意读书为学。作品：《与邢邦用》四。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷十。）</span><div id='poem_1275404' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275404' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275404?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与邢邦用书<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1170年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275404")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275404_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275404'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275404'>某自春来为建宁之行，与朱元晦相聚四十馀日，复同出至鹅湖，二陆及子澄诸兄皆集，甚有讲论之益。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275404_comment'></div>自此却无出入，可闭户读书也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275404_comment'></div>前书所论甚当，近已尝为子静详言之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275404_comment'></div>讲贯诵绎，乃百代为学通法，学者缘此支离泛滥，自是人病，非是法病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275404_comment'></div>见此而欲尽废之，正是因噎废食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275404_comment'></div>然学者苟徒能言其非，而未能反己就实，悠悠汩汩，无所底止，是又适所以坚彼之自信也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275404_comment'></div>尊兄试深思之，以为如何？</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1275404_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1171&endYear=1171')">1171年</a>　致书陈亮，言辞官事、薛季宣事，并允陈亮暇日为作要斋铭。作品：《与陈同甫》二。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷十。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1171&endYear=1171')">1171年9月16日</a>　除秘书省正字兼国史院编修官、实录院检讨官。有谢政府启。作品：《除馆职谢政府启》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷四。）</span><div id='poem_1275486' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275486' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275486?labeling=true' target='_blank'>除馆职谢政府启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1171年9月16日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275486")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275486_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275486'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275486'>奏薄技于北门，所期报罢；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275486_comment'></div>并英游于东观，乃奉诏除。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275486_comment'></div>非据之惭，不胜是惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275486_comment'></div>窃惟艺祖于县县汎扫之始，大辑群书；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275486_comment'></div>太宗于疆陲警候之时，肇新三馆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275486_comment'></div>王猷未靖，戎务方兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275486_comment'></div>属此多艰，骛熊罴于郊野；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275486_comment'></div>曷其有暇，仪鸿鹄于园林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275486_comment'></div>仰窥闳模，厥见深指。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275486_comment'></div>盖丰功茂烈，非不足以曜威灵；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275486_comment'></div>硕画老谋，非不足以供指顾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275486_comment'></div>至于崇建治本，翼扶化基，将为深长久大之规，必访希阔寂寥之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275486_comment'></div>乃辑坟籍，乃宾畯良，洗光濯翳于陈腐已蠹之馀，改容更貌于习俗共轻之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275486_comment'></div>若徒盛观，第可饰于太平；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275486_comment'></div>必有沈几，乃见尊于英主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275486_comment'></div>其用则晦，其理则微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275486_comment'></div>跳荡驰驱，争效于可知之际；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1275486_comment'></div>宴谈讽咏，潜扶于不见之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1275486_comment'></div>閒剧两涂，弛张一柄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1275486_comment'></div>于今之制，此意尚存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1275486_comment'></div>一人厉精，综覈于朝；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1275486_comment'></div>百吏竭蹶，趋承于下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1275486_comment'></div>独兹儒馆，特异常僚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1275486_comment'></div>厚廪广居，终日不离于笔墨；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1275486_comment'></div>雅游胜践，经年未识于符移。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1275486_comment'></div>匪欲养高，而忘考实，督之迫者课每易塞，期之宽者责反难酬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1275486_comment'></div>宜得轶材，以充盛选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1275486_comment'></div>如某者质则甚滞，学而弗专。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1275486_comment'></div>自其少时，既夺移于科试；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1275486_comment'></div>及乎壮齿，又堙废于隐忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1275486_comment'></div>竟失全功，徒怜初志，误见收于坯冶，辱为役于桥门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1275486_comment'></div>谫薄内惭，疏愚外见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1275486_comment'></div>置杯易涸，当思浚治之新；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1275486_comment'></div>覆块已枯，盍咎难培之旧！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1275486_comment'></div>怵然自悟，惕若反求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1275486_comment'></div>甫及终更，力祈归养，丐馀閒于定省，得毕愿于讲磨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1275486_comment'></div>诏旨甚严，私悰莫遂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1275486_comment'></div>思枯才竭，不能舒藻而为国华；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1275486_comment'></div>识眊志凋，不能献箴而达民瘼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1275486_comment'></div>分于汰斥，贲以甄升，阶是正之初筵，仍编摩之故步。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1275486_comment'></div>赐则厚矣，惧亦甚焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1275486_comment'></div>百年储养之严，未尝或滥；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1275486_comment'></div>一夫差择之误，自此将轻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1275486_comment'></div>虽佩鸿知，恐累大体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1275486_comment'></div>此盖伏遇某官道隆平施，义笃曲成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1275486_comment'></div>巢阁鸾凰，尽出网罗之获；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1275486_comment'></div>参天杞梓，悉由封殖之勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1275486_comment'></div>虽如冥顽，亦被光景。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1275486_comment'></div>某敢不藏修暇日，玩绎前闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1275486_comment'></div>名辈追随，庶发难开之蔽；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1275486_comment'></div>断编展对，少偿未足之心。</div><div id='poem_sentence_50_1275486_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='40a87490a88f45859e15b8840ef9fe73_label'><a href='javascript:
