ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1172&endYear=1172')">1172年</a>，36岁</div><div id='40a87490a88f45859e15b8840ef9fe73' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1172&endYear=1172')">1172年2月7日</a>　至家，吕大器已去世，丁忧。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1172&endYear=1172')">1172年2月</a>　复修《丧葬礼》、定《祭礼》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1172&endYear=1172')">1172年5月16日</a>　终父亲丧事，有书与朱熹，商榷《丧礼》、《祭礼》，欲践行。作品：《与朱侍讲》十四。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷七。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1172&endYear=1172')">1172年5月</a>　搜集资料补《伊洛渊源录》、《二程外书》、《震泽语录》<br /></div><div class='label1' id='d03577c65f2242588b333771c9311b25_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("d03577c65f2242588b333771c9311b25");'><span id='d03577c65f2242588b333771c9311b25_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1172&endYear=1174')">1172-1174年</a>，36-38岁</div><div id='d03577c65f2242588b333771c9311b25' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1172&endYear=1172')">1172年7月</a>　致书陈亮，谢吊亲丧，并邀约九月相聚。作品：《与陈同甫书》九。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷十。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1172&endYear=1172')">1172年11月3日</a>　葬父于明招山。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1172&endYear=1172')">1172年</a>　韩螺所生女夭折。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1173&endYear=1173')">1173年1月</a>　有《与汪端明》，论朱熹《五朝名臣言行录》多失真处。六。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷七。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1173&endYear=1173')">1173年1月</a>　有书与朱熹，与其商榷《五朝名臣言行录》作品：《与朱侍讲》二十五。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷八。）</span><div id='poem_1275255' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275255' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275255?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与朱侍讲元晦书<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其五十五 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1173年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275255")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275255_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275255'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275255'>丐祠虽未惬雅志，然诸公不欲贤者家食，虽未必由衷，然亦善意也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275255_comment'></div>但有畏不能容贤者之谤，比之全不分皂白者亦有间矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275255_comment'></div>张荆州病中请祠，亦有苦劝当途令从其请者，亦以向来之嫌，畏人议论不能容之，遂坚不肯从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275255_comment'></div>但作帅与小军垒不同，但须内外至诚相与，首尾相应，乃不误事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275255_comment'></div>既非心相与，则自有首尾衡决处，如来教数条皆是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275255_comment'></div>符节在身，不得擅去，此所以忧而至于病，病而至于死，每诵量而后入，不入而后量之语，为之泫然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275255_comment'></div>至于南康地既非要害，民又非浩穰，虽事之不如人意处固多，然无旦夕立至之忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275255_comment'></div>若且耐烦忍垢，拊摩疲民，苟稍成头绪，子重继之，必能遵守，使一方之民小小休息，亦不为无补也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275255_comment'></div>今去终更才半年馀耳，交印后身便自由，惟吾志所欲，无不可者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275255_comment'></div>或未终更，别有除改，半道引疾而归，亦甚省力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275255_comment'></div>陆子寿前日经过，留此二十馀日，幡然以鹅湖所见为非，甚欲著实看书讲论，心平气下，相识中甚难得也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275255_comment'></div>近因荆州之赴，深思渠学识分晓周正如此，而从游之士，往往不得力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275255_comment'></div>记得往年相聚时，虽未能尽领解渠说话，然觉得大段有益，不知其它从游者何故乃如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275255_comment'></div>盖五十丈不能察人情虚实，必如某之专愚毋它，其教诲乃有所施耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275255_comment'></div>若胸中多端者，虽朝夕相处，未必能有益也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275255_comment'></div>《中庸》论尽己之性，又继之以尽人之性，尽物之性，工夫无穷如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275255_comment'></div>此岂追往事，亦要高明深勉之耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1275255_comment'></div>五十丈所作《濂溪祠堂记》，告妆褫一本送示，欲挂壁间观省耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1275255_comment'></div>亲旧间多相勉撤去书册，固知此理，但旧所偏嗜，未能顿去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1275255_comment'></div>近亦十减五六矣，如时文却不曾与人看。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1275255_comment'></div>受之在此作课，亦只是舍弟辈为之点检也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1275255_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1173&endYear=1173')">1173年1月</a>　薛季宣来访，相与讨论世务及义理，约定长期的论学计划。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1173&endYear=1173')">1173年1月</a>　徐居厚来访，始从吕祖谦游。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1173&endYear=1173')">1173年闰1月</a>　魏元履卒，有挽章。作品：《魏元履国禄挽章》二首之一。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷一。）</span><div id='poem_94135' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_94135' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/94135?labeling=true' target='_blank'>魏元履国录挽章二首<span class='inlineComment2'>（淳熙元年七月二十日）</span><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1173年闰1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_94135")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_94135_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_94135'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_94135'>麻衣见天子，拜疏不知休。<div id='poem_sentence_0_94135_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_94135'>落落山林气，拳拳畎亩忧。<div id='poem_sentence_1_94135_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_94135'>极知千载遇，政用一身酬。<div id='poem_sentence_2_94135_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_94135'>绕舍闽溪水，朝宗日夜流。<div id='poem_sentence_3_94135_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_94135'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_94135_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_94134' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_94134' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/94134?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1173年闰1月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_94134_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_94134'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_94134'>群公祖疏傅，多士送阳城。<div id='poem_sentence_0_94134_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_94134'>短棹非前约，长亭及此行。<div id='poem_sentence_1_94134_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_94134'>深留移白日，共语只苍生。<div id='poem_sentence_2_94134_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_94134'>会续山阳赋，邻人笛未横。<div id='poem_sentence_3_94134_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_94134'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_94134_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1173&endYear=1173')">1173年2月</a>　答朱熹书，欢迎其子朱塾来学。作品：《与朱侍讲》十七。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷七。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1173&endYear=1173')">1173年4月</a>　致书汪应辰，讨论《五朝名臣言行录》作品：《与汪端明》八。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷七。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1173&endYear=1173')">1173年5月</a>　八叔吕大虬去世，至明招山料理丧事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1173&endYear=1173')">1173年6月</a>　致书朱熹，讨论学问，并询问朱塾到期。作品：《与朱侍讲》二十一。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷七。）</span><div id='poem_1275255' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275255' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275255?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与朱侍讲元晦书<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其五十五 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1173年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275255")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275255_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275255'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275255'>丐祠虽未惬雅志，然诸公不欲贤者家食，虽未必由衷，然亦善意也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275255_comment'></div>但有畏不能容贤者之谤，比之全不分皂白者亦有间矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275255_comment'></div>张荆州病中请祠，亦有苦劝当途令从其请者，亦以向来之嫌，畏人议论不能容之，遂坚不肯从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275255_comment'></div>但作帅与小军垒不同，但须内外至诚相与，首尾相应，乃不误事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275255_comment'></div>既非心相与，则自有首尾衡决处，如来教数条皆是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275255_comment'></div>符节在身，不得擅去，此所以忧而至于病，病而至于死，每诵量而后入，不入而后量之语，为之泫然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275255_comment'></div>至于南康地既非要害，民又非浩穰，虽事之不如人意处固多，然无旦夕立至之忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275255_comment'></div>若且耐烦忍垢，拊摩疲民，苟稍成头绪，子重继之，必能遵守，使一方之民小小休息，亦不为无补也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275255_comment'></div>今去终更才半年馀耳，交印后身便自由，惟吾志所欲，无不可者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275255_comment'></div>或未终更，别有除改，半道引疾而归，亦甚省力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275255_comment'></div>陆子寿前日经过，留此二十馀日，幡然以鹅湖所见为非，甚欲著实看书讲论，心平气下，相识中甚难得也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275255_comment'></div>近因荆州之赴，深思渠学识分晓周正如此，而从游之士，往往不得力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275255_comment'></div>记得往年相聚时，虽未能尽领解渠说话，然觉得大段有益，不知其它从游者何故乃如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275255_comment'></div>盖五十丈不能察人情虚实，必如某之专愚毋它，其教诲乃有所施耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275255_comment'></div>若胸中多端者，虽朝夕相处，未必能有益也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275255_comment'></div>《中庸》论尽己之性，又继之以尽人之性，尽物之性，工夫无穷如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275255_comment'></div>此岂追往事，亦要高明深勉之耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1275255_comment'></div>五十丈所作《濂溪祠堂记》，告妆褫一本送示，欲挂壁间观省耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1275255_comment'></div>亲旧间多相勉撤去书册，固知此理，但旧所偏嗜，未能顿去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1275255_comment'></div>近亦十减五六矣，如时文却不曾与人看。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1275255_comment'></div>受之在此作课，亦只是舍弟辈为之点检也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1275255_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1173&endYear=1173')">1173年7月</a>　薛季宣卒，遣人往吊。为薛季宣作墓志铭。作品：《薛常州墓志铭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷十。）</span><div id='poem_1275653' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275653' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275653?labeling=true' target='_blank'>薛常州墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1173年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275653")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275653_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275653'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275653'>河东之薛，有降居闽之长溪者，世久不能迹其始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275653_comment'></div>既又家于永嘉，其长老之记曰，唐补阙令之后迁焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275653_comment'></div>裔孙庠，以驯行闻于乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275653_comment'></div>庠生强立，始修补阙之旧，续其禄，盖终江宁府观察推官，赠左光禄大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275653_comment'></div>光禄四子：嘉言，尚书司封郎中；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275653_comment'></div>昌言，通判婺州；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275653_comment'></div>弼，敷文阁待制；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275653_comment'></div>徽言，起居舍人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275653_comment'></div>公讳季宣，字士龙，起居之子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275653_comment'></div>起居学于胡文定公安国，而雅为赵忠简公鼎所厚，其立朝皆有本末。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275653_comment'></div>最后秦丞相桧建与虏和，起居自殿坳直前，引义固争，反复数刻，中寒疾以卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275653_comment'></div>夫人胡氏亦继卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275653_comment'></div>于是公生六年矣，伯父待制收鞠之，任以官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275653_comment'></div>公幼逮事过江诸贤，闻中兴经理，大略已能识之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275653_comment'></div>喜从老校退卒语，得岳、韩二三大将兵间事甚悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275653_comment'></div>志尚荦荦，与常儿异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275653_comment'></div>年十七，起从妻父荆南帅孙汝翼，辟书写机宜文字。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1275653_comment'></div>荆州善袁溉道洁，虚郡斋迎致之，公遂委己师焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1275653_comment'></div>道洁及登河南程夫子之门，闻蜀隐者薛叟名，晚游蜀，以物色求之莫能得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1275653_comment'></div>末至一郡，并舍有叟旦荷笈之市，午漏下辄扃其户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1275653_comment'></div>道洁从壁间觇之，方隐几默坐，意象静深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1275653_comment'></div>问诸邻，则曰是鬻香薛翁，不知其所从来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1275653_comment'></div>道洁亟款门，以弟子礼见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1275653_comment'></div>旦往陈所学，叟漠然如不闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1275653_comment'></div>久之乃曰：「经所以载道，圣人作经以明道，子何博而寡要也」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1275653_comment'></div>始与深语。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1275653_comment'></div>未几复舍去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1275653_comment'></div>道洁漫浪沔鄂间，讳其学，绝不为人道，独与公倾倒无所靳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1275653_comment'></div>公自是笃意于学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1275653_comment'></div>道洁语公，伊洛轶书多在蜀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1275653_comment'></div>时同郡萧振方制置四川，乃往为其属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1275653_comment'></div>道洁期至蜀授以书，会偏裨有诬其所部将者，公请正阶级法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1275653_comment'></div>议不合，谢去，遇道洁于峡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1275653_comment'></div>而公既出蜀矣，调鄂州武昌令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1275653_comment'></div>武昌号难治，连败数令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1275653_comment'></div>公年尚少，郡将、部使者易之，迎谓：「是邑久不可为，子敢当之乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1275653_comment'></div>公曰：「独患在上者以县为可为，今知其不可为，则可为矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1275653_comment'></div>愿宽其衔辔，俾得自尽」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1275653_comment'></div>皆诺之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1275653_comment'></div>科徭兴发，率以公故独不及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1275653_comment'></div>唯论和籴，始不见答，欲解印绶去，卒体其诚，得罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1275653_comment'></div>公既获乎上，民赖以宽，有所废置，皆争趣和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1275653_comment'></div>乃大治，版籍、期会、简稽、出纳，悉就绳尺，密而不烦，严而不迫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1275653_comment'></div>虏亮未叛盟，公白其长，视要害，前备御，辄不省。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1275653_comment'></div>及兵交，稍稍即公咨计画。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1275653_comment'></div>虏亮悉众瞰江，诏成闵还师入援。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1275653_comment'></div>时汪枢使澈宣谕荆襄，公告：「成闵得蔡，有破竹之势，盍守便宜勿遣？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1275653_comment'></div>令闵乘虚下武昌，径陈、汝趋汴都，虏内顾且惊溃，释此成业，而聚兵相仗，鲜克以济」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1275653_comment'></div>不能用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1275653_comment'></div>闵昼夜驰不顿舍，后骑能属者三之一，而陈、蔡新附诸城，亦踵接复为虏矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1275653_comment'></div>江淮仕者大抵无固志，纷纷遣其孥系马庭木以须。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1275653_comment'></div>公独留家不遣，誓与民俱死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1275653_comment'></div>县故多盗，铁冶、营田，棋布诸乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1275653_comment'></div>亡命奸人，出没其间，所治即孙吴故宫，自古江左重地也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1275653_comment'></div>公念除盗上策，莫如联保甲，疆陲有事，唯素整者可不乱，乃访求河北、陕右弓箭手保甲法及淮西刘纲保伍要策，讨论甚具。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1275653_comment'></div>会有伍民之令，乃出其法行之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1275653_comment'></div>五家为保，二保为甲，六甲为队，因地形便合为总，不以乡为限，总首、副总首领焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1275653_comment'></div>官族、士族、富族、皆附保蠲其身，俾输财共总之小用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1275653_comment'></div>诸总必有射圃，民暇则习，无蚤暮之节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1275653_comment'></div>尽禁蒱博，独许以击刺驰射角胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1275653_comment'></div>五日更至庭阅，其尤者劳赏之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1275653_comment'></div>旗志总别为色，枪仗皆中度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1275653_comment'></div>候望干掫不幸死者，予棺，复家三岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1275653_comment'></div>诸乡皆置楼，盗发，伐鼓举烽以相号召，瞬息遍百里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1275653_comment'></div>总首白事，吏毋得预，追胥兴发，一以县檄为验。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1275653_comment'></div>环邑沟渎不渫，夏潦波道，在事者病之，役大莫敢睥睨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1275653_comment'></div>及保甲成，天大雨，公出坐通衢，传呼总队，具畚锸、赋丈尺，三日而毕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1275653_comment'></div>市多火，公戒诸队钩绳梯缶，各专其一，暮夜仓卒，随用而索，甚速且整，火不能灾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1275653_comment'></div>县治白鹿矶、安乐口，皆置戍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1275653_comment'></div>复请于宣谕司，得战舰十、甲三百，罗落之守计定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1275653_comment'></div>讫虏退，人心不摇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1275653_comment'></div>大军之屯州县，客主不相能，多为鬨暴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1275653_comment'></div>公曲得其欢心，以事至者，必微见曲直而明假借之，皆大喜且大服，誓死以报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1275653_comment'></div>内郡发粟输边，县当餫信阳，公部以往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1275653_comment'></div>先是诸将出师，部勒无法，或侵苦之，道殣相望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1275653_comment'></div>文吏董役者，则又甚焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1275653_comment'></div>民见调，辄与亲戚为死决。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1275653_comment'></div>公语父老曰：「子弟相从者，吾受其无咎」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1275653_comment'></div>皆怃然阳应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1275653_comment'></div>既发，队伍次舍悉放行军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1275653_comment'></div>亲与役夫同苦乐，病者挟医护视，始轻所负，剧则皆弛之，增剧则以马若舆载之，病者未至，队长毋得即安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1275653_comment'></div>号令齐一，道上担肩相差如引绳，无敢少蹉跌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1275653_comment'></div>观者相语曰：「此谁将军部曲耶，乃整肃如是」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1275653_comment'></div>既而知为武昌白丁，相视叹息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1275653_comment'></div>斯役也，在行者千有八百。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1275653_comment'></div>役罢，死者一人，跌伤者一人，馀还畀其父母妻子如初约。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1275653_comment'></div>当是时，诸公争知之，举辟交至，公一无所就。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1275653_comment'></div>从吏部铨得婺州司理参军，召对，首言治体有本末，愿遴三公之选，责以进人材，张纪纲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1275653_comment'></div>延端直之士，与之讲问学、求治道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1275653_comment'></div>又论中都官员多职寡，牧伯之任分为五六，唯大军胜战，将兵而下，废为隶役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1275653_comment'></div>因道远方民瘼甚悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1275653_comment'></div>王枢使炎前在鄂，熟公治行，及是新得政，求助于公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1275653_comment'></div>公语之曰：「上天资英特，群臣幸得遭时，乃忽略根本而奔走军旅之间，盍以仁义纲纪为本？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1275653_comment'></div>至于用兵，请俟十年之后」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1275653_comment'></div>改宣义郎，知平江府常熟县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1275653_comment'></div>退，待次具区滆上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1275653_comment'></div>明年，复召审察，公固辞，徘徊踰年乃就道，至则除大理寺主簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1275653_comment'></div>是岁江湖大旱，流民往往北渡江，边吏复奏淮北民多款塞者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1275653_comment'></div>虞丞相允文白遣公行淮西，收以实边。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1275653_comment'></div>公持节劳来，耄稚满车下，为之表废田、相原隰，复合肥三十六圩，立二十有二庄于黄州故治东北。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1275653_comment'></div>以户颁屋，以丁颁田，二丁共一牛，犁、杷、锄、锹、钁、镰具，六丁加一錅刀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1275653_comment'></div>每甲辘轴二，水车一，种子钱丁五千，廪其家，至食新罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1275653_comment'></div>凡为户六百八十有五，分处合肥、故黄适等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1275653_comment'></div>而合肥赢故黄三户，户授二室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1275653_comment'></div>受田之丁，合肥八百一十有五，故黄六百一十有四。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1275653_comment'></div>会其钱若米之费，财二万缗、六千石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1275653_comment'></div>流民已为大姓有者，仍隶其主户就抚之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1275653_comment'></div>并边归正者，振业之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1275653_comment'></div>合三千八百馀户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1275653_comment'></div>始公以乾道七年十二月至淮西，反命以明年之夏，计道里往来与察边郡、检麦田之属，专于田事者仅数月，垦筑、冶铸、斲削，皆受成于公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1275653_comment'></div>赋役省而功坚，度可支数十年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1275653_comment'></div>位置向背，经纬条达，民生所须，不外索而足，淮人谓耳目所未睹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1275653_comment'></div>公曰：「吾非为今日利也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1275653_comment'></div>治合肥之圩，边有警，因以断栅江，保巢湖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1275653_comment'></div>故黄，实古邾城，地直蔡冲，诸庄益辑，则西道有屏蔽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1275653_comment'></div>其措意深远矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1275653_comment'></div>光守宋端友自上招集北归户一百十七，公至固始，验新民止五户，馀皆保塞数年，端友混新旧户为一，籍以幸赏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1275653_comment'></div>异时有以善马涉淮者，杀而要夺之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1275653_comment'></div>公亟举奏端友有挟，人谓章且不下，语闻，上感悟，属廷尉治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1275653_comment'></div>方穷竟，端友以忧死，习为媒者皆竦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1275653_comment'></div>而虞丞相始不乐公矣，故为多端縻公，以缓其归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1275653_comment'></div>或迎说公：「见上，盍少自绌？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1275653_comment'></div>毋与当路者忤」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1275653_comment'></div>公曰：「上遣我视边，固欲得利害之实」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1275653_comment'></div>卒极陈之，且曰：「臣根本其敝，不计而谩为，而后外以卤莽报；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1275653_comment'></div>不思而出令，而后外以难行寝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1275653_comment'></div>号为责实，未免徇名，则趣办皆徇名之人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1275653_comment'></div>志在大功，反规小利，则迎合皆规利之辈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1275653_comment'></div>诞谩者败而不诛，谀说者察而不去，左右为欺囊橐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1275653_comment'></div>迩为援则远坚，大为间则小肆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1275653_comment'></div>其荐退人物，曾非诵言，游扬中伤，乃自不意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1275653_comment'></div>齐威之霸，不在阿、即墨之断，而在毁誉者之刑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1275653_comment'></div>臣观近政，非无阿、即墨之断，奈何毁誉之人自若」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1275653_comment'></div>上欣然开纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1275653_comment'></div>公复进曰：「外事无足道，咎根不除，抑臣深忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1275653_comment'></div>左右近侍，阴挤正士而阳浮称道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1275653_comment'></div>陛下诚圣明，傥因貌言，万一垂听，臣恐石显、王凤、郑注之智中也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1275653_comment'></div>又曰：「好名特为臣子学问之累。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1275653_comment'></div>人主为社稷计，唯恐士不好名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1275653_comment'></div>诚人人好名畏义，何乡不立」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1275653_comment'></div>上是之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1275653_comment'></div>隆兴以来，经理两淮受遣者且数十辈，发御府金缯，听施置自便阅十年，鲜有当上意者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1275653_comment'></div>及公使事有绪，恨得公晚，道进官二等，除大理正，侧席迟其至，顾问䌷绎，奏请论荐，皆报可，闻者意公且用矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1275653_comment'></div>居七日，出守湖州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1275653_comment'></div>入辞，语益恳到，上慰勉遣焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1275653_comment'></div>公既数摩切左右，而湖多权贵人田宅，与相加尤数，公平心问理如何，不为变，益害公，合力撼摇，上记其忠，独保持之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1275653_comment'></div>始至，书狱多入死，讯其由，则弃市者民间或窃祠之，名「伤神」，恶少遂轻相雠杀不顾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1275653_comment'></div>公亟屏绝，死狱大减，条境内淫祠，次第除撤，会去郡而辍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1275653_comment'></div>土俗小民悍强，甚者数十人为朋，私为约无得输主户租，前为政者或纵臾之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1275653_comment'></div>公叹曰：「郡国幸无事，而鼠辈颉颃已尔，缓急之际将何若」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1275653_comment'></div>取其首恶，黥窜远方，民始知有奴主之分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1275653_comment'></div>初陈亨伯割诸道留州钱输大农，号经制，翁彦国复附以总制，嗜进者竞裒歛以应赏格，已而遂定其多数为岁额。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1275653_comment'></div>州用日削而供亿稍饩，校军兴前五六倍，吏骪法擿抉无遗笔，犹廪廪不能给。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1275653_comment'></div>至是户部令提点刑狱司以历付场务，一钱已上皆分隶经总制如式。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1275653_comment'></div>诸郡被符，搏手无策，相顾莫敢先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1275653_comment'></div>公独言于朝曰：「自经总制立额，州郡凿空以取盈，虽有奉法吏思宽弛而不得骋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1275653_comment'></div>若复隶额外征，掇其强半郡调度，顾安所取？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1275653_comment'></div>殆复为它谬巧重取之民，民何以胜」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1275653_comment'></div>户部镌谯愈急，公争之愈强，台谏亦交疏助公，遂收前令不布。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1275653_comment'></div>凡可以纾民力者，知无不言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1275653_comment'></div>如论和籴贾贱，请更平直；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1275653_comment'></div>徙汰军宽州；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1275653_comment'></div>添差隶郡者，止今见员，后勿遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1275653_comment'></div>函封相继，多格于有司，则以病谒祠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1275653_comment'></div>朝廷惜之，却其请至八九，知不可夺，改知常州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1275653_comment'></div>未上，以乾道七年九月戊申卒于家，年四十，官止奉议郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1275653_comment'></div>娶孙氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1275653_comment'></div>子法，补太学生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1275653_comment'></div>公之没，其友张淳治丧，程以古礼，公配孙夫人能顺听不违，里中观法焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1275653_comment'></div>十二月壬申，葬于永嘉县吹台乡慈湖之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1275653_comment'></div>自周季绝学，古先制作之原晦而不章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1275653_comment'></div>若董仲舒名田，诸葛亮治军，王通河汾之讲论，千有馀年，端倪盖时一见也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1275653_comment'></div>国朝程颢氏、程颐氏、张载氏，相与发挥之，于是本原精粗，统纪大备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_172_1275653_comment'></div>门人高弟，既尽晚出者，或骛于空无，不足以涉事耦变，识者忧之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1275653_comment'></div>公之学既有所授，博揽精思几二十年，百氏群籍、山经地志、断章阙简，研索不遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_174_1275653_comment'></div>过故墟废垄，环步移日，以验其迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_175_1275653_comment'></div>参绎融液，左右逢原，凡疆里、卒乘、封国、行河，久远难分明，一经公讲画，枝叶扶疏，缕贯脉连，于经无不合，于事无不可行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_176_1275653_comment'></div>涖官随广狭，默寓之于簿领期会之间，其所部吏曹，经时而不知公为儒者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_177_1275653_comment'></div>平生所际，文武之职不同，未尝为町畦崖岸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_178_1275653_comment'></div>而去就从违之际，守义不可夺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_179_1275653_comment'></div>言兵变化若神，而在朝每以不可轻试为主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_180_1275653_comment'></div>所见疏快轩豁，潜察之，自律严饬，虽倥偬，札翰正楷，无一惰笔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_181_1275653_comment'></div>少年豪举，既知学，销落，不留省其私，泊如也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_182_1275653_comment'></div>其为人平实质确，本于简易，行于敬恕，而坚志强力，又足以充践之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_183_1275653_comment'></div>善类方共倚属公，而公则死矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_184_1275653_comment'></div>《诗》、《易》、《春秋》《、中庸》、《大学》、《论语》，皆有训义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_185_1275653_comment'></div>他所论著若《九州图志》之属，稿方立而未究也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_186_1275653_comment'></div>岁在壬午，先君子守黄，公夹江为令，归以公所为语某，固已矍然自失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_187_1275653_comment'></div>后十载，乃识公于朝，一见莫逆如故交。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_188_1275653_comment'></div>其葬也，张淳既志其圹沄，复请诗以揭之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_189_1275653_comment'></div>丧不能文，今既免丧不死矣，其可不为公一言乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_190_1275653_comment'></div>词曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_191_1275653'>坠绪茫茫，独求诸野。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_191_1275653_comment'></div>有涤其源，昼夜不舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_192_1275653_comment'></div>繄道之穷，维其尚口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_193_1275653_comment'></div>不耀其章，而躬自厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_194_1275653_comment'></div>出孚于长，于长于君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_195_1275653_comment'></div>□□施之，乃没元身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_196_1275653_comment'></div>故吴之迹，故邾之遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_197_1275653_comment'></div>既堙既平，其尚有稽。</div><div id='poem_sentence_198_1275653_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1173&endYear=1173')">1173年7月</a>　致书陈亮，论登高当自下发足。作品：《与陈同甫书》八。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷十。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1173&endYear=1173')">1173年7月</a>　致书陈亮。作品：《与陈同甫书》五。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷十。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1173&endYear=1173')">1173年7月</a>　致书陈亮论学。鼓励陈亮刊《易传》，重议编史及《春秋》等事。作品：《与陈同甫书》六。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷十。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1173&endYear=1173')">1173年7月</a>　长子朱塾前来就读。为朱塾择友，规定课程。作品：《与朱侍讲》二十二。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷七。）</span><div id='poem_1275255' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275255' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275255?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与朱侍讲元晦书<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其五十五 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1173年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275255")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275255_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275255'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275255'>丐祠虽未惬雅志，然诸公不欲贤者家食，虽未必由衷，然亦善意也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275255_comment'></div>但有畏不能容贤者之谤，比之全不分皂白者亦有间矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275255_comment'></div>张荆州病中请祠，亦有苦劝当途令从其请者，亦以向来之嫌，畏人议论不能容之，遂坚不肯从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275255_comment'></div>但作帅与小军垒不同，但须内外至诚相与，首尾相应，乃不误事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275255_comment'></div>既非心相与，则自有首尾衡决处，如来教数条皆是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275255_comment'></div>符节在身，不得擅去，此所以忧而至于病，病而至于死，每诵量而后入，不入而后量之语，为之泫然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275255_comment'></div>至于南康地既非要害，民又非浩穰，虽事之不如人意处固多，然无旦夕立至之忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275255_comment'></div>若且耐烦忍垢，拊摩疲民，苟稍成头绪，子重继之，必能遵守，使一方之民小小休息，亦不为无补也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275255_comment'></div>今去终更才半年馀耳，交印后身便自由，惟吾志所欲，无不可者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275255_comment'></div>或未终更，别有除改，半道引疾而归，亦甚省力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275255_comment'></div>陆子寿前日经过，留此二十馀日，幡然以鹅湖所见为非，甚欲著实看书讲论，心平气下，相识中甚难得也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275255_comment'></div>近因荆州之赴，深思渠学识分晓周正如此，而从游之士，往往不得力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275255_comment'></div>记得往年相聚时，虽未能尽领解渠说话，然觉得大段有益，不知其它从游者何故乃如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275255_comment'></div>盖五十丈不能察人情虚实，必如某之专愚毋它，其教诲乃有所施耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275255_comment'></div>若胸中多端者，虽朝夕相处，未必能有益也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275255_comment'></div>《中庸》论尽己之性，又继之以尽人之性，尽物之性，工夫无穷如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275255_comment'></div>此岂追往事，亦要高明深勉之耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1275255_comment'></div>五十丈所作《濂溪祠堂记》，告妆褫一本送示，欲挂壁间观省耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1275255_comment'></div>亲旧间多相勉撤去书册，固知此理，但旧所偏嗜，未能顿去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1275255_comment'></div>近亦十减五六矣，如时文却不曾与人看。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1275255_comment'></div>受之在此作课，亦只是舍弟辈为之点检也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1275255_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1173&endYear=1173')">1173年7月</a>　刊印《横渠集》。欲刊《说文》而苦无善本。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1173&endYear=1173')">1173年7月</a>　刻朱熹藏《程氏易传》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1173&endYear=1173')">1173年8月</a>　刘清之和陆九龄来访。吕祖谦与朱熹书，称道陆九龄。作品：《与朱侍讲》二。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷八。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1173&endYear=1173')">1173年8月</a>　因刊《横渠集》，遣人往汪应辰处求《横渠集》详本。作品：《与汪端明》十。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷七。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1173&endYear=1173')">1173年9月</a>　陈亮《论事录》、《欧阳文忠公文粹》成，请吕祖谦评议。吕祖谦字斟句酌，强调为学当本末并举。作品：《与陈同甫书》四。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷十。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1173&endYear=1173')">1173年9月</a>　命潘景宪为陈亮校《易传》。陈亮以所撰《伊洛正源》来议，吕祖谦有所批评。作品：《与陈同甫》五。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷十。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1173&endYear=1173')">1173年10月</a>　陆九龄再访吕祖谦，与同观《实录》，有《实录节》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1173&endYear=1173')">1173年10月</a>　作《戒谕沿边修武备诏》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史外集》卷三。）</span><div id='poem_1275117' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275117' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275117?labeling=true' target='_blank'>戒谕沿边修武备诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1173年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275117")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275117_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275117'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275117'>朕揽前世治边之策，责大指而削小文，略近利而规后效，长辔远驭，与豪杰之士共期于绳墨之外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275117_comment'></div>肆其封疆之臣，亦越拘挛之见，以为公家忠计，用能辟地却敌，显有丕功，朕甚嘉之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275117_comment'></div>朕不能远德，边虞未宁，重劳士大夫，藐然甚惭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275117_comment'></div>乃者临遣大臣，尽护群帅，夙夜为守圉计，至熟悉也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275117_comment'></div>而障塞破坏，亭候堙绝，吏气伤沮，武备衰减，便文自营，毛举细事以塞责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275117_comment'></div>或玩寇迁延，宿兵无用之地，或侵欺新附，使边骚然不安；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275117_comment'></div>或屯聚解弛，莫能相壹；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275117_comment'></div>或创艾战斗，选耎退缩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275117_comment'></div>意者跅𧿇之士，束于刀笔吏而不得骋欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275117_comment'></div>将群国之吏或不足亢一方之任欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275117_comment'></div>抑货赂上流，吏卒失职，下亡所信欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275117_comment'></div>今朕播告之修，不匿厥指。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275117_comment'></div>维尔将帅牧守，其厉锋锷，展腹心，赋车籍马必戒，挽运奉饟必丰，器械必犀利，烽燧必精明，毋拘常守，以失事机之会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275117_comment'></div>功多有厚赏，不迪有显戮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275117_comment'></div>尚克钦承，以宽朕北顾之虑，则予汝嘉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1275117_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1173&endYear=1173')">1173年11月</a>　吕祖谦以程文教朱塾。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1173&endYear=1173')">1173年12月</a>　作书与朱熹，允为《伊洛渊源录》作序，并允助朱熹向汪应辰及浙东诸人借书、搜罗事迹。索《祭礼》作品：《与朱侍讲》三。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史外集》卷八。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1173&endYear=1173')">1173年12月</a>　为朱熹刊《程氏易传》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1173&endYear=1173')">1173年12月</a>　郭养正前来就学。作品：《与郭养正》二。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史外集》卷五。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1173&endYear=1173')">1173年冬</a>　选古文四十篇示学者作文途径。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1173&endYear=1173')">1173年</a>　诸生复集，为讲《尚书》。有《癸巳手笔》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1173&endYear=1173')">1173年</a>　作学规《乾道九年直日须知》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷五《家范五·学规》）</span><div id='poem_1275624' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275624' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275624?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乾道九年直日须知</a><span class='authorDate'>（1173年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275624")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275624_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275624'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275624'>凡遇诸斋申到合吊慰人，直日即点检。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275624_comment'></div>如系今年预课人，丁父母忧，预课满百日者，据人数均敛钱拾伍贯文省，未满百日者，均敛钱十贯文省。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275624_comment'></div>城居人问受慰日分，随敛钱告报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275624_comment'></div>令诸斋某日早各备名纸，并集丽泽堂，并禀堂上，差掌仪二人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275624_comment'></div>至受慰日早，集众会丽泽堂，分两序立，直日备箱收名纸，次掌仪请齿长人率众，以齿序行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275624_comment'></div>其在道笑语諠哗，仰总直日及诸斋直日申举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275624_comment'></div>至所吊慰家，直日通名纸讫，齿长人率众入门序立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275624_comment'></div>立定，掌仪赞，云在位者皆再拜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275624_comment'></div>既拜，掌仪引齿长人诣灵位前三上香，诸齿长人跪，三奠酒<span class='inlineComment2'>（掌仪兼执尊酌酒。）</span>，俛伏，兴<span class='inlineComment2'>（后项致祭者掌仪跪，读祭文毕。）</span>，复位，立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275624_comment'></div>掌仪赞，云在位者皆再拜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275624_comment'></div>既拜，赞云：「移位少东，再拜」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275624_comment'></div>尉拜讫，齿长者一人前致慰辞毕，众皆揖，以序出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275624_comment'></div>郊居人即录慰书格式，同敛钱告报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275624_comment'></div>令诸斋各具慰书同吊祭人，限某日纳<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>，候书足，差人专往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275624_comment'></div>如系在籍今年不预课人，城居者，问受慰日分，告报诸斋各差齿长一人往慰；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275624_comment'></div>郊居，录慰书格式，告报诸斋限某日纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275624_comment'></div>慰书类聚，令本斋寻便附往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1275624_comment'></div>两项并吊而不赙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1275624_comment'></div>其身故者如系今年预课人，并如丁父母忧例，仍别敛祭钱壹贯文足，差人作祭文一通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1275624_comment'></div>如系在籍今年不预课人，吊而不赙，止敛祭钱壹贯文足，亦差人作祭文一通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1275624_comment'></div>城居斋长并往吊慰如前式，郊居者别具慰书格式，慰其父兄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1275624_comment'></div>告报限某日各写慰书，同祭，赙纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1275624_comment'></div>今年预课者，专差人往；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1275624_comment'></div>不预课者，令本斋附往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1275624_comment'></div>其遭祖、父母、亲兄弟丧，今年预课人城居者，诸斋各差齿长一人往慰，郊居人告报本斋，一面发书往慰。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1275624_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1275624'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_13_1275624_0'>⑴ 仍量吊慰道里远近差人，往回之费，计算均敛。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1275624_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1174&endYear=1174')">1174年1月</a>　以韩元吉守婺故，遣散诸生专意读书。始编《读诗记》。阅胡安国《春秋左氏传》，盛赞其揭出《礼运》“天下为公”意思。有标抹本。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1174&endYear=1174')">1174年2月</a>　入金柱山读诸子、《春秋》、《资治通鉴》并标抹。有答潘景宪书。作品：《答潘叔度》十四。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷十。）</span>《答潘叔度》十五。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷十。）</span>《答潘叔度》十六。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷十。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1174&endYear=1174')">1174年2月</a>　义乌有刊刻《精义》者与朱熹冲突，朱熹函请吕祖谦邀官介入以制止。吕祖谦复朱熹书，劝导勿以官司压人，讲学正须于日用间就事上商量。作品：《与朱侍讲》十八。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷七。）</span><div id='poem_1275206' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275206' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275206?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与朱侍讲元晦书<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其六 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1174年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275206")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275206_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275206'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275206'>某官下粗遣，学浅力薄，视职业日增愧负。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275206_comment'></div>虽不敢苟简自恕，然殊未能大有所釐正耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275206_comment'></div>至于区区课试之末，则固未尝深较也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275206_comment'></div>张丈邻墙，日夕相过讲论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275206_comment'></div>士子有志于此者，亦有一二辈，切摩工夫，粗不歇灭断续。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275206_comment'></div>又时阅来诲，策厉警省者殊多，但书不尽意，终不若侍坐隅、难疑答问为亲切耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275206_comment'></div>邪说诐行，辞而辟之，诚今日任此道者之责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275206_comment'></div>窃尝谓异端之不息，由正学之不明，此盛彼衰，互相消长，莫若尽力于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275206_comment'></div>此道光明盛大，则彼之消铄无日矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275206_comment'></div>孟子所谓「吾为此惧，闲先圣之道」，旧说以闲为闲习，意味甚长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275206_comment'></div>杨、墨肆行，政以吾道之衰耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275206_comment'></div>孟子所以不求之它，而以闲习吾先圣之道为急先务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275206_comment'></div>而淫辞诐行之放，则固自有次第也，不知吾丈以为如何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275206_comment'></div>所以为此说者，非欲含糊纵释，黑白不辨，但恐专意外攘，而内修处工夫或少耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275206_comment'></div>向来所论智仁勇，终恐难分轻重，盖三者天下之达德，通圣、贤、常人而言之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275206_comment'></div>在圣人则智也仁也勇也，皆生知安行也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275206_comment'></div>在贤人则智也仁也勇也，皆学知利行也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1275206_comment'></div>在常人则智也仁也勇也，皆困知勉行也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1275206_comment'></div>恐难指定智为学知利行，勇为困知勉行，龟山之说，终不免有疑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1275206_comment'></div>周子「仁义中正主静」之说，前书所言「仁义中正」皆主乎此，非谓中正仁义皆静之用而别有块然之静也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1275206_comment'></div>人生而静，天之性也，乃中正仁义之体，而万物之一源也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1275206_comment'></div>中则无不正矣，必并言之曰中、正、仁，则无不义矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1275206_comment'></div>必并言之曰仁、义，亦犹元可以包四德，而与亨、利、贞俱列；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1275206_comment'></div>仁可以包四端，而与义、礼、智同称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1275206_comment'></div>此所谓合之不浑，离之不散者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1275206_comment'></div>昨所云文理密察，盖亦如来谕，初非以为秘密之密，观察之察也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1275206_comment'></div>谓如《易传》中以形体谓之天，以主宰谓之帝，以功用谓之鬼神，以妙用谓之神，以性情谓之乾等语，铢分粒剖，各有攸当而未尝有割裂杌󷽥之病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1275206_comment'></div>析理精微如此，乃可谓之文理密察耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1275206_comment'></div>阴阳仁义之说，鄙意未达，终觉未安，当更潜思玩味，续得求教也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1275206_comment'></div>《中庸》「不可能」、「道不远人」两章，反覆思之，龟山之说诚为奇险，非子思本指。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1275206_comment'></div>向日不觉其非者，政缘为程文时，考观新说，馀习时有在者故耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1275206_comment'></div>所与诸生讲说《左氏》，语意伤巧，病源亦在是，自此当力扫除也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1275206_comment'></div>婺本《易传》，纳三本去，不敢加装治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1275206_comment'></div>误字皆已改，但卦画粗细、行数疏密之类，不能如人意悉釐正耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1275206_comment'></div>《遗书》建本未到，已用去冬所寄本刊板，故其间一两段更易次序处，姑仍其旧，馀皆以建本为正，闻旦夕亦毕工矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1275206_comment'></div>《二程先生集》，款曲亦当令婺人刊之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1275206_comment'></div>然新添伊川二子所为序引，殊无家风，恐适足为先生之累，欲削去之，更望一报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1275206_comment'></div>见所寄张丈所论时事，一一精当，不胜叹服，此间所共讲者亦十八九同也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1275206_comment'></div>知言往在严陵时，与张丈讲论亦尝疏出可疑者数十条，今观来示，其半亦相类，见与张丈参阅，续当咨请也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1275206_comment'></div>其馀已见于张丈书者，更不重出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1275206_comment'></div>相去之远，惟祈因便时赐教督，不惜语言，痛加砭治，乃所愿望。</div><div id='poem_sentence_40_1275206_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1174&endYear=1174')">1174年2月</a>　致书汪应辰求取伊洛事迹，并索朱熹所赠《祭仪》作品：《与汪端明》十一。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷七。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1174&endYear=1174')">1174年2月</a>　致书朱熹，论当因材施教。作品：《与朱侍讲》四。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷八。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1174&endYear=1174')">1174年2月</a>　致书郭养正论修养之道，敦促其实下工夫。作品：《与郭养正》二。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史外集》卷五。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1174&endYear=1174')">1174年2月</a>　为举子选古文在建宁刊行。作品：《与朱侍讲》六。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷八。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1174&endYear=1174')">1174年3月</a>　至明招山。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1174&endYear=1174')">1174年3月</a>　《横渠集》刊出。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1174&endYear=1174')">1174年3月</a>　收到汪应辰转寄朱熹《祭仪》，复书汪应辰讨论《祭仪》作品：《与汪端明》十二。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷七。）</span><div id='poem_1275186' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275186' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275186?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与汪端明圣锡书<span class='inlineComment2'>（一六　淳熙元年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1165年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275186")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275186_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275186'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275186'>上饶之居，有定议否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275186_comment'></div>朱元晦约来春至婺，因为天台、雁荡之游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275186_comment'></div>或谓渠久不出，今虽寻山，然适当一二公登用之时，自远而近，恐不察者或以为疑，此诚过虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275186_comment'></div>告试为斟酌，倘渠出果有嫌，则某却当入闽访之，往还必皆得款侍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275186_comment'></div>若元晦可出，亦须送之至衢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275186_comment'></div>度侍见之期，要不出三两月间，预以为慰。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1275186_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1174&endYear=1174')">1174年3月</a>　过访陈亮。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1174&endYear=1174')">1174年春</a>　遣人至长沙与张栻讲论学术，言及朱熹之出处问题。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1174&endYear=1174')">1174年4月</a>　居明招山。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='dc62d8da1a944977b23a2334a6466d01_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("dc62d8da1a944977b23a2334a6466d01");'><span id='dc62d8da1a944977b23a2334a6466d01_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1174&endYear=1174')">1174年</a>，38岁</div><div id='dc62d8da1a944977b23a2334a6466d01' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1174&endYear=1174')">1174年6月1日</a>　自衢州归，与陆九渊论学多日。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1174&endYear=1174')">1174年6月</a>　与汪应辰书，荐陆九渊。并寄《善言录》、《横渠录》、尹焞《论语跋》等。索取程颐资料，《通鉴类编》作品：《与汪端明》十四。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷七。）</span><div id='poem_1275172' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275172' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275172?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与汪端明圣锡书<span class='inlineComment2'>（二　乾道元年正月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1174年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275172")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275172_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275172'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275172'>某区区之迹，昨侍行归自黄冈，留会稽外祖处数月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275172_comment'></div>仲冬复过浙西，挈提干家叔一房归婺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275172_comment'></div>今还舍馀六旬矣，侍下无它事，得以专意书册。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275172_comment'></div>但冥顽之质，独学寡陋，殊无所发明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275172_comment'></div>瞻望函丈，在天一涯，无从侧听謦欬，下情但深企仰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275172_comment'></div>和议甫定，目前遂可奠枕，然所当虑者，政在此而不在彼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275172_comment'></div>开府方初，窃想威惠并举，以大填拊一方之民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275172_comment'></div>惟念蜀远在万里，外有邻敌，旁有师屯，下有五十四郡之众，屈信呼吸，安危系焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275172_comment'></div>敢祈覃精筹度，博稽众谋，以宽西顾之虑，幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275172_comment'></div>国博丈去就之节，凛然可以为吾道贺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275172_comment'></div>今兹荐膺召命，闻既至都下，计已有除擢矣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1275172_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1174&endYear=1174')">1174年6月</a>　复陈亮来书。作品：《与陈同甫》二十四。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷十。）</span><div id='poem_1275332' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275332' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275332?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与陈同甫书<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其十一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1174年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275332")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275332_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275332'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275332'>近悤悤奉答，未究所欲言者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275332_comment'></div>人至，荐拜手字，欣审秋暑犹剧，孝履宁谧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275332_comment'></div>某还舍近半月，适此酷暑，疲损犹未甚苏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275332_comment'></div>此月二十五日，刘国华葬，须往泉溪会之，因留明招数日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275332_comment'></div>闻月交为入城之行，若路过内白，幸遣一介至明招问某所止，庶不参差也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275332_comment'></div>《三国纪年》序引及诸赞，累日已详看，用意高深处，亦或得其一二，但大纲体制犹有未晓处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275332_comment'></div>《序》云：「魏于是乎有书，吴、蜀合而附之《魏书」》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275332_comment'></div>又云：「魏终不足以正天下，于是为《三国纪年」》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275332_comment'></div>终焉不知《魏书》与《纪年》是一书，为复两书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275332_comment'></div>观三国诸君赞，却似迁、固史法，每君为纪而参赞于后者，而《三国纪年》冠以甲子，而并列魏、蜀、吴，则又似合三国为一者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275332_comment'></div>所谓魏武以下诸赞，必不可参于此<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>，不知系于何处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275332_comment'></div>岂《三国纪年》之外，复叙每君之本末而系以赞耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275332_comment'></div>此皆未晓之大者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275332_comment'></div>《魏武赞》述来历甚当<span class='inlineComment2'>（但其末「舜、禹之事」两语未晓。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275332_comment'></div>魏文帝两赞深味词意，予夺甚有味<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275332_comment'></div>《昭烈赞》论其君臣反复于天意人事之际，所谓妙体本心，但费诗之议，却似不达时变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275332_comment'></div>汉统既绝，昭烈安得不承之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1275332_comment'></div>非高祖时比也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1275332_comment'></div>后主盖亦甚庸，所以安之不疑者，乃诸葛公工夫耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1275332_comment'></div>《武侯赞》论「以国政归丞相」，甚善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1275332_comment'></div>但谓汉侍中、中书令、尚书令皆宦者为之者，考之《汉书》，亦不皆如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1275332_comment'></div>篇末「王者之作，天犹以为未疏哉」，感慨之意甚长，但不若《后主赞》所谓「天命果可畏」辞严而义正也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1275332_comment'></div>《武烈赞》论汉末守文之弊，及启桓、王之翱翔，甚妙甚妙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1275332_comment'></div>下三赞亦然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1275332_comment'></div>鄙意窃谓吴四赞尤能尽其规摹之所止，殆无遗憾也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1275332_comment'></div>《庞统赞》论兼弱之义，甚正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1275332_comment'></div>《关羽赞》亦稳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1275332_comment'></div>但来教谓「司马子长虽高，不欲学」，而诸赞命意及笔势往往似之，何耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1275332_comment'></div>因便并望见教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1275332_comment'></div>朱元晦工夫，亦谓大概如此耳。</div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1275332_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1275332'><span class='label'>按：</span>《东莱吕太史别集》卷一○。又见邓广铭点校《陈亮集》增订本卷一六。<br /><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_10_1275332_0'>⑴ 既并列三国之年，必是通书三国事，今每君为赞，必知不系于此后。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_14_1275332_0'>⑵ 但《文帝赞》意颇晦，又文帝三驾伐吴，谓「中国庶几息肩」，亦未协。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1275332_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1174&endYear=1174')">1174年6月23日</a>　得祠主管台州崇道观。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1174&endYear=1174')">1174年6月</a>　应门人张垓之请，为其父张协作墓铭。作品：《大梁张君墓志铭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷十一。）</span><div id='poem_1275655' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275655' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275655?labeling=true' target='_blank'>大梁张君墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（淳熙元年六月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275655")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275655_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275655'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275655'>靖康之难，中原衣冠屑播荡析之馀，其变何可胜道？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275655_comment'></div>主乡论者，要当哀其不幸而体其不得已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275655_comment'></div>乃若张君者，始虽失业，终自封殖，以芘其宗，则于可哀之中又有可书者焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275655_comment'></div>君讳协，字邦和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275655_comment'></div>自其远祖谏议大夫惟则，繇泽州高平徙名数于京师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275655_comment'></div>祖复古，通议大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275655_comment'></div>父圭，朝请郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275655_comment'></div>母刘氏，封安人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275655_comment'></div>君生而丧其父，总角，崎岖兵间，又丧其母，已能悉力敛藏严饬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275655_comment'></div>久益困，寄食姻戚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275655_comment'></div>忽感愤，不持一钱，掉臂出门，周旋四方，頫拾卬取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275655_comment'></div>数航海历交阯、勃泥诸国，其货日凑，则曰：「吾向也不难自屈，惧填沟壑，陨先人宗祀耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275655_comment'></div>今可止矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275655_comment'></div>于是买田婺州郭外，教其子以学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275655_comment'></div>同宗有漂泊江浙者，往来必周其乏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275655_comment'></div>女无归者，或为资遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275655_comment'></div>故人以穷归君，忻然发橐，无纤啬态，北客多称之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1275655_comment'></div>异时公卿家子肤理丰腴，以裘马自喜，及失倚离势，大不能致人，小不能致于人，虽欲名一技以活身，枵然无有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1275655_comment'></div>以君视之，不既贤矣乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1275655_comment'></div>君晚节浮湛里闾，吐纳自养，暇则为人道夷夏土风物产、涛波岛溆、鱼龙雄奇之变，衮衮可听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1275655_comment'></div>蚤岁径赣吉境上，天大雪失道，夜投何人家，栋宇闳丽，如王侯第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1275655_comment'></div>卧未安，闻牖外嘈嘈语且泣，杂五方之声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1275655_comment'></div>起窥之，则数十女子群处一室，累然若囚系。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1275655_comment'></div>旦私问于邻，邻人吐舌曰：「君何从见耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1275655_comment'></div>主人翁岁岁剽掠子女，鬻之远郡，累赀且钜万矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1275655_comment'></div>亟闭口勿语，且并祸我」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1275655_comment'></div>君上谒请见，徐以利害祸福晓譬之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1275655_comment'></div>初愕不答，久乃领解。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1275655_comment'></div>比复过其门，有指以语君者曰：「是翁去岁遇异人，遂尽舍故业，所掠皆护致付其父母，畏事自守，一乡以安」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1275655_comment'></div>叹咤不休，不知乃君也，君亦不自言而去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1275655_comment'></div>以乾道九年十月九日终于家，年五十五。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1275655_comment'></div>淳熙元年六月庚申，葬于金华县赤松乡糁岭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1275655_comment'></div>娶董氏，生三子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1275655_comment'></div>长垓，承信郎，次蚤夭，次未名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1275655_comment'></div>六女，长适进士董滨老，次适右迪功郎阎焘，以嫠归，馀未行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1275655_comment'></div>垓尝从予游，于君之葬，以铭来请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1275655_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_36_1275655'>朔氛涨天兮邑屋墟，海涛沃日兮万货区。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1275655_comment'></div>巫阳下招兮归其居，出入阡陌兮僮骑都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1275655_comment'></div>岁时伏腊兮道往初，北幕南帆兮来坐隅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1275655_comment'></div>噫，后之人兮思拮据，蚤夜敬戒兮持门闾。</div><div id='poem_sentence_39_1275655_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1174&endYear=1174')">1174年7月</a>　函候汪应辰，催取《伊川录》、《通鉴类编》作品：《与汪端明》十五。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷七。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1174&endYear=1174')">1174年7月</a>　复陈亮来书。作品：《与陈同甫》二十五。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷十。）</span><div id='poem_1275332' class='_poem'><div
