id='poem_sentence_15_1275332_comment'></div>汉统既绝，昭烈安得不承之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1275332_comment'></div>非高祖时比也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1275332_comment'></div>后主盖亦甚庸，所以安之不疑者，乃诸葛公工夫耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1275332_comment'></div>《武侯赞》论「以国政归丞相」，甚善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1275332_comment'></div>但谓汉侍中、中书令、尚书令皆宦者为之者，考之《汉书》，亦不皆如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1275332_comment'></div>篇末「王者之作，天犹以为未疏哉」，感慨之意甚长，但不若《后主赞》所谓「天命果可畏」辞严而义正也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1275332_comment'></div>《武烈赞》论汉末守文之弊，及启桓、王之翱翔，甚妙甚妙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1275332_comment'></div>下三赞亦然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1275332_comment'></div>鄙意窃谓吴四赞尤能尽其规摹之所止，殆无遗憾也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1275332_comment'></div>《庞统赞》论兼弱之义，甚正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1275332_comment'></div>《关羽赞》亦稳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1275332_comment'></div>但来教谓「司马子长虽高，不欲学」，而诸赞命意及笔势往往似之，何耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1275332_comment'></div>因便并望见教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1275332_comment'></div>朱元晦工夫，亦谓大概如此耳。</div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1275332_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1275332'><span class='label'>按：</span>《东莱吕太史别集》卷一○。又见邓广铭点校《陈亮集》增订本卷一六。<br /><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_10_1275332_0'>⑴ 既并列三国之年，必是通书三国事，今每君为赞，必知不系于此后。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_14_1275332_0'>⑵ 但《文帝赞》意颇晦，又文帝三驾伐吴，谓「中国庶几息肩」，亦未协。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1275332_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1174&endYear=1174')">1174年7月</a>　致书陈亮论学。评议陈亮《策问》、《章侍郎行状》文气高远疏宕而议论不合。作品：《与陈同甫》一。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史外集》卷五。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1174&endYear=1174')">1174年7月</a>　遣潘景宪送朱塾归闽。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1174&endYear=1174')">1174年8月28日</a>　自金华赴绍兴省外祖母，潘景宪偕行。作《入越录》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷十五。）</span><div id='poem_1275612' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275612' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275612?labeling=true' target='_blank'>入越录</a><span class='authorDate'>（淳熙元年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275612")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275612_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275612'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275612'>淳熙元年八月二十八日，自金华与潘叔度为会稽之游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275612_comment'></div>辰后出旌孝门，五里，至关头，南折入会稽路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275612_comment'></div>二里，桐树岭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275612_comment'></div>八里，东藕塘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275612_comment'></div>城东陂塘此为大，溉田甚博。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275612_comment'></div>它时夏秋之交辄涸，今岁雨泽以时，田不卬水，秋深犹㳽漫也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275612_comment'></div>十五里，含香，民居颇成聚落。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275612_comment'></div>道旁野塘，木芙蓉初发，映水殊有思致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275612_comment'></div>十里，义井。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275612_comment'></div>五里，上下仓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275612_comment'></div>十里，孝顺镇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275612_comment'></div>十里，自驿路北折入香山路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275612_comment'></div>五里，宿杭慈潘氏庄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275612_comment'></div>凡行七十里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275612_comment'></div>是日凝阴不开，风袭人已有力，始御裌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275612_comment'></div>四山云气滃然，冈峦出没。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275612_comment'></div>申后微雨，夜遂大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1275612_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_1275612'>二十九日早，冒雨行二里，小凤林寺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1275612_comment'></div>涉溪，屈曲稻塍间，泥淖没屦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1275612_comment'></div>五里，苦山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1275612_comment'></div>二十里，梅口，邸舍蠲洁胜官道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1275612_comment'></div>盖行贾避义乌市征，往往出此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1275612_comment'></div>十五里，香山，林壑稍邃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1275612_comment'></div>八里，下稠岩景德寺，寺屋可百年，绘事皆朴质。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1275612_comment'></div>饭于小轩，方池丛竹皆有趣，然稍芜矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1275612_comment'></div>七里，塘口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1275612_comment'></div>自是复出驿路，老梧离立道旁，濯濯如青玉干。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1275612_comment'></div>又二里，宿逆旅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1275612_comment'></div>凡行五十九里，晡后雨方歇，所历大氐悤悤，不能详也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1275612_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_1275612'>三十日早发，二里，石斛桥，溪流潺潺，岸旁大石如屋，桥西走浦江道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1275612_comment'></div>度桥而北十里，石牛，有楼临路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1275612_comment'></div>楼下牖户亦明敞，主人留小语，云创以待使客，非其居也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1275612_comment'></div>所谓石牛者，道下塘卧石若牛，水满不可见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1275612_comment'></div>五里，洞井，居民依小坡植鸡冠花数百本，冠距低昂，大类尸乡咒鸡翁舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1275612_comment'></div>云薄见日，已而大霁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1275612_comment'></div>十里，新界。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1275612_comment'></div>自石斛桥道出两山间，少旷土，至此山围始宽，秋稼极目，黄云蔚然，过义乌、东阳、浦江、永康四县巡检寨，婺、越界焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1275612_comment'></div>五里，邵家湾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1275612_comment'></div>观五指山，其巅石如骈拇，然近视不若远望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1275612_comment'></div>饭民家，舍后水竹可步。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1275612_comment'></div>逢驱羊行贾者数百蹄，散漫川谷，风毛沙肋，顿有汧陇秋色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1275612_comment'></div>五里，涉枫江。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1275612_comment'></div>土俗谚云：「第一扬子江，第二钱塘江，第三枫江」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1275612_comment'></div>盖甚言其水波恶，实小溪耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1275612_comment'></div>闻春夏颇湍悍，今仅至胫而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1275612_comment'></div>南岸有覆斗山，山形正方，若斗覆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1275612_comment'></div>五里，兴乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1275612_comment'></div>槿花夹道，室庐篱落皆整。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1275612_comment'></div>五里，界牌陇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1275612_comment'></div>平坡浅草，隐隐起伏，环山城立，真监牧地也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1275612_comment'></div>五里，牌头市。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1275612_comment'></div>道分为两，北道出渔浦，度浙江，入杭；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1275612_comment'></div>东道入越，轮蹄担负，东视北不能十一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1275612_comment'></div>市傍斗子岩，岩旁狮子山，首昂背偃，略类狻猊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1275612_comment'></div>五里，寒热阪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1275612_comment'></div>五里，宿砚石村。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1275612_comment'></div>凡行六十五里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1275612_comment'></div>娄愒，逆旅墙壁横斜，多市侩榜帖，大要皆尤人语，斯其所以为市道与？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1275612_comment'></div>悚然久之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1275612_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_59_1275612'>九月一日，晨雾上横陇，东嶂出日，金晕吞吐，少焉全璧径升，晃耀不可正视。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1275612_comment'></div>升数尺，韬于云，绚采光丽，因蔽益奇，非浮翳所能掩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1275612_comment'></div>露稻风叶，皆鲜鲜有生意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1275612_comment'></div>五里，里湖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1275612_comment'></div>五里，蔡家坞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1275612_comment'></div>五里，桐木岭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1275612_comment'></div>五里，诸暨县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1275612_comment'></div>入县北门，人烟犹萧疏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1275612_comment'></div>县方筑社，南垣两松，樛枝小异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1275612_comment'></div>里许，至市。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1275612_comment'></div>自县治前东折度下桥，桥屋半圮矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1275612_comment'></div>并大溪行，流甚壮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1275612_comment'></div>其源一自东阳，一自浦江，一自孝义，至街亭合流，径县城，又径萧山浮桥，入浙江。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1275612_comment'></div>县东陶朱山颇雄，自入新界，已岿然见之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1275612_comment'></div>出县东门，山益远，川原益旷，田莱多荒，盖沮洳不宜稼而然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1275612_comment'></div>五里，放生桥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1275612_comment'></div>道左女贞新叶生，黄绿间错，如行闽粤荔枝林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1275612_comment'></div>五里，马秀才店。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1275612_comment'></div>店旁小室，随事莳花草，马久罢举矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1275612_comment'></div>三里，双桥坂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1275612_comment'></div>二里，乌石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1275612_comment'></div>其南入剡，百里而近。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1275612_comment'></div>十五里，苦李桥，溪碛颇清浅，木阴扶疏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1275612_comment'></div>百馀步，入山径。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1275612_comment'></div>五里，至新店湾，复得平地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1275612_comment'></div>五里，栗桥，登栗岭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1275612_comment'></div>五里，冷水，望东岭神祠，缥缈云间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1275612_comment'></div>下坂，稻穟垂黄，际山数十里，平铺如拭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1275612_comment'></div>洋洋乎富哉，丰年之象，道中所未见也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1275612_comment'></div>五里，宿枫桥镇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1275612_comment'></div>前岁析诸暨之十乡，即镇为义安县，今年五月废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1275612_comment'></div>凡行七十里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1275612_comment'></div>薄暮，小雨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1275612_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_92_1275612'>二日，辨色发枫桥，阴风薄寒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1275612_comment'></div>十里，乾溪，溪桥榆柳数百株，有十围者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1275612_comment'></div>过桥绕山足行十里，古博岭，岭左右皆丛筱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1275612_comment'></div>五里，洪口，有别径入明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1275612_comment'></div>自枫桥而上，美竹佳树相望，近洪口，曲折循小溪，水声㶁㶁，风物渐佳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1275612_comment'></div>十里，含晖桥亭，天章寺路口也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1275612_comment'></div>遂穿松径至寺，寺盖晋王羲之兰亭，山林秀润，气象开敞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1275612_comment'></div>寺右臂长冈，达桥亭，植以松桧，疑人力所成者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1275612_comment'></div>法堂后砌筒引水激高数尺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1275612_comment'></div>堂后登阶四五十级，有照堂，两旁修竹，木樨盛开，轩槛明洁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1275612_comment'></div>又登二十馀级，至方丈，眼界颇阔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1275612_comment'></div>寺右王右军书堂，庭下皆杉竹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1275612_comment'></div>观右军遗像，出书堂，径田间百馀步，至曲水亭，对凿两小池，云是羲之鹅池、墨池。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1275612_comment'></div>曲水乃污渠，蜿蜒若蚓，必非流觞之旧，斟酌当是寺前溪，但岁久失其处耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1275612_comment'></div>由曲水亭穿小径涉溪，复出官道数里，买舟泛鉴湖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1275612_comment'></div>湖多湮为田，所存仅如溪港，然秋水平岸，菰蒲青苍，会稽、秦望、云门诸山，互相映发，城堞楼观，跨空入云，耳目应接不暇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1275612_comment'></div>入水门，过南堰，历府学天庆观，至禹迹寺门舍舟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1275612_comment'></div>外氏寓舍此寺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1275612_comment'></div>拜外祖母温国钱夫人、伯舅、叔舅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1275612_comment'></div>温国八十一矣，气貌视听才类五六十人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1275612_comment'></div>与叔度同馆于书室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1275612_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_113_1275612'>三日，游外氏园，有梅坡、月台、菊潭、𣏌菊堂、竹隐、蒲涧、橘洲，因寺废地葺治之，十六七成矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1275612_comment'></div>最胜者梅坡，绕亭皆梅，前对蒲涧、橘洲，野水湾环，岛溆掩映，如在江湖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1275612_comment'></div>而竹隐一径深幽，阶庭清閟，亦其次也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1275612_comment'></div>又过义恩师院，院与杞菊堂邻，十年前尝识之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1275612_comment'></div>午后，自园后门穿僧庵，度小桥，转三两曲至圆通寺，旧乃兴福寺子院，去岁废兴福入圆通，合二为一，扫地更新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1275612_comment'></div>面势端直，殿庑华敞，殿后犹未毕工。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1275612_comment'></div>循旧路，复穿园中归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1275612_comment'></div>园后边河，岸木成阴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1275612_comment'></div>舅氏云此即蜀桤木也，植之方数年，往时表里无障蔽，今不复见道上车马矣，杜子美所谓饱闻桤木三年，大信然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1275612_comment'></div>是日薄阴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1275612_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_123_1275612'>四日，饭已，侍伯舅，同叔度、詹季章徽之泛小舟出南堰，绕城缘鉴湖，访苏仁仲、计议师德于偏门外，皆前日初至所历也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1275612_comment'></div>啜茶道宁堂，不甚高大，位置颇稳惬，砌下瑞香两本，面皆丈馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1275612_comment'></div>仁仲，苏子容丞相孙，致仕閒居，年垂八十，道前辈事亹亹不厌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1275612_comment'></div>出旧书数种，《管子》后子容手书：「庆历乙酉家君面付」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1275612_comment'></div>犹苏河阳所藏也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1275612_comment'></div>纸尾铭款云：「惟苏氏世官学以儒，何以遗后？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1275612_comment'></div>其在此书，非学何立，非书何习？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1275612_comment'></div>终以不倦，圣贤可及」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1275612_comment'></div>其曰「书秩铭戒」者，子容所识；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1275612_comment'></div>其曰「先公铭戒」者，铭语亦同，盖子容之子所识也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1275612_comment'></div>纸背多废，笺简刺字异今制者，末云：「牒件状如前，谨牒」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1275612_comment'></div>如前辈所记，署衔多杭州官，称子容云「知府舍人」，乃知杭州时也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1275612_comment'></div>归舟，烟雨晻霭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1275612_comment'></div>游大能仁寺，闳壮光丽，甲于会稽，重殿复阁，金碧相照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1275612_comment'></div>寺，吴越钱氏所建，颓废久矣，新于今主僧常坦之手。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1275612_comment'></div>二十年前见坦于此寺，方为板下僧，相与步败檐毁垣间，慨然有兴作意，具道规模次第，果不愆其素，有志者事竟成如此，然益知民力之困也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1275612_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_139_1275612'>五日，义恩师约饭，偕者苏仁仲、伯舅、叔舅、潘叔度、詹季章、丁茂才松年、六七表弟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1275612_comment'></div>暨中食开霁，晴光发窗，心目颇快，饭罢复阴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1275612_comment'></div>晚步过寺桥，历沈氏、李氏园，皆荒芜，独脩竹犹森然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1275612_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_142_1275612'>六日，偕石天民斗文、潘叔度，自寺桥直道过郡庠，道傍多流水乔木，殊不类廛市。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1275612_comment'></div>教授厅后环碧亭小愒，环亭皆水，败荷折苇，秋思甚浓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1275612_comment'></div>石应之宗昭、高应朝宗商亦继来，遂自直舍入学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1275612_comment'></div>夫子殿居中，修廊广庭，长松错列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1275612_comment'></div>讲堂榜以明伦，后有稽古阁，制作皆雄伟而阁下尤胜，疏达开豁，拥墙密竹如云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1275612_comment'></div>晚冒雨归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1275612_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_148_1275612'>七日，雨不可出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1275612_comment'></div>过詹季章位小阁，因重屋楼板，其间纵三弓，横半之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1275612_comment'></div>南北取屋山为明远山，竹树历历如画，芦簟仰承，穹窿若船背，幽洁极可爱，名以越舲，其状真类小舟也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1275612_comment'></div>八日早，过大中戒珠寺，王右军故宅也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1275612_comment'></div>屋多人少，颇牢落。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1275612_comment'></div>门有两池，亦称右军鹅池、墨池，略无意趣，政如天章者，皆后人彊名之耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1275612_comment'></div>殿后地渐峻，石应之寓居在焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1275612_comment'></div>遂与应之登雪轩，轩占卧佛殿右偏，湖山聚落，皆来献状，以宜于观雪得名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1275612_comment'></div>今虽不与雪值，然雾雨空濛，亦奇观也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1275612_comment'></div>寺后即蕺山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1275612_comment'></div>蕺，菜名，《图经》云越王嗜蕺，尝采于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1275612_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_159_1275612'>九日早，雨少止，侍伯舅，同潘叔度、詹季章泛舟赴苏仁仲饭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1275612_comment'></div>舟经卧龙山下，竹洲柳岸，略如苕霅，卧枝拂水，尤奇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1275612_comment'></div>饭罢登舟，中涂小泊，步游西园，郡圃也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1275612_comment'></div>其北飞盖堂，下临大池。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1275612_comment'></div>其中集春堂，四隅各一亭，东春荣、西秋芳、南夏阴、北冬瑞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1275612_comment'></div>其南扬波堂，面城水木幽茂，两小亭对峙，东曰逍遥，西曰裴回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1275612_comment'></div>园之西即曲水，先入敷荣门，右转至右军祠，穿修竹坞，遂登山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1275612_comment'></div>山盖版筑所成，缭绕深邃，曲径回复，迷藏亭观，乍入者惶惑不知南北。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1275612_comment'></div>山背有流杯岩，凿城引鉴湖为小溪，穿岩下，键以横闸，激浪怒鸣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1275612_comment'></div>过闸遂为曲水，长庑华敞，榱栋椽柱，皆涂斲象竹，绕以清流，甃以苍石，犬牙参错，殆若天成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1275612_comment'></div>俯砌水中为礅，流杯至礅傍辄自近岸，盖庑中为三井，吸水势使然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1275612_comment'></div>曲水之上，激湍亭、惠风阁，规模若都下王公家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1275612_comment'></div>山顶崇峻庵，其胁骋怀亭，面亭依山，为岩壑然，皆涂塈不可支久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1275612_comment'></div>下山，右绕至清真轩，刻桷象栟榈，平阶荼蘼架甚茂，但为蔓草萦乱刺眼耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_172_1275612_comment'></div>曲水乃前守史丞相浩所凿，往年见其新成，今竹树皆成阴而亭榭稍稍圮剥矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1275612_comment'></div>复登舟还禹迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_174_1275612_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_175_1275612'>十日，午后，同叔度泛舟过南堰，出门穿鉴湖支港，斜雨入篷，衣袂沾濡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_175_1275612_comment'></div>七里，独山野桥，烟树可画。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_176_1275612_comment'></div>出山口，港渐狭，又七里道树，舍舟步田间，泥潦没屐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_177_1275612_comment'></div>一里许，至坚密庵，拜外大父墓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_178_1275612_comment'></div>庵屋才八九閒，窗槛幽洁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_179_1275612_comment'></div>夜分，四山风雨翛然，始闻秋声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_180_1275612_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_181_1275612'>十一日，晨起，冒雨蹑屐，登舟入城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_181_1275612_comment'></div>至能仁寺，赴常坦师饭，七六弟在焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_182_1275612_comment'></div>遂过报恩光孝寺，寺后飞来山，即《图经》所谓怪山也，传云自琅琊飞至，其说不经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_183_1275612_comment'></div>其巅有塔，采绚甚华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_184_1275612_comment'></div>塔下有鳗井，乃小石窍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_185_1275612_comment'></div>自唐以来神之，谓鳗能时出妖祥，近世不复见矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_186_1275612_comment'></div>井故依山坳坡陁，有古意，近僧甃使就整，遂无可观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_187_1275612_comment'></div>有濮安懿王祠庙寓此寺，有园令领吏卒守之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_188_1275612_comment'></div>主僧明哲，往岁尝识之新昌，设蜜术汤甚清美，晚还禹迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_189_1275612_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_190_1275612'>十二日，雨不可出，借《图经》寻近城名山，须雨霁遍游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_190_1275612_comment'></div>晚，石应之来宿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_191_1275612_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_192_1275612'>十三日，过午雨止，诸葛寿之千龄、高应朝、石应之、孙季和应时，约往丁氏园。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_192_1275612_comment'></div>遂同汎舟至新河，步入园。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_193_1275612_comment'></div>园多海桧，但绾结阏其天性。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_194_1275612_comment'></div>后墙皆密竹，轩楹大敞，宜夏不宜冬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_195_1275612_comment'></div>宿东偏小室，会宿者叔度、应之、季和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_196_1275612_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_197_1275612'>十四日，自丁氏园偕叔度、寿之、应朝、应之、季和登舟出五云门，入鉴湖，湖面独此为阔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_197_1275612_comment'></div>隆兴初，吴给事芾浚湖未一二尺，多得古棺，皆刳木为之，盖汉未凿湖前冢墓也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_198_1275612_comment'></div>然后知古人为湖，特因地势筑堤，堤立而湖成，不待深疏凿也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_199_1275612_comment'></div>今自五云门，重堤隐然达于曹娥五六十里，民间谓之省塘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_200_1275612_comment'></div>此乃故湖堤，湖田之民，每毁堤以决积水，故堤缺而湖废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_201_1275612_comment'></div>异时有意复湖者，第修完省塘，则盗湖之田，不待废而自为陂泺矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_202_1275612_comment'></div>自湖尾入若耶溪，过后汉郑弘庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_203_1275612_comment'></div>传所记樵风蚤暮，迎送舟楫，采薪者云至今犹然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_204_1275612_comment'></div>半里，石帆山，山横若张帆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_205_1275612_comment'></div>又数十步，秦始皇酒瓮，乃山脚两石，粗类瓮盎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_206_1275612_comment'></div>又一二里，舣舟游龙瑞宫，方士谓之阳明洞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_207_1275612_comment'></div>天穿松径数百步，至宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_208_1275612_comment'></div>宫后三峰，翔舞飞动，势若覆压，大略如栖贤望五老，特欠其二耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_209_1275612_comment'></div>中峰乃会稽山，祠官春秋用事焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_210_1275612_comment'></div>由西庑循山径，观龙见坛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_211_1275612_comment'></div>其旁即禹穴，乃大石中断成罅，殊不古，殆非司马子长所探也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_212_1275612_comment'></div>又数步，飞来石，老木槎枒，石壁如削。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_213_1275612_comment'></div>缘磴道至钱秀才庵，遂自东庑出院。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_214_1275612_comment'></div>院皆扃闭，独遇一客道士，云绵州人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_215_1275612_comment'></div>复登舟径鉴湖，湖天夕照，水村渔屋，皆被光景。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_216_1275612_comment'></div>日所入，诸山如在全雾中，天下绝境也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_217_1275612_comment'></div>暮泊告成观，宿于明远堂下小室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_218_1275612_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_219_1275612'>十五日，晨，谒大禹祠。</div><div id='poem_sentence_219_1275612_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1174&endYear=1174')">1174年8月</a>　应门人汪仲仪请为其母作墓铭。作品：《金华汪仲仪母王氏墓志铭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷十一。）</span><div id='poem_1275656' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275656' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275656?labeling=true' target='_blank'>金华汪仲仪母王氏墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（淳熙元年八月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275656")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275656_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275656'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275656'>谱学、昏议，不相为谋而相为用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275656_comment'></div>昔者氏族之学尝行矣，南有王、谢，北有崔、卢，品第甲乙，聘娶一失其班，则俗以为大耻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275656_comment'></div>放乎末流，乃或挟以相市，于是氏族反为昏姻病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275656_comment'></div>及其既衰，则又混为一区。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275656_comment'></div>由卑援高者，厥咎僭，厥罚常辱，厥妖妇乘夫；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275656_comment'></div>由高耦卑者厥咎贪，厥罚常骄，厥妖夫虐妇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275656_comment'></div>视乡者之患，未知其孰先后也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275656_comment'></div>以吾观于州闾之嫁娶，不外慕，不远求，族望既称，情义亦通，宜其家而蕃其后者，常必由之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275656_comment'></div>尚氏族者诚若是，亦何负于世乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275656_comment'></div>言金华之门阀者，汪与王为显姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275656_comment'></div>夫人受氏于王，出适于汪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275656_comment'></div>汪王之睦，有自来矣，盖予所谓族望称而情义通者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275656_comment'></div>自初盥馈讫于终，勤俭自律，未尝袨服冶容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275656_comment'></div>内外亲以窭谒者，随多寡及之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275656_comment'></div>曰：「彼以亲亲之道来，空行空反，吾恧焉，聊以致吾心耳」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275656_comment'></div>其诲诸子则曰：「汝曹第专意经史，毋以货败尔志」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275656_comment'></div>婢妾童仆，拊循一以和厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1275656_comment'></div>条理家事方有绪，而夫人则死矣，寿甫五十一，实乾道九年十二月癸未。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1275656_comment'></div>葬以淳熙元年八月甲申，其乡惠日，其原九里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1275656_comment'></div>曾祖本，赠宣教郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1275656_comment'></div>祖登，承议郎，累赠特进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1275656_comment'></div>考师古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1275656_comment'></div>夫曰浩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1275656_comment'></div>子曰仲仪、仲俨、仲侃、仲称、仲僖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1275656_comment'></div>女六，长以疾在室，次适曹著，次适曹庄，次适时伯茂，馀未行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1275656_comment'></div>时氏妇后夫人七月亦卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1275656_comment'></div>孙男四，女二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1275656_comment'></div>仲仪尝从予游，先葬，请识。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1275656_comment'></div>乃铭之曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_1275656'>钧其匹，燕其宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1275656_comment'></div>相其原，安其宫。</div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1275656_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1174&endYear=1174')">1174年8月</a>　作书与朱熹讨论《伊洛渊源录》编撰问题。作品：《与朱侍讲》二十八。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷八。）</span><br /></div><div class='label1' id='831355a7359141159f26678093f571ce_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("831355a7359141159f26678093f571ce");'><span id='831355a7359141159f26678093f571ce_link' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1174&endYear=1174')">1174年10月</a>　作诗哭芮烨。作品：《祭酒芮公既殁四年，门人吕某始以十诗哭之》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷一。）</span><div id='poem_94073' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_94073' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/94073?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭酒芮公既殁四年门人吕某始以十诗哭之<span class='inlineComment2'>（淳熙元年）</span><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1174年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_94073")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_94073_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_94073'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_94073'>少年把笔便班扬，咳唾珠玑落四方。<div id='poem_sentence_0_94073_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_94073'>岁晚寒窗浑忘却，瓦炉香细雨声长。<div id='poem_sentence_1_94073_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_94073'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_94073_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_94072' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_94072' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/94072?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1174年10月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_94072_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_94072'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_94072'>际野尘埃扑面来，万人蚁聚拨难<span class='inlineComment2'>（金华本作不）</span>开。<div id='poem_sentence_0_94072_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_94072'>手中杓柄长多少，蛰尽饥肠十月雷<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_94072_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_94072'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_94072_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_94072'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_94072_0'>⑴ 自注：公为仁和尉，岁荒，殍者满野，区处赈恤，各有条理。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_94072_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_94064' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_94064' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/94064?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1174年10月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_94064_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_94064'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_94064'>小醉初醒日半昏，森森赤棒绕篱门。<div id='poem_sentence_0_94064_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_94064'>慨然投袂无难色，不识从来狱吏尊<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_94064_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_94064'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_94064_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_94064'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_94064_0'>⑴ 自注：公尝为某道，坐诗（金华本作诏）狱时如此。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_94064_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_94069' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_94069' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/94069?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其四 </span></a><span id='poem_sentence_0_94069'>交广归来里巷迎，破囊又比去时轻。<div id='poem_sentence_0_94069_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_94069'>何须更酌廉泉水，夫子胸中万斛清。<div id='poem_sentence_1_94069_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_94069'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_94069_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_94068' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_94068' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/94068?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其五 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1174年10月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_94068_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_94068'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_94068'>殿前拜疏阅群公，献替从违各异同。<div id='poem_sentence_0_94068_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_94068'>陛楯诸郎自相语，白头祭酒最由衷。<div id='poem_sentence_1_94068_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_94068'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_94068_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_94070' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_94070' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/94070?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其六 </span></a><span id='poem_sentence_0_94070'>出祖津头六馆空，帽檐齐侧挂帆风。<div id='poem_sentence_0_94070_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_94070'>吴兴盛事人能数，直自胡公到芮公。<div id='poem_sentence_1_94070_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_94070'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_94070_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_94066' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_94066' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/94066?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其七 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1174年10月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_94066_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_94066'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_94066'>闻人有善己伸眉，倒廪倾囷更不疑。<div id='poem_sentence_0_94066_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_94066'>菶菶萋萋竟何许，卷阿空老凤皇枝。<div id='poem_sentence_1_94066_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_94066'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_94066_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_94067' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_94067' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/94067?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其八 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1174年10月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_94067_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_94067'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_94067'>胸怀北海与南溟，却要涓涓一勺清。<div id='poem_sentence_0_94067_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_94067'>相对蹴然如重客，无人信道是门生。<div id='poem_sentence_1_94067_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_94067'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_94067_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_94065' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_94065' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/94065?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其九 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1174年10月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_94065_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_94065'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_94065'>璧水经年奉宴居，天和袭物自舒徐。<div id='poem_sentence_0_94065_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_94065'>凭谁寄谢朱公掞，才向春风坐月馀<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_94065_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_94065'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_94065_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_94065'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_94065_0'>⑴ 自注：朱公掞见明道于汝州，归语人曰：光庭在春风中坐一月。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_94065_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_94071' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_94071' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/94071?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其十 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1174年10月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_94071_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_94071'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_94071'>先生墓木绿成围，弟子摧颓昼掩扉。<div id='poem_sentence_0_94071_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_94071'>大雪繁霜心已死，有时清梦尚抠衣。<div id='poem_sentence_1_94071_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_94071'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_94071_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1174&endYear=1174')">1174年10月</a>　作书与周必大，并录呈哭芮烨十诗。作品：《与周丞相》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷九。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1174&endYear=1174')">1174年10月</a>　为门生乔德瞻作墓铭。作品：《乔德瞻墓志铭》<div id='poem_1275657' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275657' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275657?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乔德瞻墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（淳熙元年十月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275657")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275657_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275657'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275657'>吾友乔拱德瞻，质甚茂，貌甚和，志乡甚正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275657_comment'></div>从前辈游，深绎默味，盖非易其言者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275657_comment'></div>其事亲油油然，若不足也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275657_comment'></div>其奉兄惓惓然，左右之欲不违也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275657_comment'></div>其处宗族乡党惕惕然，恐恩意之或不孚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275657_comment'></div>其讲习将求尽乎此，其践行亦既深知其难矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275657_comment'></div>方用力于是也，乾道九年十一月一日，以疾卒，年二十有九。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275657_comment'></div>妻楼氏，后百二十日亦卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275657_comment'></div>以淳熙元年十月五日，葬于东阳之西山冈里原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275657_comment'></div>曾祖应，祖瓘，考松，母杜氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275657_comment'></div>二子，豫、临。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275657_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_1275657'>莫之为而为者，其天乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275657_comment'></div>苗而不秀者，有矣夫？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275657_comment'></div>呜呼！</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1275657_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1174&endYear=1174')">1174年10月</a>　应刘邦翰请，为其妻作墓铭。作品：《郭宜人墓志铭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷十。）</span><div id='poem_1275651' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275651' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275651?labeling=true' target='_blank'>郭宜人墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（乾道八年十月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275651")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275651_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275651'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275651'>泉溪刘氏兆域，有别卜清溪之原者，是为户部公之配郭宜人墓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275651_comment'></div>既葬二年，户部以书来谂曰：「邦翰老而哭妻，墓草再易矣，见故奁尘箧，依然有馀思，是非若小儿曹戚戚歔欷也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275651_comment'></div>吾妻无恙时，自闑以内，裘葛釜鬲，醪醴臡醯，孰水而冻，孰火而燔，孰社而酿，孰腊而储，吾未尝过而问焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275651_comment'></div>饥至知食，寒至知衣，客至知献酬而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275651_comment'></div>视己出若妾媵所出，拊育惟一，族党无纤介薄厚之议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275651_comment'></div>授室以来，袖手旁观，每谓家政直差易耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275651_comment'></div>及失吾妻，治官文书，腕脱入户，将少休，问米谒盐者旁午，喟然而叹，始知其难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275651_comment'></div>益念吾妻四十年代予劳之不可忘也，故过时而哀未衰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275651_comment'></div>子尝有意铭其藏，幸卒成之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275651_comment'></div>某先垄实在婺之武义，于泉溪盖同县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275651_comment'></div>与户部游再世矣，岁时往来，占壸职于杯盘，固得其略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275651_comment'></div>诸子相从讲学，履屐装赍之属，皆宜人均一之德所形见也，铭敢不诺？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275651_comment'></div>宜人卒以乾道六年十一月七日，享年六十有四。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275651_comment'></div>时户部知常德府，归葬以乾道八年十月某日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275651_comment'></div>曾祖宗元，赠少傅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275651_comment'></div>祖瑑，赠太师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275651_comment'></div>考三益，左中大夫、同知枢密院事，赠光禄大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1275651_comment'></div>妣孟氏，齐安郡夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1275651_comment'></div>子男子八人，粹中，迪功郎、新衢州龙游县尉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1275651_comment'></div>敏中，迪功郎、新衢州江山县主簿；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1275651_comment'></div>允中、时中，应进士举；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1275651_comment'></div>居中、虚中，皆夭；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1275651_comment'></div>馀未名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1275651_comment'></div>子女子六人，长适从事郎、永州军事推官应材，次适朝请郎、尚书司封郎中巩湘，次适承议郎周权，次适太学生淩颙，次适进士黄闬，次未行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1275651_comment'></div>于是户部方为朝散大夫、尚书户部员外郎，总领湖广京西财赋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1275651_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_1275651'>维斗之枢，系隆地高。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1275651_comment'></div>妇于素门，乃锄其骄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1275651_comment'></div>《风》有《芣苢》，捋之撷之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1275651_comment'></div>我心和平，诸御是绥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1275651_comment'></div>子舍连甍，女车交道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1275651_comment'></div>岁时晨昏，来面来告。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1275651_comment'></div>并耦而耕，穫失其一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1275651_comment'></div>里人作诗，飏于姻戚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_32_1275651_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1174&endYear=1174')">1174年11月</a>　应门人卢汝雱请，为其父卢大经作墓铭。作品：《淳安卢君墓志铭》<div id='poem_1275658' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275658' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275658?labeling=true' target='_blank'>淳安卢君墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（淳熙元年十一月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275658")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275658_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275658'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275658'>新定之有淳安，壮县也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275658_comment'></div>淳安之有卢氏，闻家也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275658_comment'></div>君讳大经，字子权，于诸卢为尊老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275658_comment'></div>年七十有八，以乾道九年九月十三日终于家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275658_comment'></div>明年改元淳熙，十一月二十三日，葬于县之翰林村。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275658_comment'></div>始予为新定校官，君之季子实缀弟子员，后其叔介季以见，既因弟而见其兄；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275658_comment'></div>叔、季游居数年，益习其家庭之训，复因子以得其父。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275658_comment'></div>及是以铭来谒，乃论其可载者著之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275658_comment'></div>盖君少入郡庠，三舍法未罢，当升名大司成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275658_comment'></div>吏方析锱铢，于贡法疑，典教者导君自理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275658_comment'></div>君曰：「以诉得贡，吾耻之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275658_comment'></div>且友人刘南武第居次，不若以就南武」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275658_comment'></div>遂不自言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275658_comment'></div>久之，数诎于有司，尽弃科试业，归辑其家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275658_comment'></div>疆畎、垣屋、埘圈、陂浍、无细大皆釐饬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275658_comment'></div>遇其暇时，翻史赋诗以自适。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275658_comment'></div>聚族虽众，阃内外不键而严。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1275658_comment'></div>交际意所不合，愤愤色上面；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1275658_comment'></div>至所倾乡，则掀髯谈噱，连日夜不休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1275658_comment'></div>其质易大氐若此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1275658_comment'></div>晚岁召诸子立堂下，命之曰：「汝震、汝雱，毋远游以纾吾劳；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1275658_comment'></div>汝琰、汝琯，毋怀安以成吾志」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1275658_comment'></div>既授以职，嗒然宴坐，绝口不挂外事，从容自颐，竟于耄耋，庶几善佚其老者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1275658_comment'></div>曾祖文照，祖庆孙，父哲，母宋氏，娶亦宋也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1275658_comment'></div>四子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1275658_comment'></div>五女，监应山税杨九思、进士徐孝祥、迪功郎段子亨、进士方胄、张百之，其婿也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1275658_comment'></div>五孙，长曰枢，馀皆幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1275658_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_1275658'>閒之燕之，糜寿绥之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1275658_comment'></div>基之堂之，既右翼之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1275658_comment'></div>有鬣者丘，于彼中林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1275658_comment'></div>纳诗其藏，匪今斯今。</div><div id='poem_sentence_30_1275658_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1174&endYear=1174')">1174年11月</a>　应门人陈锡请，为其母作墓铭。作品：《义务陈锡母朱氏墓志铭》<div id='poem_1275659' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275659' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275659?labeling=true' target='_blank'>义乌陈锡母朱氏墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（淳熙元年十一月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275659")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275659_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275659'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275659'>乌伤陈生踵门言曰：「锡也执经坐下，生养死葬之节，槩尝有闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275659_comment'></div>今也不幸母之丧，功衰既御矣，大惧不克终大事，为师友羞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275659_comment'></div>我家君卜稽于陈氏之祖考，粤甲午十一月壬寅食，百用既戒，独幽堂之铭，有其石而阙其辞，敢稽颡以请」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275659_comment'></div>予进之席，问其世，曰：系朱氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275659_comment'></div>曾祖绩，祖存，考逢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275659_comment'></div>生十有九年归于家君，名则登也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275659_comment'></div>问其后，曰：男五。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275659_comment'></div>肇，将仕郎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275659_comment'></div>仲仁，进武校尉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275659_comment'></div>集，将仕郎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275659_comment'></div>次乃锡，又次镒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275659_comment'></div>女二，长适詹允恭，次适叶松。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275659_comment'></div>孙男六，若古、若麟、若虚、若川、若讷、馀未名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275659_comment'></div>女五，长适朱大明，次适杨烈，馀尚幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275659_comment'></div>问其行，曰：母氏资勤俭，佐家君理内事，自始馈至发有二色犹不怠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275659_comment'></div>于训子尤笃，姻娅邻里，大抵不失其欢心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275659_comment'></div>问其寿，曰：六十有四，其没实乾道八年九月十八日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1275659_comment'></div>问其葬，曰：金华县之龙盘原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1275659_comment'></div>于是次第其语而系以铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_1275659'>畴敷而绵兮，曷晻而泉兮，维以章其阡兮。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1275659_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1174&endYear=1174')">1174年12月</a>　周必大被召，作书为善类贺之。作品：《与周丞相》二。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷九。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1174&endYear=1174')">1174年12月</a>　应薛季宣子之请，为薛季宣作墓铭成。作品：《薛常州墓志铭》<div id='poem_1275653' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275653' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275653?labeling=true' target='_blank'>薛常州墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1173年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275653")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275653_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275653'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275653'>河东之薛，有降居闽之长溪者，世久不能迹其始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275653_comment'></div>既又家于永嘉，其长老之记曰，唐补阙令之后迁焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275653_comment'></div>裔孙庠，以驯行闻于乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275653_comment'></div>庠生强立，始修补阙之旧，续其禄，盖终江宁府观察推官，赠左光禄大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275653_comment'></div>光禄四子：嘉言，尚书司封郎中；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275653_comment'></div>昌言，通判婺州；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275653_comment'></div>弼，敷文阁待制；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275653_comment'></div>徽言，起居舍人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275653_comment'></div>公讳季宣，字士龙，起居之子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275653_comment'></div>起居学于胡文定公安国，而雅为赵忠简公鼎所厚，其立朝皆有本末。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275653_comment'></div>最后秦丞相桧建与虏和，起居自殿坳直前，引义固争，反复数刻，中寒疾以卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275653_comment'></div>夫人胡氏亦继卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275653_comment'></div>于是公生六年矣，伯父待制收鞠之，任以官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275653_comment'></div>公幼逮事过江诸贤，闻中兴经理，大略已能识之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275653_comment'></div>喜从老校退卒语，得岳、韩二三大将兵间事甚悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275653_comment'></div>志尚荦荦，与常儿异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275653_comment'></div>年十七，起从妻父荆南帅孙汝翼，辟书写机宜文字。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1275653_comment'></div>荆州善袁溉道洁，虚郡斋迎致之，公遂委己师焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1275653_comment'></div>道洁及登河南程夫子之门，闻蜀隐者薛叟名，晚游蜀，以物色求之莫能得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1275653_comment'></div>末至一郡，并舍有叟旦荷笈之市，午漏下辄扃其户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1275653_comment'></div>道洁从壁间觇之，方隐几默坐，意象静深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1275653_comment'></div>问诸邻，则曰是鬻香薛翁，不知其所从来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1275653_comment'></div>道洁亟款门，以弟子礼见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1275653_comment'></div>旦往陈所学，叟漠然如不闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1275653_comment'></div>久之乃曰：「经所以载道，圣人作经以明道，子何博而寡要也」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1275653_comment'></div>始与深语。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1275653_comment'></div>未几复舍去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1275653_comment'></div>道洁漫浪沔鄂间，讳其学，绝不为人道，独与公倾倒无所靳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1275653_comment'></div>公自是笃意于学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1275653_comment'></div>道洁语公，伊洛轶书多在蜀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1275653_comment'></div>时同郡萧振方制置四川，乃往为其属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1275653_comment'></div>道洁期至蜀授以书，会偏裨有诬其所部将者，公请正阶级法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1275653_comment'></div>议不合，谢去，遇道洁于峡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1275653_comment'></div>而公既出蜀矣，调鄂州武昌令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1275653_comment'></div>武昌号难治，连败数令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1275653_comment'></div>公年尚少，郡将、部使者易之，迎谓：「是邑久不可为，子敢当之乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1275653_comment'></div>公曰：「独患在上者以县为可为，今知其不可为，则可为矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1275653_comment'></div>愿宽其衔辔，俾得自尽」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1275653_comment'></div>皆诺之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1275653_comment'></div>科徭兴发，率以公故独不及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1275653_comment'></div>唯论和籴，始不见答，欲解印绶去，卒体其诚，得罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1275653_comment'></div>公既获乎上，民赖以宽，有所废置，皆争趣和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1275653_comment'></div>乃大治，版籍、期会、简稽、出纳，悉就绳尺，密而不烦，严而不迫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1275653_comment'></div>虏亮未叛盟，公白其长，视要害，前备御，辄不省。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1275653_comment'></div>及兵交，稍稍即公咨计画。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1275653_comment'></div>虏亮悉众瞰江，诏成闵还师入援。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1275653_comment'></div>时汪枢使澈宣谕荆襄，公告：「成闵得蔡，有破竹之势，盍守便宜勿遣？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1275653_comment'></div>令闵乘虚下武昌，径陈、汝趋汴都，虏内顾且惊溃，释此成业，而聚兵相仗，鲜克以济」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1275653_comment'></div>不能用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1275653_comment'></div>闵昼夜驰不顿舍，后骑能属者三之一，而陈、蔡新附诸城，亦踵接复为虏矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1275653_comment'></div>江淮仕者大抵无固志，纷纷遣其孥系马庭木以须。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1275653_comment'></div>公独留家不遣，誓与民俱死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1275653_comment'></div>县故多盗，铁冶、营田，棋布诸乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1275653_comment'></div>亡命奸人，出没其间，所治即孙吴故宫，自古江左重地也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1275653_comment'></div>公念除盗上策，莫如联保甲，疆陲有事，唯素整者可不乱，乃访求河北、陕右弓箭手保甲法及淮西刘纲保伍要策，讨论甚具。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1275653_comment'></div>会有伍民之令，乃出其法行之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1275653_comment'></div>五家为保，二保为甲，六甲为队，因地形便合为总，不以乡为限，总首、副总首领焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1275653_comment'></div>官族、士族、富族、皆附保蠲其身，俾输财共总之小用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1275653_comment'></div>诸总必有射圃，民暇则习，无蚤暮之节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1275653_comment'></div>尽禁蒱博，独许以击刺驰射角胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1275653_comment'></div>五日更至庭阅，其尤者劳赏之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1275653_comment'></div>旗志总别为色，枪仗皆中度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1275653_comment'></div>候望干掫不幸死者，予棺，复家三岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1275653_comment'></div>诸乡皆置楼，盗发，伐鼓举烽以相号召，瞬息遍百里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1275653_comment'></div>总首白事，吏毋得预，追胥兴发，一以县檄为验。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1275653_comment'></div>环邑沟渎不渫，夏潦波道，在事者病之，役大莫敢睥睨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1275653_comment'></div>及保甲成，天大雨，公出坐通衢，传呼总队，具畚锸、赋丈尺，三日而毕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1275653_comment'></div>市多火，公戒诸队钩绳梯缶，各专其一，暮夜仓卒，随用而索，甚速且整，火不能灾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1275653_comment'></div>县治白鹿矶、安乐口，皆置戍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1275653_comment'></div>复请于宣谕司，得战舰十、甲三百，罗落之守计定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1275653_comment'></div>讫虏退，人心不摇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1275653_comment'></div>大军之屯州县，客主不相能，多为鬨暴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1275653_comment'></div>公曲得其欢心，以事至者，必微见曲直而明假借之，皆大喜且大服，誓死以报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1275653_comment'></div>内郡发粟输边，县当餫信阳，公部以往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1275653_comment'></div>先是诸将出师，部勒无法，或侵苦之，道殣相望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1275653_comment'></div>文吏董役者，则又甚焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1275653_comment'></div>民见调，辄与亲戚为死决。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1275653_comment'></div>公语父老曰：「子弟相从者，吾受其无咎」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1275653_comment'></div>皆怃然阳应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1275653_comment'></div>既发，队伍次舍悉放行军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1275653_comment'></div>亲与役夫同苦乐，病者挟医护视，始轻所负，剧则皆弛之，增剧则以马若舆载之，病者未至，队长毋得即安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1275653_comment'></div>号令齐一，道上担肩相差如引绳，无敢少蹉跌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1275653_comment'></div>观者相语曰：「此谁将军部曲耶，乃整肃如是」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1275653_comment'></div>既而知为武昌白丁，相视叹息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1275653_comment'></div>斯役也，在行者千有八百。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1275653_comment'></div>役罢，死者一人，跌伤者一人，馀还畀其父母妻子如初约。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1275653_comment'></div>当是时，诸公争知之，举辟交至，公一无所就。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1275653_comment'></div>从吏部铨得婺州司理参军，召对，首言治体有本末，愿遴三公之选，责以进人材，张纪纲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1275653_comment'></div>延端直之士，与之讲问学、求治道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1275653_comment'></div>又论中都官员多职寡，牧伯之任分为五六，唯大军胜战，将兵而下，废为隶役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1275653_comment'></div>因道远方民瘼甚悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1275653_comment'></div>王枢使炎前在鄂，熟公治行，及是新得政，求助于公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1275653_comment'></div>公语之曰：「上天资英特，群臣幸得遭时，乃忽略根本而奔走军旅之间，盍以仁义纲纪为本？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1275653_comment'></div>至于用兵，请俟十年之后」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1275653_comment'></div>改宣义郎，知平江府常熟县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1275653_comment'></div>退，待次具区滆上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1275653_comment'></div>明年，复召审察，公固辞，徘徊踰年乃就道，至则除大理寺主簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1275653_comment'></div>是岁江湖大旱，流民往往北渡江，边吏复奏淮北民多款塞者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1275653_comment'></div>虞丞相允文白遣公行淮西，收以实边。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1275653_comment'></div>公持节劳来，耄稚满车下，为之表废田、相原隰，复合肥三十六圩，立二十有二庄于黄州故治东北。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1275653_comment'></div>以户颁屋，以丁颁田，二丁共一牛，犁、杷、锄、锹、钁、镰具，六丁加一錅刀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1275653_comment'></div>每甲辘轴二，水车一，种子钱丁五千，廪其家，至食新罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1275653_comment'></div>凡为户六百八十有五，分处合肥、故黄适等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1275653_comment'></div>而合肥赢故黄三户，户授二室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1275653_comment'></div>受田之丁，合肥八百一十有五，故黄六百一十有四。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1275653_comment'></div>会其钱若米之费，财二万缗、六千石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1275653_comment'></div>流民已为大姓有者，仍隶其主户就抚之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1275653_comment'></div>并边归正者，振业之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1275653_comment'></div>合三千八百馀户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1275653_comment'></div>始公以乾道七年十二月至淮西，反命以明年之夏，计道里往来与察边郡、检麦田之属，专于田事者仅数月，垦筑、冶铸、斲削，皆受成于公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1275653_comment'></div>赋役省而功坚，度可支数十年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1275653_comment'></div>位置向背，经纬条达，民生所须，不外索而足，淮人谓耳目所未睹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1275653_comment'></div>公曰：「吾非为今日利也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1275653_comment'></div>治合肥之圩，边有警，因以断栅江，保巢湖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1275653_comment'></div>故黄，实古邾城，地直蔡冲，诸庄益辑，则西道有屏蔽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1275653_comment'></div>其措意深远矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1275653_comment'></div>光守宋端友自上招集北归户一百十七，公至固始，验新民止五户，馀皆保塞数年，端友混新旧户为一，籍以幸赏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1275653_comment'></div>异时有以善马涉淮者，杀而要夺之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1275653_comment'></div>公亟举奏端友有挟，人谓章且不下，语闻，上感悟，属廷尉治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1275653_comment'></div>方穷竟，端友以忧死，习为媒者皆竦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1275653_comment'></div>而虞丞相始不乐公矣，故为多端縻公，以缓其归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1275653_comment'></div>或迎说公：「见上，盍少自绌？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1275653_comment'></div>毋与当路者忤」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1275653_comment'></div>公曰：「上遣我视边，固欲得利害之实」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1275653_comment'></div>卒极陈之，且曰：「臣根本其敝，不计而谩为，而后外以卤莽报；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1275653_comment'></div>不思而出令，而后外以难行寝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1275653_comment'></div>号为责实，未免徇名，则趣办皆徇名之人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1275653_comment'></div>志在大功，反规小利，则迎合皆规利之辈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1275653_comment'></div>诞谩者败而不诛，谀说者察而不去，左右为欺囊橐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1275653_comment'></div>迩为援则远坚，大为间则小肆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1275653_comment'></div>其荐退人物，曾非诵言，游扬中伤，乃自不意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1275653_comment'></div>齐威之霸，不在阿、即墨之断，而在毁誉者之刑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1275653_comment'></div>臣观近政，非无阿、即墨之断，奈何毁誉之人自若」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1275653_comment'></div>上欣然开纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1275653_comment'></div>公复进曰：「外事无足道，咎根不除，抑臣深忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1275653_comment'></div>左右近侍，阴挤正士而阳浮称道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1275653_comment'></div>陛下诚圣明，傥因貌言，万一垂听，臣恐石显、王凤、郑注之智中也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1275653_comment'></div>又曰：「好名特为臣子学问之累。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1275653_comment'></div>人主为社稷计，唯恐士不好名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1275653_comment'></div>诚人人好名畏义，何乡不立」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1275653_comment'></div>上是之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1275653_comment'></div>隆兴以来，经理两淮受遣者且数十辈，发御府金缯，听施置自便阅十年，鲜有当上意者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1275653_comment'></div>及公使事有绪，恨得公晚，道进官二等，除大理正，侧席迟其至，顾问䌷绎，奏请论荐，皆报可，闻者意公且用矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1275653_comment'></div>居七日，出守湖州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1275653_comment'></div>入辞，语益恳到，上慰勉遣焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1275653_comment'></div>公既数摩切左右，而湖多权贵人田宅，与相加尤数，公平心问理如何，不为变，益害公，合力撼摇，上记其忠，独保持之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1275653_comment'></div>始至，书狱多入死，讯其由，则弃市者民间或窃祠之，名「伤神」，恶少遂轻相雠杀不顾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1275653_comment'></div>公亟屏绝，死狱大减，条境内淫祠，次第除撤，会去郡而辍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1275653_comment'></div>土俗小民悍强，甚者数十人为朋，私为约无得输主户租，前为政者或纵臾之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1275653_comment'></div>公叹曰：「郡国幸无事，而鼠辈颉颃已尔，缓急之际将何若」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1275653_comment'></div>取其首恶，黥窜远方，民始知有奴主之分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1275653_comment'></div>初陈亨伯割诸道留州钱输大农，号经制，翁彦国复附以总制，嗜进者竞裒歛以应赏格，已而遂定其多数为岁额。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1275653_comment'></div>州用日削而供亿稍饩，校军兴前五六倍，吏骪法擿抉无遗笔，犹廪廪不能给。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1275653_comment'></div>至是户部令提点刑狱司以历付场务，一钱已上皆分隶经总制如式。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1275653_comment'></div>诸郡被符，搏手无策，相顾莫敢先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1275653_comment'></div>公独言于朝曰：「自经总制立额，州郡凿空以取盈，虽有奉法吏思宽弛而不得骋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1275653_comment'></div>若复隶额外征，掇其强半郡调度，顾安所取？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1275653_comment'></div>殆复为它谬巧重取之民，民何以胜」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1275653_comment'></div>户部镌谯愈急，公争之愈强，台谏亦交疏助公，遂收前令不布。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1275653_comment'></div>凡可以纾民力者，知无不言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1275653_comment'></div>如论和籴贾贱，请更平直；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1275653_comment'></div>徙汰军宽州；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1275653_comment'></div>添差隶郡者，止今见员，后勿遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1275653_comment'></div>函封相继，多格于有司，则以病谒祠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1275653_comment'></div>朝廷惜之，却其请至八九，知不可夺，改知常州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1275653_comment'></div>未上，以乾道七年九月戊申卒于家，年四十，官止奉议郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1275653_comment'></div>娶孙氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1275653_comment'></div>子法，补太学生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1275653_comment'></div>公之没，其友张淳治丧，程以古礼，公配孙夫人能顺听不违，里中观法焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1275653_comment'></div>十二月壬申，葬于永嘉县吹台乡慈湖之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1275653_comment'></div>自周季绝学，古先制作之原晦而不章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1275653_comment'></div>若董仲舒名田，诸葛亮治军，王通河汾之讲论，千有馀年，端倪盖时一见也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1275653_comment'></div>国朝程颢氏、程颐氏、张载氏，相与发挥之，于是本原精粗，统纪大备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_172_1275653_comment'></div>门人高弟，既尽晚出者，或骛于空无，不足以涉事耦变，识者忧之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1275653_comment'></div>公之学既有所授，博揽精思几二十年，百氏群籍、山经地志、断章阙简，研索不遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_174_1275653_comment'></div>过故墟废垄，环步移日，以验其迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_175_1275653_comment'></div>参绎融液，左右逢原，凡疆里、卒乘、封国、行河，久远难分明，一经公讲画，枝叶扶疏，缕贯脉连，于经无不合，于事无不可行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_176_1275653_comment'></div>涖官随广狭，默寓之于簿领期会之间，其所部吏曹，经时而不知公为儒者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_177_1275653_comment'></div>平生所际，文武之职不同，未尝为町畦崖岸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_178_1275653_comment'></div>而去就从违之际，守义不可夺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_179_1275653_comment'></div>言兵变化若神，而在朝每以不可轻试为主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_180_1275653_comment'></div>所见疏快轩豁，潜察之，自律严饬，虽倥偬，札翰正楷，无一惰笔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_181_1275653_comment'></div>少年豪举，既知学，销落，不留省其私，泊如也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_182_1275653_comment'></div>其为人平实质确，本于简易，行于敬恕，而坚志强力，又足以充践之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_183_1275653_comment'></div>善类方共倚属公，而公则死矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_184_1275653_comment'></div>《诗》、《易》、《春秋》《、中庸》、《大学》、《论语》，皆有训义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_185_1275653_comment'></div>他所论著若《九州图志》之属，稿方立而未究也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_186_1275653_comment'></div>岁在壬午，先君子守黄，公夹江为令，归以公所为语某，固已矍然自失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_187_1275653_comment'></div>后十载，乃识公于朝，一见莫逆如故交。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_188_1275653_comment'></div>其葬也，张淳既志其圹沄，复请诗以揭之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_189_1275653_comment'></div>丧不能文，今既免丧不死矣，其可不为公一言乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_190_1275653_comment'></div>词曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_191_1275653'>坠绪茫茫，独求诸野。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_191_1275653_comment'></div>有涤其源，昼夜不舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_192_1275653_comment'></div>繄道之穷，维其尚口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_193_1275653_comment'></div>不耀其章，而躬自厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_194_1275653_comment'></div>出孚于长，于长于君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_195_1275653_comment'></div>□□施之，乃没元身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_196_1275653_comment'></div>故吴之迹，故邾之遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_197_1275653_comment'></div>既堙既平，其尚有稽。</div><div id='poem_sentence_198_1275653_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1174&endYear=1174')">1174年12月</a>　应门人王中孚、王中实请，为其父王日就作墓铭。作品：《分水王君墓志铭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷十一。）</span><div id='poem_1275660' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275660' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275660?labeling=true' target='_blank'>分水王君墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（淳熙元年十二月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275660")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275660_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275660'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275660'>君讳日就，字成德，姓王氏，新定分水人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275660_comment'></div>君少以侠气盖里中，尝夜猎，从骑四出，即兽无在者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275660_comment'></div>有畜犬呜呜衔衣，箠之不却，且导且前，公独怪之，亟随以归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275660_comment'></div>明日覆视其处，左右虎迹纵横，乃叹曰：「犬，人畜也，犹知爱其主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275660_comment'></div>吾奉父母遗体，不自爱可乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275660_comment'></div>于是解鞲断绁，尽谢猎徒，闭户䌷架上书阅之，领略其大指，不为缴绕章句学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275660_comment'></div>读史至三国二晋豪杰，辄击节不能自已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275660_comment'></div>遇其意适，或为人诵之，音节清厉，听者咸竦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275660_comment'></div>中年丧明，传家政于其子，坚坐晦默馀二十载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275660_comment'></div>时从方士语以自虞，若其吐纳屈伸之术，盖薄之不深信也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275660_comment'></div>尝病乡邻贫者死无所藏，表隙地畀之，今五十馀冢矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275660_comment'></div>将没，命子孙以薄葬，正衣冠，泊然而终，享年六十有六，实淳熙元年八月二十二日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275660_comment'></div>以其年十二月八日，葬于县之柳柏乡金堂源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275660_comment'></div>曾祖思应，祖僎，考綝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275660_comment'></div>娶方氏，前公卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275660_comment'></div>二子：琪，太学生；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275660_comment'></div>偊，乡贡进士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1275660_comment'></div>十孙：男六，长中孚、次中实、馀未名；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1275660_comment'></div>女四。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1275660_comment'></div>曾孙男女三，皆幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1275660_comment'></div>分水之王，中兴以来，淳则清范，仍世不陨，遂为东南望族。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1275660_comment'></div>君虽不试，以其概见一二推之，殆非浮沈闾巷者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1275660_comment'></div>予不及识君，而中孚、中实皆从予游，退抑惇饬，众皆目之，意其必有所自。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1275660_comment'></div>予是以知君之教信行于其家也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1275660_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_1275660'>是何人斯，一榻欲冰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1275660_comment'></div>孰知其初，长雄五陵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1275660_comment'></div>支床之龟，摩云之鹗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1275660_comment'></div>二虫得失，谁厚谁薄。</div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1275660_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1174&endYear=1174')">1174年12月</a>　应门人汪大度、汪大明请，为其父汪灌作墓志铭。作品：《金华汪君将仕墓志铭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷十一。）</span><div id='poem_1275661' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275661' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275661?labeling=true' target='_blank'>金华汪君将仕墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（淳熙元年十二月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275661")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275661_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275661'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275661'>役，重事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275661_comment'></div>于朝廷为大议，于郡邑为大政，于编氓为大命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275661_comment'></div>求诸故府，弛张废置之变悉矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275661_comment'></div>异时或以义役为请，有司方持之，而闾里稍相与约，上不违县官律令，而下以全其族党之欢，其意美甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275661_comment'></div>然合散作辍，靡克坚定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275661_comment'></div>以予耳目所及言之，久而不败者，独金华、西山为然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275661_comment'></div>是乡也，盖有人焉，其姓名字曰汪灌庆衍，实基创而纪纲之者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275661_comment'></div>始君以役之病民，聚大姓谋曰：「吾乡之人，非父兄即子弟，顾鬨于役，隳恩弛义，为耆老羞，职是嚣竞者，追胥科徭之惮耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275661_comment'></div>率为里正一岁，长短相覆，亡虑费三十万。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275661_comment'></div>吾侪盍自实其赀，为三等，定著役之差次于籍，众裒金以畀当役者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275661_comment'></div>役之先后视其籍，金之多寡视其等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275661_comment'></div>他日户有升降，则告于众而进退之焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275661_comment'></div>名虽役而实仰给于众，尚何惮」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275661_comment'></div>众杂然称善，即日立要束，无违者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275661_comment'></div>既又以裒金之烦也，则众割田百亩庾之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275661_comment'></div>约成，登其书于县而各藏其副于家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275661_comment'></div>岁三月，乡众咸会，击豕酾酒，旧里正以田授新里正，成礼而退。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1275661_comment'></div>自绍兴己巳迄于今几三十年，西山役讼不至于公门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1275661_comment'></div>往岁郡守吴公芾嘉君之为，号其乡曰「循理」，里曰「信义」，以风其馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1275661_comment'></div>于是君之名与乡皆显。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1275661_comment'></div>君资廉直，急人之难，不避风雨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1275661_comment'></div>乡有大事，如经界、如隅官，令长皆倚君以办。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1275661_comment'></div>岁恶，饥民群剽，为政者请君画，且调兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1275661_comment'></div>君曰：「此直丐升斗以纾死，片纸可致，闻兵出则穷而搏矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1275661_comment'></div>乃遣巡检与君俱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1275661_comment'></div>君止巡检于家，独以数十辈持符逮之，至暮皆集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1275661_comment'></div>已而吏觊赏，将悉论以死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1275661_comment'></div>君伏太守庭曰：「是曹束手随檄，未尝捍格，今弃信而就功，后复无凶岁乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1275661_comment'></div>且灌实召之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1275661_comment'></div>守感悟，亟解散，其狱黥者财二人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1275661_comment'></div>君义著于乡，大氐若此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1275661_comment'></div>其举义役，所以倡之而和，谕之而孚，持之而坚且久也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1275661_comment'></div>君少以赀补将仕郎，卒以乾道九年十一月十六日，寿六十有七。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1275661_comment'></div>葬以淳熙元年十二月十九日，兆于其乡之乌石屏山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1275661_comment'></div>曾祖文岳，祖浚，考宗达。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1275661_comment'></div>娶郭氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1275661_comment'></div>男五，大任、大亨、大度、大明、大声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1275661_comment'></div>女五，长适迪功郎、江州德化县尉徐廷玉，次适项嵚而卒，次适曹结，次适时之望，次适孟龟年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1275661_comment'></div>大度、大明，久从予游，先窆谒铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1275661_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_39_1275661'>循理之乡，信义之里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1275661_comment'></div>惟名之令，其自君始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1275661_comment'></div>亦即始之，曷又终之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1275661_comment'></div>瞻彼墓门，毋或替之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_42_1275661_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1174&endYear=1174')">1174年12月</a>　将陈亮《孟子说》奉还，约定中春面议。作品：《与陈同甫》三。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷十。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1174&endYear=1174')">1174年12月</a>　函候汪应辰，告知来春造访事。作品：《与汪端明》十六。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷七。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1174&endYear=1174')">1174年</a>　本年作《左氏手记》作品：《甲午左传手记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷十三。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1174&endYear=1174')">1174年</a>　为楼蕴作墓铭。作品：《义乌楼君墓志铭》<div id='poem_1275652' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275652' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275652?labeling=true' target='_blank'>义乌楼君墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（乾道八年十二月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275652")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275652_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275652'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275652'>太史氏凡例，登于策者有彝品，惟以孝著，则虽岭隈水涯、凋瘁嫠独，亦编名达官显人后，并藏于金匮石室甚严，风劝隆尚之意远矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275652_comment'></div>自予少时，广坐间往往剽楼君孝行，既而君诸子从予游，益熟其为人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275652_comment'></div>盖君笃于孝，服母丧，废栉沐盐，酪不入口，结庐墓左，旦暮绕冢，哀号冢下，耕者皆徘徊为堕泪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275652_comment'></div>日负土筑冢，自课三十肩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275652_comment'></div>比外除，冢高数仞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275652_comment'></div>其行实应史法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275652_comment'></div>及执笔隶太史，阅郡国所上义夫节妇，君名独没不见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275652_comment'></div>退而问尝交君者，则曰前数十年，乡人合辞列君于县、于州、于部刺史，州遣从事即其庐劳君，且问状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275652_comment'></div>君固谢：「此人子之常，不愿赏」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275652_comment'></div>邻里要说再三，迄不能强。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275652_comment'></div>予闻而太息，世衰道微，或伪孝以奸利，君躬人之所难，乃以常自居，匪质之厚不能也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275652_comment'></div>以君之质而约之以礼，翼之以师友，可涯哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275652_comment'></div>君讳蕴，字季发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275652_comment'></div>曾祖训，祖琳，父中立，占籍婺之义乌，乡则崇德也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275652_comment'></div>娶周氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275652_comment'></div>男五，长公重、蚤夭，次孟恺、仲恺、叔恺、季恺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275652_comment'></div>女五，婿曰黄昭祖、何尧夫、杨若讷、龚世英，季未行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1275652_comment'></div>以乾道七年十月初四日终于家，寿七十有一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1275652_comment'></div>明年十二月二十日，葬于盘松里九江原，距先墓才数十步，成君志也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1275652_comment'></div>君少游场屋，亲终即罢举，环舍培松菊自娱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1275652_comment'></div>意独乡古，岁时祭享，撤楮币，去浮图、老子之位，终君世巫祝不至门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1275652_comment'></div>性刚介，朋友有过，每面数之，然遇困踬者，亦发橐赈恤，无所靳，故皆严惮之而不敢怨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1275652_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_1275652'>跨都而议，觕得其肤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1275652_comment'></div>坐闾而语，釐锱析铢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1275652_comment'></div>乌伤之评，于君则俞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1275652_comment'></div>次诗伐石，贲于幽墟。</div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1275652_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1174&endYear=1174')">1174年</a>　作《送朱叔赐赴闽中》二首。二首之一。<div id='poem_94060' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_94060' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/94060?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送朱叔赐赴闽中幕府二首<span class='inlineComment2'>（淳熙元年）</span><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1174年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_94060")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_94060_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_94060'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_94060'>止戈堂上屐声閒，飞盖相追杳霭间。<div id='poem_sentence_0_94060_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_94060'>君到定知难入眼，倚天灊霍是家山。<div id='poem_sentence_1_94060_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_94060'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_94060_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_94059' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_94059' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/94059?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1174年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_94059_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_94059'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_94059'>路逢十客九衿青，半是同窗旧弟兄。<div id='poem_sentence_0_94059_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_94059'>最忆市桥灯火静，巷南巷北读书声。<div id='poem_sentence_1_94059_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_94059'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_94059_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年1月</a>　在明招。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年2月</a>　在明招，作文盛赞袁枢作《通鉴》，并发其微旨。作品：《袁机仲国录通鉴纪事本末后》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷七。）</span><div id='poem_1275515' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275515' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275515?labeling=true' target='_blank'>书袁机仲国录通鉴纪事本末后</a><span class='authorDate'>（1175年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275515")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275515_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275515'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275515'>《通鉴纪事本末》，袁子所辑，章首则杨子之笔也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275515_comment'></div>庚寅、辛卯之间，袁、杨风节，隐然在两学间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275515_comment'></div>予辱为僚，相与讲肄，盖日有得焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275515_comment'></div>忧患索居，旧业湮废，袁子官旁郡，悯其孤陋，乃以是书开予。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275515_comment'></div>予慨然曰：《通鉴》之行百年矣，综理经纬，学者鲜或知之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275515_comment'></div>习其读而不识其纲，则所同病也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275515_comment'></div>今袁子掇其体大者，区别终始，使司马公之微旨自是可考，躬其难而遗学者以易，意亦笃矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275515_comment'></div>昔者司马公与二刘氏、范氏，翻中秘外邸之书馀二十年，其定为二百九十四卷者，盖百取其一，千取其十也，览者犹难之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275515_comment'></div>若袁子之纪本末，亦自其少年玩绎参订，本之以经术，验之以世故，广之以四方贤士大夫之议论，而后部居条流，较然易见，夫岂一日之积哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275515_comment'></div>学者毋徒乐其易而深思其所以难，则几矣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1275515_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年3月21日</a>　携潘景宪自婺出发赴闽访朱熹，始作《入闽录》<br /></div><div class='label1' id='5e880bf9eff24fe7b1bf4184727cdd88_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("5e880bf9eff24fe7b1bf4184727cdd88");'><span id='5e880bf9eff24fe7b1bf4184727cdd88_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1176')">1175-1176年</a>，39-40岁</div><div id='5e880bf9eff24fe7b1bf4184727cdd88' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年6月</a>　过三衢归婺州，作书与陈亮，论其《三国纪年序引》与诸人物赞作法，强调以论者言之，蜀当继汉为正统。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年6月</a>　致书邢邦用，讲为学之法。作品：《与邢邦用》一。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷十。）</span><div id='poem_1275407' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275407' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275407?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与邢邦用书<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其四 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1175年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275407")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275407_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275407'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275407'>某自明招入城，复至衢、婺两境迓大人之归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275407_comment'></div>弛担方半月，侍旁闭户读书，渐觉成趣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275407_comment'></div>向时过从士子往来者，不过时有三数辈耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275407_comment'></div>累求祠未报，而有召试之命，已复申前请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275407_comment'></div>倘得如志，得以一意休愒为学，侥倖多矣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1275407_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年6月</a>　作书与张栻，言及朱熹修养尚有不足处。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年7月</a>　致书与陈亮，约会见，并详论其《三国纪年序引》之不足。作品：《与陈同甫》十一。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷十。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年</a>　门人刘刚中之父刘国华葬。吕祖谦至武义会葬。因游刘氏山园，有诗。作品：《题刘氏绿映亭》二首之一。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷一。）</span>《题刘氏绿映亭》二首之二。<span
