class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷一。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年7月</a>　应刘刚中请，为其父刘国华作墓铭。作品：《通判沅州刘公墓志铭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷十一。）</span><div id='poem_1275662' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275662' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275662?labeling=true' target='_blank'>通判沅州刘公墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（淳熙二年七月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275662")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275662_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275662'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275662'>淳熙二年秋七月甲辰，朝奉郎、通判沅州军州事、赐绯鱼袋刘公及其夫人赵氏，合葬于婺州武义太平乡之清溪原，其孤刚中先期请曰：「吾父、吾母携持小子，至于湖水之北、沅水之旁，而大弃之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275662_comment'></div>累然孤身，东望故乡数千里，乃负乃载，乃陟乃降，更一寒暑，而柩克达于家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275662_comment'></div>躬锸肩畚，祓除榛翳，乃规乃恳，乃涂乃甃，又一寒暑而葬克安于兆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275662_comment'></div>惟是识竁之铭，苟有辞以质诸幽，刚中死且不朽」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275662_comment'></div>予游公父子间旧矣，其何可辞？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275662_comment'></div>公讳邦光，字国华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275662_comment'></div>曾祖政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275662_comment'></div>祖仲申，将作监主簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275662_comment'></div>考绘，赠通议大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275662_comment'></div>妣何氏，累赠太硕人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275662_comment'></div>公少尝举进士，一上不第，妻父广陵侯任以官，主邵武之光泽簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275662_comment'></div>土俗多盗，枹鼓鸣，尉、巡检悉所部奔命，邑虚无备，奸侠睥睨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275662_comment'></div>公与令议，籍材勇蠲其徭役，县兵或尽出，俾之捍防，居者始得奠枕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275662_comment'></div>徙处之遂昌令，始视事，阅杨氏讼，母子兄弟更忿阋，更数政不能决。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275662_comment'></div>公亲以酒酌其母，喻以天性之爱，皆感悟，数年之讼，一朝而平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275662_comment'></div>用荐者改秩，知湖州长兴县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275662_comment'></div>岁恶，发圭田之粟为民先，赵夫人亦脱簪珥为粥以食饿者，邑人纪之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1275662_comment'></div>终事沅州，安静不扰，没而有馀思焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1275662_comment'></div>其卒实乾道九年十月二日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1275662_comment'></div>赵夫人盖怀王宗暄之曾孙，济国公仲訦之孙，而广陵侯士碝之女也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1275662_comment'></div>虽出公族，能自屈卑服妇事，族娅无违言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1275662_comment'></div>母文安郡章夫人，嫠居旁郡，夫人奏芳鲜，问寒燠，凡可娱其老者无不用其极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1275662_comment'></div>以郊恩封孺人，前公一岁，正月十二日卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1275662_comment'></div>一男，刚中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1275662_comment'></div>一女，适奉议郎、新通判无为军梁桷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1275662_comment'></div>孙男一，女四。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1275662_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_1275662'>刘为温人，其徙则婺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1275662_comment'></div>八世其昌，迎天之祜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1275662_comment'></div>骈青联紫，覃延厥宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1275662_comment'></div>公居其间，别驾治中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1275662_comment'></div>沅江之祖，民夷罢市。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1275662_comment'></div>清溪之会，里人是记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1275662_comment'></div>维祢相望，俪实同藏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1275662_comment'></div>于窆有石，款诗在旁。</div><div id='poem_sentence_33_1275662_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年8月1日</a>　复归明招山。阅《通鉴》，有标抹本。学子多有来从学者。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年8月</a>　作王某挽章。作品：《王通直挽章》<div id='poem_94083' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_94083' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/94083?labeling=true' target='_blank'>王通直挽章<span class='inlineComment2'>（淳熙二年八月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1175年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_94083")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_94083_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_94083'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_94083'>近来南国冢，半是北人坟。<div id='poem_sentence_0_94083_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_94083'>异县谁怜我，同乡又失君。<div id='poem_sentence_1_94083_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_94083'>深居传雅尚，坚坐挹清芬。<div id='poem_sentence_2_94083_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_94083'>日落长安第，三槐拂暮云。<div id='poem_sentence_3_94083_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_94083'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_94083_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年9月</a>　作刘某挽章。作品：《刘梧州挽章》<div id='poem_94087' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_94087' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/94087?labeling=true' target='_blank'>刘梧州挽章<span class='inlineComment2'>（淳熙二年八月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1175年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_94087")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_94087_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_94087'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_94087'>驷马高车照路光，幡然改辙兴何长。<div id='poem_sentence_0_94087_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_94087'>空山猿鹤惊无恙，同社鸡豚乐未央。<div id='poem_sentence_1_94087_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_94087'>祗见岁华来冉冉，不知耆旧去堂堂。<div id='poem_sentence_2_94087_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_94087'>北邙道上麒麟冢，谁得归休十载强。<div id='poem_sentence_3_94087_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_94087'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_94087_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年9月</a>　陈傅良门人林安之来访。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年9月</a>　叶衡罢相归婺州，吕祖谦下旬自明招山还婺州与相见。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年9月</a>　应门人曹起宗之请，为其父曹烨作墓铭。作品：《金华曹君墓志铭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷十一。）</span><div id='poem_1275663' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275663' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275663?labeling=true' target='_blank'>金华曹君墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（淳熙二年九月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275663")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275663_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275663'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275663'>君讳晔，字彦华，姓曹氏，东阳金华人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275663_comment'></div>其先避五季之乱，自桐庐徙焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275663_comment'></div>曾祖伯夔，祖君宝，考熙，皆不仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275663_comment'></div>君少愿悫居闾里，畏事自守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275663_comment'></div>与人交，曲有恩意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275663_comment'></div>不忍岸狱之苦，夏置汤沐、冬市薪炭输之，岁以为常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275663_comment'></div>卒以淳熙二年三月八日，享年六十有八。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275663_comment'></div>是岁九月二十八日，葬于婺女乡盘龙岭之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275663_comment'></div>其配施氏祔焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275663_comment'></div>三子：曰起宗，曰绍宗，曰世昌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275663_comment'></div>一女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275663_comment'></div>孙男女凡四，皆幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275663_comment'></div>君笃意教子，起宗、世昌皆从予游，将葬，拜哭请铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275663_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_1275663'>出入里门，顺而祗兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275663_comment'></div>纳子于庠，俨履綦兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275663_comment'></div>令龟献兆，告厥时兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275663_comment'></div>我作斯铭，燕其归兮。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1275663_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年9月</a>　陈亮请吕祖谦为祖父作墓铭，为作。作品：《永康陈君迪功墓志铭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷十二。）</span><div id='poem_1275667' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275667' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275667?labeling=true' target='_blank'>永康陈君迪功墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（淳熙二年九月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275667")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275667_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275667'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275667'>陈在婺为右族，名数布于七县，其谱或通族为之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275667_comment'></div>其籍永康之前黄者，不知于婺何别也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275667_comment'></div>盖传至数世而得高安府君，而前黄之陈始为儒家，邑人纪焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275667_comment'></div>公讳持，字守之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275667_comment'></div>质厚而悫，蚤以事母闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275667_comment'></div>隆于兄弟，白首无违言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275667_comment'></div>迩之里闾，远之郡国，所交耋稚良楛不同，一接以恩意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275667_comment'></div>年十三，入郡庠，下笔亹亹，诸生皆畏避之，意气甚盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275667_comment'></div>已而靖康之难，其父赴京师捍御，没不反，家事益落，遂连蹇不耦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275667_comment'></div>绍兴开太学，故时侪辈强之行，公勉为出，即缀弟子员。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275667_comment'></div>往来二十年，竟无所遇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275667_comment'></div>晚以累举恩授迪功郎、筠州高安县主簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275667_comment'></div>或谓钩校朱墨，殆非老人所宜，而公耆事乐识，蚤夜不怠，若欲少自见者，诸公稍稍知之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275667_comment'></div>代还，未及调官，以淳熙二年八月十一日卒于家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275667_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275667_comment'></div>士方少时，心壮力强，谓天下事直差易耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275667_comment'></div>年运而往，更涉险难，仅得一官，欣然俯首就之，姑以少偿其铅椠之劳，曾不得须臾以死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1275667_comment'></div>盛衰之变，可胜道哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1275667_comment'></div>公雅能自宽，婆娑嬉游，无憔悴留落态。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1275667_comment'></div>暇则为诗文自娱，至老不辍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1275667_comment'></div>有《左氏国类》二十卷、《遂志斋录》十卷、《筠阳杂箸》二卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1275667_comment'></div>以其年九月二十四日葬于朱旺，距所居五里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1275667_comment'></div>曾祖讳援；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1275667_comment'></div>祖讳贺；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1275667_comment'></div>考讳知元，承节郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1275667_comment'></div>公享年七十有二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1275667_comment'></div>娶蔡氏，敦武郎秉圭之女，前公十五年卒，今祔公葬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1275667_comment'></div>子男一人，次皋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1275667_comment'></div>女一人，适进士曹源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1275667_comment'></div>孙男五人，长曰充，馀尚幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1275667_comment'></div>予虽未及识公，而公之从孙亮相与友，实来速铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1275667_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_31_1275667'>髧如髫如，孙箧之初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1275667_comment'></div>阅五星终，甫从走趋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1275667_comment'></div>不酢其勤，卧起于于。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1275667_comment'></div>命也奈何，保于其墟。</div><div id='poem_sentence_34_1275667_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年9月</a>　应门人徐文虎之请，为其父徐时乂作墓铭。作品：《分水徐君墓志铭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷十二。）</span><div id='poem_1275665' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275665' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275665?labeling=true' target='_blank'>分水徐君墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（淳熙三年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275665")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275665_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275665'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275665'>广川穹谷之间，群然而居，熙然而游，生无爵，死无谥，灏灏乎太古同风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275665_comment'></div>改其乡之旧，封之表之，斲雕以铭之，无乃放于文而没其质乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275665_comment'></div>惟孝子慈孙，哀其亲之志盖无终穷，欲托于辞以发其中心之至痛，固非所以为文也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275665_comment'></div>自予屏处里闾，四方之士，或不鄙辱，从予游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275665_comment'></div>有徐生文虎者，来自严之分水，相与居者数年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275665_comment'></div>今年春，衰杖款门，出其考之世系，拜且泣，蕲得铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275665_comment'></div>予以游居之旧不可却，乃次第其本末以遗之归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275665_comment'></div>君讳时乂，字亨仲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275665_comment'></div>曾祖宝，祖宗永，父舜元，皆不仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275665_comment'></div>分水地狭而瘠，山居其九而田居其一，故其民大氐行贾，铢裒釐积，堇堇自足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275665_comment'></div>君幼尝爱书，中遭家难，虽辍业从其俗，而于昆弟，厚薄多寡，一无所计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275665_comment'></div>趣其子从师友讲习甚笃，至课试利不利则未尝深督过之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275665_comment'></div>与乡人处无违言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275665_comment'></div>其没也，吊者皆有戚容，寿七十有一，实淳熙二年八月四日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275665_comment'></div>是岁九月二十八日，葬于县南涌泉岩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275665_comment'></div>娶丁氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275665_comment'></div>三子，长文渊，次即文虎、文富。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1275665_comment'></div>二女，将仕郎沈俊彦、进士俞哲，其婿也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1275665_comment'></div>铭之作，后其葬盖一年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1275665_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_1275665'>葬以其乡，铭以其子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1275665_comment'></div>泉冽麓深，尚安于此。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1275665_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年9月</a>　为曹佃作墓铭。作品：《金华曹君将仕墓志铭》<div id='poem_1275668' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275668' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275668?labeling=true' target='_blank'>金华曹君将仕墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（淳熙二年十月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275668")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275668_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275668'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275668'>国朝之开吴越，凡板授之秩皆命以王官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275668_comment'></div>金华之曹，有以司录从其主朝京师者，未及颁爵而卒，子孙因不仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275668_comment'></div>推其谱，由司录而下，三传曰随，四传曰介，五传曰韶，六传而得公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275668_comment'></div>公讳佃，字耕道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275668_comment'></div>少游郡庠，贡法犹未罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275668_comment'></div>既升于辟廱矣，睦寇乱东南，亟舍以归，已而仍岁执大丧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275668_comment'></div>公为人閒澹，其随群辈上下，徒欲虞其亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275668_comment'></div>自是遂绝意进取，阖门以书史自适且数十年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275668_comment'></div>今天子即位，下赦令在贡籍久故者予初等官，欲得祠禄者畀之，毋拘以吏部格，公于是例补将仕郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275668_comment'></div>始命，一御冠裳拜于庭，退则褐衣如他日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275668_comment'></div>同等多已受禄，或谓公盍亦自言，公谢不答。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275668_comment'></div>异时朝路戚友力能得之者甚众，娄以谂公，卒亦不能强也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275668_comment'></div>季年神观平粹，瞻听疏彻，道学校旧闻、京辅遗事，语端络绎无穷，听者忘倦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275668_comment'></div>内外亲伏腊燕聚，黄发鸠杖，皤然在位，长少䜣䜣就列，皆视归于公，弟顺之风兴焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275668_comment'></div>元配汪氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275668_comment'></div>次配时氏，其先夫亦汪也，死于寇，独遗二稚女，公为置后，悉授以先君之财，二女亦皆得其所从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275668_comment'></div>当是时，郡县新被兵，条纲未立，乏祀之家彊弗友者并缘姻连，或更券剂以自利，故人以公为难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1275668_comment'></div>公虽不试于事，经界之兴也，吏骇于创见，莫知所为，公与为甲长，令以公儒者倚属之，公亦乐为之尽，故视旁邑力半而功倍焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1275668_comment'></div>其没以淳熙二年八月丙辰，享年八十有五。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1275668_comment'></div>一子，次何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1275668_comment'></div>一女，适承议郎、新通判建宁府王涣，其孙女复适涣之子楷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1275668_comment'></div>五孙：著、庄、𦬊、蒙、芬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1275668_comment'></div>曾孙六，尚幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1275668_comment'></div>以其年十月乙酉，葬于赤松乡沙溪原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1275668_comment'></div>时夫人前公八年卒，实同兆异域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1275668_comment'></div>铭之曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_1275668'>畸于其出，退之所繇坚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1275668_comment'></div>啬于其禄，齿之所繇蕃也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1275668_comment'></div>有崇彼丘，其亦莫之干也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1275668_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年9月</a>　为方元恪作墓铭。作品：《严陵方君墓志铭》<div id='poem_1275664' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275664' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275664?labeling=true' target='_blank'>严陵方君墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（淳熙二年九月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275664")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275664_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275664'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275664'>桐君所庐下上数十里间，言台者以严遵，言石者以郭文，言山者以戴颙，其迹皆隐者之遗迹，其绪或没不见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275664_comment'></div>独白云原唐末方处士干始居之，后出而枝叶最蕃，一原数百家，联谱合牒，衣冠人物之盛，邦人纪之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275664_comment'></div>至于里居之良，虽事业无所试，厖然秀眉，集享全福，彼其中盖可占也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275664_comment'></div>君讳元恪，字几先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275664_comment'></div>少游郡庠，已而舍业归养，惇俭经缉，以厚其生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275664_comment'></div>既衍既盈，则推以覆被其族而覃其乡闾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275664_comment'></div>饭饥薪寒，槥死药疾，旁及桥梁涂路之属，力之所逮者，未尝有爱焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275664_comment'></div>故秘书监元若于诸方为长，望临搢绅，遴于许可，顾独乐君之淳固，恩意笃备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275664_comment'></div>异日干戈抢攘，中朝名胜，往往来依秘监，嘉时令节，杯酒流行，谈赏讽咏，听者皆倾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275664_comment'></div>君颓然在席，漠乎不以槩意，人亦莫能轻重浅深之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275664_comment'></div>绍兴己卯，诏赐高年爵，授承务郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275664_comment'></div>久之，复用恩增秩承奉郎，贲以银绯，于是君年八十矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275664_comment'></div>命服在躬，子孙诸婿，簪笏成列，耳目肤革，视前日既无所损，而光耀舄奕，处之夷澹，视前日亦无所加也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275664_comment'></div>如是康宁者又十馀年，年九十有二，以淳熙二年七月癸巳终于家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275664_comment'></div>曾祖仁拱，祖举中，考玠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275664_comment'></div>娶陈氏，先卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275664_comment'></div>二子：伯曰行之，迪功郎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1275664_comment'></div>仲曰望之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1275664_comment'></div>一女，归吴寘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1275664_comment'></div>孙八人：炳，迪功郎、南剑州司户参军；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1275664_comment'></div>次烨、煜、焕、炤、烜、焞、炜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1275664_comment'></div>女孙七人，迪功郎、建康府上元县尉郑尧，从政郎、平江府府学教授刘适正，朝奉郎、新知江州范端臣、王璞、钱膺、王中，实其婿也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1275664_comment'></div>季者在室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1275664_comment'></div>曾孙男五，女七。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1275664_comment'></div>男之长者曰楶、曰㮤，馀未名；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1275664_comment'></div>女之长者适沈宏祖，次适詹孝述，馀未行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1275664_comment'></div>玄孙女三人，尚幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1275664_comment'></div>葬以其年九月辛酉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1275664_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_1275664'>坐阅六朝，不出户庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1275664_comment'></div>云来四世，陪导緌缨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1275664_comment'></div>吊壮北原，唁殇东坰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1275664_comment'></div>大耋一丘，休哉永宁。</div><div id='poem_sentence_31_1275664_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年9月</a>　为刘墉作墓铭。作品：《刘梧州墓志铭》<div id='poem_1275666' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275666' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275666?labeling=true' target='_blank'>刘梧州墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（淳熙二年九月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275666")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275666_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275666'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275666'>梧州刺史刘公食祠官之禄于里中，暇日子孙侍左右，公命之曰：「大夫七十而致事，礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275666_comment'></div>吾赖先人馀泽，服王事者五十年，以爵以齿，幸济登兹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275666_comment'></div>若免于官谤，以朝大夫秩老于家，岂小子实能，吾先祖先父其嘉相之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275666_comment'></div>汝趣为我具章」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275666_comment'></div>皆顿首曰诺，如大人命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275666_comment'></div>章上，诏报可，赐一子官，以宠其归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275666_comment'></div>同邑若旁邑之姻连世旧，舟于水，车于陆，凑门趋贺，乐饭旬日乃罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275666_comment'></div>自是遂深居不出，静养恬适。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275666_comment'></div>又数年乃卒，寿七十有四，实淳熙二年正月晦日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275666_comment'></div>其年九月丙午，葬于婺州武义县泉溪西山学士原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275666_comment'></div>其孤以公之阀阅、行治来速铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275666_comment'></div>谨按泉溪刘氏，系出温之荆溪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275666_comment'></div>其徙于武义，距公盖八世矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275666_comment'></div>公讳墉，字叔翰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275666_comment'></div>曾祖仲思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275666_comment'></div>祖升，承事郎，赠中奉大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275666_comment'></div>考滂，朝请郎、知建昌军，赠光禄大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1275666_comment'></div>妣汤氏，赠齐安郡夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1275666_comment'></div>公蚤以光禄恤典入官，历温州乐清县尉、监潭州南岳庙、福州录事参军，知徽州歙县，通判蕲州军州事，主管台州崇道观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1275666_comment'></div>除知梧州，未上，复请还崇道观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1275666_comment'></div>积官至朝请大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1275666_comment'></div>其在乐清，每行部，舆卫胥史，鞋屦糗粮，一主办于己，不以烦里正，邑人纪之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1275666_comment'></div>福大而狱繁，歙小而民瘠，公书狱：「予生而拊民，必依惠」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1275666_comment'></div>职用不堕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1275666_comment'></div>佐蕲，两摄黄守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1275666_comment'></div>始至，老校旅拜庭下，曰：「旄稚旦暮馁死，惟公哀之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1275666_comment'></div>视其券，不朌者且期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1275666_comment'></div>公蹴然不安，亟发库金，益以私帑，尪瘠以苏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1275666_comment'></div>归自蕲春，无复当世意，比告老，领祠官者四焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1275666_comment'></div>少嗜书，晚岁犹展玩不置。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1275666_comment'></div>每得名章俊语，辄欣然忘食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1275666_comment'></div>资和厚，不与物忤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1275666_comment'></div>居乡无贵贱，皆得其驩心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1275666_comment'></div>没之日，吊客及门，哭之必哀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1275666_comment'></div>初娶胡氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1275666_comment'></div>继室王氏，朝议大夫升之女，封宜人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1275666_comment'></div>三子：长晫，迪功郎、绍兴府上虞县主簿，先卒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1275666_comment'></div>次绍，迪功郎、处州青田县主簿；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1275666_comment'></div>次续，将仕郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1275666_comment'></div>一女，适朝散郎、通判婺州林信厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1275666_comment'></div>孙男三人：成孙、传孙、豹孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1275666_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_41_1275666'>前望不跂，后顾不庳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1275666_comment'></div>平进之辙，未驱而止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1275666_comment'></div>其止曷以，以其乐易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1275666_comment'></div>风于后人，勿坠勿替。</div><div id='poem_sentence_44_1275666_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年闰9月</a>　复书周必大荐士约，冀其多得实材。作品：《与周丞相》五。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷九。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年闰9月</a>　陈亮来信讨论所删正《文中子》、《文中子序引》。吕祖谦复书评议，欲月内相见。作品：《与陈同甫》七。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷十。）</span><div id='poem_1275344' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275344' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275344?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与陈同甫书<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二十三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1175年闰9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275344")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275344_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275344'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275344'>前此幸得款聚，归涂亟欲投宿寿山，故不得复见，殊歉然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275344_comment'></div>辱手教，恭审剧暑，孝履支持。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275344_comment'></div>某归后十馀日，即为三衢之行，往反近两旬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275344_comment'></div>汪丈静阅之久，论事益深稳综练，因知经历信不可不多也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275344_comment'></div>示谕蔼然忠厚，有以知别后进德之深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275344_comment'></div>微指固已钦佩，第衰退之人，惟当闭门反己，著实以求其所未至，然此心则不敢忘也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275344_comment'></div>未往三衢时，吴益恭得半日款语，语间极称叶蔚宗之为人，尊兄同里闬，亦知其详否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275344_comment'></div>益恭亦甚以不得一见为恨也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275344_comment'></div>此月旦日，自三衢归，陆子静已相待累日，又留七八日，昨日始行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275344_comment'></div>笃实淳直工夫甚有力，朋游间未易多得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275344_comment'></div>渠云虽未相见识，每见吾兄文字开阔轩翥，甚欲得相聚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275344_comment'></div>觉其意勤甚，渠非论文者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275344_comment'></div>人回，略此上布，它祈厚为远业节抑。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1275344_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年10月1日</a>　作《台州修城记》，称赞州守赵汝愚不劳民而有功。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷六。）</span><div id='poem_1275596' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275596' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275596?labeling=true' target='_blank'>台州修城记</a><span class='authorDate'>（淳熙二年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275596")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275596_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275596'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275596'>临海郡南、东、西三方岸江湖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275596_comment'></div>秋水时至，北限大山，蹙不得骋，怒齧堤足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275596_comment'></div>生聚廪廪，恃城以为命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275596_comment'></div>距海馀百里，逋亡剽侠之所曹，恶岁辄睢盱洲溆，睥睨郛郭，徼警者不敢弛柝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275596_comment'></div>故闭修之政，在是郡为首务，盖所以远灾害、销奸萌，非徒区画封表，备侯邦之制也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275596_comment'></div>庆历之水，几不为郡，元章简公绛来守而城复立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275596_comment'></div>宣和中，盗发仙居，闯虚深入，肉薄欲登。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275596_comment'></div>时则有户掾滕君膺，帅厉吏士，圉以方略，寇不为患，父老纪焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275596_comment'></div>乾道九年，里旅不戒于火，延及郡城，堵隤甃陀径踰无禁，害气来格，民讹不宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275596_comment'></div>间一岁，太史赵侯汝愚自信徙镇，暇日循行廧落，属丞掾而告之曰：「置守所以卫民，顾屏蔽废撤若是，其何以待不虞？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275596_comment'></div>土功于古虽有常律，传《春秋》者复出启塞从时之例，岂非城闉之启塞，实有邦之大纪，随时筑治，有不得而已者耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275596_comment'></div>况壮城之卒，月粟岁帛，凡以为此益其食而宽其程，宜无不可」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275596_comment'></div>于是军事判官苏延寿受役要司輂辇金毂之稽，兵马都监胡胜督裁巡功，察其勉与不勉者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275596_comment'></div>命群有司各保其所奠地，守傅众力，埤增卑薄，涂塞空郤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275596_comment'></div>环城诸门，作新者四，曰镇宁、曰兴善、曰丰泰、曰栝苍；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275596_comment'></div>修旧者五，曰崇和、曰靖越、曰朝天、曰顺政、曰延庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275596_comment'></div>起淳熙二年六月癸酉，讫闰九月某日，累日积工，凡九千九百有八，大抵取具于壮城之籍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1275596_comment'></div>閒民愿即工者，厚酬之，不欲勿彊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1275596_comment'></div>会其数，视役兵财十之一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1275596_comment'></div>鍜斲、镘塈、黝垩之工，畀僦直如其素。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1275596_comment'></div>醪醴之馈，劳来之问，相及于道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1275596_comment'></div>其材瓦石甓之用，积若干万若干千若干百。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1275596_comment'></div>钱以贯计、米以石计者，合若干千若干百有奇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1275596_comment'></div>维侯忧民急病之意既达于下，而精知周虑，又足以综理之，故公无羡费，人无留力，工无馀技。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1275596_comment'></div>役事首尾历再时，版锸并作，观堞堀兴，而近郊之氓初未尝释垄亩也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1275596_comment'></div>始侯之至，诏奉计最朝十月报政之期，甫半岁而赢，或谓是邦特侯假道休沐之地，缮营之钜者，必姑存以须后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1275596_comment'></div>乃独于入国阡陌未习之时，骤举力政，百年之迹，还于指顾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1275596_comment'></div>邦人德其赐而乐其成，请书劳于石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1275596_comment'></div>抑不知因事而功见，已事而迹泯，一垒培之绪业，于侯何有哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1275596_comment'></div>至于不以久暂易意，眇然长虑于耳目之外，以无负于寄诿，识此者盖亦鲜矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1275596_comment'></div>遂书以谂台之君子。</div><div id='poem_sentence_30_1275596_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年10月</a>　应陈傅良之请，为林安之作墓铭。作品：《林安之墓志铭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷十二。）</span><div id='poem_1275671' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275671' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275671?labeling=true' target='_blank'>林安之墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（淳熙二年十二月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275671")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275671_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275671'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275671'>自予与永嘉陈君举傅艮游，每道其学者林安之居实不去口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275671_comment'></div>岁在壬辰，安之始来婺，相与共学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275671_comment'></div>其冬以病归，间二年复自温来会，甚瘠且惫，形貌非复昔人，而志愈强识愈明，其学亦非复昔人也，予忧喜参半。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275671_comment'></div>别去馀月，君举以书赴曰：「噫，安之死矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275671_comment'></div>哀甚，不能执笔，其为我铭之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275671_comment'></div>盖安之之为人，隆于师友，一日不见则惝然若有所亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275671_comment'></div>至其合堂同席，心融意浃，身之休戚、年之蚤莫、乡闾之远若近，皆不暇知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275671_comment'></div>病益侵，尚讲贯绎绎不休，献疑者、纳忠者、代之忧者、动之以危语悲辞者，日交于前，安之盖自如也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275671_comment'></div>士而有志于学者盖鲜，亦既有其意矣，怵焉辄移，挠焉辄止，莫大于死生，莫切于疾疢疴痛之贼其体肤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275671_comment'></div>及是而犹不舍业，使充其志，庸可限其所至耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275671_comment'></div>安之以淳熙二年十月十九日卒，是岁十二月二十日，其父母兄葬之于其乡，年实三十有四。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275671_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_1275671'>若是而不可谓之成耶，彼挑达者竟何成也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275671_comment'></div>若是而可谓之成耶，夫岂自以为成也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275671_comment'></div>哀哉！</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1275671_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年11月</a>　应抚州守赵烨请，为作《抚州新作浮桥记》，记其捐资作桥解民之困。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷六。）</span><div id='poem_1275597' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275597' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275597?labeling=true' target='_blank'>抚州新作浮桥记<span class='inlineComment2'>（淳熙间）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1175年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275597")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275597_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275597'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275597'>抚之溪故无桥，乾道初元，知州事陈侯森始作浮梁，以通往来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275597_comment'></div>淳熙二年秋七月，甚雨，淫潦漂航断笮，无一存者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275597_comment'></div>吾友赵景明适为此州，复新之，以书请曰：「烨试郡未几而桥毁，约己啬用，不敢赋诸民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275597_comment'></div>造端以十月戊寅，告具以十一月丁丑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275597_comment'></div>部使者周侯嗣武实佐其费，而属役于知临川县江霖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275597_comment'></div>桥东西相维，其修百丈，联舟为梁，合五十有四艘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275597_comment'></div>愿记其成，以谂来者」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275597_comment'></div>予报之曰：桥梁，郡政之一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275597_comment'></div>子不忍涉者之病，政以时举，亦庶乎长民者之心矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275597_comment'></div>然城闉之近，易察也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275597_comment'></div>水潦之害，易知也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275597_comment'></div>道路之谤誉，易闻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275597_comment'></div>至于不瞩之地，未形之患，弗能自达之呻吟慨叹，昔之君子惴惴焉惟此之畏，子尚戒之哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275597_comment'></div>盖心不在民，固负于师帅父母之名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275597_comment'></div>虑不能周四封，则亦无以亢一方之任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275597_comment'></div>所存者笃，所综者博，其开塞建置，继此而讲者，则有次第矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275597_comment'></div>是桥也，特发政之始，邦人将惟子之视焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1275597_comment'></div>无是心而有是政者，否也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1275597_comment'></div>有是心而无是政，非制于上而不骋，则壅于下而不流也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1275597_comment'></div>抚去吾州且千里，孰临子上，孰承子下，吾皆不能知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1275597_comment'></div>独以桥役言之，有部使者劝相佽助，以启厥功；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1275597_comment'></div>有县令奔走服劳，以集厥事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1275597_comment'></div>以是而观子之州，上下之际辑矣，为子之所为，其何所惮，亦何所诿乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1275597_comment'></div>邦人匪徒子之视，将惟子之望且责也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1275597_comment'></div>因次其语，以遗抚人，俾立石水厓以俟。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1275597_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年11月</a>　开始修订《书说》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年12月</a>　为时汝翼作《金华时君德辅墓志铭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷十二。）</span><div id='poem_1275670' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275670' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275670?labeling=true' target='_blank'>金华时君德辅墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（淳熙二年十二月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275670")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275670_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275670'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275670'>婺之群室以地系姓者，皆其闻家，清江之时盖其一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275670_comment'></div>清江于婺为近郊，时氏之居，百年于此矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275670_comment'></div>君讳汝翼，字德辅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275670_comment'></div>为人庄整，寡言笑，重然诺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275670_comment'></div>少孤，更帮源之寇，馀屋数椽，勤俭自力，以封殖其家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275670_comment'></div>始而充，中而裕，末而丰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275670_comment'></div>其所以制节内外，临长族属，约敕童仆者，凛凛不可犯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275670_comment'></div>子若孙若子孙之妇，酬赠馈问必告，朌赋禀给必均，阖门千指，无敢私烹炊者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275670_comment'></div>岁时乡闾聚会，君在坐，谑者为止，哗者为默，其严惮之若是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275670_comment'></div>子孙胜衣冠以上，皆使之从师肄习。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275670_comment'></div>晨起盥栉，未问家事，亟往劳来之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275670_comment'></div>在塾者以次侍，各陈其业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275670_comment'></div>或当其意，欣然为之忘食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275670_comment'></div>虽有疾，闻弦诵声辄拊髀击节，不知病之去体也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275670_comment'></div>每言曰：「吾生而多难，不得极意于书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275670_comment'></div>今老矣，平生所嗜销落向尽，独于文墨眷眷有馀怀，儿曹其尚成吾志乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275670_comment'></div>里中畯秀，后出新进，皆折辈行与交。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1275670_comment'></div>门临逵道，道上往来者装赍类逢掖，辄延致之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1275670_comment'></div>偶得胜士，馆饩款绎，连日夜不厌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1275670_comment'></div>于禨祥禁忌无所信，尝大筑垣屋，邻人挟方士以进，曰是太岁所直，犯之且有大殃，君不为辍，卒亦无他。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1275670_comment'></div>先墓在舍东数里，岁远芜废，君次第经缉，自始祖而下十馀冢，甓甃榱桷，髹垩相照，春秋帅其族洒扫，终其世不怠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1275670_comment'></div>君没以淳熙元年七月二十五日，享年六十有五。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1275670_comment'></div>明年十二月初七日，葬于循理乡九里原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1275670_comment'></div>曾祖则，祖理，考焕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1275670_comment'></div>娶邵氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1275670_comment'></div>三子：镐、锜、錝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1275670_comment'></div>二女，邵晏、陈褒其婿也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1275670_comment'></div>孙男七：沄、源、淇、演、溱、法、潚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1275670_comment'></div>女长适陈之望，馀尚幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1275670_comment'></div>予与君兄之子铸皆癸未进士，自锜以下，多从予游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1275670_comment'></div>晚始识君，则既病矣，犹危坐相对，指授顾役，皆中品式。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1275670_comment'></div>时氏之昌也，有以哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1275670_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_32_1275670'>既圮而升，将队而兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1275670_comment'></div>饬家以严，子孙绳绳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1275670_comment'></div>胜复合离，靡所止戾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1275670_comment'></div>尚承其初，之铭之视。</div><div id='poem_sentence_35_1275670_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年12月</a>　应门人王颐之请，为其父王恬作墓铭。作品：《永康王君墓志铭》<div id='poem_1275669' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275669' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275669?labeling=true' target='_blank'>永康王君墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（淳熙二年十二月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275669")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275669_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275669'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275669'>始予官太学，日从四方之士游，于永康王颐者一再见，气下而语温，予洒然异之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275669_comment'></div>退质其同舍生，杂然许其修谨，无异辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275669_comment'></div>自余还金华，于永康为旁县，益习其为人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275669_comment'></div>他日衰绖踵门，拜且泣曰：「颐不孝，将奉考妣之丧归于吾邑白眉山之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275669_comment'></div>昊天罔极，亡以自致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275669_comment'></div>昔者敦化之席，颐幸有位焉，敢扳此义，问铭于门下」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275669_comment'></div>乃序次而述之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275669_comment'></div>君讳恬，字道夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275669_comment'></div>其先来自天台，距今七世矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275669_comment'></div>曾祖利用，祖自然，父有朋，世为儒家，以惇饬相授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275669_comment'></div>子弟拱立父兄侧，竟日不敢跛倚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275669_comment'></div>长者对客，其亚虽发有二色，犹奉匜洗爵，奔走执事，里中诸儒皆自以为不及也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275669_comment'></div>君就学未几，不忍尊老亲井臼之劳，亟废业以专子职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275669_comment'></div>出入阡陌，与物少忤，质朴和厚，不知世间有钩谲廋谑事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275669_comment'></div>自少至老，以畏谨持门户，府县之庭无履迹焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275669_comment'></div>家虽贫，遇人急难，时弛服辍食以周之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275669_comment'></div>岁入甚微，或意君长者，夺攘无所忌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1275669_comment'></div>君果不校，其友尤之，君曰：「吾岂以尺寸地败宗姻恩义哉」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1275669_comment'></div>娶同县吕师传之女，亦与君协德，服廑妇事，不择剧易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1275669_comment'></div>继母嫠，姊穷无依，迎致馈养，没身不衰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1275669_comment'></div>实生五子：颐、颖、觊、颀、硕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1275669_comment'></div>一女，适进士刘鼎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1275669_comment'></div>男孙女孙合六人，皆幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1275669_comment'></div>盖君寿六十有五，卒以淳熙元年十二月十日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1275669_comment'></div>吕夫人寿五十九，卒以乾道七年八月三日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1275669_comment'></div>其葬以淳熙二年十二月五日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1275669_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_1275669'>其生也足不出乎里，其死也葬不出乎乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1275669_comment'></div>敦然太朴，帅彼民常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1275669_comment'></div>是谓吉人之藏。</div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1275669_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年12月</a>　应门人徐一夔之请，为其父徐宗盛作墓铭。作品：《徐君墓志铭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史外集》卷五。）</span><div id='poem_1275686' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275686' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275686?labeling=true' target='_blank'>徐君墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（淳熙二年十二月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275686")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275686_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275686'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275686'>明招，婺之名山，予家三世葬焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275686_comment'></div>负山之民，气俗敦悫，乐田亩而畏官府，傲嬉侈丽之习，独不入其乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275686_comment'></div>予岁时上冢，过其父老，或旬月忘返，稍稍遣子弟从予游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275686_comment'></div>未几，方领矩步，俨然出与郡邑之士齿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275686_comment'></div>盖将继此益进而熏沐之，则于其亲之丧，亟问亟吊，而又为之铭，有所不得已也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275686_comment'></div>君讳宗盛，字德元，以愿朴称于里闾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275686_comment'></div>淳熙元年五月十五日卒，享年三十有八。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275686_comment'></div>明年十二月五日，葬于乡之下车塘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275686_comment'></div>君无恙时，实命其子一夔来请业，及是复来请铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275686_comment'></div>文弊甚矣，幸是乡质之未彫也，申之孝弟之义，引翼充养，于古之学者或庶几焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275686_comment'></div>苟自厌其质而文华是耆，外观日胜，中实日销，则岂父兄所以属予之意哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275686_comment'></div>遂并书于君之圹，以识其初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275686_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_1275686'>父菑子播兮，将求其实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275686_comment'></div>道阻且脩兮，无辱斯石。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1275686_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年12月</a>　邢邦杰去世，为作祭文。作品：《祭邢邦杰》<div id='poem_1275704' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275704' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275704?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭邢邦杰文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1175年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275704")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275704_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275704'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275704'>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275704_comment'></div>越绝之区，学者方兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275704_comment'></div>一门孝友，旧推诸邢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275704_comment'></div>内外交映，韡韡嘤嘤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275704_comment'></div>人之可愿，于子而并。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275704_comment'></div>猗左提而右挈，纷前导而后承。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275704_comment'></div>霣霜雹于春阳，久此乐而莫能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275704_comment'></div>喟予戚于伤弓，骇弦音于䳭鸰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275704_comment'></div>陶近忧其未憖，集遐感而相仍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275704_comment'></div>理镜湖之桂楫，践前诺于岁更。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275704_comment'></div>访旧闻于故老，采新益于友朋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275704_comment'></div>怆独逢于仲氏，同此哀于折肱。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1275704_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年12月</a>　幼弟丧，至明招营丧。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年12月</a>　《近思录》刻板。吕祖谦与朱熹议朱塾婚事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年</a>　苏师德卒，为作挽幛二首。作品：《苏仁仲计议挽幛二首》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷一。）</span><div id='poem_94102' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_94102' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/94102?labeling=true' target='_blank'>苏仁仲计议挽章二首<span class='inlineComment2'>（师德）</span><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1175年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_94102")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_94102_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_94102'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_94102'>幽栖略具便休官，帝遣蒲轮唤不还。<div id='poem_sentence_0_94102_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_94102'>大似文元居道院，又如退<span class='inlineComment2'>（金华本作白）</span>傅过香山。<div id='poem_sentence_1_94102_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_94102'>梦回帷幄青冥上<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：尝为密院计议官。）</span>，醉堕风波浩荡间<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：尝谪汀州。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_94102_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_94102'>向使胸<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>中有荣辱，那能八十鬓毛班。<div id='poem_sentence_3_94102_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_94102'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_94102_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_94102'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_94102_0'>⑴ 二字原缺，据小集本、金华本补</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_94102_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_94101' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_94101' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/94101?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1175年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_94101_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_94101'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_94101'>登门畴昔奉从容，婺越之间一水通。<div id='poem_sentence_0_94101_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_94101'>今日江东无贺老，去年床下拜庞公。<div id='poem_sentence_1_94101_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_94101'>旧来论议多遗落，新出传闻或异同。<div id='poem_sentence_2_94101_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_94101'>已矣从谁判<span class='inlineComment2'>（原校：一作辨）</span>真赝，汗青连屋未施功。<div id='poem_sentence_3_94101_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_94101'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_94101_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年</a>　有《乙未手笔》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1176&endYear=1176')">1176年1月</a>　以邢邦杰去世，致书邢世材慰问，约其春暖讲论。作品：《与邢邦用》五。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷十。）</span><div id='poem_1275406' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275406' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275406?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与邢邦用书<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1176年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275406")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275406_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275406'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275406'>某自五月间亡妇之丧，冒暑治丧，悲怆疲薾，殊无聊赖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275406_comment'></div>祔葬甫毕，而闻张丈之出，又闻刘丈之讣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275406_comment'></div>出处死生，固亦常理，然消长之势如此，可惧可愕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275406_comment'></div>以是尤觉意绪忽忽，寝食殊少味也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1275406_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='c4507acb9b6b42ecb968db07eff6b20d_label'><a href='javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1176&endYear=1176')">1176年</a>，40岁</div><div id='c4507acb9b6b42ecb968db07eff6b20d' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1176&endYear=1176')">1176年1月18日</a>　自三衢归婺州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1176&endYear=1176')">1176年1月22日</a>　闻周必大升迁，有书冀其以国事为重。作品：《与周丞相》六。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷九。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1176&endYear=1176')">1176年1月</a>　致书陈亮，附寄《通鉴论》作品：《与陈同甫》十七。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷十。）</span><div id='poem_1275344' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275344' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275344?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与陈同甫书<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二十三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1175年闰9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275344")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275344_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275344'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275344'>前此幸得款聚，归涂亟欲投宿寿山，故不得复见，殊歉然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275344_comment'></div>辱手教，恭审剧暑，孝履支持。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275344_comment'></div>某归后十馀日，即为三衢之行，往反近两旬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275344_comment'></div>汪丈静阅之久，论事益深稳综练，因知经历信不可不多也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275344_comment'></div>示谕蔼然忠厚，有以知别后进德之深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275344_comment'></div>微指固已钦佩，第衰退之人，惟当闭门反己，著实以求其所未至，然此心则不敢忘也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275344_comment'></div>未往三衢时，吴益恭得半日款语，语间极称叶蔚宗之为人，尊兄同里闬，亦知其详否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275344_comment'></div>益恭亦甚以不得一见为恨也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275344_comment'></div>此月旦日，自三衢归，陆子静已相待累日，又留七八日，昨日始行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275344_comment'></div>笃实淳直工夫甚有力，朋游间未易多得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275344_comment'></div>渠云虽未相见识，每见吾兄文字开阔轩翥，甚欲得相聚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275344_comment'></div>觉其意勤甚，渠非论文者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275344_comment'></div>人回，略此上布，它祈厚为远业节抑。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1275344_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1176&endYear=1176')">1176年1月</a>　为吕祖平母作《方夫人志》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史外集》卷五。）</span><div id='poem_1275684' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275684' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275684?labeling=true' target='_blank'>方夫人志</a><span class='authorDate'>（淳熙三年二月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275684")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275684_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275684'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275684'>先夫人姓方氏，尚书驾部员外郎讳楷之曾孙，朝散郎、尚书屯田员外郎讳蒙之孙，朝散郎、知建州讳元矩、安人孔氏之女，我先君从事郎吕公讳某之配也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275684_comment'></div>外王父之没，夫人尚幼，服勤外王母左右，母子相恃为命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275684_comment'></div>盖生三十有一年而归于先君，又十一年先君即世，是时伯姊五岁，祖平财四岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275684_comment'></div>夫人提携鞠育，更历艰苦，十有八年，然后伯姊始出适迪功郎曾棐，祖平亦始得临安府司户参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275684_comment'></div>未及禄养，以淳熙二年十一月十五日不起，享年四十有八。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275684_comment'></div>吕氏自东莱公而下皆葬婺州武义县明招山，惟我先祖暨先君兆域别在信州上饶县之德源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275684_comment'></div>不肖孤哀荒颠冥，未克合祔，恐旦暮即死，不能终大事，亟以次年二月二十日奉夫人之丧葬于东莱公兆域之旁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275684_comment'></div>至于夫人志节履行之懿，则俟它日详焉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1275684_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1176&endYear=1176')">1176年3月23日</a>　长女华年归于进士潘景良。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1176&endYear=1176')">1176年3月</a>　有与周必大书谈及为学将循序渐进。作品：《与周丞相》八。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷九。）</span><div id='poem_1275267' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275267' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275267?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与周丞相子充书<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1176年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275267")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275267_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275267'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275267'>某八月末暂往会稽省外祖母，留二十馀日乃归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275267_comment'></div>初欲迤逦为天台、雁荡之行，偶得朱元晦书，欲来春同游，须少俟之，今冬遂不复出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275267_comment'></div>闭门却扫，乃无一事，读书亦稍有趣，第恨相望邈然，无由款奉燕谈，每深浩叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275267_comment'></div>迩来日用践修之详，与夫游泳笔墨，因风示以一二，沃此虚渴，不胜系望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275267_comment'></div>子中兄官期不远否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275267_comment'></div>会次望致敬仰之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275267_comment'></div>刘子澄时通问否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275267_comment'></div>近偶作哭苪丈十绝，向来欲出数语，中间忧制，故迤逦至今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275267_comment'></div>诗初非所习，正以其往时有不敢作诗之语。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275267_comment'></div>深愧此意，聊挂延陵之剑耳，亦漫录呈。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1275267_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1'
