ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1176&endYear=1176')">1176年5月</a>　作《读书记》，纵论读《诗》、《书》、《易》、《戴记》、《通鉴》、《左传》、西汉书、杜子美诗、韩退之、柳子厚等文，以为即此亦足以使人立世。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1176&endYear=1176')">1176年5月</a>　以郑伯熊入朝、郑鉴入对等事，致书周必大当爱养警惕。作品：《与周丞相》九。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷九。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1176&endYear=1176')">1176年夏</a>　有诗《宣城李君尝游东湖居士之门，袖诗见过次韵以谢》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1176&endYear=1176')">1176年7月10日</a>　迁塾于右司斋，复编《读诗记》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1176&endYear=1176')">1176年7月</a>　有代叔祖知录作《送宋子华通判长沙》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷一。）</span><div id='poem_94152' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_94152' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/94152?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送宋子华通判长沙<span class='inlineComment2'>（代叔祖知录作）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1176年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_94152")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_94152_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_94152'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_94152'>骚人故悲秋，九辨播三楚。<div id='poem_sentence_0_94152_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_94152'>宋公旧题壁，文采照潭府。<div id='poem_sentence_1_94152_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_94152'>千载得君侯，遥遥接华绪。<div id='poem_sentence_2_94152_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_94152'>还当初秋天，又进湖湘橹。<div id='poem_sentence_3_94152_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_94152'>当家多胜事，此役可兼取。<div id='poem_sentence_4_94152_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_94152'>江山日日新，似若相劳苦。<div id='poem_sentence_5_94152_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_94152'>木脱献群峰，云生失前浦。<div id='poem_sentence_6_94152_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_94152'>况持别乘权，光华动徒旅。<div id='poem_sentence_7_94152_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_94152'>元戎下分庭，百吏群趋庑。<div id='poem_sentence_8_94152_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_94152'>后车载仁风，习习被南土。<div id='poem_sentence_9_94152_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_94152'>预知潢池盗，无复惊桴鼓。<div id='poem_sentence_10_94152_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_94152'>政当劝卖剑，不必禁挟弩。<div id='poem_sentence_11_94152_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_94152'>岭头镜面平<span class='inlineComment2'>（小集本作入献有吁谟）</span>，论赏骈圭组。<div id='poem_sentence_12_94152_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_94152'>临分一杯酒，不为离愁举。<div id='poem_sentence_13_94152_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_94152'></div><div id='poem_sentence_14_94152_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1176&endYear=1176')">1176年8月17日</a>　周必大至婺州，二人同游灵洞。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1176&endYear=1176')">1176年8月</a>　为邢邦用作墓铭。作品：《邢邦用墓志铭》<div id='poem_1275672' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275672' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275672?labeling=true' target='_blank'>邢邦用墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（淳熙三年八月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275672")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275672_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275672'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275672'>群献精微之缊，质文始终之绪，天典民彝之统纪，合而系之曰人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275672_comment'></div>众则昌，寡则悴，咸无焉则晻昧而不章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275672_comment'></div>道之无穷也，善之难择也，气质之参错不齐也，有从事于斯，固未可必其至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275672_comment'></div>茍其弗措，则亦安知其必不至也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275672_comment'></div>故乡是焉者，毋问其久近浅深，皆可为斯文助。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275672_comment'></div>不幸夺之，毋问其久近浅深，亦皆可为斯文惜也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275672_comment'></div>况其志浸确而其行事既有可见者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275672_comment'></div>此予于邦用之没，哭之而不能已也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275672_comment'></div>邦用姓邢氏，名世材。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275672_comment'></div>其先青州人，中徙汴，绍兴间始家会稽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275672_comment'></div>邦用为人重实，幼孤，事母以孝闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275672_comment'></div>母亡，事其兄如父，动息必咨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275672_comment'></div>拊教诸弟，经纪族姻，恩意笃备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275672_comment'></div>既举进士得官，尽弃故学，遍从先生长者游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275672_comment'></div>深思力索，有所未达，愤悱见于辞色，退则汲汲求践其所闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275672_comment'></div>出为南康军司户参军，适岁大侵，日夜条画方略告上官，虽半用半不用，迄无尤其出位者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275672_comment'></div>郡檄摄令都昌，下车亟发常平仓粟赡饥民，随自劾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1275672_comment'></div>部使者始怒，已乃荐之朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1275672_comment'></div>盖其恻怛发中，故虽数而不见谓渎，迫而不见谓讦，度越规矩而亦不见谓干名采誉也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1275672_comment'></div>秩满，迁从政郎、婺州金华县丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1275672_comment'></div>未上，卒于家，年三十七，实淳熙三年三月二十八日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1275672_comment'></div>其年八月十二日，葬于山阴县温泉乡光相坞之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1275672_comment'></div>曾祖讳荣，祖讳皋，父讳佐，妣陈氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1275672_comment'></div>初娶和氏，先卒，再娶曾氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1275672_comment'></div>子男三人：淳、淑、湛，淑为叔父世元后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1275672_comment'></div>女四人，尚幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1275672_comment'></div>予于邦用有连而相与讲学非一日，知之为深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1275672_comment'></div>邦用平生它可纪尚众，顾其自任者厚，非蕲以此自名，故独论其所存以告来世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1275672_comment'></div>千载之下，尚有哀其志者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1275672_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_1275672'>昆仑旁薄，浩无际兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1275672_comment'></div>端车正辙，随所至兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1275672_comment'></div>命之不融，志则诣兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1275672_comment'></div>体魄攸降，塈斯竁兮。</div><div id='poem_sentence_32_1275672_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1176&endYear=1176')">1176年8月</a>　为潘谦之作墓铭。作品：《潘朝散墓志铭》<div id='poem_1275673' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275673' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275673?labeling=true' target='_blank'>潘朝散墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（淳熙三年八月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275673")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275673_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275673'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275673'>自建炎省方吴会，二浙之民，渐王泽为近。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275673_comment'></div>溪皋谷陬，往往化韦褐为簪组。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275673_comment'></div>其士大夫家，仕者亦蕃于初，一门之内或四三，或六七，或累十数而未止也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275673_comment'></div>衣冠之盛，固人所喜道，至于爵秩，虽未甚通显，而遵畏涯分，不失前人靖厚淳质之绪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275673_comment'></div>尚论风俗者，亦将有考于斯焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275673_comment'></div>公讳好谦，字伯益，一字损之，松阳人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275673_comment'></div>松阳之潘，自复州史君宗回以进士起家而族浸大，公实其子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275673_comment'></div>已而以祖命为寿昌县丞后，寿昌于复州伯仲也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275673_comment'></div>生三年，知书偏傍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275673_comment'></div>复州暇日陈金石刻，阿保剑之于旁，试摘问之，通者泰半。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275673_comment'></div>稍长，益嗜文史，恂恂驯饬，不敢以气加人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275673_comment'></div>生十有七年，寿昌没旁郡，已能护柩还里，哀毁动行路，结庐墓次，竟祥禫乃复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275673_comment'></div>初尉丽水，与乡县封畛相入，以职则迕旧故，以情则废绳墨，公一接以和，而官事亦不旷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275673_comment'></div>历泉州司理参军、福建安抚司准备差遣、监户部激赏酒库籴场、通判镇江府京口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275673_comment'></div>江淮间都会，大军所壁，杂五方之俗，号难治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275673_comment'></div>前是为贰者，每诿事于其长，廪食无所预。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275673_comment'></div>公始至，慨然曰：「是岂不足行志邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1275673_comment'></div>在我前者相导而弥缝之，在我后者尉接而推掖之，庶其有济」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1275673_comment'></div>久之不得伸，则又慨然曰：「吾幸有故田庐，亦何为久于此」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1275673_comment'></div>亟移病，僚属挽之不能止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1275673_comment'></div>数年，复通判绍兴府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1275673_comment'></div>未上，卒于家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1275673_comment'></div>官讫朝散郎，寿讫五十有九。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1275673_comment'></div>其岁月日，淳熙二年四月己卯也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1275673_comment'></div>公虽入官四十馀年，卧家之日三之二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1275673_comment'></div>其去丽水，去籴场，去京口，皆请祠禄以归，乐閒澹乃如是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1275673_comment'></div>廉靖畏事，在官未尝以私故役公皂，廛居地产之珍，终更犹不知其名物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1275673_comment'></div>松阳小邑，易雄伯氓隶謼嘂庭下，县吏辄为之动色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1275673_comment'></div>公秩郎位，要银艾，乃独凌竞，若有所惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1275673_comment'></div>夏秋必趣家人具所输，丝必练治，粟必精凿，毋以盬恶输有司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1275673_comment'></div>曰：「吾先人之训，不敢改也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1275673_comment'></div>居处简朴，游晏阔希，舆马服用无所纷华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1275673_comment'></div>曰：「吾先人之旧，不敢加也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1275673_comment'></div>县政中失，里闾长短薄厚，举不以挂口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1275673_comment'></div>曰：「吾先人数以是厉子弟，不敢队也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1275673_comment'></div>天雨雪，劳赐并舍贫者，岁有常，其尤厚者，月有秩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1275673_comment'></div>年凶民流，则间发囷氾给之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1275673_comment'></div>曰：「此谁非吾先人之族姻者，吾力及焉，不敢爱也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1275673_comment'></div>噫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1275673_comment'></div>若公者，其所谓遵畏涯分，不失前人靖厚淳质之绪者耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1275673_comment'></div>曾祖讳干。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1275673_comment'></div>祖讳珂，宣州泾县主簿，累赠朝议大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1275673_comment'></div>考讳宗说，严州寿昌县丞，累赠朝散郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1275673_comment'></div>妣毛氏，赠安人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1275673_comment'></div>先娶陈氏，赠秘阁修撰东之女，赠安人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1275673_comment'></div>初，朝廷录陈公睢阳之节，官其子弟若婿，而公与焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1275673_comment'></div>再娶闾丘氏，朝请大夫泳之女，封安人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1275673_comment'></div>子男子四：景连，迪功郎、监户部激赏中酒库；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1275673_comment'></div>次景夔、次景尹、次景达。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1275673_comment'></div>子女子五：长适宣义郎、两浙东路提点刑狱司干办公事郑愿中，蚤卒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1275673_comment'></div>次适进士叶近，馀在室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1275673_comment'></div>孙男女四人，尚幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1275673_comment'></div>没之明年八月甲申，葬于县之布和乡兰湾，其孤以临川陆九渊之状来谒铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1275673_comment'></div>盖公晚岁笃于教子，余虽未及际公，景夔、景尹皆越数百里遣从余游，岁时还书络绎，未尝不属其子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1275673_comment'></div>且谋徙家于婺，以便其学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1275673_comment'></div>呜呼，此意厚矣，其可忘哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1275673_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_56_1275673'>布和之原，兰被其厓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1275673_comment'></div>有车之萃，则克宅之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1275673_comment'></div>维出不絿，维居不󲇺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1275673_comment'></div>维传不踬，施于来裔。</div><div id='poem_sentence_59_1275673_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1176&endYear=1176')">1176年9月19日</a>　游赤松山。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1176&endYear=1176')">1176年9月</a>　作书与周必大，言将深求其所未至，不敢怠惰。作品：《与周丞相》三。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷九。）</span><br /></div><div class='label1' id='62954e75cf034aeea511d1e73e6266fc_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("62954e75cf034aeea511d1e73e6266fc");'><span id='62954e75cf034aeea511d1e73e6266fc_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1176&endYear=1176')">1176年</a>，40岁</div><div id='62954e75cf034aeea511d1e73e6266fc' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1176&endYear=1176')">1176年10月26日</a>　归自会稽。孝宗重修《徽宗实录》，以李焘荐除秘书省秘书郎，兼国史院编修官，实录院检讨官。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1176&endYear=1176')">1176年10月</a>　因即将赴临安任职，将朱塾交与潘景宪书院。作品：《与朱侍讲》八。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷八。）</span><br /></div><div class='label1' id='abf3d87071994977bee9a0fd3d1c31e5_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("abf3d87071994977bee9a0fd3d1c31e5");'><span id='abf3d87071994977bee9a0fd3d1c31e5_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1179&endYear=1181')">1179-1181年</a>，43-45岁</div><div id='abf3d87071994977bee9a0fd3d1c31e5' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1179&endYear=1179')">1179年4月13日</a>　归至婺州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1179&endYear=1179')">1179年4月</a>　朱熹再遣朱塾来学。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1179&endYear=1179')">1179年5月</a>　买宅城西北隅，与唐仲友为邻，将原居归官。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1179&endYear=1179')">1179年5月</a>　周必大为《皇朝文鉴》作序成，观之不悦。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1179&endYear=1179')">1179年6月7日</a>　主管建宁府武夷山冲祐观。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1179&endYear=1179')">1179年6月</a>　应朱熹之请，为其作大字。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1179&endYear=1179')">1179年7月28日</a>　芮氏妻病卒。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1179&endYear=1179')">1179年8月</a>　致书周必大，建议听朱熹丐祠之请。作品：《与周丞相》十二。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷九。）</span><div id='poem_1275276' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275276' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275276?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与周丞相子充书<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其十 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1179年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275276")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275276_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275276'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275276'>某屏居粗安适，日来读书，视旧颇不卤莽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275276_comment'></div>若得十数年休假，无它病挠恼，于句读训诂间或粗有毫分之益也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275276_comment'></div>祠禄至十二月初乃满，冗食官仓，甚觉不安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275276_comment'></div>若自此复得一两任，则南亩铢积，亦可供伏腊，便不须仰禄矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275276_comment'></div>惰退之迹，不欲自通于诸公，若是时吾丈犹在朝，为致一言，甚幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275276_comment'></div>今未须也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275276_comment'></div>沈叔晦直谅确实，士人中极不易得，莫已有所授否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275276_comment'></div>刘子澄绝不得书，念之每往来于心也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275276_comment'></div>潘严州女子，适其弟在婺，往还甚熟，为郡有爱民之意，甚知敬慕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275276_comment'></div>所以欲达姓名之意无它，恐州郡间时有合整顿利病，欲得咨禀耳。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1275276_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1179&endYear=1179')">1179年9月15日</a>　葬芮氏于明招山。作品：《祔芮氏志》<div id='poem_1275677' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275677' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275677?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祔芮氏志</a><span class='authorDate'>（淳熙六年九月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275677")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275677_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275677'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275677'>夫人芮氏，吴兴先生之季女，东莱吕某之继室也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275677_comment'></div>生十有一年而先生没。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275677_comment'></div>及长，澹静驯饬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275677_comment'></div>母王夫人隆爱之，严于择对，不轻诺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275677_comment'></div>某少获事诸公长者，而海内知心，则实维先生之门，夙夜念无以酬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275677_comment'></div>适中馈乏主，闻夫人之贤，乃委币以请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275677_comment'></div>既庙见，慨然曰：「吾他日有以拜先生墓矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275677_comment'></div>归之明年，某病废，夫人护视劬瘁，得羸疾以卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275677_comment'></div>曾祖宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275677_comment'></div>祖彦辅，赠朝议大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275677_comment'></div>先生讳烨，终右文殿修撰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275677_comment'></div>夫人生以绍兴三十二年九月五日，卒以淳熙六年七月二十八日，是年九月十五日，祔于婺州武义县明招山先君兆域之左。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1275677_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1179&endYear=1179')">1179年10月</a>　在新居为诸生讲说《诗》、《书》等。作品：《己亥秋所记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史外集》卷五。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1179&endYear=1179')">1179年10月</a>　陆九龄来访。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1179&endYear=1179')">1179年10月</a>　谢光中自长沙来从学。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1179&endYear=1179')">1179年10月</a>　作《桐乡志》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1179&endYear=1179')">1179年10月</a>　《吕氏家塾读诗记》初稿定本。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1179&endYear=1179')">1179年11月</a>　致书周必大，劝其不必奏请《依字》文字，恐助长孝宗独裁。作品：《与周丞相》十四。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷九。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1179&endYear=1179')">1179年11月</a>　应门人王自得请为其祖母傅氏作墓铭。作品：《王自得祖母傅氏墓志铭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史外集》卷五。）</span><div id='poem_1275685' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275685' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275685?labeling=true' target='_blank'>王自得祖母傅氏墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（淳熙六年十二月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275685")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275685_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275685'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275685'>义乌王君瓘之夫人，同县傅氏女也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275685_comment'></div>县之第氏族者，谱王为右姓，族党根据连都邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275685_comment'></div>夫人来归，小大无违言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275685_comment'></div>姑余夫人律阃内甚严，诸妇屏气侧足，候伺颜色，少当其意者，独夫人事之顺焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275685_comment'></div>帮源之乱，民十百相保聚捍贼，议长，皆相顾不敢而属之王君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275685_comment'></div>官军临境，里中豪效首虏者率命官，姻戚或说王君无后时，夫人尸之，曰：「君居兵间，蕲以屏蔽闾井，非利之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275685_comment'></div>即拜爵，其谁明吾心」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275685_comment'></div>王君慨然亟谢罢说者，兵解，佐王君综理其家者，具有条秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275685_comment'></div>盖年七十有五，以乾道二年十二月十六日终于寝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275685_comment'></div>淳熙六年十二月初二日，始克葬于乡之高麓原青口里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275685_comment'></div>二子：长安诗，将仕郎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275685_comment'></div>次安远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275685_comment'></div>三女，长适俞持国，次胡延，次乡贡进士周宪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275685_comment'></div>孙男女十，男曰自昭、自强、自得、自牧、自求，婿其女孙者，曰宣教郎、鄂州州学教授俞麟，曰国子免解进士何堮，曰迪功郎、信州上饶县尉钱逖，馀在室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275685_comment'></div>曾孙男十二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275685_comment'></div>自得久从予游，实来谒铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275685_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_1275685'>吁嗟夫人，蹈柔则兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1275685_comment'></div>百世之下，安此室兮。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1275685_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1179&endYear=1179')">1179年12月</a>　复书周必大，勉其不必求退。又议张栻处事太疏。作品：《与周丞相》十一。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷九。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1179&endYear=1179')">1179年12月</a>　为潘景宪夫人作墓铭。作品：《潘叔度妻朱夫人墓志铭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷十三。）</span><div id='poem_1275678' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275678' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275678?labeling=true' target='_blank'>潘叔度妻朱夫人墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（淳熙六年十一月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275678")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275678_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275678'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275678'>吾同年友潘叔度景宪，有贤配曰桐乡朱氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275678_comment'></div>始叔度谋继室，习于朱氏者皆称夫人之贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275678_comment'></div>及归，践妇职过所闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275678_comment'></div>叔度自律甚严，人少当其意，夫人独事之顺焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275678_comment'></div>其于子若女，叔度不独咨美其均壹，又每咎其厚于慈也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275678_comment'></div>既没，自尊嫜至于娣姒，哭之过时而哀，中外有连者，皆惋叹失声，或涕泣不能已也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275678_comment'></div>生二十七年而嫁，嫁七年而卒，实淳熙己亥七月十九日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275678_comment'></div>是岁十一月七日，葬于婺州金华县叶山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275678_comment'></div>曾祖廙，赠朝议大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275678_comment'></div>祖载上，司农卿，赠徽猷阁待制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275678_comment'></div>父翌，中书舍人，终敷文阁待制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275678_comment'></div>子男二人：自厚、自晦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275678_comment'></div>子女子三人，长适朱塾，馀在室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275678_comment'></div>予与叔度共学久矣，其兢兢于母子昆弟之间，如恐伤之者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275678_comment'></div>盖深知其所存，故其得内助则窃为之喜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275678_comment'></div>迨其悼亡，见其用力之难而私忧其失其相也，虽病且废，忍不铭？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275678_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_1275678'>匪偏匪颇，匪嘻匪嗃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1275678_comment'></div>理从数违，质厚气薄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1275678_comment'></div>厚焉培之，薄焉委之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1275678_comment'></div>我作斯铭，允无愧辞。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1275678_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1179&endYear=1179')">1179年冬</a>　口授《尚书讲义》于弟子时澜等。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1179&endYear=1179')">1179年</a>　本年复修《读诗记》等。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1180&endYear=1180')">1180年1月1日</a>　始建家庙，修《宗法》及《祭礼》，始作《日记》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1180&endYear=1180')">1180年1月</a>　始编《大事记》，作《大事记》序。作品：《大事记序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷十五《庚子辛丑日记》）</span><div id='poem_1275501' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275501' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275501?labeling=true' target='_blank'>大事记序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1180年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275501")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275501_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275501'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275501'>司马子长《年表》、《大事记》，盖古策书遗法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275501_comment'></div>获麟以上，既见于《春秋经》，周敬王三十九年以下，今采《左氏传》、历代史、邵康节先生《皇极经世》、司马文正公《稽古录》、《资治通鉴目录》、《举要历》，辑而广之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275501_comment'></div>意所未安，参稽百氏，颇为增损。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275501_comment'></div>书法视太史公所录，不尽用策书凡例云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275501_comment'></div>起春秋后，讫于五代，分为若干卷，《通释》若干卷，《解题》若干卷，合若干卷。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1275501_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1180&endYear=1180')">1180年1月</a>　始作《庚子辛丑日记》，修《宗法》及《祭礼》。修《读诗记》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1180&endYear=1180')">1180年1月</a>　《白鹿洞书院记》初稿成，交朱熹讨论。作《卧龙庵记》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1180&endYear=1180')">1180年2月</a>　编《大事记》，修《读诗记》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1180&endYear=1180')">1180年2月</a>　《白鹿洞书院记》定稿，朱熹赞其“辞约义正”<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷六。）</span><div id='poem_1275600' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275600' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275600?labeling=true' target='_blank'>白鹿洞书院记</a><span class='authorDate'>（淳熙七年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275600")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275600_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275600'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275600'>淳熙六年，南康军秋雨不时，高卬之田告病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275600_comment'></div>郡守新安朱侯熹行视陂塘，并庐山而东，得白鹿洞书院废址，慨然顾其僚曰：「是盖唐李渤之隐居，而太宗皇帝驿送九经，俾生徒肄业之地也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275600_comment'></div>书院创于南唐，其事至鲜浅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275600_comment'></div>太宗于汎扫区宇、日不暇给之际，奖劝封殖，如恐弗及，规摹远矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275600_comment'></div>中兴五十年，释老之宫圮于寇戎者，斧斤之声相闻，各复其初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275600_comment'></div>独此地委于榛莽，过者太息，庸非吾徒之耻哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275600_comment'></div>郡虽贫薄，顾不能筑屋数楹，上以宣布本朝崇建人文之大指，下以续先贤之风声于方来乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275600_comment'></div>乃属军学教授杨君大法、星子县令王君仲杰董其事，又以书命某记其成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275600_comment'></div>某窃尝闻之诸公长者，国初斯民新脱五季锋镝之阨，学者尚寡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275600_comment'></div>海内向平，文风日起，儒先往往依山林、即閒旷以讲授，大师多至数千百人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275600_comment'></div>嵩阳、岳麓、睢阳及是洞为尤著，天下所谓四书院者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275600_comment'></div>祖宗尊右儒术，分之官书，命之禄秩，锡之扁榜，所以宠绥之者甚备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275600_comment'></div>当是时，士皆上质实，下新奇，敦行义而不偷，守训故而不凿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275600_comment'></div>虽学问之渊源统纪或未深究，然甘受和，白受采，既有进德之地矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275600_comment'></div>庆历、嘉祐之间，豪杰并出，讲治益精。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275600_comment'></div>至于河南程氏、横渠张氏，相与倡明正学，然后三代孔孟之教始终条理，于是乎可考。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275600_comment'></div>熙宁初，明道先生在朝，建白学制，教养考察宾兴之法，纲条甚悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1275600_comment'></div>不幸王氏之学方兴，其议遂格，有志之士未尝不叹息于斯焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1275600_comment'></div>建炎再造，典刑文宪，浸还旧观，关洛绪言，稍出于毁弃剪灭之馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1275600_comment'></div>晚进小生，骤闻其语，不知亲师取友以讲求用力之实，躐等陵节，忽近慕远，未能窥程、张之门庭而先有王氏高自贤圣之病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1275600_comment'></div>如是洞之所传习，道之者或鲜矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1275600_comment'></div>然则书院之复，岂茍云哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1275600_comment'></div>此邦之士，盍相与揖先儒淳固悫实之馀风，服《大学》离经辨志之始教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1275600_comment'></div>由博而约，自下而高，以答扬熙陵开迪乐育之大德，则于贤侯之劝学，斯无负矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1275600_comment'></div>至于考方志、纪人物，亦有土者所当谨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1275600_comment'></div>若李浚之之遗迹，固不得而略也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1275600_comment'></div>侯于是役，重民之劳，赋功已狭，率损其旧十七八，力不足而意则有馀矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1275600_comment'></div>兴废始末，具于当涂郭祥正所记者，皆不书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1275600_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1180&endYear=1180')">1180年2月2日</a>　惊闻张栻病卒，几至委顿。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1180&endYear=1180')">1180年2月</a>　复书周必大，为朱熹请祠求助。作品：《与周丞相》十五。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷九。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1180&endYear=1180')">1180年3月</a>　读《宗法》。编《大事记》，修《读诗记》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1180&endYear=1180')">1180年3月17日</a>　陆九龄自越来访。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1180&endYear=1180')">1180年3月19日</a>　为张栻作祭文。作品：《张五十丈祭文》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷十五《庚子辛丑日记》）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1180&endYear=1180')">1180年3月</a>　托吕祖俭携书信并所作张栻祭文送朱熹。作品：《与朱侍讲》二十九。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷八。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1180&endYear=1180')">1180年3月</a>　长沙谢光中辞归省亲，有书相送。作品：《书鹿鸣之五送谢光中题其后》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷七。）</span><div id='poem_1275521' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275521' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275521?labeling=true' target='_blank'>书鹿鸣之五送谢光中题其后</a><span class='authorDate'>（1180年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275521")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275521_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275521'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275521'>长沙谢敬之光中，以淳熙己亥十月来婺讲学，以明年三月辞归省亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275521_comment'></div>将别请言，予病不能也，诸友乃取《读诗记》小雅五篇，共书以馈其行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275521_comment'></div>《常棣》之卒章曰：「是究是图，亶其然乎」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275521_comment'></div>敬之其勉之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275521_comment'></div>时方闻张荆州之讣，三复和平之句，为之泫然。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1275521_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1180&endYear=1180')">1180年春</a>　复书郭养正，谈为官当自尽职事。作品：《与郭养正》三。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史外集》卷五。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1180&endYear=1180')">1180年春</a>　令诸弟读《大传》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1180&endYear=1180')">1180年4月</a>　读《宗法》。编《大事记》，修《读诗记》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1180&endYear=1180')">1180年4月</a>　陆九龄来访，论学二十余日，颇为吕说所动。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1180&endYear=1180')">1180年4月17日</a>　磨勘，转朝请郎。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1180&endYear=1180')">1180年5月</a>　读《宗法》。编《大事记》，修《读诗记》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1180&endYear=1180')">1180年5月</a>　建家庙将成，实践祭仪。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1180&endYear=1180')">1180年5月20日</a>　应婺州守萧燧约作《重修钓台记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷六。）</span><div id='poem_1275601' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275601' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275601?labeling=true' target='_blank'>重修钓台记</a><span class='authorDate'>（淳熙七年五月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275601")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275601_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275601'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275601'>由东阳江而下，径新定郡五十里，得严陵濑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275601_comment'></div>盖东汉严先生遁世不屈，耕钓于富春山，后人因以名其地也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275601_comment'></div>孙吴析富春为桐庐，是濑亦来属焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275601_comment'></div>顾野王《舆地志》曰：「桐庐县南有严子陵渔钓处，石上平，可坐十人，名为钓坛」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275601_comment'></div>即今之钓台也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275601_comment'></div>独两台对峙，野王所不载，盖亦觕言之耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275601_comment'></div>明道二年，范文正公自右司谏守是邦，始筑屋祠先生而为之记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275601_comment'></div>濑之傍白云源，乃唐诗人方处士故庐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275601_comment'></div>文正公之游钓台也，尝绝江访其旧迹，以其象寘祠之左。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275601_comment'></div>文正公没，郡人思之，遂侑食于右坐焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275601_comment'></div>岁祀浸远，此意弗嗣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275601_comment'></div>淳熙五年，侍郎萧公出镇，道祠下，慨然曰：「国家稽用唐武德旧典，姓是州曰严，则先生之祠乃名教之首，颓圮若是可乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275601_comment'></div>顾急于民瘼未暇也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275601_comment'></div>居二年，政成化洽，以馀力新之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275601_comment'></div>时某病废卧旁郡，公以书见诿记其成，固辞不可，乃复于公曰：方王氏移国，以光武之大志，先生之高气，相与共学，夫岂区区呻吟佔毕之末哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275601_comment'></div>汉官威仪既复，薄海内外，臣子之责皆塞矣，亦何必奋臂其间哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275601_comment'></div>没身丘壑，固先生之素尚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1275601_comment'></div>帝眷焉有怀，俾以形旁求于天下，得非在廷诸臣奉令承教之不给，未有当帝意者邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1275601_comment'></div>三聘而至，车驾即日幸其馆，勉其相助为理，所以处先生者不薄矣，匪徒屈万乘之重为故人之光宠也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1275601_comment'></div>先生虽以巢、由自命，视一世若不足以浼之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1275601_comment'></div>观与侯霸尺牍，劘切之意，见于言外，岂于帝惓惓未能忘邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1275601_comment'></div>浩然而归，使人主有终身瞻望不及之叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1275601_comment'></div>施及后世，宾友耆俊，遂为家法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1275601_comment'></div>士之闻风兴起者，坚节正操，见危受命，项背相望，其有益人之国，与朝夕献纳云台之下者，未知其孰多孰少也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1275601_comment'></div>枝必类本，响必报声，使先生微有意于傲世立名，一再传之后，且将为西晋之清虚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1275601_comment'></div>而东京之俗，久而益励，名检之外，综理干略，亦往往高出后世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1275601_comment'></div>溯其流而寻其源，则建武之高节，孰可訾耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1275601_comment'></div>至于节义之弊，变为亢激，特上无建用皇极之君均调消息之尔，非造端者之过也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1275601_comment'></div>后先生且千年，文正公来主斯地，祀典始举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1275601_comment'></div>旷百世而相感者，固自不常遇耶！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1275601_comment'></div>今公作牧，复大葺祠宇，以续前人之绪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1275601_comment'></div>继自今以往，溯沿下上者，款门而心开，升堂而容肃，风清樾，濯寒泉，哦山高水长之诗，致足乐也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1275601_comment'></div>则公岂专为一邦劝哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1275601_comment'></div>祠之前则羊裘轩，其东则客星阁、招隐堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1275601_comment'></div>岸江立表以识路，缭山作亭以待憩，或革或因，面势位置各有思致，皆受成于公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1275601_comment'></div>以非大指所存，故不详列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1275601_comment'></div>公名燧，字照邻，临江人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1275601_comment'></div>主其役者，司户参军吴桂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1275601_comment'></div>淳熙七年五月二十二日，朝请郎、直秘阁、主管建宁府冲佑观吕祖谦记，朝请郎、新潼川府路转运判官虞似良书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_38_1275601_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1180&endYear=1180')">1180年5月</a>　陈亮、徐居厚结伴来访。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1180&endYear=1180')">1180年6月</a>　读《宗法》。编《大事记》，修《读诗记》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1180&endYear=1180')">1180年6月</a>　复朱熹书，称赞陆九渊兄弟不易得。答朱熹问家庙事。作品：《与朱侍讲》三十。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷八。）</span><div id='poem_1275222' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275222' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275222?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与朱侍讲元晦书<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二十二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1180年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275222")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275222_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275222'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275222'>某哀苦待尽，它无足言者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275222_comment'></div>引辞今有报否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275222_comment'></div>格以近制，以事势观之，恐未必得伸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275222_comment'></div>祠禄正协「周之则受」之义，独改秩有当商量处，然前代于贤者不能致而就官之者盖多矣，窃谓少逡巡而受之可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275222_comment'></div>若确然不回，则名愈高而礼愈加，异时有难居者耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275222_comment'></div>君子之谋，始终皆举之，要须审虑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275222_comment'></div>令嗣气质甚淳，已令就潘叔度舍傍书室寝处<span class='inlineComment2'>（不在其家。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275222_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1275222", 1275222, "Clauses/18/Comments/1")'>同窗</span>者乃叔度之弟景愈<span class='inlineComment2'>（字叔昌。）</span>，年三十馀，甚有志趣，有意务实，相处当有益<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275222_comment'></div>已立定课程，令嗣当自寄呈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275222_comment'></div>唯每日到某处，则与叔度兄弟偕来，不许过它斋舍<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275222_comment'></div>自馀虑之所及，不敢不尽，幸少宽念也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275222_comment'></div>别纸疏谕，以不欲滞此介，未得详禀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275222_comment'></div>令嗣更留一兵在此，俟半月诸事及课程见得次第，当遣归，恐欲知其肄习居处之详也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275222_comment'></div>周教授《论语》方借看，并俟遣此兵时缕缕求教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275222_comment'></div>此间方刊《横渠集》，断手当首拜纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275222_comment'></div>《说文》苦无善本，见令嗣说方雠校，昨见刘子澄说赣州方欲刊书，自可径送渠令锓木也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275222_comment'></div>「洙泗言仁」未合处，因便望录示，亦欲得思索也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1275222_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1275222'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_7_1275222_0'>⑴ 叔昌亦自工于程试，足可商量。五六年前，尝为太学解魁。近三两岁来，却都放下举业，专意为学。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_9_1275222_0'>⑵ 虽到某处，亦不许独来，盖城市间不得不如此过防。又众中人亦多端，恐志未定，或迁易耳。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1275222_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1180&endYear=1180')">1180年6月</a>　论朱熹作《再祭张五十丈文》当“弘大平粹”作品：《与朱侍讲》三十二。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷八。）</span><div id='poem_1275222' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275222' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275222?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与朱侍讲元晦书<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二十二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1180年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1275222", 1275222, "Clauses/18/Comments/1")'>同窗</span>者乃叔度之弟景愈<span class='inlineComment2'>（字叔昌。）</span>，年三十馀，甚有志趣，有意务实，相处当有益<sup class='reference id='poem_sentence_10_1275222_comment'></div>别纸疏谕，以不欲滞此介，未得详禀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275222_comment'></div>令嗣更留一兵在此，俟半月诸事及课程见得次第，当遣归，恐欲知其肄习居处之详也。<div class='inline'
