id='poem_sentence_16_1275222_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1275222'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_7_1275222_0'>⑴ 叔昌亦自工于程试，足可商量。五六年前，尝为太学解魁。近三两岁来，却都放下举业，专意为学。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_9_1275222_0'>⑵ 虽到某处，亦不许独来，盖城市间不得不如此过防。又众中人亦多端，恐志未定，或迁易耳。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1275222_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1180&endYear=1180')">1180年6月</a>　周必大以吏部尚书参知政事，作书相勉励，兼及陈傅良、朱熹事。作品：《与周丞相》十五。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷九。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1180&endYear=1180')">1180年6月</a>　致书陈亮，痛悼张栻之逝。作品：《与陈同甫》六。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史外集》卷五。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1180&endYear=1180')">1180年7月</a>　读《宗法》。编《大事记》，修《读诗记》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1180&endYear=1180')">1180年7月</a>　复项平甫来书。作品：《答项平甫》一。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷十。）</span><div id='poem_1275395' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275395' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275395?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答项平甫书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1180年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275395")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275395_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275395'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275395'>某往岁侍郎舅氏自荆南归，具道左右年虽少而志操坚正，下至诸表弟，人人敬慕，是时慨然有愿见之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275395_comment'></div>今春闻分教山阴，相距虽不远，又以病废无从会面为恨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275395_comment'></div>便中忽奉手笔，所以见属者，虽非衰惰之所敢当，然详味辞气，恳切质实，益知所存之不苟也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275395_comment'></div>自张丈去世之后，至今心折，左右游从既久，讲绎必甚精详，然愿深思力践，体衣锦尚絅之义，卑以自牧，驯致充实光大之地，则吾道之幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275395_comment'></div>石天民、沈叔晦诸兄，莫时款聚否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275395_comment'></div>萎痹不能多作字。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275395_comment'></div>秋暑，以时自重<span class='inlineComment2'>（《东莱吕太史别集》卷一○。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275395_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_1275395'>充：原无，据库本、金华本补。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1275395_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1180&endYear=1180')">1180年7月</a>　致书周必大，冀其致力于远大。作品：《与周丞相》十六。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷九。）</span><div id='poem_1275277' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275277' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275277?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与周丞相子充书<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其十一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1180年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275277")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275277_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275277'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275277'>某近自婺来越省外祖母，弛担始见除目，窃知独出推毂之力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275277_comment'></div>前书所以拜禀复求祠禄，实繇向来一出讲论灭裂，病败如牛毛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275277_comment'></div>忧患以来，涉历难艰，读书方似粗有蹊径，意欲更得数年之间，极力寻绎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275277_comment'></div>今复驱驰之，遽从事役，爱念则厚，然非所以长养成就之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275277_comment'></div>名在仕版，身非己有，岂敢苟遂私志？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275277_comment'></div>但离婺时，都无所闻，数日间须且归治行装，到家已是二十左右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275277_comment'></div>而提举叔祖母葬期，近在此月二十六日，势须过此乃能之官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275277_comment'></div>后月初四五间，当得瞻见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275277_comment'></div>某以韩丈所遣送堂帖人在婺未来，未有被受，故未能作政府书，敢告先为白诸公，并及行期曲折，幸甚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1275277_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1180&endYear=1180')">1180年8月</a>　读《宗法》。编《大事记》，修《读诗记》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1180&endYear=1180')">1180年8月</a>　门生徐暄来访。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1180&endYear=1180')">1180年9月</a>　读《医经》。编《大事记》，修《读诗记》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1180&endYear=1180')">1180年9月25日</a>　再除著作郎兼国史院编修官，以病辞。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1180&endYear=1180')">1180年9月26日</a>　作书与朱熹荐门生毛大方。作品：《与朱侍讲》三十五。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷八。）</span><div id='poem_1275222' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275222' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275222?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与朱侍讲元晦书<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二十二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1180年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275222")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275222_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275222'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275222'>某哀苦待尽，它无足言者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275222_comment'></div>引辞今有报否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275222_comment'></div>格以近制，以事势观之，恐未必得伸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275222_comment'></div>祠禄正协「周之则受」之义，独改秩有当商量处，然前代于贤者不能致而就官之者盖多矣，窃谓少逡巡而受之可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275222_comment'></div>若确然不回，则名愈高而礼愈加，异时有难居者耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275222_comment'></div>君子之谋，始终皆举之，要须审虑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275222_comment'></div>令嗣气质甚淳，已令就潘叔度舍傍书室寝处<span class='inlineComment2'>（不在其家。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275222_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1275222", 1275222, "Clauses/18/Comments/1")'>同窗</span>者乃叔度之弟景愈<span class='inlineComment2'>（字叔昌。）</span>，年三十馀，甚有志趣，有意务实，相处当有益<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275222_comment'></div>已立定课程，令嗣当自寄呈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275222_comment'></div>唯每日到某处，则与叔度兄弟偕来，不许过它斋舍<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275222_comment'></div>自馀虑之所及，不敢不尽，幸少宽念也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275222_comment'></div>别纸疏谕，以不欲滞此介，未得详禀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275222_comment'></div>令嗣更留一兵在此，俟半月诸事及课程见得次第，当遣归，恐欲知其肄习居处之详也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275222_comment'></div>周教授《论语》方借看，并俟遣此兵时缕缕求教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275222_comment'></div>此间方刊《横渠集》，断手当首拜纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275222_comment'></div>《说文》苦无善本，见令嗣说方雠校，昨见刘子澄说赣州方欲刊书，自可径送渠令锓木也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275222_comment'></div>「洙泗言仁」未合处，因便望录示，亦欲得思索也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1275222_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1275222'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_7_1275222_0'>⑴ 叔昌亦自工于程试，足可商量。五六年前，尝为太学解魁。近三两岁来，却都放下举业，专意为学。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_9_1275222_0'>⑵ 虽到某处，亦不许独来，盖城市间不得不如此过防。又众中人亦多端，恐志未定，或迁易耳。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1275222_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1180&endYear=1180')">1180年9月</a>　寄《祭张荆州文》与刘清之。作品：《与刘衡州》二。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史外集》卷五。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1180&endYear=1180')">1180年10月</a>　读《医经》。编《大事记》，修《读诗记》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1180&endYear=1180')">1180年10月1日</a>　作辞免札子，辞官请祠。作品：《再除著作郎史官辞免札子》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷三。）</span><div id='poem_1275162' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275162' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275162?labeling=true' target='_blank'>再除著作郎史官辞免劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1180年10月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275162")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275162_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275162'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275162'>恭准尚书省劄子：「九月二十五日，三省同奉圣旨：吕某除秘书省著作郎、兼国史院编修官」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275162_comment'></div>伏念某顷者备数著庭，以病自免，圣上录其铅椠之微勤，畀之贴职，以宠其归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275162_comment'></div>绥奖覆护，夐无近比。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275162_comment'></div>卧家以来，未及两载，公朝记识不替，除目已颁，既还旧职，复隶史观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275162_comment'></div>深惟尪残小臣至愚极陋，仍岁所蒙被者，虽麋捐九死无以仰酬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275162_comment'></div>使筋骸仅可自比于人，所当奔走就列，勉思称塞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275162_comment'></div>实以右支风痹，久成废疾，戴大恩而莫报，顾薄命而自怜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275162_comment'></div>冒昧控陈，诚非得已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275162_comment'></div>伏望特赐敷奏，收还新命，依旧差注宫观，庶沾微禄，以养馀齿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275162_comment'></div>候指挥。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1275162_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1180&endYear=1180')">1180年10月29日</a>　添差两浙东路安抚司参议官。以病再辞。作品：《除参议官辞免札子》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷三。）</span><div id='poem_1275163' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275163' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275163?labeling=true' target='_blank'>除参议官辞免劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1180年10月29日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275163")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275163_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275163'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275163'>右，某近以病控免恩命，十月二十九日，准敕特添差两浙东路安抚司参议官，仍釐务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275163_comment'></div>某窃自惟念一介妄庸，无所取似，疾病沈痼，已为废人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275163_comment'></div>公朝记识不忘，始则欲加祓饰，俾之厕于东观图书之间，终则怜其病贫，又复寘于职优俸厚之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275163_comment'></div>人微恩重，感极涕零。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275163_comment'></div>岂不欲舆疾之官，以拜大赐？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275163_comment'></div>实以抱病之久，驱驰道路，力所不能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275163_comment'></div>欲望特赐陶铸一宫观差遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275163_comment'></div>候指挥。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1275163_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1180&endYear=1180')">1180年10月</a>　为辞官事作书与周必大，冀其调护。作品：《与周丞相》十七。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷九。）</span><div id='poem_1275281' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275281' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275281?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与周丞相子充书<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其十五 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1176年春）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275281")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275281_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275281'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275281'>某荐辱教况，不胜感尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275281_comment'></div>春来气候不齐，医者深戒作劳，故久不拜状，然惓惓尊仰，则未始忘也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275281_comment'></div>其病躯萎痹，虽无增损，然心闲事省，神思却胜前冬侍坐时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275281_comment'></div>但常保此，幸已多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275281_comment'></div>钦夫之传，极为之惊忧，第细观牍尾乃二十七日，距二日已两旬，不应江陵尚未申到，犹觊消息之不真也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275281_comment'></div>元晦为人不耐，前此娄尝箴切之，候有便当委曲晓譬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275281_comment'></div>但不若调护，且令得祠，乃所以爱之也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1275281_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1180&endYear=1180')">1180年10月</a>　作书与潘景圭论学。并望助辞官事。作品：《与潘侍郎》六。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷九。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1180&endYear=1180')">1180年11月</a>　读《祭礼》。编《大事记》，修《读诗记》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1180&endYear=1180')">1180年11月22日</a>　主管亳州明道宫。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1180&endYear=1180')">1180年11月23日</a>　复陈亮来书，称陈亮“横飞直上，凌厉千载之表，真可谓大矣”作品：《与同甫书》二十六。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷十。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1180&endYear=1180')">1180年11月</a>　以奉祠致书周必大，冀其积极进取。作品：《与周丞相》十九。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷九。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1180&endYear=1180')">1180年11月26日</a>　家庙成，行时祭。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1180&endYear=1180')">1180年12月</a>　读《宗法》。编《大事记》，修《读诗记》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1180&endYear=1180')">1180年12月</a>　为东阳郭澄作墓铭。作品：《郭伯清墓志铭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷十三。）</span><div id='poem_1275679' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275679' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275679?labeling=true' target='_blank'>郭伯清墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（淳熙七年十二月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275679")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275679_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275679'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275679'>君讳澄，字伯清，姓郭氏，婺之东阳人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275679_comment'></div>曾祖招；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275679_comment'></div>祖知常；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275679_comment'></div>父良臣，将仕郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275679_comment'></div>绍兴末，军兴，入赀佐县官者，赐爵视任子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275679_comment'></div>将仕以伯清名上，补迪功郎，调隆兴府南昌县主簿，再调台州黄岩县主簿，皆不行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275679_comment'></div>尝请两浙转运司解，亦终不遂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275679_comment'></div>淳熙六年八月十二日，以疾卒，年始三十。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275679_comment'></div>娶朝奉郎、江南东路转运司主管文字吴良骥之女，后七十有九日亦卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275679_comment'></div>七年十二月初六日，合祔于罗青原将仕墓之左。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275679_comment'></div>三子，曰木、曰绍、曰爱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275679_comment'></div>伯清少时，将仕奇其敏悟，为筑西园舍旁，延名士讲授，乡之秀民愿请业者，悉聚而馆焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275679_comment'></div>伯清既用力于学，益知师友之可亲，辞气悃款，未尝不以善其身、迪其族、衣被其乡闾为主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275679_comment'></div>退而验其语，随其力之所至，皆有以自见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275679_comment'></div>识者始竦然，不敢以内交要誉期之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275679_comment'></div>岁尝大侵，乡人有不忍高其籴以牟利者，问之，则曰此吾在西园所讲也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275679_comment'></div>于是又知伯清之志非特信于朋友，且有从而化者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1275679_comment'></div>将仕没，里闾意伯清书生易与，睥睨者甚众，母杨夫人亦忧之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1275679_comment'></div>及涖家政，物情土俗，洞见表里，而一本于厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1275679_comment'></div>环田庐四旁，悍者驯，媢者弭，无有尝以事者，既服其能而重感其意也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1275679_comment'></div>平生所闻于师友者，方将次第出之，而伯清则死矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1275679_comment'></div>予每患学者颛固而窒于用才，如伯清乃遽夺之，不得极其所如往，予非特为郭氏惜也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1275679_comment'></div>伯清死今期年，往来者皆道西园弦诵之声不衰，兄弟朋友相厉以学，若有督趣之者，曰吾伯清不可负也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1275679_comment'></div>呜呼，是岂声音笑貌所能为哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1275679_comment'></div>予之知伯清盖有不尽者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1275679_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_1275679'>西园之木，与日升兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1275679_comment'></div>维子之植，众所冯兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1275679_comment'></div>西园之木，与岁老兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1275679_comment'></div>维子之志，神所保兮。</div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1275679_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1180&endYear=1180')">1180年12月</a>　应陆九渊请为陆九龄作墓铭，朱熹盛赞叙述发明有功，用意深至。作品：《陆先生墓志铭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷十三。）</span><div id='poem_1275680' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275680' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275680?labeling=true' target='_blank'>陆先生墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（淳熙七年十二月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275680")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275680_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275680'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275680'>陆氏出妫姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275680_comment'></div>陈公子敬仲适齐，别其氏为田。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275680_comment'></div>田氏有国，宣王封其少子通于平原陆乡，又别其氏为陆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275680_comment'></div>五代末有占名数抚之金溪者，曰德迁，盖唐乾宁宰相希声之孙也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275680_comment'></div>德迁生有祥，有祥生演，演生戬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275680_comment'></div>戬生居士贺，以学行为里人所宗，有子六人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275680_comment'></div>先生讳九龄，字子寿，于次为第五，幼明悟端重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275680_comment'></div>十年丧母，哀毁如成人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275680_comment'></div>少长，补郡博士弟子员。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275680_comment'></div>时秦丞相当国，场屋无道程氏学者，先生从故编得其说，独委心焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275680_comment'></div>久之，新博士且至，闻其雅以魏晋放逸自许，慨然叹曰：「此非吾所愿学也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275680_comment'></div>赋诗径归，结茅舍傍，讲习兼晨夜不怠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275680_comment'></div>先生年犹未冠，于取舍向背已知所择如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275680_comment'></div>吏部郎襄陵许公忻直道清节，在中朝名论甚高，屏居临川，闭门少所宾接，一见先生，亟折辈行与深语，恨相遇之晚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275680_comment'></div>他日许公起守邵阳，思与先生游，先生亦乐从其招。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275680_comment'></div>凡治体之升降，旧章之损益，前闻人之律度轨辙，每亹亹为先生言不厌，所以属之者厚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275680_comment'></div>既归，益大肆其力于学，广揽博咨，深观默养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1275680_comment'></div>如是者盖十馀年，乃束书入太学，太学知名士闻声争愿交。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1275680_comment'></div>始则乐其可亲，久则知其可事，屏所挟北面而称弟子者甚众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1275680_comment'></div>祭酒、司业，酌众论举，以为学录。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1275680_comment'></div>先之以身，正之以渐，行之以无事，虽跌宕见镌谯者，退亦心服，不知怨之所在焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1275680_comment'></div>登乾道五年进士第，迪功郎、桂阳军军学教授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1275680_comment'></div>以母老道远，改调兴国军军学教授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1275680_comment'></div>地濒大江，民寒啬，罕游校官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1275680_comment'></div>先生不以职閒自佚，端矩矱，肃衣冠，如临大众，劝绥引翼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1275680_comment'></div>士方兴于学，而先生以家难去官矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1275680_comment'></div>服除，调全州州学教授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1275680_comment'></div>未上，以疾终于家，实淳熙七年九月戊寅，享年四十有九。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1275680_comment'></div>母饶氏，继母邓氏，用光尧庆寿恩封太孺人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1275680_comment'></div>娶王氏，知通州瑊之女而元丰左丞之曾孙也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1275680_comment'></div>子艮之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1275680_comment'></div>女二人，皆幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1275680_comment'></div>是岁十二月甲申，葬于乡之万石塘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1275680_comment'></div>初，居士潜德不试，采司马氏冠昏丧祭仪行之家，至先生又绎先志而修明之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1275680_comment'></div>晨昏伏腊，奉盥请衽，觞豆饎爨，阖门千指，男女以班，各供其职，俭而安，庄而舒，薄而均。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1275680_comment'></div>礼俗既成，隽者不敢踔厉，朴者有所据依，顺弟之风，被于乡社而闻于天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1275680_comment'></div>其仪节品式，江西士大夫多能道之，至于先生忠敬乐易，优而柔之，曲而畅之，遂济登兹者，则非言语形容之所及矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1275680_comment'></div>先生兄弟皆志古耆学，燕居从容讲论道义，訚訚衎衎，和而不同，伯仲之间，自为师友。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1275680_comment'></div>虽先生所以成德，其资取者非一端，然家庭追琢封植之功与为多焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1275680_comment'></div>休暇则与子弟适场圃习射，曰是固男子之事也，自是里中士始不敢鄙弓矢为武夫末艺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1275680_comment'></div>岁恶多剽劫，或欲睥睨垣墙，曹耦必摇手相戒，是家射多命中，毋取死，故独无犬吠之警。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1275680_comment'></div>庐陵尝有茶寇，声摇旁郡，聚落皆入保。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1275680_comment'></div>并舍民走郡，请先生主之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1275680_comment'></div>郡如其请，门人多不悦，先生曰：「古者比闾之长，即五两之率也，士而耻此，则豪侠武断者专之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1275680_comment'></div>今文移动以军兴从事，郡县欲事之集，势必假借主者，彼乘是取必于里闾，亦何所不至哉」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1275680_comment'></div>寇虽不入境，闲习屯御，皆可为后法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1275680_comment'></div>其在兴国，学廪名存实亡，簿书漫漶不可考。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1275680_comment'></div>先生为覈实催理受输之法白郡，授有司行之，科条简明，士得其养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1275680_comment'></div>凡经世之务，职分所当知者，未有闻而不讲，讲而不究，此一二条特因事而见者耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1275680_comment'></div>先生和顺不违物，而非意自不能干；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1275680_comment'></div>简直不徇人，而与居久益有味。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1275680_comment'></div>四方学者，踵门请益，群疑塞胸，纠缠轇轕，虽善辨者不能解。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1275680_comment'></div>先生从容启告，莫不涣然失其疑而退。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1275680_comment'></div>非惟动悟孚格，固有所本，亦其用力于自治者，既专且久，人之疢疾皆尝折肱，浮湛滑涩，适中其病，听之者于其心有戚戚焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1275680_comment'></div>至于捍格不入，必宽养以俟其可，未尝无益而杂施之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1275680_comment'></div>天下之治方术者多矣，囿于异端小道者既不足与议，晚进新学，间有闻君子之馀论者，又多既其文而不既其实，摹规而画圆，拟矩而作方，虽或似之，而卒非也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1275680_comment'></div>方先生勇于求道之时，愤悱直前，盖有不由阶序者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1275680_comment'></div>然其所志者大，所据者实，有肯綮之阻，虽积九仞之功不敢遂有毫釐之偏，虽立万夫之表不敢安，公听并观，却立四顾，弗造于至平至粹之地弗措也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1275680_comment'></div>属纩之夕，与其昆弟语，犹以天下学术人才为念。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1275680_comment'></div>少焉正卧，整衣衾，理须髯，恬然而终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1275680_comment'></div>所谓仁以为己任，死而后已者，盖于此见之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1275680_comment'></div>荆州牧广汉张公栻，与先生不相识，晚岁还书，相与讲学问大端，期以世道之重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1275680_comment'></div>无几何而张公没，又半岁而先生下世矣，岂道之显晦果有数存乎其间邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1275680_comment'></div>虽然，来者无穷，而义理之在人心者不可泯也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1275680_comment'></div>先生之志，必有嗣之者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1275680_comment'></div>葬有日，其友吕某为铭二十九字识其窆曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_65_1275680'>自古皆有死，尽其道而终者几希。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1275680_comment'></div>是维宋陆先生之墓，百世之下，尚永保之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_66_1275680_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1180&endYear=1180')">1180年</a>　本年魏国佐多书问，有复函，道思念之情。作品：《与魏寺丞》一。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷九。）</span><div id='poem_1275308' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275308' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275308?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与魏寺丞国佐书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1180年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275308")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275308_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275308'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275308'>某一病垂死，两年来稍稍调理，饮食起居皆不须人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275308_comment'></div>虽右支萎弱，既不仕官，闭门养疾，袖手缓步，初不知疾之在亡也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275308_comment'></div>以此日用间极自适。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275308_comment'></div>百念灰冷，但思见君子，犹往来胸次耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275308_comment'></div>今岁辱诲墨，至于四五，爱念之笃，发于篇什。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275308_comment'></div>病中不敢劳心，无由赓续，然此意何可忘也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275308_comment'></div>家食之久，公论甚咈然，及此暇日，政可澄汰磨治，多阅天下之义理，以发挥世业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275308_comment'></div>临纸不胜拳拳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275308_comment'></div>恐欲知即今病状，故力疾强作数字，腕弱不能详布。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1275308_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1180&endYear=1180')">1180年</a>　为诸生说《周礼》等。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1181&endYear=1181')">1181年1月</a>　读《论语》、《欧阳公集》。编《大事记》，修《读诗记》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1181&endYear=1181')">1181年2月</a>　读《论语》、编《大事记》，修《读诗记》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1181&endYear=1181')">1181年2月</a>　门人巩丰来访。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1181&endYear=1181')">1181年2月19日</a>　王安自鄱阳徒步来请吕祖谦为母作墓铭，遂扶病作墓表、墓铭。作品：《鄱阳王安母程氏墓志铭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷十五《庚子辛丑日记》）</span><div id='poem_1275681' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275681' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275681?labeling=true' target='_blank'>鄱阳王安母程氏墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（淳熙七年二月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275681")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275681_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275681'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275681'>自予病废，退居婺之金华，杜门谢客。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275681_comment'></div>姻戚哀其羸而重于数劳之也，亦罕过之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275681_comment'></div>今年春，大雪十日，穷巷无行者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275681_comment'></div>午睡起，闻啄剥声，顾童奴曰：「是必有异，趣视之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275681_comment'></div>往应门，则曰：「是东莱吕氏乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275681_comment'></div>启关以谒，入曰：「鄱阳哀子王安」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275681_comment'></div>予亟扶曳，与为礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275681_comment'></div>且拜且泣曰：「安不幸丧母，不自意忍死图大事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275681_comment'></div>既斩板矣，又不自量，欲传载吾母之德善，以纾罔极之痛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275681_comment'></div>用敢请于家君，聚粮趼足，自归于门下」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275681_comment'></div>予蹙然曰：「子于亲则笃矣，以某之罢惰，尚无以自见于今世，属以千世不朽之托，则非其人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275681_comment'></div>手足挛痹，三岁于兹，强以冶金伐石之事，则非其时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275681_comment'></div>不宁惟是，妇人名不出阃而墓之有碑，盖汉氏之末造也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275681_comment'></div>子苟尚志饬身，使后世知有子姓名，为之亲者斯不泯矣，何以文为」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275681_comment'></div>则又泣数行下，曰：「先生之教既闻命矣，抑中心有不能自已者，敢试陈之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275681_comment'></div>安之家聚口众，度伏腊堇堇耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275681_comment'></div>吾母佐吾父，缩衣节食，聘士教子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1275681_comment'></div>塾师姜君庆贫甚，独与二女居，吾母亲为拊养，已而皆资遣之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1275681_comment'></div>姜君有消渴疾，每讲罢，索巨觥引满，如奉漏瓮沃焦釜，少辽缓则殆不济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1275681_comment'></div>阅数年，吾母终无倦色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1275681_comment'></div>鄱阳，士乡也，安之椎钝，而有司两寘之贡籍，闾巷之人皆为王氏贺，吾母独未以为足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1275681_comment'></div>安未敢以是为报也，三十年间，龊龌拘畏，虽无能短长，乡之长者以其不叛于士检，稍稍遣子弟从安游，安始少自慰，而吾母则亡矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1275681_comment'></div>苟免丧，犹视息于人间，固不敢自画以负吾母之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1275681_comment'></div>道远年徂，惧不克济，先生幸赐之言，此志岂不益可保」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1275681_comment'></div>予矍然曰：「子之志及此，岂敢以疾病为解」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1275681_comment'></div>考其家世本末，孺人姓程氏，饶之德兴人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1275681_comment'></div>曾祖守益，祖万，父棫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1275681_comment'></div>适同邑王君彦晖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1275681_comment'></div>淳熙三年，天子称觞德寿宫，赐高年者爵，孺人实始封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1275681_comment'></div>后三年十月二十六日，以疾卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1275681_comment'></div>子男子四人：长宾，次安，次宪，次宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1275681_comment'></div>子女子二人，皆已嫁而卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1275681_comment'></div>孙男女十二人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1275681_comment'></div>十二月六日，葬于县之唐原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1275681_comment'></div>又明年二月，乃表其墓，又为诗遗之曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_34_1275681'>藐是吾身，吾亲之枝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1275681_comment'></div>可舟可梁，干者百围。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1275681_comment'></div>死事皇皇，生事业业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1275681_comment'></div>毋俾斯文，独有枝叶。</div><div id='poem_sentence_37_1275681_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1181&endYear=1181')">1181年2月</a>　与朱熹书，议及陆九渊为学病处，但亦有所长。陆九渊有约来访。作品：《与朱侍讲》三十九。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷八。）</span><div id='poem_1275222' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275222' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275222?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与朱侍讲元晦书<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二十二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1180年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275222")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275222_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275222'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275222'>某哀苦待尽，它无足言者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275222_comment'></div>引辞今有报否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275222_comment'></div>格以近制，以事势观之，恐未必得伸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275222_comment'></div>祠禄正协「周之则受」之义，独改秩有当商量处，然前代于贤者不能致而就官之者盖多矣，窃谓少逡巡而受之可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275222_comment'></div>若确然不回，则名愈高而礼愈加，异时有难居者耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275222_comment'></div>君子之谋，始终皆举之，要须审虑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275222_comment'></div>令嗣气质甚淳，已令就潘叔度舍傍书室寝处<span class='inlineComment2'>（不在其家。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275222_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1275222", 1275222, "Clauses/18/Comments/1")'>同窗</span>者乃叔度之弟景愈<span class='inlineComment2'>（字叔昌。）</span>，年三十馀，甚有志趣，有意务实，相处当有益<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275222_comment'></div>已立定课程，令嗣当自寄呈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275222_comment'></div>唯每日到某处，则与叔度兄弟偕来，不许过它斋舍<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275222_comment'></div>自馀虑之所及，不敢不尽，幸少宽念也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275222_comment'></div>别纸疏谕，以不欲滞此介，未得详禀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275222_comment'></div>令嗣更留一兵在此，俟半月诸事及课程见得次第，当遣归，恐欲知其肄习居处之详也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275222_comment'></div>周教授《论语》方借看，并俟遣此兵时缕缕求教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275222_comment'></div>此间方刊《横渠集》，断手当首拜纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275222_comment'></div>《说文》苦无善本，见令嗣说方雠校，昨见刘子澄说赣州方欲刊书，自可径送渠令锓木也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275222_comment'></div>「洙泗言仁」未合处，因便望录示，亦欲得思索也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1275222_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1275222'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_7_1275222_0'>⑴ 叔昌亦自工于程试，足可商量。五六年前，尝为太学解魁。近三两岁来，却都放下举业，专意为学。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_9_1275222_0'>⑵ 虽到某处，亦不许独来，盖城市间不得不如此过防。又众中人亦多端，恐志未定，或迁易耳。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1275222_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1181&endYear=1181')">1181年2月</a>　朱熹在南康修石堤成，为作记。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1181&endYear=1181')">1181年3月</a>　读《宗法》。编《大事记》，修《读诗记》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1181&endYear=1181')">1181年3月8日</a>　送诸葛诚之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1181&endYear=1181')">1181年闰3月</a>　读《医经》。编《大事记》，修《读诗记》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1181&endYear=1181')">1181年闰3月13日</a>　应游玠请，为其母作墓铭。作品：《邵武游玠母墓志》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷十五《庚子辛丑日记》）</span><div id='poem_1275682' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275682' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275682?labeling=true' target='_blank'>金华游玠母陈氏墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（淳熙八年四月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275682")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275682_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275682'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275682'>出赤松门十二里，并驿道，得支径，右折而南，冈阜迤逦相属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275682_comment'></div>行三里许，至后湖之原，有墓焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275682_comment'></div>是为郡贡士陈敏之女、迪功郎致仕游夔之妻、迪功郎新澧州州学教授玠之母。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275682_comment'></div>生十有七年归游氏，又四十一年以疾卒，实淳熙七年十二月二日，其葬以明年四月四日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275682_comment'></div>男五人，长即玠也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275682_comment'></div>次璞，次玑，次珙，次瑀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275682_comment'></div>女三人，长适钟麟，次适汪知古，幼在室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275682_comment'></div>前葬，玠奉贽币请曰：「玠之母本儒家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275682_comment'></div>方三舍法行时，郡以外祖充赋，贫不能上道，竟老于布衣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275682_comment'></div>吾母尝恨之，故相家君教诸子尤力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275682_comment'></div>玠每游学，纫补炮烹，米盐靡密，悉出吾母之手。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275682_comment'></div>甫得一官，未及致钟釜之养，而遽悼弃之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275682_comment'></div>邻里莫不为玠酸鼻，而玠之穷毒，则人有不及知者焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275682_comment'></div>建安之游，唐德宗世有别居邵武者，入国朝枝叶益蕃，独玠之系无仕者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275682_comment'></div>崇宁中，吾祖舆母隃岭徙名数于婺之金华，今七十有八年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275682_comment'></div>玠既赐第，家君诲之曰：『汝曾祖以上，兆域皆在邵武，汝祖岁或一再往省焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275682_comment'></div>汝诸父虽不及汝祖之数，犹间往省焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1275682_comment'></div>自吾之老，不能蒙霜露、犯寒暑，以问讯松槚，然每往来吾心也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1275682_comment'></div>汝幸免于课试之累，盍趣装代吾行』？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1275682_comment'></div>玠再拜受命，比还，吾母已属疾，且喜且劳曰：『吾儿始识先世丘垄矣，跋涉无恙乎』？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1275682_comment'></div>改月，遂至大故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1275682_comment'></div>治汤液护衾裯之日，视诸弟为独少，此玠终天之恨也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1275682_comment'></div>祖墓岸城濠，湫隘，无以族昭穆，乃卜地于城之东。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1275682_comment'></div>妇人无外事，法不当有铭，然玠不孝之罪，上通于天，一旦殒灭，诸弟稚昧，未胜洒扫之职，将不暝目于地下矣，愿先生哀而识之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1275682_comment'></div>予告之曰：「子之家常如今日，虽八百里之邵武，不知其远，况十馀里之后湖乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1275682_comment'></div>苟其不然，则负城之阡，犹可忧也，子盍反其本矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1275682_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_1275682'>北门之池，蔽芾其阴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1275682_comment'></div>东门之原，封之自今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1275682_comment'></div>我图其新，而旧勿替。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1275682_comment'></div>勿替引之，维昭武是视。</div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1275682_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1181&endYear=1181')">1181年闰3月28日</a>　与范元章、黄英甫诸人会饭。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1181&endYear=1181')">1181年闰3月29日</a>　送黄几先。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1181&endYear=1181')">1181年春</a>　致书周必大，称许陆游，冀周必大为之说赵汝愚。作品：《与周丞相》二十。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷九。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1181&endYear=1181')">1181年春</a>　曾撙以吕本中与曾信道尺牍墨本来，作文陈述吕氏家族与江西学者之间的密切关系。作品：《书伯祖紫微翁与曾信道手简后》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷七。）</span><div id='poem_1275522' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275522' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275522?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题伯祖紫微翁与曾信道手简后</a><span class='authorDate'>（1181年春）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275522")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275522_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275522'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275522'>先君子尝诲某曰：「吾家全盛时，与江西诸贤特厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275522_comment'></div>文靖公与晏公戮力王室，正献公静默自守，名实加于上下，盖自欧阳公发之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275522_comment'></div>平生交友如王荆公、刘侍读、曾舍人，屈指不满十。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275522_comment'></div>虽中间以国论与荆公异同，元丰末守广陵，钟山犹有书来，甚惓惓，且有绝江款郡斋之约，会公召归乃止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275522_comment'></div>已而自讲筵还政路，遂相元祐二刘、三孔，曾子开、黄鲁直诸公，皆公所甄叙也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275522_comment'></div>侍讲于荆公乃通家子弟，李泰伯入汴，亦尝讲绎焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275522_comment'></div>绍圣后，始与李君行游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275522_comment'></div>晚节居党籍，右丞以筦库之禄养亲，虽门可设爵罗，然四方有志之士多不远千里从公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275522_comment'></div>谢无逸、汪信民、饶德操自临川至，奉几杖、侍左右如子侄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275522_comment'></div>退见右丞，亦卑抑严事，不敢用钧敌之礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275522_comment'></div>舍人以长孙应接宾客，三君一见，折辈行为忘年交，谈赏篇什，闻于天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275522_comment'></div>是时吾家筐筥琐碎，僮仆能言，诸名胜无不谙悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275522_comment'></div>南渡以来，此事便废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275522_comment'></div>绍兴初，寇贼稍定，舍人与诸父相扶携出桂岭，愒临川，访旧友，多死生，慨然太息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275522_comment'></div>乃收聚故人子曾益父、裘父辈，与吾兄弟共学，亲指画，孳孳不怠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275522_comment'></div>既又作诗勉之，今集中寄临川聚学诸生数诗是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275522_comment'></div>自秦氏专国，风俗日益隘陋，吾几案间无江西书札久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1275522_comment'></div>盖江西人物之盛衰，观人文者将于此乎考。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1275522_comment'></div>而吾家江西贤士大夫之疏密，亦门户兴替之一验也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1275522_comment'></div>言毕复蹙然久之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1275522_comment'></div>某再拜识之，不敢忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1275522_comment'></div>建昌曾信道丈，以学问识度为舍人伯祖所许，不幸早世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1275522_comment'></div>其子撙节夫，复与某为同年进士，而节夫外舅李夔州，则某少所承事者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1275522_comment'></div>故虽未得与节夫合堂同席，而知其父子之贤为详。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1275522_comment'></div>病废三年，不复知户限外事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1275522_comment'></div>今年春，节夫以伯祖与信道丈尺牍墨本见遗，反复展玩，不能去手。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1275522_comment'></div>顾诸弟曰：「吾家其犹庶几乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1275522_comment'></div>今日真得江西书札矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1275522_comment'></div>因录先君之语寄节夫，且以交相厉云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1275522_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1181&endYear=1181')">1181年4月</a>　读《医经》、《正蒙》。编《大事记》，修《读诗记》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1181&endYear=1181')">1181年4月19日</a>　门人黄人杰离别。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1181&endYear=1181')">1181年4月30日</a>　林鼐来访。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1181&endYear=1181')">1181年春</a>　复朱熹来函，请朱熹将其《通鉴纲目》录示。作品：《与朱侍讲》四十。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷八。）</span><div id='poem_1275228' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275228' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275228?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与朱侍讲元晦书<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二十八 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1181年春）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275228")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275228_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275228'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275228'>某祥祭又复改月，追慕荼毒，无复生意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275228_comment'></div>数日前携受之及两舍弟过坟旁十数里至小庵中，在瀑泉之下，山水雄峻，人迹罕到，耳目清净，殊可翻阅也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275228_comment'></div>自春初谢遣生徒，应接既简，遂得专意读书，亦渐似靠实，但相远未得质正咨请为恨耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275228_comment'></div>所谕致知、克己不可偏，甚善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275228_comment'></div>前此多见友朋，每校量义理，而于践履处少点检，故发「裒多益寡」之论，然要如来谕乃完粹耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275228_comment'></div>吴林老之说，就解《论语》上看则有味，原其所发，则渠平生坐在记诵考究处，故凡见何必读书之类，辨之必力，其发亦自偏也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275228_comment'></div>拣择时文杂文之类，向者特为举子辈课试计耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275228_comment'></div>如去冬再择四十篇，正是见作举业者，明白则少曲折，轻快则欠典重，故各举其一使之类为耳，亦别无深意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275228_comment'></div>今思稽其所敝，诚为至论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275228_comment'></div>此等文字，自是以往，决不复再拈出，非特讱其出而已也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275228_comment'></div>《礼运》诚是展转附益之差，但胡氏以此为纲领，则可疑耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275228_comment'></div>《学记》、《中庸集解》及它石刻，皆领。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275228_comment'></div>《学记》所论甚正，但《序》述县尹语言微似过重<span class='inlineComment2'>（若「深造自得」等语。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275228_comment'></div>虽曰文字之常，然闻石子重乃笃志于学者，吾人分上所以相期，政当损饰就实耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275228_comment'></div>大抵论义理，谈治道，辟异端，则不当有一毫回避屈挠，至于说自己及著实朋友，只当一味敛缩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275228_comment'></div>时义与工夫，皆当然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275228_comment'></div>《集解》序引指出高奇等弊，极有益。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1275228_comment'></div>但李翱似不足言，而「哀公问政」以下六章，虽载在《家语》，皆同时问答之言，然安知非子思裁取之以备《中庸》之义乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1275228_comment'></div>有未然处，望见教。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1275228_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1181&endYear=1181')">1181年5月</a>　读《论语》、《易》。编《大事记》，修《读诗记》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1181&endYear=1181')">1181年5月15日</a>　定《古周易》十二篇成，门人王莘叟笔受《音训》一篇。作《书所定古周易十二篇后》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷七。）</span><div id='poem_1275523' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275523' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275523?labeling=true' target='_blank'>书所定古周易十二篇后</a><span class='authorDate'>（1181年5月15日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275523")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275523_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275523'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275523'>汉兴，言《易》者六家，独费氏传古文《易》，而不立于学官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275523_comment'></div>刘向以中古文《易经》校施、孟、梁丘经，或脱去旡咎、悔亡，惟费氏经与古文同，然则真孔氏遗书也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275523_comment'></div>东京马融、郑玄皆为费氏学，其书始盛行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275523_comment'></div>今学官所立王弼《易》，虽宗庄、老，其书固郑氏书也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275523_comment'></div>费氏《易》在汉诸家中最近古，最见排摈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275523_comment'></div>千载之后，岿然独存，岂非天哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275523_comment'></div>自康成、辅嗣合《彖》、《象》、《文言》于经，学者遂不见古本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275523_comment'></div>近世嵩山晁氏编《古周易》，将以复于其旧，而其刊补离合之际，览者或以为未安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275523_comment'></div>某谨因晁氏书，参考传记，复定为十二篇，篇目卷帙，一以古为断，其说具于音训。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1275523_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1181&endYear=1181')">1181年5月24日</a>　送陈正己。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1181&endYear=1181')">1181年6月</a>　读《近思录》。编《大事记》，修《读诗记》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1181&endYear=1181')">1181年夏</a>　石应之来访，居四十八日而别，并有秋约。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1181&endYear=1181')">1181年7月</a>　读《论语》。编《大事记》，修《读诗记》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1181&endYear=1181')">1181年7月26日</a>　作《大事记》已两年。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1181&endYear=1181')">1181年7月27日</a>　修《读诗记·公刘》。修诗至此结束，朱熹有《吕氏家塾读诗记序》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1181&endYear=1181')">1181年7月28日</a>　《庚子辛丑日记》封笔，至此已一年七个月。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1181&endYear=1181')">1181年7月</a>　是月詹仪之送葵轩《论语》来，以为为文更稳密。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1181&endYear=1181')">1181年7月</a>　函请朱熹批评《文鉴》，并痛悼郑伯熊病逝。作品：《与朱侍讲》四十二。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷八。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1181&endYear=1181')">1181年7月</a>　有与石应之手札。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1181&endYear=1181')">1181年</a>　本年有抹荆公目录。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1181&endYear=1181')">1181年</a>　有《欧公本末》、《卧游录》、《坐右录》。阅《熙宁奏对》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1181&endYear=1181')">1181年</a>　定《宗法条目》并行于家中。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷一。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1181&endYear=1181')">1181年</a>　本年尤袤有函候起居，有复函。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1181&endYear=1181')">1181年7月29日</a>　终于正寝，享年四十五。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1181&endYear=1181')">1181年11月3日</a>　葬明招山。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
黄冈
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='9e5fdc9bf0794e16b6a092be9052f8e5_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("9e5fdc9bf0794e16b6a092be9052f8e5");'><span id='9e5fdc9bf0794e16b6a092be9052f8e5_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1164&endYear=1164')">1164年</a>，28岁</div><div id='9e5fdc9bf0794e16b6a092be9052f8e5' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1164&endYear=1164')">1164年4月</a>　如黄州省父，过九江，访同门陈芷。作品：《过九江赠同舍陈伯秀》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史外集》卷五。）</span><div id='poem_94141' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_94141' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/94141?labeling=true' target='_blank'>过九江赠同舍陈伯秀<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（1164年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_94141")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_94141_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_94141_0'>① 伯秀名芷，少与太史同游三山林少颖先生之门，此诗赋以赠之（四字原缺，据续金华本补）</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_94141'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_94141'>异时夫子门，论交心独可。<div id='poem_sentence_0_94141_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_94141'>晨窗并几案，莫檠共灯火。<div id='poem_sentence_1_94141_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_94141'>同升大宗伯，道阻山砐硪。<div id='poem_sentence_2_94141_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_94141'>淡墨湿栖鸦，天开棘闱锁。<div id='poem_sentence_3_94141_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_94141'>高张三百丈，遍数不及我。<div id='poem_sentence_4_94141_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_94141'>咫尺判飞沈，鹏抟笑鸢堕。<div id='poem_sentence_5_94141_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_94141'>音尘两疏阔，岁月悉箭笴。<div id='poem_sentence_6_94141_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_94141'>风吹樊口帆，雨系浔阳柁。<div id='poem_sentence_7_94141_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_94141'>故人尚一尉，旌旗穿紫逻。<div id='poem_sentence_8_94141_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_94141'>相逢话旧游，拨置朱墨夥。<div id='poem_sentence_9_94141_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_94141'>握手忘寒温，屈指半轗轲。<div id='poem_sentence_10_94141_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_94141'>官居岸平湖，波涛日舂簸。<div id='poem_sentence_11_94141_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_94141'>饱看五老面，此计殊未左。<div id='poem_sentence_12_94141_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_94141'>山房旧闻名，欲往辄不果。<div id='poem_sentence_13_94141_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_94141'>须君发其藏，万卷书绕坐<span class='inlineComment2'>（以上《东莱吕太史文集》外集卷五）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_14_94141_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_94141'></div><div id='poem_sentence_15_94141_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

-----title
东阳
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='69d5d810ac5a448d811b72b44d60d65c_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("69d5d810ac5a448d811b72b44d60d65c");'><span id='69d5d810ac5a448d811b72b44d60d65c_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1168&endYear=1168')">1168年</a>，32岁</div><div id='69d5d810ac5a448d811b72b44d60d65c' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1168&endYear=1168')">1168年冬</a>　在曹家巷授业，讲授《左传》，有《左氏博议》，不论经旨，传播颇广。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱博议》卷首。）</span><div id='poem_1275507' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275507' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275507?labeling=true' target='_blank'>左氏博议序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1168年冬）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275507")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275507_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275507'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275507'>《左氏博议》者，为诸生课试之作也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275507_comment'></div>始予屏处东阳之武川，仰林俯壑，出户而望，目尽无来人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275507_comment'></div>居半岁，里中稍稍披蓬藋从予游，谈馀语隙，波及课试之文，予思有以佐其笔端，乃取《左氏书》理乱得失之迹，疏其说于下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275507_comment'></div>旬储月积，浸就编帙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275507_comment'></div>诸生岁时休沐，必抄寘楮中，解其归装无虚者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275507_comment'></div>并舍姻党，复从而广之，曼衍四出，漫不可收。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275507_comment'></div>客或咎予之易其言，予徐应之曰：子亦闻乡邻之求医者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275507_comment'></div>深痼隐疾，人所羞道而讳称者，揭之大涂，惟恐行者不阅，阅者不播，彼岂腼然忘耻哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275507_comment'></div>德欲蓄而病欲彰也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275507_comment'></div>予离群而索居有年矣，过而莫予辅也，跌而莫予挽也，心术之差，见闻之误而莫予正也，幸因是书而胸中所存、所操、所识、所习，毫愆发谬，随笔呈露，举无留藏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275507_comment'></div>又幸而假课试以为媒，借逢掖以为邮，遍致于诸公长者之侧，或矜而谪，或愠而谪，或侮而谯，一语闻则一病瘳，其获不既丰矣乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275507_comment'></div>传愈博，病愈白，益愈众于予也，奚损？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275507_comment'></div>遂次第其语以谂观者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275507_comment'></div>凡《春秋》经旨，概不敢僣论，而枝辞赘喻，则举子所以资课试者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275507_comment'></div>东莱吕祖谦伯恭序。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1275507_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1275507'><span class='label'>按：</span>《左氏博议》卷首，影印文渊阁四库全书本。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1275507_comment'></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

-----title
德清
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='978886286f1b480d87f075285d96d759_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("978886286f1b480d87f075285d96d759");'><span id='978886286f1b480d87f075285d96d759_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年</a>，33岁</div><div id='978886286f1b480d87f075285d96d759' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年5月9日</a>　因亲迎韩氏及除太学博士事遣散诸生，有学规《己丑规约》、《谢遣初学约束》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年5月20日</a>　亲迎韩元吉季女韩氏（螺）为继室。<br /><a href="javascript:
