id='poem_title_1275722' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275722?labeling=true' target='_blank'>修德清慈相寺月池疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1169年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275722")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275722_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275722'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275722'>断崖吐月，才出半规；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275722_comment'></div>古甃涵星，尚怀全璧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275722_comment'></div>久矣宝奁之废，时哉玉斧之修。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275722_comment'></div>护此寒清，被其氛翳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275722_comment'></div>名高诗社，再传和仲之符；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275722_comment'></div>价重帝城，复置文饶之递。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275722_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1275722_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年5月</a>　有与潘景宪书，安置学中事务，强调和肃为上。作品：《答潘叔度》二十六。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷十。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年6月6日</a>　除太学博士，待阙。作谢宰相启。作品：《除太学博士谢陈丞相启》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷四。）</span><div id='poem_1275482' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275482' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275482?labeling=true' target='_blank'>除太学博士谢陈丞相启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1169年6月6日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275482")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275482_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275482'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275482'>里闬堙沈，久安分守；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275482_comment'></div>胶庠清邃，骤被诏除。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275482_comment'></div>夫何逖远之踪，犹在选抡之数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275482_comment'></div>窃以合烝髦于万县，课以度程；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275482_comment'></div>嗣绝学于六经，司其训故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275482_comment'></div>名挂成均之属，号为儒者之先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275482_comment'></div>于秩虽微，所系实大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275482_comment'></div>苟训迪渐摩之本，曾弗玩心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275482_comment'></div>则呻吟佔毕之馀，焉能塞责？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275482_comment'></div>厥职升降，视人重轻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275482_comment'></div>如某者气禀颛蒙，志尚疏阔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275482_comment'></div>定交铅椠，不知岁月之多；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275482_comment'></div>借助韦弦，未觉悔尤之寡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275482_comment'></div>每因宴豫，窃自揣量。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275482_comment'></div>惟材谫故不足俎豆英游，惟识眊故不足权衡世变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275482_comment'></div>继以闵忧之积，益于宠利之疏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275482_comment'></div>于命义而徼求，匪惟失己；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1275482_comment'></div>饰庸虚而衒鬻，又复欺人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1275482_comment'></div>徒欲粗试于州县簿领之间，曷敢自通于廊庙钧陶之上？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1275482_comment'></div>忽冒除书之及，罔知拜赐之端。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1275482_comment'></div>意者概视戚疏，曲加诱掖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1275482_comment'></div>畀教导之任，使预怀芜废之惭；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1275482_comment'></div>宽奔走之期，使尚有讨论之暇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1275482_comment'></div>进之以作其怠，缓之以俟其成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1275482_comment'></div>自视缺然，何以领此？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1275482_comment'></div>斯盖伏遇某官翼宣天縡，弼亮皇猷，深惟封殖于丕基，畴若招徕于群献。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1275482_comment'></div>荆金梁铁，贡九牧以并登；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1275482_comment'></div>粤镈燕函，列百工而咸在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1275482_comment'></div>多取或容于舛误，广求遂逮于孱愚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1275482_comment'></div>某敢不䌷绎旧闻，研思微旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1275482_comment'></div>千年蠹简，倘输毫发之劳；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1275482_comment'></div>一世龙门，庶答丘山之施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1275482_comment'></div>过此以往，未知所裁。</div><div id='poem_sentence_32_1275482_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年6月</a>　使人送信给朱熹即《与朱侍讲》，代人向朱熹求取《伊川易传》锓板。一。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷七。）</span><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
衢州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='ec14a9de167544e69f2dd5c58f330fef_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("ec14a9de167544e69f2dd5c58f330fef");'><span id='ec14a9de167544e69f2dd5c58f330fef_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年</a>，33岁</div><div id='ec14a9de167544e69f2dd5c58f330fef' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年9月27日</a>　如三衢见汪应辰及刘子澄。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='b19ef10f2c2e4d2d928dccb0987cc3d9_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("b19ef10f2c2e4d2d928dccb0987cc3d9");'><span id='b19ef10f2c2e4d2d928dccb0987cc3d9_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年</a>，33岁</div><div id='b19ef10f2c2e4d2d928dccb0987cc3d9' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年10月2日</a>　赴衢州信安吊张淑坚。作墓铭。作品：《张监镇墓志铭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷十三。）</span><div id='poem_1275674' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275674' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275674?labeling=true' target='_blank'>张监镇墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（淳熙三年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275674")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275674_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275674'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275674'>乾道五年，信安张杰赴于其友吕某曰：「先君以七月二十五日弃诸孤，敢告于执事」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275674_comment'></div>某既与使者为礼，即办装，粤十月二日会其葬于衢之西安县靖安乡九龙山已下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275674_comment'></div>杰拜且哭曰：「先君之葬也，遽未有辞以识诸幽，将惟子是属」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275674_comment'></div>授以汴人赵焯行状一通，某再拜兴受，退而于役于仕，于丧于疾，栖置笔研，未克具藁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275674_comment'></div>杰以书趣曰：「己丑之会，吾子尝坠言焉，今墓木之叶七易矣，吾子独无意乎」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275674_comment'></div>某矍然惊谢，乃序而铭之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275674_comment'></div>君讳淑坚，字正卿，其先自开封迁于衢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275674_comment'></div>曾祖智全，尚书都官郎中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275674_comment'></div>祖咏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275674_comment'></div>考彦琦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275674_comment'></div>君蚤向意文学，虽以季父任为承信郎，年馀四十，足未尝至吏部门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275674_comment'></div>研索典籍，矻矻如诸生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275674_comment'></div>周览旁浃，星历、方剂、篆籀之属，无所不窥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275674_comment'></div>浮湛里闾，遇疾痛呻吟者，或和药饮之，随失其疾，世医莫能识其节度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275674_comment'></div>谒者浸众，君悠然应之，不为彼此薄厚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275674_comment'></div>晚岁始出，监信州汭口镇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275674_comment'></div>镇居往来之冲，课额夥甚，前政数负殿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1275674_comment'></div>君通商平酤，经入用登。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1275674_comment'></div>铜官铁官漕卒，将输如织，颉颃侵暴，镇官素不能令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1275674_comment'></div>自君之至，道镇境者皆抑首屏气，无敢哗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1275674_comment'></div>庀局甫四月，卒官下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1275674_comment'></div>镇民相与负其柩还衢，其孤强之僦直，委去不顾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1275674_comment'></div>盖君于是年四十有八，官止承节郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1275674_comment'></div>有《诗》、《书》解合三十卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1275674_comment'></div>始君程督诸子，诵肄蚤夜不置。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1275674_comment'></div>已而长子策名，人意其绳约当少宽，君所以训厉之者益峻，甚于他子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1275674_comment'></div>然则君之期其子，其诸异乎人之期者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1275674_comment'></div>娶叶氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1275674_comment'></div>三子：杰，迪功郎、宁国府府学教授；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1275674_comment'></div>次皋、次舆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1275674_comment'></div>一女，适袁焕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1275674_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_31_1275674'>缓己之进，匪辰之竞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1275674_comment'></div>急人之忧，匪艺之羞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1275674_comment'></div>期子之大，匪胜之怠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1275674_comment'></div>不怠其昌，视此石章。</div><div id='poem_sentence_34_1275674_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='693f1887a56c4da6aa8d421db07afbb3_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("693f1887a56c4da6aa8d421db07afbb3");'><span id='693f1887a56c4da6aa8d421db07afbb3_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1171&endYear=1171')">1171年</a>，35岁</div><div id='693f1887a56c4da6aa8d421db07afbb3' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1171&endYear=1171')">1171年7月6日</a>　吕大器自吉州奉祠归，吕祖谦至龙游迎父。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='e20ff4b948d848c69ba6eb1872d96dad_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("e20ff4b948d848c69ba6eb1872d96dad");'><span id='e20ff4b948d848c69ba6eb1872d96dad_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1174&endYear=1174')">1174年</a>，38岁</div><div id='e20ff4b948d848c69ba6eb1872d96dad' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1174&endYear=1174')">1174年5月13日</a>　如衢州探望汪应辰。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1174&endYear=1174')">1174年5月</a>　应门人戚如圭、戚如玉、戚如璧、戚如琥之请，为其母作墓铭。作品：《金华戚如圭母周氏墓志铭》<div id='poem_1275654' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275654' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275654?labeling=true' target='_blank'>金华戚如圭母周氏墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（淳熙元年五月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275654")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275654_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275654'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275654'>门内之治，女美、妇德、母道，三而有一焉，既足自附女史，具是而始终衷者，实维金华戚君杨之夫人周氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275654_comment'></div>夫人，戚君同县人，生七年而丧其父。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275654_comment'></div>属睦寇陷郡城，母杜夫人提以匿林薮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275654_comment'></div>乱定，又丧其母，于是祖母老矣，家人惧伤其意，撤几筵不能如期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275654_comment'></div>夫人与伯姊饭必先祭，见者为涕下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275654_comment'></div>蚤夜祖母侧，油油亹亹不少懈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275654_comment'></div>已而祖母没，无所归，鞠于母家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275654_comment'></div>弟赘刘氏，复偕夫人依焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275654_comment'></div>卑身祗饬，刘氏媪爱之过所生，褚囊键闭，一以诿夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275654_comment'></div>为择嘉对，以归于戚君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275654_comment'></div>戚君惇学自持，夫人以简淡相之益协。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275654_comment'></div>姑高夫人临诸妇甚严，懔懔如奉槃水，犹莫能当其意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275654_comment'></div>夫人始盥馈拜堂下，高夫人一见大说，游处独进夫人与俱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275654_comment'></div>时有所不乐，愀然危坐，却肉不御，小大侧足，旁睨无敢出一语。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275654_comment'></div>夫人差甘鲜、伺颜色而共之，高夫人每为举匕箸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275654_comment'></div>居无何，高夫人忽得风痹疾，竟其身卧起皆须夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275654_comment'></div>盖归戚氏十有八年，而戚君卒，四子一女皆幼，田财数十亩，族党忧不能济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1275654_comment'></div>夫人攻苦食淡，身处其劳，而佚诸子于学，米盐薪刍之问不至其耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1275654_comment'></div>方未就外傅，《孝经》、《论语》，率夫人口授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1275654_comment'></div>稍长，每反面，必问其所与游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1275654_comment'></div>善士也，则笑语异他日，否则神色辄不怡，故多以谨恪闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1275654_comment'></div>蚕事起，自课甚苦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1275654_comment'></div>诸子晨省，夫人已仆仆筥箔间；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1275654_comment'></div>夜分诵习怠且寝，壁后络织犹未绝也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1275654_comment'></div>丝入有经，口众，不足于衣，则又缕絮缉絁以佐其阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1275654_comment'></div>天暑，汗浃背不休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1275654_comment'></div>诸子更劝夫人少纾其勤，夫人曰：「吾职也，吾敢废职而嬉」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1275654_comment'></div>下至麻枲蔬茹，料理靡密，老农圃者不能加。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1275654_comment'></div>资慈祥，虽呼指婢仆，如恐伤之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1275654_comment'></div>岁时祭享，前事或病，自力戒具，旁舍人曰：「夫人病，意是祭阙矣，昨暮爨下有声，乃能强起乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1275654_comment'></div>季年，长子以进士入官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1275654_comment'></div>间一岁，次子亦游太学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1275654_comment'></div>闾里相谓夫人当喜不自胜，瞷之泊如也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1275654_comment'></div>以淳熙元年二月己卯终于寝，年六十有二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1275654_comment'></div>五月戊戌，祔于县之东阳县午塘坞戚君之兆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1275654_comment'></div>曾祖馀庆，祖旼，父彦昭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1275654_comment'></div>子如圭，迪功郎、新绍兴府嵊县尉，次如玉、如璧、如珵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1275654_comment'></div>女适进士周天麟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1275654_comment'></div>孙女一，尚幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1275654_comment'></div>夫人晚时观书，辄能举大义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1275654_comment'></div>尝读上蔡谢良佐氏《语录》，顾诸子曰：「既不为禄利，复不求人知，斯所谓问学者耶」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1275654_comment'></div>夫人期诸子者盖如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1275654_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_42_1275654'>震风凌雨集初龄，百忧所坚湔明冰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1275654_comment'></div>厥逑既辑琴锵鸣，馌空案坠昼哭声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1275654_comment'></div>四雏未翼巢欹倾，手梭足机口授经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1275654_comment'></div>翩翩相顾骞修翎，可以下报午塘君。</div><div id='poem_sentence_45_1275654_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='bb77543073364bb0b70582ec4b45b42e_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("bb77543073364bb0b70582ec4b45b42e");'><span id='bb77543073364bb0b70582ec4b45b42e_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年</a>，39岁</div><div id='bb77543073364bb0b70582ec4b45b42e' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年3月23日</a>　过衢州访汪应辰，遍访朋旧。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年3月24日</a>　在超化寺见汪筑。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='f123639516b54232994e00b94a6d746a_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("f123639516b54232994e00b94a6d746a");'><span id='f123639516b54232994e00b94a6d746a_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1176&endYear=1176')">1176年</a>，40岁</div><div id='f123639516b54232994e00b94a6d746a' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1176&endYear=1176')">1176年1月12日</a>　以汪应辰去世，亲往三衢哭吊。有祭文，盛赞汪应辰学则正统，文则正宗。作品：《祭汪端明》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷八。）</span><div id='poem_1275705' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275705' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275705?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭汪端明文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1176年1月12日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275705")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275705_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275705'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275705'>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275705_comment'></div>开之大者，若将有属；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275705_comment'></div>聚之粹者，其不徒生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275705_comment'></div>猗众万之弗齐，公取数其独赢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275705_comment'></div>培之以岳，镇之浑厚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275705_comment'></div>瀹之以涧，𤄊之清明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275705_comment'></div>其任重则轶材绝识不能足其志，其道远则贵名显仕不能留其行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275705_comment'></div>既予其资，又乘其会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275705_comment'></div>盖南渡群贤皆在之时，而北方馀论未衰之际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275705_comment'></div>款门墙而遍历，跻堂奥而独诣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275705_comment'></div>合诸老之规摹而融其异同，总一代之统纪而揽其精粹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275705_comment'></div>更侍从于两朝，凛大节之弗渝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275705_comment'></div>虑先根本则或以为缓，动据宪章则或以为拘，奋发陈义则或尤其亟，弥纶藏用则或咎其徐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275705_comment'></div>少而论和，既不诡随于小人之党；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275705_comment'></div>晚而议战，复不苟同于君子之徒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275705_comment'></div>虽娄起而娄仆，守常度而自如。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275705_comment'></div>外屏卫于翰藩，亦大体之可识。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1275705_comment'></div>明振毫末而终出于恕，智兼僚寀而各付以职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1275705_comment'></div>外视高雅而中实密察，外视宽舒而中实肃给。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1275705_comment'></div>填拊经远，不求岁月之效；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1275705_comment'></div>悃愊务实，不事耳目之饰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1275705_comment'></div>虽权胁而势摇，迄岿然而山立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1275705_comment'></div>晚进后出，自相长雄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1275705_comment'></div>广坐众席，旧人罕逢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1275705_comment'></div>大雅之音，尚闻于公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1275705_comment'></div>学则正统，文则正宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1275705_comment'></div>乐易平旷，前辈之风；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1275705_comment'></div>崇深简重，前辈之容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1275705_comment'></div>士骇未见，或姗或攻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1275705_comment'></div>以身存法，独殿其冲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1275705_comment'></div>典刑不坠，繄公之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1275705_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1275705_comment'></div>进退有义，弛张有时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1275705_comment'></div>其用其舍，我不敢知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1275705_comment'></div>至于濩落丛祠之秩，所取者甚狭；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1275705_comment'></div>荒寒萧寺之居，所处者甚卑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1275705_comment'></div>假十数年之寿考，作二三子之指归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1275705_comment'></div>共箪瓢之淡泊，缉简编之阙遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1275705_comment'></div>于造物其何费，乃一夕而夺之！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1275705_comment'></div>然则开之大者，竟复何意；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1275705_comment'></div>聚之粹者，盖亦胡为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1275705_comment'></div>瞻天运之鸿濛，非小夫之所窥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1275705_comment'></div>謼苍旻而上愬，则匪公之素期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1275705_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1275705_comment'></div>继自今以往，镇定大事，顾盼系轻重者不复嗣矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1275705_comment'></div>敷建大论，呼吸判成败者不复闻矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1275705_comment'></div>百年未明之心迹，不复究其实矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1275705_comment'></div>群籍未辨之真赝，不复审其是矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1275705_comment'></div>斯文将安所寄，而斯民将安所徯矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1275705_comment'></div>某佩韘趋隅，木行两周。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1275705_comment'></div>录其世旧，教育绸缪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1275705_comment'></div>肝膈洞照，泯然相投。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1275705_comment'></div>大何理之不讲，细何事之不诹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1275705_comment'></div>幸二邦之接畛，谓卒业之可酬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1275705_comment'></div>阔謦欬其未几，忽赴车之停辀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1275705_comment'></div>亟宿舂而听役，泪淋浪而莫收。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1275705_comment'></div>炯话言之如在，策蹇步而敢媮！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1275705_comment'></div>蠲此心而明荐，夫何有乎醪羞！</div><div id='poem_sentence_57_1275705_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='3742e4ec632e4586871647a9fd68eb90_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("3742e4ec632e4586871647a9fd68eb90");'><span id='3742e4ec632e4586871647a9fd68eb90_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1176&endYear=1176')">1176年</a>，40岁</div><div id='3742e4ec632e4586871647a9fd68eb90' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1176&endYear=1176')">1176年3月28日</a>　赴约往会朱熹于衢州石岩寺，多有论辩。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1176&endYear=1176')">1176年3月</a>　作《祭张季清文》<div id='poem_1275706' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275706' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275706?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭张季清文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1176年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275706")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275706_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275706'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275706'>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275706_comment'></div>游于师友之间，敛然自持，岂其无人！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275706_comment'></div>舍业而归，耳目改前，移养铄夺，不失其初心者，盖或寡矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275706_comment'></div>子之在吾门，侃侃和饬，执经不怠，于是时犹未知其为独异也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275706_comment'></div>自我不见，于今五年，有来自西者，皆道子于兄弟无违言，于里闾无违行，安常谨礼，不受变于俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275706_comment'></div>吾方喜于得子，迨此暇日，将过子之庐，而子则死矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275706_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275706_comment'></div>庠序之籍日增，而务实之士不加。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275706_comment'></div>益一觞之恸，岂独故旧之情而已哉！</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1275706_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1176&endYear=1176')">1176年春</a>　致书周必大荐举刘清之，且勉周必大积极进取。作品：《与周丞相》七。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史别集》卷九。）</span><div id='poem_1275281' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275281' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275281?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与周丞相子充书<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其十五 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1176年春）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275281")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275281_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275281'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275281'>某荐辱教况，不胜感尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275281_comment'></div>春来气候不齐，医者深戒作劳，故久不拜状，然惓惓尊仰，则未始忘也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275281_comment'></div>其病躯萎痹，虽无增损，然心闲事省，神思却胜前冬侍坐时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275281_comment'></div>但常保此，幸已多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275281_comment'></div>钦夫之传，极为之惊忧，第细观牍尾乃二十七日，距二日已两旬，不应江陵尚未申到，犹觊消息之不真也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275281_comment'></div>元晦为人不耐，前此娄尝箴切之，候有便当委曲晓譬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275281_comment'></div>但不若调护，且令得祠，乃所以爱之也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1275281_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1176&endYear=1176')">1176年春</a>　与叶衡等同游南园，有诗。作品：《次韵叶丞相陈尚书游南园》<div id='poem_94092' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_94092' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/94092?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵叶丞相陈尚书游南园<span class='inlineComment2'>（淳熙三年春）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1176年春）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_94092")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_94092_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_94092'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_94092'>乐事良辰古所难，三分春色一分宽。<div id='poem_sentence_0_94092_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_94092'>润花雨过红裙湿，倚竹风斜翠袖寒。<div id='poem_sentence_1_94092_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_94092'>自有南堂谁举白，可无东绢为施丹。<div id='poem_sentence_2_94092_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_94092'>两翁醉墨曾题品，便作平泉草木看。<div id='poem_sentence_3_94092_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_94092'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_94092_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1176&endYear=1176')">1176年春</a>　为何叔京作挽章。作品：《何叔京挽章二首》<div id='poem_94095' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_94095' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/94095?labeling=true' target='_blank'>何叔京挽章二首<span class='inlineComment2'>（镐　淳熙三年）</span><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1176年春）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_94095")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_94095_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_94095'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_94095'>濮州以谏死，何氏得其真。<div id='poem_sentence_0_94095_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_94095'>天下中庸义，人间父子亲。<div id='poem_sentence_1_94095_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_94095'>再传犹易简，小出复逡巡。<div id='poem_sentence_2_94095_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_94095'>埋骨虽南土，倾心向北辰。<div id='poem_sentence_3_94095_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_94095'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_94095_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_94094' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_94094' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/94094?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1176年春）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_94094_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_94094'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_94094'>倾盖黄亭夜，翛然涧壑姿。<div id='poem_sentence_0_94094_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_94094'>倚天唯直干，到地绝旁枝。<div id='poem_sentence_1_94094_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_94094'>亹亹今何许，悠悠只自知。<div id='poem_sentence_2_94094_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_94094'>寒碑卧风雨，千载有深期。<div id='poem_sentence_3_94094_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_94094'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_94094_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1176&endYear=1176')">1176年4月4日</a>　作《题近思录》，说编撰次第及用意。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《东莱吕太史文集》卷七。）</span><div id='poem_1275516' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275516' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275516?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题近思录</a><span class='authorDate'>（1176年4月4日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25154, "南宋", "吕祖谦", "poem_title_1275516")'>吕祖谦</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275516_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275516'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275516'>《近思录》既成，或疑首卷阴阳变化性命之说，大氐非始学者之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275516_comment'></div>某窃尝与闻次辑之意，后出晚进，于义理之本原，虽未容骤语，苟茫然不识其梗概，则亦何所底止？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275516_comment'></div>列之篇端，特使之知其名义，有所向望而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275516_comment'></div>至于馀卷所载讲学之方，日用躬行之实，具有科级，循是而进，自卑升高，自近及远，庶几不失纂集之指。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275516_comment'></div>若乃厌卑近而骛高远，躐等淩节，流于空虚，迄无所依据，则岂所谓近思者耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275516_comment'></div>览者宜详之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1275516_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1176&endYear=1176')">1176年4月10日</a>　辞别朱熹，自三衢归。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
崇安街道（崇安）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='a7907d6963a34d009bd6227302e0b56c_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("a7907d6963a34d009bd6227302e0b56c");'><span id='a7907d6963a34d009bd6227302e0b56c_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年</a>，39岁</div><div id='a7907d6963a34d009bd6227302e0b56c' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年3月29日</a>　邂逅张体仁、李俨、李侃兄弟。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年4月1日</a>　至武夷五夫访朱熹，馆于朱熹书室。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年4月2日</a>　在五夫见刘充甫、刘平甫、范瑄等。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年4月3日</a>　与朱熹、潘景愈、刘充甫、刘平甫、范瑄同游刘氏园，报本庵。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年4月4日</a>　与朱熹、潘景愈、刘充甫、刘平甫、范瑄、徐周宾同游密庵，遂宿。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年4月5日</a>　自密庵返五夫，王光朝来见。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年4月13日</a>　与朱熹同考《吕氏乡约》、《蓝田吕氏乡仪》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年4月</a>　观朱熹社仓赈贷，欲归后纠结士友，自出谷物，赈恤乡民，效法为之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年4月21日</a>　同至朱熹寒泉精舍，共阅关洛诸书，同编《近思录》。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年4月</a>　在寒泉精舍商议删定《程氏遗书》为《程子格言》<br /></div><div class='label1' id='7d41ace6f79a4b658dcbbbdb956039fd_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("7d41ace6f79a4b658dcbbbdb956039fd");'><span id='7d41ace6f79a4b658dcbbbdb956039fd_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年</a>，39岁</div><div id='7d41ace6f79a4b658dcbbbdb956039fd' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>同年时铸之父时汝功卒，有吊问。<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>朱熹送吕祖谦离闽赴铅山鹅湖。<br /></div>
-----end

id='poem_sentence_0_94053'>五年不说空山雨，今夜鱼梁著钓船。<div id='poem_sentence_0_94053_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_94053'>为问故人今健否，桄榔叶暗瘴江边。<div class='authorDate'>（1175年4月28日）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_94052_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_94052'><div class='poemSentence' -----title
铅山
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='3cb0713ac90f40aeb0696231e8549156_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("3cb0713ac90f40aeb0696231e8549156");'><span id='3cb0713ac90f40aeb0696231e8549156_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年</a>，39岁</div><div id='3cb0713ac90f40aeb0696231e8549156' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年5月</a>　下旬至鹅湖寺，鹅湖之会。陆九龄、陆九渊、赵景昭、赵景明、刘清之、詹体仁、徐季益等同至论学。朱熹与陆氏兄弟初识。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年5月</a>　接潘景宪来书并复，教导门人。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年6月8日</a>　与诸人道别归婺。与朱熹有再游天台之约。<br /></div>
-----end
